iliad.
 



book i.
 

argument.[40]
 

contention achilles agamemnon.
 

war troy, greeks sacked neighbouring
 towns, taken thence two beautiful captives, chryseïs and
 briseïs, allotted first agamemnon, last achilles.
 chryses, father chryseïs, priest apollo, comes the
 grecian camp ransom her; action poem opens, in
 tenth year siege. priest refused, insolently
 dismissed agamemnon, entreats vengeance god; who
 inflicts pestilence greeks. achilles calls council, and
 encourages chalcas declare cause it; attributes the
 refusal chryseïs. king, obliged send back captive,
 enters furious contest achilles, nestor pacifies;
 however, absolute command army, seizes on
 briseïs revenge. achilles discontent withdraws his
 forces rest greeks; complaining thetis, she
 supplicates jupiter render sensible wrong done her
 son, giving victory trojans. jupiter, granting suit,
 incenses juno: debate runs high, till are
 reconciled address vulcan.
 time two-and-twenty days taken book: nine
 plague, one council quarrel princes,
 twelve jupiter’s stay Æthiopians, whose return
 thetis prefers petition. scene lies grecian camp,
 changes chrysa, lastly olympus.
 

achilles’ wrath, greece direful spring
 woes unnumber’d, heavenly goddess, sing!
 wrath hurl’d pluto’s gloomy reign
 souls mighty chiefs untimely slain;
 whose limbs unburied naked shore,
 devouring dogs hungry vultures tore.[41]
 since great achilles atrides strove,
 sovereign doom, will jove![42]
 
declare, muse! ill-fated hour[43]
 sprung fierce strife, offended power
 latona’s dire contagion spread,[44]
 heap’d camp mountains dead;
 king men reverent priest defied,[45]
 king’s offence people died.
 
chryses sought costly gifts gain
 captive daughter victor’s chain.
 suppliant venerable father stands;
 apollo’s awful ensigns grace hands:
 begs; lowly bending down,
 extends sceptre laurel crown.
 sued all, chief implored grace
 brother-kings, atreus’ royal race[46]
 
“ye kings warriors! may vows crown’d,
 troy’s proud walls lie level ground.
 may jove restore toils o’er
 safe pleasures native shore.
 but, oh! relieve wretched parent’s pain,
 give chryseïs arms again;
 mercy fail, yet let presents move,
 dread avenging phœbus, jove.”
 
greeks shouts joint assent declare,
 priest reverence, release fair.
 atrides; he, kingly pride,
 repulsed sacred sire, thus replied:
 “hence thy life, fly hostile plains,
 ask, presumptuous, king detains:
 
hence, thy laurel crown, golden rod,
 trust far ensigns thy god.
 mine thy daughter, priest, shall remain;
 prayers, tears, bribes, shall plead vain;
 till time shall rifle every youthful grace,
 age dismiss cold embrace,
 daily labours loom employ’d,
 doom’d deck bed enjoy’d.
 hence then; argos shall maid retire,
 far native soil weeping sire.”
 

[illustration: ] homer invoking muse
 

trembling priest along shore return’d,
 anguish father mourn’d.
 disconsolate, daring complain,
 silent wander’d sounding main;
 till, safe distance, god prays,
 god darts around world rays.
 
“o smintheus! sprung fair latona’s line,[47]
 thou guardian power cilla divine,[48]
 thou source light! tenedos adores,
 whose bright presence gilds thy chrysa’s shores.
 e’er wreaths hung thy sacred fane,[49]
 fed flames fat oxen slain;
 god silver bow! thy shafts employ,
 avenge thy servant, greeks destroy.”
 
thus chryses pray’d:—the favouring power attends,
 olympus’ lofty tops descends.
 bent bow, grecian hearts wound;[50]
 fierce moved, silver shafts resound.
 breathing revenge, sudden night spread,
 gloomy darkness roll’d head.
 fleet view, twang’d deadly bow,
 hissing fly feather’d fates below.
 mules dogs infection first began;[51]
 last, vengeful arrows fix’d man.
 nine long nights, dusky air,
 pyres, thick-flaming, shot dismal glare.
 ere tenth revolving day run,
 inspired juno, thetis’ godlike son
 convened council grecian train;
 much goddess mourn’d heroes slain.[52]
 assembly seated, rising o’er rest,
 achilles thus king men address’d:
 
“why leave fatal trojan shore,
 measure back seas cross’d before?
 plague destroying sword spare,
 ’tis time save remains war.
 let prophet, sacred sage,
 explore cause great apollo’s rage;
 learn wasteful vengeance remove
 mystic dreams, dreams descend jove.[53]
 broken vows heavy curse laid,
 let altars smoke, hecatombs paid.
 heaven, atoned, shall dying greece restore,
 phœbus dart burning shafts more.”
 
said, sat: chalcas thus replied;
 chalcas wise, grecian priest guide,
 sacred seer, whose comprehensive view,
 past, present, future knew:
 uprising slow, venerable sage
 thus spoke prudence fears age:
 
“beloved jove, achilles! would’st thou know
 angry phœbus bends fatal bow?
 first give thy faith, plight prince’s word
 sure protection, thy power sword:
 must speak wisdom conceal,
 truths, invidious great, reveal,
 bold task, subjects, grown wise,
 instruct monarch error lies;
 though deem short-lived fury past,
 ’tis sure mighty will revenge last.”
 pelides:—“from thy inmost soul
 speak thou know’st, speak without control.
 e’en god swear rules day,
 thy hands vows greece convey.
 whose bless’d oracles thy lips declare;
 long achilles breathes vital air,
 daring greek, numerous band,
 priest shall lift impious hand;
 e’en chief hosts led,
 king kings, shall touch sacred head.”
 
encouraged thus, blameless man replies:
 “nor vows unpaid, slighted sacrifice,
 he, chief, provoked raging pest,
 apollo’s vengeance injured priest.
 will god’s awaken’d fury cease,
 plagues shall spread, funeral fires increase,
 till great king, without ransom paid,
 chrysa send black-eyed maid.[54]
 perhaps, added sacrifice prayer,
 priest may pardon, god may spare.”
 
prophet spoke: gloomy frown
 monarch started shining throne;
 black choler fill’d breast boil’d ire,
 eye-balls flash’d living fire:
 “augur accursed! denouncing mischief still,
 prophet plagues, ever boding ill!
 still must tongue wounding message bring,
 still thy priestly pride provoke thy king?
 phœbus’ oracles explored,
 teach greeks murmur lord?
 falsehood honour stain’d,
 heaven offended, priest profaned;
 prize, beauteous maid, hold,
 heavenly charms prefer proffer’d gold?
 maid, unmatch’d manners face,
 skill’d art, crown’d every grace;
 half dear clytæmnestra’s charms,
 first blooming beauties bless’d arms.
 yet, gods demand her, let sail;
 cares public weal:
 let deem’d hateful cause all,
 suffer, rather people fall.
 prize, beauteous prize, will resign,
 dearly valued, justly mine.
 since common good yield fair,
 private loss let grateful greece repair;
 unrewarded let prince complain,
 alone fought bled vain.”
 “insatiate king (achilles thus replies),
 fond power, fonder prize!
 would’st thou greeks lawful prey yield,
 due reward many well-fought field?
 
spoils cities razed warriors slain,
 share justice, toil gain;
 resume whate’er thy avarice craves
 (that trick tyrants) may borne slaves.
 yet chief plunder fight,
 spoils ilion shall thy loss requite,
 whene’er, jove’s decree, conquering powers
 shall humble dust lofty towers.”
 
thus king: “shall prize resign
 tame content, thou possess’d thine?
 great thou art, like god fight,
 think rob soldier’s right.
 thy demand shall restore maid?
 first let just equivalent paid;
 king might ask; let be
 treasure worthy her, worthy me.
 grant this, monarch’s claim
 hand shall seize captive dame.
 mighty ajax shall prize resign;[55]
 ulysses’ spoils, even thy own, mine.
 man suffers, loudly may complain;
 rage may, shall rage vain.
 time requires.—it now remains
 launch bark plough watery plains,
 waft sacrifice chrysa’s shores,
 chosen pilots, labouring oars.
 soon shall fair sable ship ascend,
 deputed prince charge attend:
 creta’s king, ajax shall fulfil,
 wise ulysses see perform’d will;
 or, royal pleasure shall ordain,
 achilles’ self conduct o’er main;
 let fierce achilles, dreadful rage,
 god propitiate, pest assuage.”
 

[illustration: ] mars
 

this, pelides, frowning stern, replied:
 “o tyrant, arm’d insolence pride!
 inglorious slave interest, ever join’d
 fraud, unworthy royal mind!
 generous greek, obedient thy word,
 shall form ambush, shall lift sword?
 cause war thy decree?
 distant trojans never injured me;
 phthia’s realms hostile troops led:
 safe vales warlike coursers fed;
 far hence removed, hoarse-resounding main,
 walls rocks, secure native reign,
 whose fruitful soil luxuriant harvests grace,
 rich fruits, martial race.
 hither sail’d, voluntary throng,
 avenge private, public wrong:
 else troy assembled nations draws,
 thine, ungrateful, thy brother’s cause?
 pay blood toils deserve;
 disgraced injured man serve?
 darest thou threat snatch prize away,
 due deeds many dreadful day?
 prize small, tyrant! match’d thine,
 thy actions compared mine.
 thine conquest wealthy prey,
 though mine sweat danger day.
 trivial present ships bear:
 barren praises pay wounds war.
 know, proud monarch, i’m thy slave more;
 fleet shall waft thessalia’s shore:
 left achilles trojan plain,
 spoils, conquests, shall atrides gain?”
 
king: “fly, mighty warrior! fly;
 thy aid need not, thy threats defy.
 want chiefs cause fight,
 jove shall guard monarch’s right.
 kings (the god’s distinguish’d care)
 power superior none hatred bear:
 strife debate thy restless soul employ,
 wars horrors thy savage joy,
 thou hast strength, ’twas heaven strength bestow’d;
 know, vain man! thy valour god.
 haste, launch thy vessels, fly speed away;
 rule thy realms arbitrary sway;
 heed thee not, prize equal rate
 thy short-lived friendship, thy groundless hate.
 go, threat thy earth-born myrmidons:—but here[56]
 ’tis mine threaten, prince, thine fear.
 know, god beauteous dame demand,
 bark shall waft native land;
 prepare, imperious prince! prepare,
 fierce thou art, yield thy captive fair:
 even thy tent i’ll seize blooming prize,
 thy loved briseïs radiant eyes.
 hence shalt thou prove might, curse hour
 thou stood’st rival imperial power;
 hence, hosts shall known,
 kings subject gods alone.”
 
achilles heard, grief rage oppress’d,
 heart swell’d high, labour’d breast;
 distracting thoughts turns bosom ruled;
 now fired wrath, now reason cool’d:
 prompts hand draw deadly sword,
 force greeks, pierce haughty lord;
 whispers soft vengeance control,
 calm rising tempest soul.
 just anguish suspense stay’d,
 half unsheathed appear’d glittering blade,[57]
 minerva swift descended above,
 sent sister wife jove
 (for princes claim’d equal care);
 behind stood, golden hair
 achilles seized; alone confess’d;
 sable cloud conceal’d rest.
 sees, sudden goddess cries,
 known flames sparkle eyes:
 

[illustration: ] minerva repressing fury achilles
 

“descends minerva, guardian care,
 heavenly witness wrongs bear
 atreus’ son?—then let eyes view
 daring crime, behold vengeance too.”
 
“forbear (the progeny jove replies)
 calm thy fury forsake skies:
 let great achilles, gods resign’d,
 reason yield empire o’er mind.
 awful juno command given;
 king care heaven.
 force keen reproaches let feel;
 sheathe, obedient, thy revenging steel.
 pronounce (and trust heavenly power)
 thy injured honour fated hour,
 proud monarch shall thy arms implore,
 bribe thy friendship boundless store.
 let revenge longer bear sway;
 command thy passions, gods obey.”
 
pelides:—“with regardful ear,
 ’tis just, goddess! thy dictates hear.
 hard is, vengeance suppress:
 revere gods gods will bless.”
 said, observant blue-eyed maid;
 sheath return’d shining blade.
 goddess swift high olympus flies,
 joins sacred senate skies.
 
yet rage boiling breast forsook,
 thus redoubling atrides broke:
 “o monster! mix’d insolence fear,
 thou dog forehead, heart deer!
 wert thou known ambush’d fights dare,
 nobly face horrid front war?
 ’tis ours, chance fighting fields try;
 thine look on, bid valiant die:
 much ’tis safer camp go,
 rob subject, despoil foe.
 scourge thy people, violent base!
 sent jove’s anger slavish race;
 who, lost sense generous freedom past,
 tamed wrongs;—or thy last.
 now sacred sceptre hear swear,
 never shall leaves blossoms bear,
 sever’d trunk (as thee)
 bare mountains left parent tree;
 sceptre, form’d temper’d steel prove
 ensign delegates jove,
 power laws justice springs
 (tremendous oath! inviolate kings);
 swear:—when bleeding greece again
 shall call achilles, shall call vain.
 when, flush’d slaughter, hector comes spread
 purpled shore mountains dead,
 shalt thou mourn affront thy madness gave,
 forced deplore impotent save:
 rage bitterness soul know
 act made bravest greek thy foe.”
 
spoke; furious hurl’d ground
 sceptre starr’d golden studs around:
 sternly silent sat. like disdain
 raging king return’d frowns again.
 
calm passion words age,
 slow seat arose pylian sage,
 experienced nestor, persuasion skill’d;
 words, sweet honey, lips distill’d:[58]
 two generations now pass’d away,
 wise rules, happy sway;
 two ages o’er native realm reign’d,
 now example third remain’d.
 view’d awe venerable man;
 thus mild benevolence began:—
 
“what shame, woe greece! joy
 troy’s proud monarch, friends troy!
 adverse gods commit stern debate
 best, bravest, grecian state.
 young ye are, youthful heat restrain,
 think nestor’s years wisdom vain.
 godlike race heroes knew,
 aged eyes shall view!
 lives chief match pirithous’ fame,
 dryas bold, ceneus’ deathless name;
 theseus, endued mortal might,
 polyphemus, like gods fight?
 old, toils battle bred,
 early youth hardy days led;
 fired thirst virtuous envy breeds,
 smit love honourable deeds,
 strongest men, pierced mountain boar,
 ranged wild deserts red monsters’ gore,
 hills shaggy centaurs tore:
 yet soft persuasive arts sway’d;
 nestor spoke, listen’d obey’d.
 youth, even esteem’d wise;
 you, young warriors, hear age advise.
 atrides, seize beauteous slave;
 prize greeks common suffrage gave:
 thou, achilles, treat prince pride;
 let kings just, sovereign power preside.
 thee, first honours war adorn,
 like gods strength, goddess born;
 him, awful majesty exalts above
 powers earth, sceptred sons jove.
 let unite well-consenting mind,
 shall authority strength join’d.
 leave me, king! calm achilles’ rage;
 rule thou thyself, advanced age.
 forbid it, gods! achilles lost,
 pride greece, bulwark host.”
 
said, ceased. king men replies:
 “thy years awful, thy words wise.
 imperious, unconquer’d soul,
 laws can limit, respect control.
 pride must superiors fall;
 word law, lord all?
 must hosts, chiefs, ourself obey?
 king can bear rival sway?
 grant gods matchless force given;
 foul reproach privilege heaven?”
 
monarch’s speech achilles broke,
 furious, thus, interrupting spoke:
 “tyrant, well deserved thy galling chain,
 live thy slave, still serve vain,
 submit unjust decree:—
 command thy vassals, command me.
 seize briseïs, grecians doom’d
 prize war, yet tamely see resumed;
 seize secure; achilles draws
 conquering sword woman’s cause.
 gods command forgive past:
 let first invasion last:
 know, thy blood, next thou darest invade,
 shall stream vengeance reeking blade.”
 
ceased: stern debate expired:
 chiefs sullen majesty retired.
 
achilles patroclus took way
 near tents hollow vessels lay.
 meantime atrides launch’d numerous oars
 well-rigg’d ship chrysa’s sacred shores:
 high deck fair chryseïs placed,
 sage ulysses conduct graced:
 safe sides hecatomb stow’d,
 swiftly sailing, cut liquid road.
 
host expiate next king prepares,
 pure lustrations, solemn prayers.
 wash’d briny wave, pious train[59]
 cleansed; cast ablutions main.
 along shore whole hecatombs laid,
 bulls goats phœbus’ altars paid;
 sable fumes curling spires arise,
 waft grateful odours skies.
 
army thus sacred rites engaged,
 atrides still deep resentment raged.
 wait will two sacred heralds stood,
 talthybius eurybates good.
 “haste fierce achilles’ tent (he cries),
 thence bear briseïs royal prize:
 submit must; will part,
 ourself arms shall tear heart.”
 
unwilling heralds act lord’s commands;
 pensive walk along barren sands:
 arrived, hero tent find,
 gloomy aspect arm reclined.
 awful distance long silent stand,
 loth advance, speak hard command;
 decent confusion! godlike man
 perceived, thus accent mild began:
 
“with leave honour enter abodes,
 ye sacred ministers men gods![60]
 know message; constraint came;
 you, imperious lord blame.
 patroclus, haste, fair briseïs bring;
 conduct captive haughty king.
 witness, heralds, proclaim vow,
 witness gods above, men below!
 first, loudest, prince declare
 (that lawless tyrant whose commands bear),
 unmoved death achilles shall remain,
 though prostrate greece shall bleed every vein:
 raging chief frantic passion lost,
 blind himself, useless host,
 unskill’d judge future past,
 blood slaughter shall repent last.”
 

[illustration: ] departure briseis tent achilles
 

patroclus now unwilling beauty brought;
 she, soft sorrows, pensive thought,
 pass’d silent, heralds held hand,
 oft look’d back, slow-moving o’er strand.
 loss fierce achilles bore;
 sad, retiring sounding shore,
 o’er wild margin deep hung,
 kindred deep whence mother sprung:[61]
 bathed tears anger disdain,
 thus loud lamented stormy main:
 
“o parent goddess! since early bloom
 thy must fall, severe doom;
 sure short race glory born,
 great jove justice span adorn:
 honour fame least thunderer owed;
 ill pays promise god,
 yon proud monarch thus thy defies,
 obscures glories, resumes prize.”
 
far deep recesses main,
 aged ocean holds watery reign,
 goddess-mother heard. waves divide;
 like mist rose tide;
 beheld mourning naked shores,
 thus sorrows soul explores.
 “why grieves son? thy anguish let share;
 reveal cause, trust parent’s care.”
 
deeply sighing said: “to tell woe
 mention well know.
 thebé, sacred apollo’s name[62]
 (aëtion’s realm), conquering army came,
 treasure loaded triumphant spoils,
 whose just division crown’d soldier’s toils;
 bright chryseïs, heavenly prize! led,
 vote selected, general’s bed.
 priest phœbus sought gifts gain
 beauteous daughter victor’s chain;
 fleet reach’d, and, lowly bending down,
 held forth sceptre laurel crown,
 intreating all; chief implored grace
 brother-kings atreus’ royal race:
 generous greeks joint consent declare,
 priest reverence, release fair;
 atrides: he, wonted pride,
 sire insulted, gifts denied:
 insulted sire (his god’s peculiar care)
 phœbus pray’d, phœbus heard prayer:
 dreadful plague ensues: avenging darts
 incessant fly, pierce grecian hearts.
 prophet then, inspired heaven, arose,
 points crime, thence derives woes:
 first assembled chiefs incline
 avert vengeance power divine;
 rising wrath, monarch storm’d;
 incensed threaten’d, threats perform’d:
 fair chryseïs sire sent,
 offer’d gifts make god relent;
 now seized briseïs’ heavenly charms,
 valour’s prize defrauds arms,
 defrauds votes grecian train;[63]
 service, faith, justice, plead vain.
 but, goddess! thou thy suppliant attend.
 high olympus’ shining court ascend,
 urge ties former service owed,
 sue vengeance thundering god.
 oft hast thou triumph’d glorious boast,
 thou stood’st forth ethereal host,
 bold rebellion shook realms above,
 undaunted guard cloud-compelling jove:
 bright partner awful reign,
 warlike maid, monarch main,
 traitor-gods, mad ambition driven,
 durst threat chains omnipotence heaven.
 then, call’d thee, monster titan came
 (whom gods briareus, men Ægeon name),
 wondering skies enormous stalk’d along;
 shakes solid earth strong:
 giant-pride jove’s high throne stands,
 brandish’d round hundred hands:
 affrighted gods confess’d awful lord,
 dropp’d fetters, trembled, adored.[64]
 this, goddess, remembrance call,
 embrace knees, tribunal fall;
 conjure far drive grecian train,
 hurl headlong fleet main,
 heap shores copious death, bring
 greeks know curse king.
 let agamemnon lift haughty head
 o’er wide dominion dead,
 mourn blood e’er durst disgrace
 boldest warrior grecian race.”
 

[illustration: ] thetis calling briareus assistance jupiter
 

“unhappy son! (fair thetis thus replies,
 tears celestial trickle eyes)
 borne thee mother’s throes,
 fates averse, nursed future woes?[65]
 short space light heaven view!
 short space! fill’d sorrow too!
 might parent’s careful wish prevail,
 far, far ilion thy vessels sail,
 thou, camps remote, danger shun
 now, alas! nearly threats son.
 yet (what can) move thy suit i’ll go
 great olympus crown’d fleecy snow.
 meantime, secure within thy ships, far
 behold field, mingle war.
 sire gods ethereal train,
 warm limits farthest main,
 now mix mortals, disdain grace
 feasts Æthiopia’s blameless race,[66]
 twelve days powers indulge genial rite,
 returning twelfth revolving light.
 will mount brazen dome, move
 high tribunal immortal jove.”
 
goddess spoke: rolling waves unclose;
 steep plunged whence rose,
 left sorrowing lonely coast,
 wild resentment fair lost.
 
chrysa’s port now sage ulysses rode;
 beneath deck destined victims stow’d:
 sails furl’d, lash mast aside,
 dropp’d anchors, pinnace tied.
 next shore hecatomb land;
 chryseïs last descending strand.
 her, thus returning furrow’d main,
 ulysses led phœbus’ sacred fane;
 solemn altar, maid
 gave chryses, thus hero said:
 
“hail, reverend priest! phœbus’ awful dome
 suppliant great atrides come:
 unransom’d, receive spotless fair;
 accept hecatomb greeks prepare;
 may thy god scatters darts around,
 atoned sacrifice, desist wound.”[67]
 
this, sire embraced maid again,
 sadly lost, lately sought vain.
 near altar darting king,
 disposed rank hecatomb bring;
 water purify hands, take
 sacred offering salted cake;
 thus arms devoutly raised air,
 solemn voice, priest directs prayer:
 
“god silver bow, thy ear incline,
 whose power incircles cilla divine;
 whose sacred eye thy tenedos surveys,
 gilds fair chrysa distinguish’d rays!
 if, fired vengeance thy priest’s request,
 thy direful darts inflict raging pest:
 attend! avert wasteful woe,
 smile propitious, unbend thy bow.”
 
chryses pray’d. apollo heard prayer:
 now greeks hecatomb prepare;
 horns salted barley threw,
 and, heads heaven, victims slew:[68]
 limbs sever inclosing hide;
 thighs, selected gods, divide:
 these, double cauls involved art,
 choicest morsels lay every part.
 priest altar stands,
 burns offering holy hands.
 pours black wine, sees flames aspire;
 youth instruments surround fire:
 thighs thus sacrificed, entrails dress’d,
 assistants part, transfix, roast rest:
 spread tables, repast prepare;
 takes seat, receives share.
 now rage hunger repress’d,
 pure libations conclude feast;
 youths wine copious goblets crown’d,[69]
 and, pleased, dispense flowing bowls around
 hymns divine joyous banquet ends,
 pæans lengthen’d till sun descends:
 greeks, restored, grateful notes prolong;
 apollo listens, approves song.
 
’twas night; chiefs beside vessel lie,
 till rosy morn purpled o’er sky:
 launch, hoist mast: indulgent gales,
 supplied phœbus, fill swelling sails;
 milk-white canvas bellying blow,
 parted ocean foams roars below:
 bounding billows swift flew,
 till now grecian camp appear’d view.
 far beach haul bark land,
 (the crooked keel divides yellow sand,)
 part, stretch’d along winding bay,
 ships tents mingled prospect lay.
 
raging still, amidst navy sat
 stern achilles, stedfast hate;
 mix’d combat, council join’d;
 wasting cares lay heavy mind:
 black thoughts revenge slaughter roll,
 scenes blood rise dreadful soul.
 
twelve days past, now dawning light
 gods summon’d olympian height:
 jove, first ascending watery bowers,
 leads long order ethereal powers.
 when, like morning-mist early day,
 rose flood daughter sea:
 seats divine flight address’d.
 there, far apart, high rest,
 thunderer sat; old olympus shrouds
 hundred heads heaven, props clouds.
 suppliant goddess stood: one hand placed
 beneath beard, one knees embraced.
 “if e’er, father gods! (she said)
 words please thee, actions aid,
 marks honour bestow,
 pay glory life owe.
 fame least heavenly promise due
 life short, now dishonour’d too.
 avenge wrong, ever just wise!
 let greece humbled, trojans rise;
 till proud king achaian race
 shall heap honours now disgrace.”
 

[illustration: ] thetis entreating jupiter honour achilles
 

thus thetis spoke; jove silence held
 sacred counsels breast conceal’d.
 repulsed, goddess closer press’d,
 still grasp’d knees, urged dear request.
 “o sire gods men! thy suppliant hear;
 refuse, grant; jove fear?
 oh! declare, powers above,
 wretched thetis least care jove?”
 
said; and, sighing, thus god replies,
 rolls thunder o’er vaulted skies:
 
“what hast thou ask’d? ah, jove engage
 foreign contests domestic rage,
 gods’ complaints, juno’s fierce alarms,
 i, partial, aid trojan arms?
 go, lest haughty partner sway
 jealous eyes thy close access survey;
 part peace, secure thy prayer sped:
 witness sacred honours head,
 nod ratifies will divine,
 faithful, fix’d, irrevocable sign;
 seals thy suit, fulfils thy vows—”
 spoke, awful bends sable brows,[70]
 shakes ambrosial curls, gives nod,
 stamp fate sanction god:
 high heaven trembling dread signal took,
 olympus centre shook.[71]
 
swift seas profound goddess flies,
 jove starry mansions skies.
 shining synod immortals wait
 coming god, thrones state
 arising silent, wrapp’d holy fear,
 majesty heaven appear.
 trembling stand, jove assumes throne,
 all, god’s imperious queen alone:
 late view’d silver-footed dame,
 passions kindled flame.
 “say, artful manager heaven (she cries),
 now partakes secrets skies?
 thy juno knows decrees fate,
 vain partner imperial state.
 favourite goddess cares divides,
 jove prudence consort hides?”
 
thunderer: “seek thou find
 sacred counsels almighty mind:
 involved darkness lies great decree,
 can depths fate pierced thee.
 fits thy knowledge, thou first shalt know;
 first gods above, men below;
 thou, they, shall search thoughts roll
 deep close recesses soul.”
 
full sire goddess skies
 roll’d large orbs majestic eyes,
 thus return’d:—“austere saturnius, say,
 whence wrath, controls thy sway?
 thy boundless will, me, remains force,
 thy counsels take destined course.
 ’tis greece fear: late seen,
 close consult, silver-footed queen.
 jove thetis nothing deny,
 signal vain shook sky.
 fatal favour goddess won,
 grace fierce, inexorable son?
 perhaps grecian blood drench plain,
 glut vengeance people slain.”
 
thus god: “o restless fate pride,
 strives learn heaven resolves hide;
 vain search, presumptuous abhorr’d,
 anxious thee, odious thy lord.
 let suffice: immutable decree
 force can shake: is, be.
 goddess, submit; dare will withstand,
 dread power avenging hand:
 united strength gods above
 vain resists omnipotence jove.”
 

[illustration: ] vulcan
 

thunderer spoke, durst queen reply;
 reverent horror silenced sky.
 feast disturb’d, sorrow vulcan saw
 mother menaced, gods awe;
 peace heart, pleasure design,
 thus interposed architect divine:
 “the wretched quarrels mortal state
 far unworthy, gods! debate:
 let men days senseless strife employ,
 we, eternal peace constant joy.
 thou, goddess-mother, sire comply,
 break sacred union sky:
 lest, roused rage, shake bless’d abodes,
 launch red lightning, dethrone gods.
 submit, thunderer stands appeased;
 gracious power willing pleased.”
 
thus vulcan spoke: rising bound,
 double bowl sparkling nectar crown’d,[72]
 held juno cheerful way,
 “goddess (he cried), patient obey.
 dear are, jove arm extend,
 can grieve, unable defend.
 god daring aid move,
 lift hand force jove?
 cause felt matchless might,
 hurl’d headlong ethereal height;[73]
 toss’d day rapid circles round,
 till sun descended touch’d ground.
 breathless fell, giddy motion lost;
 sinthians raised lemnian coast;[74]
 
said, hands goblet heaved,
 which, smile, white-arm’d queen received
 then, rest fill’d; turn,
 lips applied nectar’d urn,
 vulcan awkward grace office plies,
 unextinguish’d laughter shakes skies.
 
thus blest gods genial day prolong,
 feasts ambrosial, celestial song.[75]
 apollo tuned lyre; muses round
 voice alternate aid silver sound.
 meantime radiant sun mortal sight
 descending swift, roll’d rapid light:
 starry domes gods depart,
 shining monuments vulcan’s art:
 jove couch reclined awful head,
 juno slumber’d golden bed.

[illustration: ] apotheosis homer
 



book ii.
 

argument.
 

trial army, catalogue forces.
 

jupiter, pursuance request thetis, sends deceitful
 vision agamemnon, persuading lead army battle, in
 order make greeks sensible want achilles. the
 general, deluded hopes taking troy without his
 assistance, fears army discouraged absence, the
 late plague, well length time, contrives make trial
 disposition stratagem. first communicates design
 princes council, propose return the
 soldiers, put stop proposal was
 embraced. assembles whole host, upon moving a
 return greece, unanimously agree it, run prepare the
 ships. detained management ulysses, chastises
 insolence thersites. assembly recalled, several speeches
 made occasion, length advice nestor followed,
 make general muster troops, divide them
 several nations, proceeded battle. gives
 occasion poet enumerate forces greeks and
 trojans, large catalogue.
 time employed book consists entirely one day.
 scene lies grecian camp, upon sea-shore; towards
 end removes troy.
 

now pleasing sleep seal’d mortal eye,
 stretch’d tents grecian leaders lie:
 immortals slumber’d thrones above;
 all, ever-wakeful eyes jove.[76]
 honour thetis’ bends care,
 plunge greeks woes war:
 bids empty phantom rise sight,
 thus commands vision night.
 
“fly hence, deluding dream! light air,[77]
 agamemnon’s ample tent repair.
 bid arms draw forth embattled train,
 lead grecians dusty plain.
 declare, e’en now ’tis given destroy
 lofty towers wide-extended troy.
 now gods fate contend,
 juno’s suit heavenly factions end.
 destruction hangs o’er yon devoted wall,
 nodding ilion waits impending fall.”
 
swift word vain illusion fled,
 descends, hovers o’er atrides’ head;
 clothed figure pylian sage,
 renown’d wisdom, revered age:
 around temples spreads golden wing,
 thus flattering dream deceives king.
 

[illustration: ] jupiter sending evil dream agamemnon
 

“canst thou, monarch’s cares oppress’d,
 atreus’ son! canst thou indulge thy rest?[78]
 ill fits chief mighty nations guides,
 directs council, war presides,
 safety whole people owes,
 waste long nights indolent repose.[79]
 monarch, awake! ’tis jove’s command bear;
 thou, thy glory, claim heavenly care.
 just array draw forth embattled train,
 lead thy grecians dusty plain;
 e’en now, king! ’tis given thee destroy
 lofty towers wide-extended troy.
 now gods fate contend,
 juno’s suit heavenly factions end.
 destruction hangs o’er yon devoted wall,
 nodding ilion waits impending fall.
 awake, waking advice approve,
 trust vision descends jove.”
 
phantom said; vanish’d sight,
 resolves air, mixes night.
 thousand schemes monarch’s mind employ;
 elate thought sacks untaken troy:
 vain was, future blind,
 saw jove secret fate design’d,
 mighty toils either host remain,
 scenes grief, numbers slain!
 eager rises, fancy hears
 voice celestial murmuring ears.
 first limbs slender vest drew,
 around next regal mantle threw,
 embroider’d sandals feet tied;
 starry falchion glitter’d side;
 last, arm massy sceptre loads,
 unstain’d, immortal, gift gods.
 
now rosy morn ascends court jove,
 lifts light, opens day above.
 king despatch’d heralds commands
 range camp summon bands:
 gathering hosts monarch’s word obey;
 fleet atrides bends way.
 black ship pylian prince found;
 calls senate peers around:
 assembly placed, king men express’d
 counsels labouring artful breast.
 
“friends confederates! attentive ear
 receive words, credit hear.
 late slumber’d shades night,
 dream divine appear’d sight;
 whose visionary form like nestor came,
 habit, mien same.[80]
 heavenly phantom hover’d o’er head,
 ‘and, dost thou sleep, atreus’ son? (he said)
 ill fits chief mighty nations guides,
 directs council, war presides;
 safety whole people owes,
 waste long nights indolent repose.
 monarch, awake! ’tis jove’s command bear,
 thou thy glory claim heavenly care.
 just array draw forth embattled train,
 lead grecians dusty plain;
 e’en now, king! ’tis given thee destroy
 lofty towers wide-extended troy.
 now gods fate contend,
 juno’s suit heavenly factions end.
 destruction hangs o’er yon devoted wall,
 nodding ilion waits impending fall.
 
hear observant, gods obey!’
 vision spoke, pass’d air away.
 now, valiant chiefs! since heaven alarms,
 unite, rouse sons greece arms.
 first, caution, try yet dare,
 worn nine years unsuccessful war.
 move troops measure back main,
 mine; province detain.”
 
spoke, sat: nestor, rising said,
 (nestor, pylos’ sandy realms obey’d,)
 “princes greece, faithful ears incline,
 doubt vision powers divine;
 sent great jove rules host,
 forbid it, heaven! warning lost!
 let us haste, obey god’s alarms,
 join rouse sons greece arms.”
 
thus spoke sage: kings without delay
 dissolve council, chief obey:
 sceptred rulers lead; following host,
 pour’d forth thousands, darkens coast.
 rocky cleft shepherd sees
 clustering heaps heaps driving bees,
 rolling blackening, swarms succeeding swarms,
 deeper murmurs hoarse alarms;
 dusky spread, close embodied crowd,
 o’er vale descends living cloud.[81]
 so, tents ships, lengthen’d train
 spreads beach, wide o’ershades plain:
 along region runs deafening sound;
 beneath footsteps groans trembling ground.
 fame flies messenger jove,
 shining soars, claps wings above.
 nine sacred heralds now, proclaiming loud[82]
 monarch’s will, suspend listening crowd.
 soon throngs order ranged appear,
 fainter murmurs died upon ear,
 king kings awful figure raised:
 high hand golden sceptre blazed;
 golden sceptre, celestial flame,
 vulcan form’d, jove hermes came.
 pelops immortal gift resign’d;
 immortal gift great pelops left behind,
 atreus’ hand, atreus ends,
 rich thyestes next prize descends;
 now mark agamemnon’s reign,
 subjects argos, controls main.[83]
 
bright sceptre now king reclined,
 artful thus pronounced speech design’d:
 “ye sons mars, partake leader’s care,
 heroes greece, brothers war!
 partial jove justice complain,
 heavenly oracles believed vain
 safe return promised toils,
 renown’d, triumphant, enrich’d spoils.
 now shameful flight alone can save host,
 blood, treasure, glory lost.
 jove decrees, resistless lord all!
 whose command whole empires rise fall:
 shakes feeble props human trust,
 towns armies humbles dust.
 shame greece fruitful war wage,
 oh, lasting shame every future age!
 great arms, common scorn grow,
 repulsed baffled feeble foe.
 small number, wars ceased,
 greece triumphant held general feast,
 rank’d tens, whole decades dine
 must want trojan slave pour wine.[84]
 forces hopes o’erthrown,
 troy prevails armies own.
 now nine long years mighty jove run,
 since first labours war begun:
 cordage torn, decay’d vessels lie,
 scarce insure wretched power fly.
 haste, then, ever leave trojan wall!
 weeping wives, tender children call:
 love, duty, safety, summon us away,
 ’tis nature’s voice, nature obey.
 shatter’d barks may yet transport us o’er,
 safe inglorious, native shore.
 fly, grecians, fly, sails oars employ,
 dream heaven-defended troy.”
 
deep design unknown, hosts approve
 atrides’ speech. mighty numbers move.
 roll billows icarian shore,
 east south winds begin roar,
 burst dark mansions clouds, sweep
 whitening surface ruffled deep.
 corn western gusts descend,[85]
 blast lofty harvests bend:
 thus o’er field moving host appears,
 nodding plumes groves waving spears.
 gathering murmur spreads, trampling feet
 beat loose sands, thicken fleet;
 long-resounding cries urge train
 fit ships, launch main.
 toil, sweat, thick clouds dust arise,
 doubling clamours echo skies.
 e’en greeks left hostile plain,
 fate decreed fall troy vain;
 jove’s imperial queen flight survey’d,
 sighing thus bespoke blue-eyed maid:
 
“shall grecians fly! dire disgrace!
 leave unpunish’d perfidious race?
 shall troy, shall priam, adulterous spouse,
 peace enjoy fruits broken vows?
 bravest chiefs, helen’s quarrel slain,
 lie unrevenged yon detested plain?
 no: let greeks, unmoved vain alarms,
 refulgent shine brazen arms.
 haste, goddess, haste! flying host detain,
 let one sail hoisted main.”
 
pallas obeys, olympus’ height
 swift ships precipitates flight.
 ulysses, first public cares, found,
 prudent counsel like gods renown’d:
 oppress’d generous grief hero stood,
 drew sable vessels flood.
 “and thus, divine laertes’ son,
 thus fly greeks (the martial maid begun),
 thus country bear disgrace,
 fame eternal leave priam’s race?
 shall beauteous helen still remain unfreed,
 still unrevenged, thousand heroes bleed!
 haste, generous ithacus! prevent shame,
 recall armies, chiefs reclaim.
 resistless eloquence employ,
 immortals trust fall troy.”
 
voice divine confess’d warlike maid,
 ulysses heard, uninspired obey’d:
 meeting first atrides, hand
 received imperial sceptre command.
 thus graced, attention respect gain,
 runs, flies grecian train;
 prince name, chief arms approved,
 fired praise, persuasion moved.
 
“warriors like you, strength wisdom bless’d,
 brave examples confirm rest.
 monarch’s will yet reveal’d appears;
 tries courage, resents fears.
 unwary greeks fury may provoke;
 thus king secret council spoke.
 jove loves chief, jove honour springs,
 beware! dreadful wrath kings.”
 
clamorous vile plebeian rose,
 reproof check’d tamed blows.
 “be still, thou slave, thy betters yield;
 unknown alike council field!
 ye gods, dastards host command!
 swept war, lumber land.
 silent, wretch, think allow’d
 worst tyrants, usurping crowd.
 one sole monarch jove commits sway;
 laws, let obey.”[86]
 
words like troops ulysses ruled,
 loudest silenced, fiercest cool’d.
 back assembly roll thronging train,
 desert ships, pour upon plain.
 murmuring move, old ocean roars,
 heaves huge surges trembling shores;
 groaning banks burst bellowing sound,
 rocks remurmur deeps rebound.
 length tumult sinks, noises cease,
 still silence lulls camp peace.
 thersites clamour’d throng,
 loquacious, loud, turbulent tongue:
 awed shame, respect controll’d,
 scandal busy, reproaches bold:
 witty malice studious defame,
 scorn joy, laughter aim:—
 chief gloried licentious style
 lash great, monarchs revile.
 figure might soul proclaim;
 one eye blinking, one leg lame:
 mountain shoulders half breast o’erspread,
 thin hairs bestrew’d long misshapen head.
 spleen mankind envious heart possess’d,
 much hated all, best:
 ulysses achilles still theme;
 royal scandal delight supreme,
 long lived scorn every greek,
 vex’d spoke, yet still heard speak.
 sharp voice; shrillest tone,
 thus injurious taunts attack’d throne.
 
“amidst glories bright reign,
 moves great atrides complain?
 ’tis thine whate’er warrior’s breast inflames,
 golden spoil, thine lovely dames.
 wealth wars blood bestow,
 thy tents crowded thy chests o’erflow.
 thus full ease heaps riches roll’d,
 grieves monarch? thirst gold?
 say, shall march unconquer’d powers
 (the greeks i) ilion’s hostile towers,
 bring race royal bastards here,
 troy ransom price dear?
 safer plunder thy host supplies;
 say, wouldst thou seize valiant leader’s prize?
 or, thy heart generous love led,
 captive fair, bless thy kingly bed?
 whate’er master craves submit must,
 plagued pride, punish’d lust.
 oh women achaia; men more!
 hence let us fly, let waste store
 loves pleasures phrygian shore.
 may wanted busy day,
 hector comes: great achilles may:
 forced prize jointly gave,
 him, fierce, fearless, brave:
 durst he, ought, resent wrong,
 mighty tyrant tyrant long.”
 
fierce seat ulysses springs,[87]
 generous vengeance king kings.
 indignation sparkling eyes,
 views wretch, sternly thus replies:
 
“peace, factious monster, born vex state,
 wrangling talents form’d foul debate:
 curb impetuous tongue, rashly vain,
 singly mad, asperse sovereign reign.
 known thee, slave! host,
 man acts least, upbraids most?
 think greeks shameful flight bring,
 let lips profane name king.
 return trust heavenly powers;
 care; fight like men ours.
 grant host wealth general load,
 except detraction, hast thou bestow’d?
 suppose hero spoils resign,
 art thou hero, spoils thine?
 gods! let perish hateful shore,
 let eyes behold more;
 if, thy next offence, hand forbear
 strip arms thou ill deserv’st wear,
 expel council princes meet,
 send thee scourged howling fleet.”
 
said, cowering dastard bends,
 weighty sceptre back descends.[88]
 round bunch bloody tumours rise:
 tears spring starting haggard eyes;
 trembling sat, shrunk abject fears,
 vile visage wiped scalding tears;
 neighbour express’d thought:
 
“ye gods! wonders ulysses wrought!
 fruits conduct courage yield!
 great council, glorious field.
 generous rises crown’s defence,
 curb factious tongue insolence,
 just examples offenders shown,
 sedition silence, assert throne.”
 
’twas thus general voice hero praised,
 who, rising, high imperial sceptre raised:
 blue-eyed pallas, celestial friend,
 (in form herald,) bade crowds attend.
 expecting crowds still attention hung,
 hear wisdom heavenly tongue.
 deeply thoughtful, pausing ere spoke,
 silence thus prudent hero broke:
 
“unhappy monarch! grecian race
 shame deserting, heap vile disgrace.
 argos generous vow:
 voice, ah! forgotten now:
 ne’er return, common cry,
 till troy’s proud structures ashes lie.
 behold weeping native shore;
 wives helpless children more?
 heart melts leave tender train,
 and, one short month, endure wintry main?
 leagues removed, wish peaceful seat,
 ship tosses, tempests beat:
 well may long stay provoke tears,
 tedious length nine revolving years.
 grief grecian host blame;
 vanquish’d! baffled! oh, eternal shame!
 expect time troy’s destruction given.
 try faith chalcas heaven.
 pass’d aulis, greece can witness bear,[89]
 live breathe phrygian air.
 beside fountain’s sacred brink raised
 verdant altars, victims blazed:
 ’twas plane-tree spread shades around,
 altars heaved; crumbling ground
 mighty dragon shot, dire portent;
 jove dreadful sign sent.
 straight tree sanguine spires roll’d,
 curl’d around many winding fold;
 topmost branch mother-bird possess’d;
 eight callow infants fill’d mossy nest;
 ninth; serpent, hung,
 stretch’d black jaws crush’d crying young;
 hovering near, miserable moan,
 drooping mother wail’d children gone.
 mother last, round nest flew,
 seized beating wing, monster slew;
 long survived: marble turn’d, stands
 lasting prodigy aulis’ sands.
 will jove; hence dare
 trust omen, support war.
 around gazed wondering eyes,
 trembling sought powers sacrifice,
 full god, reverend chalcas cried,[90]
 ‘ye grecian warriors! lay fears aside.
 wondrous signal jove displays,
 long, long labours, eternal praise.
 many birds snake slain,
 many years toils greece remain;
 wait tenth, ilion’s fall decreed:’
 thus spoke prophet, thus fates succeed.
 obey, ye grecians! submission wait,
 let flight avert trojan fate.”
 said: shores loud applauses sound,
 hollow ships deafening shout rebound.
 nestor thus—“these vain debates forbear,
 ye talk like children, like heroes dare.
 now high resolves last?
 leagues concluded, engagements past?
 vow’d libations victims then,
 now vanish’d like smoke: faith men!
 useless words consume unactive hours,
 wonder troy long resists powers.
 rise, great atrides! courage sway;
 march war, thou direct way.
 leave dare resist thy laws,
 mean deserters grecian cause,
 grudge conquests mighty jove prepares,
 view envy successful wars.
 great day, first martial train,
 big fate ilion, plough’d main,
 jove, right, prosperous signal sent,
 thunder rolling shook firmament.
 encouraged hence, maintain glorious strife,
 till every soldier grasp phrygian wife,
 till helen’s woes full revenged appear,
 troy’s proud matrons render tear tear.
 day, greek invite
 country’s troops base, inglorious flight,
 stand forth greek! hoist sail fly,
 die dastard first, dreads die.
 now, monarch! thy chiefs advise:[91]
 offer, thou thyself despise.
 among counsels, let mine vain;
 tribes nations divide thy train:
 separate troops let every leader call,
 strengthen each, encourage all.
 chief, soldier, numerous band,
 bravely fights, ill obeys command,
 thus distinct war, shall soon known
 cause ilion o’erthrown;
 fate resists, arms slow,
 gods prevent, men below.”
 
king: “how much thy years excel
 arts counsel, speaking well!
 gods, love greece, decree
 ten sages grant thee;
 wisdom soon priam’s force destroy,
 soon fall haughty towers troy!
 jove forbids, plunges hates
 fierce contention vain debates:
 now great achilles aid withdraws,
 provoked; captive maid cause:
 e’er friends join, trojan wall
 must shake, heavy will vengeance fall!
 now, ye warriors, take short repast;
 and, well refresh’d, bloody conflict haste.
 sharpen’d spear let every grecian wield,
 every grecian fix brazen shield,
 let excite fiery steeds war,
 combat fit rattling car.
 day, dreadful day, let contend;
 rest, respite, till shades descend;
 till darkness, till death, shall cover all:
 let war bleed, let mighty fall;
 till bathed sweat every manly breast,
 huge shield brawny arm depress’d,
 aching nerve refuse lance throw,
 spent courser chariot blow.
 dares, inglorious, ships stay,
 dares tremble signal day;
 wretch, mean fall martial power,
 birds shall mangle, dogs devour.”
 
monarch spoke; straight murmur rose,
 loud surges tempest blows,
 dash’d broken rocks tumultuous roar,
 foam thunder stony shore.
 straight tents troops dispersing bend,
 fires kindled, smokes ascend;
 hasty feasts sacrifice, pray,
 avert dangers doubtful day.
 steer five years’ age, large limb’d, fed,[92]
 jove’s high altars agamemnon led:
 bade noblest grecian peers;
 nestor first, advanced years.
 next came idomeneus,[93] tydeus’ son,[94]
 ajax less, ajax telamon;[95]
 wise ulysses rank placed;
 menelaus came, unbid, last.[96]
 chiefs surround destined beast, take
 sacred offering salted cake:
 thus king prefers solemn prayer;
 “o thou! whose thunder rends clouded air,
 heaven heavens hast fixed thy throne,
 supreme gods! unbounded, alone!
 hear! burning sun descends,
 night gloomy veil extends,
 low dust laid yon hostile spires,
 priam’s palace sunk grecian fires.
 hector’s breast plunged shining sword,
 slaughter’d heroes groan around lord!”
 
thus prayed chief: unavailing prayer
 great jove refused, toss’d empty air:
 god averse, yet fumes arose,
 prepared new toils, doubled woes woes.
 prayers perform’d chiefs rite pursue,
 barley sprinkled, victim slew.
 limbs sever inclosing hide,
 thighs, selected gods, divide.
 these, double cauls involved art,
 choicest morsels lie every part,
 cleft wood crackling flames aspire
 fat victims feed sacred fire.
 thighs thus sacrificed, entrails dress’d
 assistants part, transfix, roast rest;
 spread tables, repast prepare,
 takes seat, receives share.
 soon rage hunger suppress’d,
 generous nestor thus prince address’d.
 
“now bid thy heralds sound loud alarms,
 call squadrons sheathed brazen arms;
 now seize occasion, now troops survey,
 lead war heaven directs way.”
 
said; monarch issued commands;
 straight loud heralds call gathering bands;
 chiefs inclose king; hosts divide,
 tribes nations rank’d either side.
 high midst blue-eyed virgin flies;
 rank rank darts ardent eyes;
 dreadful ægis, jove’s immortal shield,
 blazed arm, lighten’d field:
 round vast orb hundred serpents roll’d,
 form’d bright fringe, seem’d burn gold,
 grecian’s manly breast warms,
 swells bold hearts, strings nervous arms,
 sigh, inglorious, return,
 breathe revenge, combat burn.
 
mountain, lofty grove,
 crackling flames ascend, blaze above;
 fires expanding, winds arise,
 shoot long beams, kindle half skies:
 polish’d arms, brazen shields,
 gleamy splendour flash’d along fields.
 less number embodied cranes,
 milk-white swans asius’ watery plains.
 that, o’er windings cayster’s springs,[97]
 stretch long necks, clap rustling wings,
 now tower aloft, course airy rounds,
 now light noise; noise field resounds.
 thus numerous confused, extending wide,
 legions crowd scamander’s flowery side;[98]
 rushing troops plains cover’d o’er,
 thundering footsteps shake sounding shore.
 along river’s level meads stand,
 thick spring flowers adorn land,
 leaves trees; thick insects play,
 wandering nation summer’s day:
 that, drawn milky steams, evening hours,
 gather’d swarms surround rural bowers;
 pail pail busy murmur run
 gilded legions, glittering sun.
 throng’d, close, grecian squadrons stood
 radiant arms, thirst trojan blood.
 leader now scatter’d force conjoins
 close array, forms deepening lines.
 ease skilful shepherd-swain
 collects flocks thousands plain.
 king kings, majestically tall,
 towers o’er armies, outshines all;
 like proud bull, round pastures leads
 subject herds, monarch meads,
 great gods, exalted chief seen,
 strength like neptune, like mars mien;[99]
 jove o’er eyes celestial glories spread,
 dawning conquest played around head.
 
say, virgins, seated round throne divine,
 all-knowing goddesses! immortal nine![100]
 since earth’s wide regions, heaven’s umneasur’d height,
 hell’s abyss, hide nothing sight,
 (we, wretched mortals! lost doubts below,
 guess rumour, boast know,)
 say heroes, fired thirst fame,
 urged wrongs, troy’s destruction came.
 count all, demands thousand tongues,
 throat brass, adamantine lungs.
 daughters jove, assist! inspired you
 mighty labour dauntless pursue;
 crowded armies, climes bring,
 names, numbers, chiefs sing.

 far regions sun refines
 ripening silver alybean mines.
 
mighty chromis led mysian train,
 augur ennomus, inspired vain;
 stern achilles lopp’d sacred head,
 roll’d scamander vulgar dead.
 
phorcys brave ascanius unite
 ascanian phrygians, eager fight.
 
round mæonia’s realms reside,
 vales shades tmolus hide,
 mestles antiphus charge partake,
 born banks gyges’ silent lake.
 there, fields wild mæander flows,
 high mycale, latmos’ shady brows,
 proud miletus, came carian throngs,
 mingled clamours barbarous tongues.[107]
 amphimachus naustes guide train,
 naustes bold, amphimachus vain,
 who, trick’d gold, glittering car,
 rode like woman field war.
 fool was! fierce achilles slain,
 river swept briny main:
 whelm’d waves gaudy warrior lies
 valiant victor seized golden prize.
 
forces last fair array succeed,
 blameless glaucus sarpedon lead
 warlike bands distant lycia yields,
 gulfy xanthus foams along fields.
 



book iii.
 

argument.
 

duel menelaus paris.
 

armies ready engage, single combat agreed upon
 menelaus paris (by intervention hector) the
 determination war. iris sent call helen behold the
 fight. leads walls troy, priam sat his
 counsellers observing grecian leaders plain below, whom
 helen gives account chief them. kings either part
 take solemn oath conditions combat. duel ensues;
 wherein paris overcome, snatched away cloud venus,
 transported apartment. calls helen walls,
 brings lovers together. agamemnon, part grecians,
 demands restoration helen, performance articles.
 three-and-twentieth day still continues throughout book.
 scene sometimes fields troy, sometimes in
 troy itself.
 

thus leaders’ care martial band
 moves ranks, stretches o’er land.
 shouts trojans, rushing afar,
 proclaim motions, provoke war.
 inclement winters vex plain
 piercing frosts, thick-descending rain,
 warmer seas cranes embodied fly,[108]
 noise, order, midway sky;
 pigmy nations wounds death bring,
 war descends upon wing,
 silent, breathing rage, resolved skill’d[109]
 mutual aids fix doubtful field,
 swift march greeks: rapid dust around
 darkening arises labour’d ground.
 thus flaggy wings notus sheds
 night vapours round mountain heads,
 swift-gliding mists dusky fields invade,
 thieves grateful midnight shade;
 scarce swains feeding flocks survey,
 lost confused amidst thicken’d day:
 wrapp’d gathering dust, grecian train,
 moving cloud, swept on, hid plain.
 
now front front hostile armies stand,
 eager fight, wait command;
 when, van, sons fame
 troy sent forth, beauteous paris came:
 form god! panther’s speckled hide
 flow’d o’er armour easy pride:
 bended bow across shoulders flung,
 sword beside negligently hung;
 two pointed spears shook gallant grace,
 dared bravest grecian race.
 
thus, glorious air proud disdain,
 boldly stalk’d, foremost plain,
 menelaus, loved mars, espies,
 heart elated, joyful eyes:
 joys lion, branching deer,
 mountain goat, bulky prize, appear;
 eager seizes devours slain,
 press’d bold youths baying dogs vain.
 thus fond vengeance, furious bound,
 clanging arms leaps upon ground
 high chariot: him, approaching near,
 beauteous champion views marks fear,
 smit conscious sense, retires behind,
 shuns fate well deserved find.
 shepherd, rustling trees[110]
 shot forth view, scaly serpent sees,
 trembling pale, starts wild affright
 confused precipitates flight:
 king shining warrior flies,
 plunged amid thickest trojans lies.
 
godlike hector sees prince retreat,
 thus upbraids generous heat:
 “unhappy paris![111] women brave!
 fairly form’d, deceive!
 oh, hadst thou died first thou saw’st light,
 died least thy nuptial rite!
 better fate vainly thus boast,
 fly, scandal thy trojan host.
 gods! scornful greeks exult see
 fears danger undeceived thee!
 thy figure promised martial air,
 ill thy soul supplies form fair.
 former days, thy gallant pride,
 thy tall ships triumphant stemm’d tide,
 greece beheld thy painted canvas flow,
 crowds stood wondering passing show,
 say, thus, baffled mien,
 met approaches spartan queen,
 thus realm convey’d beauteous prize,
 warlike lords outshined helen’s eyes?
 deed, thy foes’ delight, thy disgrace,
 thy father’s grief, ruin thy race;
 deed recalls thee proffer’d fight;
 hast thou injured thou dar’st right?
 soon thy cost field make thee know
 thou keep’st consort braver foe.
 thy graceful form instilling soft desire,
 thy curling tresses, thy silver lyre,
 beauty youth; vain trust,
 youth beauty shall laid dust:
 troy yet may wake, one avenging blow
 crush dire author country’s woe.”
 
silence here, blushes, paris breaks:
 “’tis just, brother, anger speaks:
 like thee can boast soul sedate,
 firmly proof shocks fate?
 thy force, like steel, temper’d hardness shows,
 still edged wound, still untired blows,
 like steel, uplifted strenuous swain,
 falling woods strew wasted plain.
 thy gifts praise; thou despise charms
 lover golden venus arms;
 soft moving speech, pleasing outward show,
 wish can gain them, gods bestow.
 yet, would’st thou proffer’d combat stand,
 greeks trojans seat either hand;
 let midway space hosts divide,
 and, stage war, cause tried:
 paris spartan king fought,
 beauteous helen wealth brought;
 rival can arms subdue,
 fair, treasure too.
 thus lasting league toils may cease,
 troy possess fertile fields peace;
 thus may greeks review native shore,
 much famed generous steeds, beauty more.”
 
said. challenge hector heard joy,
 spear restrain’d youth troy,
 held midst, athwart; near foe
 advanced steps majestically slow:
 round dauntless head grecians pour
 stones arrows mingled shower.
 
thus monarch, great atrides, cried:
 “forbear, ye warriors! lay darts aside:
 parley hector asks, message bears;
 know various plume wears.”
 awed high command greeks attend,
 tumult silence, fight suspend.
 
centre hector rolls eyes
 either host, thus applies:
 “hear, ye trojan, ye grecian bands,
 paris, author war, demands.
 shining swords within sheath restrain,
 pitch lances yielding plain.
 midst, either army’s sight,
 dares spartan king single fight;
 wills helen ravish’d spoil,
 caused contest, shall reward toil.
 let brave triumphant victor grace,
 different nations part leagues peace.”
 
spoke: still suspense either side
 army stood: spartan chief replied:
 
“me too, ye warriors, hear, whose fatal right
 world engages toils fight.
 labour field resign;
 paris injured; war mine.
 fall must, beneath rival’s arms;
 live rest, secure future harms.
 two lambs, devoted country’s rite,
 earth sable, sun white,
 prepare, ye trojans! third bring
 select jove, inviolable king.
 let reverend priam truce engage,
 add sanction considerate age;
 sons faithless, headlong debate,
 youth empty wavering state;
 cool age advances, venerably wise,
 turns hands deep-discerning eyes;
 sees befell, may yet befall,
 concludes both, best provides all.
 
nations hear rising hopes possess’d,
 peaceful prospects dawn every breast.
 within lines drew steeds around,
 chariots issued ground;
 next, unbuckling rich mail wore,
 laid bright arms along sable shore.
 either side meeting hosts seen
 lances fix’d, close space between.
 two heralds now, despatch’d troy, invite
 phrygian monarch peaceful rite.
 
talthybius hastens fleet, bring
 lamb jove, inviolable king.
 
meantime beauteous helen, skies
 various goddess rainbow flies:
 (like fair laodice form face,
 loveliest nymph priam’s royal race:)
 palace, loom found;
 golden web sad story crown’d,
 trojan wars weaved (herself prize)
 dire triumphs fatal eyes.
 goddess painted bow:
 “approach, view wondrous scene below![112]
 hardy greek, valiant trojan knight,
 dreadful late, furious fight,
 now rest spears, lean upon shields;
 ceased war, silent fields.
 paris alone sparta’s king advance,
 single fight toss beamy lance;
 met arms, fate combat tries,
 thy love motive, thy charms prize.”
 
said, many-coloured maid inspires
 husband’s love, wakes former fires;
 country, parents, dear,
 rush thought, force tender tear,
 o’er fair face snowy veil threw,
 and, softly sighing, loom withdrew.
 handmaids, clymene Æthra, wait
 silent footsteps scæan gate.
 
sat seniors trojan race:
 (old priam’s chiefs, priam’s grace,)
 king first; thymœtes side;
 lampus clytius, long council tried;
 panthus, hicetaon, strong;
 next, wisest reverend throng,
 antenor grave, sage ucalegon,
 lean’d walls bask’d sun:
 chiefs, bloody fights engage,
 wise time, narrative age,
 summer days, like grasshoppers rejoice,
 bloodless race, send feeble voice.
 these, spartan queen approach’d tower,
 secret own’d resistless beauty’s power:
 cried, “no wonder[113] celestial charms
 nine long years set world arms;
 winning graces! majestic mien!
 moves goddess, looks queen!
 yet hence, heaven, convey fatal face,
 destruction save trojan race.”
 
good old priam welcomed her, cried,
 “approach, child, grace thy father’s side.
 see plain thy grecian spouse appears,
 friends kindred thy former years.
 crime thine present sufferings draws,
 thou, heaven’s disposing will, cause
 gods armies force employ,
 hostile gods conspire fate troy.
 lift thy eyes, say, greek he
 (far hence aged orbs can see)
 around whose brow martial graces shine,
 tall, awful, almost divine!
 though larger stature tread green,
 none match grandeur exalted mien:
 seems monarch, country’s pride.”
 thus ceased king, thus fair replied:
 
“before thy presence, father, appear,
 conscious shame reverential fear.
 ah! died, ere walls fled,
 false country, nuptial bed;
 brothers, friends, daughter left behind,
 false all, paris kind!
 mourn, till grief dire disease
 shall waste form whose fault please!
 king kings, atrides, survey,
 great war, great arts sway:
 brother once, days shame!
 oh! still bore brother’s name!”
 
wonder priam view’d godlike man,
 extoll’d happy prince, thus began:
 “o bless’d atrides! born prosperous fate,
 successful monarch mighty state!
 vast thy empire! matchless train
 numbers lost, numbers yet remain!
 phrygia gallant armies known,
 ancient time, otreus fill’d throne,
 godlike mygdon led troops horse,
 i, join them, raised trojan force:
 manlike amazons stood,[114]
 sangar’s stream ran purple blood.
 far inferior those, martial grace,
 strength numbers, grecian race.”
 
said, view’d warrior train;
 “what’s he, whose arms lie scatter’d plain?
 broad breast, shoulders larger spread,
 though great atrides overtops head.
 yet appear care conduct small;
 rank rank moves, orders all.
 stately ram thus measures o’er ground,
 and, master flock, surveys round.”
 
helen thus: “whom discerning eyes
 singled out, ithacus wise;
 barren island boasts glorious birth;
 fame wisdom fills spacious earth.”
 
antenor took word, thus began:[115]
 “myself, king! seen wondrous man
 when, trusting jove hospitable laws,
 troy came, plead grecian cause;
 (great menelaus urged request;)
 house honour’d royal guest:
 knew persons, admired parts,
 brave arms, approved arts.
 erect, spartan engaged view;
 ulysses seated, greater reverence drew.
 atreus’ harangued listening train,
 just sense, expression plain,
 words succinct, yet full, without fault;
 spoke just thing ought.
 ulysses rose, thought profound,[116]
 modest eyes fix’d upon ground;
 one unskill’d dumb, seem’d stand,
 raised head, stretch’d sceptred hand;
 but, speaks, elocution flows!
 soft fleeces descending snows,[117]
 copious accents fall, easy art;
 melting fall, sink heart!
 wondering hear, fix’d deep surprise,
 ears refute censure eyes.”
 
king ask’d (as yet camp view’d)
 “what chief that, giant strength endued,
 whose brawny shoulders, whose swelling chest,
 lofty stature, far exceed rest?
 “ajax great, (the beauteous queen replied,)
 host: grecian strength pride.
 see! bold idomeneus superior towers
 amid yon circle cretan powers,
 great god! saw before,
 menelaus spartan shore.
 rest know, order name;
 valiant chiefs, men mighty fame.
 yet two wanting numerous train,
 long eyes sought, sought vain:
 castor pollux, first martial force,
 one bold foot, one renown’d horse.
 brothers these; native shore,
 one house contain’d us, one mother bore.
 perhaps chiefs, warlike toils ease,
 distant troy refused sail seas;
 perhaps swords nobler quarrel draws,
 ashamed combat sister’s cause.”
 
spoke fair, knew brothers’ doom;[118]
 wrapt cold embraces tomb;
 adorn’d honours native shore,
 silent slept, heard wars more.
 
meantime heralds, crowded town,
 bring rich wine destined victims down.
 idæus’ arms golden goblets press’d,[119]
 thus venerable king address’d:
 “arise, father trojan state!
 nations call, thy joyful people wait
 seal truce, end dire debate.
 paris, thy son, sparta’s king advance,
 measured lists toss weighty lance;
 rival shall arms subdue,
 dame, treasure too.
 thus lasting league toils may cease,
 troy possess fertile fields peace:
 shall greeks review native shore,
 much famed generous steeds, beauty more.”
 
grief heard, bade chiefs prepare
 join milk-white coursers car;
 mounts seat, antenor side;
 gentle steeds scæa’s gates guide:[120]
 next car descending plain,
 amid grecian host trojan train,
 slow proceed: sage ulysses then
 arose, rose king men.
 either side sacred herald stands,
 wine mix, monarch’s hands
 pour full urn; draws grecian lord
 cutlass sheathed beside ponderous sword;
 sign’d victims crops curling hair;[121]
 heralds part it, princes share;
 loudly thus attentive bands
 calls gods, spreads lifted hands:
 
“o first greatest power! obey,
 high ida’s holy mountain sway,
 eternal jove! bright orb roll
 east west, view pole pole!
 thou mother earth! ye living floods!
 infernal furies, tartarean gods,
 rule dead, horrid woes prepare
 perjured kings, falsely swear!
 hear, witness. if, paris slain,
 great menelaus press fatal plain;
 dame treasures let trojan keep,
 greece returning plough watery deep.
 brother’s lance trojan bleed,
 wealth beauteous dame decreed:
 appointed fine let ilion justly pay,
 every age record signal day.
 phrygians shall refuse yield,
 arms must revenge, mars decide field.”
 
chief tender victims slew,
 dust bleeding bodies threw;
 vital spirit issued wound,
 left members quivering ground.
 urn drink mingled wine,
 add libations powers divine.
 thus prayers united mount sky,
 “hear, mighty jove! hear, ye gods high!
 may blood, first league confound,
 shed like wine, disdain thirsty ground;
 may consorts serve promiscuous lust,
 lust scatter’d dust!”
 thus either host imprecations join’d,
 jove refused, mingled wind.
 
rites now finish’d, reverend priam rose,
 thus express’d heart o’ercharged woes:
 “ye greeks trojans, let chiefs engage,
 spare weakness feeble age:
 yonder walls object let shun,
 view danger dear son.
 whose arms shall conquer prince shall fall,
 heaven knows; heaven disposes all.”
 
said, hoary king longer stay’d,
 car slaughter’d victims laid:
 seized reins gentle steeds guide,
 drove troy, antenor side.
 
bold hector ulysses now dispose
 lists combat, ground inclose:
 next decide, sacred lots prepare,
 first shall launch pointed spear air.
 people pray elevated hands,
 words like heard bands:
 “immortal jove, high heaven’s superior lord,
 lofty ida’s holy mount adored!
 whoe’er involved us dire debate,
 give author war fate
 shades eternal! let division cease,
 joyful nations join leagues peace.”
 
eyes averted hector hastes turn
 lots fight shakes brazen urn.
 then, paris, thine leap’d forth; fatal chance
 ordain’d first whirl weighty lance.
 armies sat combat survey.
 beside chief azure armour lay,
 round lists generous coursers neigh.
 beauteous warrior now arrays fight,
 gilded arms magnificently bright:
 purple cuishes clasp thighs around,
 flowers adorn’d, silver buckles bound:
 lycaon’s corslet fair body dress’d,
 braced fitted softer breast;
 radiant baldric, o’er shoulder tied,
 sustain’d sword glitter’d side:
 youthful face polish’d helm o’erspread;
 waving horse-hair nodded head:
 figured shield, shining orb, takes,
 hand pointed javelin shakes.
 equal speed fired equal charms,
 spartan hero sheathes limbs arms.
 
now round lists admiring armies stand,
 javelins fix’d, greek trojan band.
 amidst dreadful vale, chiefs advance,
 pale rage, shake threatening lance.
 trojan first shining javelin threw;
 full atrides’ ringing shield flew,
 pierced brazen orb, bound[122]
 leap’d buckler, blunted, ground.
 atrides massy lance prepares,
 act throw, first prefers prayers:
 
“give me, great jove! punish lawless lust,
 lay trojan gasping dust:
 destroy aggressor, aid righteous cause,
 avenge breach hospitable laws!
 let example future times reclaim,
 guard wrong fair friendship’s holy name,”
 said, poised air javelin sent,
 paris’ shield forceful weapon went,
 corslet pierces, garment rends,
 glancing downward, near flank descends.
 wary trojan, bending blow,
 eludes death, disappoints foe:
 fierce atrides waved sword, strook
 full casque: crested helmet shook;
 brittle steel, unfaithful hand,
 broke short: fragments glitter’d sand.
 raging warrior spacious skies
 raised upbraiding voice angry eyes:
 “then vain jove trust?
 thus gods assist just?
 crimes provoke us, heaven success denies;
 dart falls harmless, falchion flies.”
 furious said, towards grecian crew
 (seized crest) unhappy warrior drew;
 struggling followed, embroider’d thong
 tied helmet, dragg’d chief along.
 ruin crown’d atrides’ joy,
 venus trembled prince troy:
 unseen came, burst golden band;
 left empty helmet hand.
 casque, enraged, amidst greeks threw;
 greeks smiles polish’d trophy view.
 then, lifts deadly dart,
 thirst vengeance, rival’s heart;
 queen love favour’d champion shrouds
 (for gods can things) veil clouds.
 raised field panting youth led,
 gently laid bridal bed,
 pleasing sweets fainting sense renews,
 dome perfumes heavenly dews.
 meantime brightest female kind,
 matchless helen, o’er walls reclined;
 her, beset trojan beauties, came,
 borrow’d form, laughter-loving dame.
 (she seem’d ancient maid, well-skill’d cull
 snowy fleece, wind twisted wool.)
 goddess softly shook silken vest,
 shed perfumes, whispering thus address’d:
 

[illustration: ] venus, disguised, inviting helen chamber of
 paris
 

“haste, happy nymph! thee thy paris calls,
 safe fight, yonder lofty walls,
 fair god; odours round spread,
 lies, waits thee well-known bed;
 like warrior parted foe,
 gay dancer public show.”
 
spoke, helen’s secret soul moved;
 scorn’d champion, man loved.
 fair venus’ neck, eyes sparkled fire,
 breast, reveal’d queen soft desire.[123]
 struck presence, straight lively red
 forsook cheek; trembling, thus said:
 “then still thy pleasure deceive?
 woman’s frailty always believe!
 say, new nations must cross main,
 carry wars soft asian plain?
 must helen break second vow?
 paris thy darling now?
 left atrides, (victor strife,)
 odious conquest captive wife,
 hence let sail; thy paris bear
 absence ill, let venus ease care.
 handmaid goddess side wait,
 renounce glories thy heavenly state,
 fix’d ever trojan shore,
 spouse, slave; mount skies more.
 me, lawless love longer led,
 scorn coward, detest bed;
 else merit everlasting shame,
 keen reproach, every phrygian dame:
 ill suits now joys love know,
 deep anguish, wild woe.”
 

[illustration: ] venus presenting helen paris
 

thus incensed, paphian queen replies:
 “obey power thy glories rise:
 venus leave thee, every charm must fly,
 fade thy cheek, languish thy eye.
 cease provoke me, lest make thee more
 world’s aversion, love before;
 now bright prize mankind engage,
 than, sad victim, public rage.”
 
this, fairest sex obey’d,
 veil’d blushes silken shade;
 unseen, silent, train moves,
 led goddess smiles loves.
 arrived, enter’d palace gate,
 maids officious round mistress wait;
 then, dispersing, various tasks attend;
 queen goddess prince ascend.
 full paris’ sight, queen love
 placed beauteous progeny jove;
 where, view’d charms, turn’d away
 glowing eyes, thus began say:
 
“is chief, who, lost sense shame,
 late fled field, yet survives fame?
 hadst thou died beneath righteous sword
 brave man call’d lord!
 boaster paris oft desired day
 sparta’s king meet single fray:
 go now, thy rival’s rage excite,
 provoke atrides, renew fight:
 yet helen bids thee stay, lest thou unskill’d
 shouldst fall easy conquest field.”
 
prince replies: “ah cease, divinely fair,
 add reproaches wounds bear;
 day foe prevail’d pallas’ power:
 yet may vanquish happier hour:
 want gods favour us above;
 let business life love:
 softer moments let delights employ,
 kind embraces snatch hasty joy.
 thus loved thee, sparta’s shore
 forced, willing heavenly prize bore,
 first entranced cranae’s isle lay,[124]
 mix’d thy soul, dissolved away!”
 thus spoke, enamour’d phrygian boy
 rush’d bed, impatient joy.
 helen follow’d slow bashful charms,
 clasp’d blooming hero arms.
 
love’s delicious rapture yield,
 stern atrides rages round field:
 fell lion woods obey,
 roars desert, demands prey.
 paris seeks, impatient destroy,
 seeks vain along troops troy;
 even yielded foe brave
 recreant warrior, hateful grave.
 speaking thus, king kings arose,
 “ye trojans, dardans, generous foes!
 hear attest! heaven conquest crown’d,
 brother’s arms just success found:
 therefore now spartan wealth restor’d,
 let argive helen lawful lord;
 appointed fine let ilion justly pay,
 age age record signal day.”
 
ceased; army’s loud applauses rise,
 long shout runs echoing skies.
