book iv.
 

argument.
 

breach truce, first battle.
 

gods deliberate council concerning trojan war: agree
 upon continuation it, jupiter sends minerva break
 truce. persuades pandarus aim arrow menelaus, is
 wounded, cured machaon. meantime trojan
 troops attack greeks. agamemnon distinguished parts
 good general; reviews troops, exhorts leaders, some
 praises others reproof. nestor particularly celebrated for
 military discipline. battle joins, great numbers slain
 sides.
 day continues last book (as it
 also two following, almost end the
 seventh book). scene wholly field troy.
 

now olympus’ shining gates unfold;
 gods, jove, assume thrones gold:
 immortal hebe, fresh bloom divine,
 golden goblet crowns purple wine:
 full bowls flow round, powers employ
 careful eyes long-contended troy.
 
jove, disposed tempt saturnia’s spleen,
 thus waked fury partial queen,
 “two powers divine atreus aid,
 imperial juno, martial maid;[125]
 high heaven sit, gaze far,
 tame spectators deeds war.
 thus fair venus helps favour’d knight,
 queen pleasures shares toils fight,
 danger wards, constant care,
 saves moment last despair.
 act rescued paris’ forfeit life,
 though great atrides gain’d glorious strife.
 say, ye powers! signal issue waits
 crown deed, finish fates!
 shall heaven peace bleeding kingdoms spare,
 rouse furies, awake war?
 yet, gods human good provide,
 atrides soon might gain beauteous bride,
 still priam’s walls peaceful honours grow,
 gates crowding nations flow.”
 
thus spoke, queen heaven, enraged,
 queen war, close consult engaged:
 apart sit, deep designs employ,
 meditate future woes troy.
 though secret anger swell’d minerva’s breast,
 prudent goddess yet wrath suppress’d;
 juno, impotent passion, broke
 sullen silence, fury spoke:
 

[illustration: ] council gods
 

“shall then, tyrant ethereal reign!
 schemes, labours, hopes vain?
 i, this, shook ilion alarms,
 assembled nations, set two worlds arms?
 spread war, flew shore shore;
 immortal coursers scarce labour bore.
 length ripe vengeance o’er heads impends,
 jove faithless race defends.
 loth thou art punish lawless lust,
 gods partial unjust.”
 
sire whose thunder shakes cloudy skies,
 sighs inmost soul, thus replies:
 “oh lasting rancour! oh insatiate hate
 phrygia’s monarch, phrygian state!
 high offence fired wife jove?
 can wretched mortals harm powers above,
 troy, troy’s whole race thou wouldst confound,
 yon fair structures level ground!
 haste, leave skies, fulfil thy stern desire,
 burst gates, wrap walls fire!
 let priam bleed! yet thirst more,
 bleed sons, ilion float gore:
 boundless vengeance wide realm given,
 till vast destruction glut queen heaven!
 let be, jove peace enjoy,[126]
 heaven longer hears name troy.
 arm prepare wreak hate
 thy loved realms, whose guilt demands fate;
 presume thou lifted bolt stay,
 remember troy, give vengeance way.
 know, numerous towns rise
 beneath rolling sun starry skies,
 gods raised, earth-born men enjoy,
 none stands dear jove sacred troy.
 mortals merit distinguish’d grace
 godlike priam, priam’s race.
 still name hecatombs expire,
 altars blaze unextinguish’d fire.”
 
goddess rolled radiant eyes,
 thunderer fix’d them, replies:
 “three towns juno’s grecian plains,
 dear extended earth contains,
 mycenæ, argos, spartan wall;[127]
 
thou mayst raze, forbid fall:
 ’tis vengeance remove;
 crime’s sufficient share love.
 power superior complain?
 resent may, must resent vain.
 yet distinction juno might require,
 sprung thyself one celestial sire,
 goddess born, share realms above,
 styled consort thundering jove;
 thou wife sister’s right deny;[128]
 let consent, terms comply;
 shall gods joint decrees obey,
 heaven shall act direct way.
 see ready pallas waits thy high commands
 raise arms greek phrygian bands;
 sudden friendship arts may cease,
 proud trojans first infringe peace.”
 
sire men monarch sky
 advice approved, bade minerva fly,
 dissolve league, arts employ
 make breach faithless act troy.
 fired charge, headlong urged flight,
 shot like lightning olympus’ height.
 red comet, saturnius sent
 fright nations dire portent,
 (a fatal sign armies plain,
 trembling sailors wintry main,)
 sweeping glories glides along air,
 shakes sparkles blazing hair:[129]
 armies thus, open sight
 shot bright goddess trail light,
 eyes erect gazing hosts admire
 power descending, heavens fire!
 “the gods (they cried), gods signal sent,
 fate now labours vast event:
 jove seals league, bloodier scenes prepares;
 jove, great arbiter peace wars.”
 
said, pallas trojan throng,
 (in shape mortal,) pass’d disguised along.
 like bold laodocus, course bent,
 antenor traced high descent.
 amidst ranks lycaon’s found,
 warlike pandarus, strength renown’d;
 whose squadrons, led black Æsepus’ flood,[130]
 flaming shields martial circle stood.
 goddess: “phrygian! canst thou hear
 well-timed counsel willing ear?
 praise thine, couldst thou direct thy dart,
 amidst triumph, spartan’s heart?
 gifts troy, paris wouldst thou gain,
 thy country’s foe, grecian glory slain?
 seize occasion, dare mighty deed,
 aim breast, may aim succeed!
 first, speed shaft, address thy vow
 lycian phœbus silver bow,
 swear firstlings thy flock pay,
 zelia’s altars, god day.”[131]
 
heard, madly motion pleased,
 polish’d bow hasty rashness seized.
 ’twas form’d horn, smooth’d artful toil:
 mountain goat resign’d shining spoil.
 pierced long since beneath arrows bled;
 stately quarry cliffs lay dead,
 sixteen palms brow’s large honours spread:
 workmen join’d, shaped bended horns,
 beaten gold taper point adorns.
 this, greeks unseen, warrior bends,
 screen’d shields surrounding friends:
 meditates mark; couching low,
 fits sharp arrow well-strung bow.
 one hundred feather’d deaths chose,
 fated wound, cause future woes;
 offers vows hecatombs crown
 apollo’s altars native town.
 
now full force yielding horn bends,
 drawn arch, joins doubling ends;
 close breast strains nerve below,
 till barb’d points approach circling bow;
 impatient weapon whizzes wing;
 sounds tough horn, twangs quivering string.
 
thee, atrides! dangerous hour
 gods forget not, thy guardian power,
 pallas assists, (weakened force)
 diverts weapon destined course:
 babe, slumber seals eye,
 watchful mother wafts envenom’d fly.
 just belt golden buckles join’d,
 linen folds double corslet lined,
 turn’d shaft, which, hissing above,
 pass’d broad belt, corslet drove;
 folds pierced, plaited linen tore,
 razed skin, drew purple gore.
 stately trappings decreed
 grace monarch bounding steed,
 nymph caria mæonia bred,
 stains pure ivory lively red;
 equal lustre various colours vie,
 shining whiteness, tyrian dye:
 great atrides! show’d thy sacred blood,
 thy snowy thigh distill’d streaming flood.
 horror seized, king men descried
 shaft infix’d, saw gushing tide:
 less spartan fear’d, found
 shining barb appear wound,
 then, sigh, heaved manly breast,
 royal brother thus grief express’d,
 grasp’d hand; greeks around
 answering sighs return’d plaintive sound.
 
“oh, dear life! agree
 solemn truce, fatal truce thee!
 wert thou exposed hostile train,
 fight greece, conquer, slain!
 race trojans thy ruin join,
 faith scorn’d perjured line.
 thus vows, confirm’d wine gore,
 hands plighted, oaths swore,
 shall vain: heaven’s revenge slow,
 jove prepares strike fiercer blow.
 day shall come, great avenging day,
 troy’s proud glories dust shall lay,
 priam’s powers priam’s self shall fall,
 one prodigious ruin swallow all.
 see god, already, pole
 bare red arm, bid thunder roll;
 see eternal fury shed,
 shake ægis o’er guilty head.
 mighty woes perjured princes wait;
 thou, alas! deserv’st happier fate.
 still must mourn period thy days,
 mourn, without share praise?
 deprived thee, heartless greeks more
 shall dream conquests hostile shore;
 troy seized helen, glory lost,
 thy bones shall moulder foreign coast;
 proud trojan thus insulting cries,
 (and spurns dust menelaus lies,)
 ‘such trophies greece ilion brings,
 conquest king kings!
 proud vessels scatter’d o’er main,
 unrevenged, mighty brother slain.’
 oh! ere dire disgrace shall blast fame,
 o’erwhelm me, earth! hide monarch’s shame.”
 
said: leader’s brother’s fears
 possess soul, thus spartan cheers:
 “let thy words warmth greece abate;
 feeble dart guiltless fate:
 stiff rich embroider’d work around,
 varied belt repell’d flying wound.”
 
king: “my brother friend,
 thus, always thus, may heaven thy life defend!
 now seek skilful hand, whose powerful art
 may stanch effusion, extract dart.
 herald, swift, bid machaon bring
 speedy succour spartan king;
 pierced winged shaft (the deed troy),
 grecian’s sorrow, dardan’s joy.”
 
hasty zeal swift talthybius flies;
 thick files darts searching eyes,
 finds machaon, sublime stands[132]
 arms incircled native bands.
 thus: “machaon, king repair,
 wounded brother claims thy timely care;
 pierced lycian dardanian bow,
 grief us, triumph foe.”
 
heavy tidings grieved godlike man:
 swift succour ranks ran.
 dauntless king yet standing firm found,
 chiefs deep concern around.
 steely point reed join’d,
 shaft drew, left head behind.
 straight broad belt gay embroidery graced,
 loosed; corslet breast unbraced;
 suck’d blood, sovereign balm infused,[133]
 chiron gave, Æsculapius used.
 
round prince greeks employ care,
 trojans rush tumultuous war;
 glitter refulgent arms,
 fields fill’d dire alarms.
 seen king men appear
 confused, unactive, surprised fear;
 fond glory, severe delight,
 beating bosom claim’d rising fight.
 longer warlike steeds stay’d,
 press’d car polish’d brass inlaid
 left eurymedon reins guide;
 fiery coursers snorted side.
 foot martial ranks moves
 encourages, reproves.
 “brave men!” cries, (to boldly dare
 urge swift steeds face coming war),
 “your ancient valour foes approve;
 jove greece, let us trust jove.
 ’tis us, guilty troy, dread,
 whose crimes sit heavy perjured head;
 sons matrons greece shall lead chains,
 dead warriors strew mournful plains.”
 
thus new ardour brave inspires;
 thus fearful reproaches fires:
 “shame country, scandal kind;
 born fate ye well deserve find!
 stand ye gazing round dreadful plain,
 prepared flight, doom’d fly vain?
 confused panting thus, hunted deer
 falls flies, victim fear.
 still must ye wait foes, still retire,
 till yon tall vessels blaze trojan fire?
 trust ye, jove valiant foe shall chase,
 save trembling, heartless, dastard race?”
 
said, stalk’d ample strides along,
 crete’s brave monarch martial throng;
 high head saw chief appear,
 bold meriones excite rear.
 king generous joy express’d,
 clasp’d warrior armed breast.
 “divine idomeneus! thanks owe
 worth like thine! praise shall bestow?
 thee foremost honours decreed,
 first fight every graceful deed.
 this, banquets, generous bowls
 restore blood, raise warriors’ souls,
 though rest stated rules bound,
 unmix’d, unmeasured, thy goblets crown’d.
 still thyself, arms mighty name;
 maintain thy honours, enlarge thy fame.”
 cretan thus speech address’d:
 “secure me, king! exhort rest.
 fix’d thy side, every toil share,
 thy firm associate day war.
 let signal moment given;
 mix fight ask heaven.
 field shall prove perjuries succeed,
 chains death avenge impious deed.”
 
charm’d heat, king course pursues,
 next troops either ajax views:
 one firm orb bands ranged around,
 cloud heroes blacken’d ground.
 thus lofty promontory’s brow
 swain surveys gathering storm below;
 slow main heavy vapours rise,
 spread dim streams, sail along skies,
 till black night swelling tempest shows,
 cloud condensing west-wind blows:
 dreads impending storm, drives flock
 close covert arching rock.
 
such, thick, embattled squadrons stood,
 spears erect, moving iron wood:
 shady light shot glimmering shields,
 brown arms obscured dusky fields.
 
“o heroes! worthy dauntless train,
 whose godlike virtue urge vain,
 (exclaim’d king), raise eager bands
 great examples, loud commands.
 ah! gods breathe rest
 souls burn exalted breast,
 soon arms just success crown’d,
 troy’s proud walls lie smoking ground.”
 
next general bends course;
 (his heart exults, glories force);
 reverend nestor ranks pylian bands,
 inspiring eloquence commands;
 strictest order sets train arms,
 chiefs advises, soldiers warms.
 alastor, chromius, haemon, round wait,
 bias good, pelagon great.
 horse chariots front assign’d,
 foot (the strength war) ranged behind;
 middle space suspected troops supply,
 inclosed both, left power fly;
 gives command “curb fiery steed,
 cause confusion, ranks exceed:
 rest let none rashly ride;
 strength skill, just time, tried:
 charge made, warrior turn rein,
 fight, fall; firm embodied train.
 fortune field shall cast
 forth chariot, mount next haste;
 seek unpractised direct car,
 content javelins provoke war.
 great forefathers held prudent course,
 thus ruled ardour, thus preserved force;
 laws like immortal conquests made,
 earth’s proud tyrants low ashes laid.”
 
spoke master martial art,
 touch’d transport great atrides’ heart.
 “oh! hadst thou strength match thy brave desires,
 nerves second thy soul inspires!
 wasting years, wither human race,
 exhaust thy spirits, thy arms unbrace.
 thou wert, oh ever mightst thou be!
 age lot chief thee.”
 
thus experienced prince atrides cried;
 shook hoary locks, thus replied:
 “well might wish, mortal wish renew[134]
 strength boiling youth knew;
 was, ereuthalion, slain
 beneath arm, fell prostrate plain.
 heaven gifts bestows,
 years wisdom crowns, action those:
 field combat fits young bold,
 solemn council best becomes old:
 glorious conflict resign,
 let sage advice, palm age, mine.”
 
said. joy monarch march’d before,
 found menestheus dusty shore,
 firm athenian phalanx stands;
 next ulysses, subject bands.
 remote forces lay, knew far
 peace infringed, heard sounds war;
 tumult late begun, stood intent
 watch motion, dubious event.
 king, saw squadrons yet unmoved,
 hasty ardour thus chiefs reproved:
 
“can peleus’ forget warrior’s part.
 fears ulysses, skill’d every art?
 stand distant, rest expect
 mix combat neglect?
 ’twas hoped among first dare
 shock armies, commence war;
 names call’d rest,
 share pleasures genial feast:
 can you, chiefs! without blush survey
 whole troops labouring fray?
 say, thus honours requite?
 first banquets, last fight.”
 
ulysses heard: hero’s warmth o’erspread
 cheek blushes: severe, said:
 “take back unjust reproach! behold stand
 sheathed bright arms, expect command.
 glorious deeds afford thy soul delight,
 behold plunging thickest fight.
 give thy warrior-chief warrior’s due,
 dares act whate’er thou dar’st view.”
 struck generous wrath, king replies:
 
“o great action, council wise!
 ours, thy care ardour same,
 need commend, aught blame.
 sage thou art, learn’d human kind,
 forgive transport martial mind.
 haste fight, secure just amends;
 gods make, shall keep worthy, friends.”
 
said, pass’d great tydides lay,
 steeds chariots wedged firm array;
 (the warlike sthenelus attends side;)[135]
 stern reproach monarch cried:
 “o tydeus! (he, whose strength tame
 bounding steed, arms mighty name)
 canst thou, remote, mingling hosts descry,
 hands unactive, careless eye?
 thus thy sire fierce encounter fear’d;
 still first front matchless prince appear’d:
 glorious toils, wonders recite,
 view’d labouring ranks fight?
 saw once, gathering martial powers,
 peaceful guest, sought mycenæ’s towers;
 armies ask’d, armies given,
 denied, jove forbade heaven;
 dreadful comets glaring afar,
 forewarn’d horrors theban war.[136]
 next, sent greece asopus flows,
 fearless envoy, approach’d foes;
 thebes’ hostile walls unguarded alone,
 dauntless enters, demands throne.
 tyrant feasting chiefs found,
 dared combat chiefs around:
 dared, subdued haughty lord;
 pallas strung arm edged sword.
 stung shame, within winding way,
 bar passage fifty warriors lay;
 two heroes led secret squadron on,
 mason fierce, hardy lycophon;
 fifty slaughter’d gloomy vale.
 spared one bear dreadful tale,
 tydeus was, martial fire;
 gods! degenerates sire!”
 
words godlike diomed return’d,
 heard respectful, secret burn’d:
 fierce capaneus’ undaunted son;
 stern sire, boaster thus begun:
 
“what needs, monarch! invidious praise,
 lessen, sire raise?
 dare just, atrides! confess
 value equal, though fury less.
 fewer troops storm’d theban wall,
 happier saw sevenfold city fall,[137]
 impious acts guilty father died;
 sons subdued, heaven side.
 far heirs parents’ fame,
 glories darken diminish’d name.”
 
tydides thus: “my friend, forbear;
 suppress thy passion, king revere:
 high concern may well excuse rage,
 whose cause follow, whose war wage:
 first praise, ilion’s towers o’erthrown,
 and, fail, chief disgrace own.
 let greeks hardy toils excite,
 ’tis labour glorious fight.”
 
spoke, ardent, trembling ground
 sprung car: ringing arms resound.
 dire clang, dreadful afar,
 arm’d tydides rushing war.
 winds, ascending degrees,[138]
 first move whitening surface seas,
 billows float order shore,
 wave behind rolls wave before;
 till, growing storm, deeps arise,
 foam o’er rocks, thunder skies.
 fight thick battalions throng,
 shields urged shields, men drove men along
 sedate silent move numerous bands;
 sound, whisper, chief’s commands,
 heard; awe rest obey,
 god snatch’d voice away.
 trojans; host ascends
 general shout region rends.
 fleecy flocks unnumber’d stand
 wealthy folds, wait milker’s hand,
 hollow vales incessant bleating fills,
 lambs reply neighbouring hills:
 clamours rose various nations round,
 mix’d murmur, confused sound.
 host now joins, god inspires,
 mars incites, minerva fires,
 pale flight around, dreadful terror reign;
 discord raging bathes purple plain;
 discord! dire sister slaughtering power,
 small birth, rising every hour,
 scarce skies horrid head can bound,
 stalks earth, shakes world around;[139]
 nations bleed, where’er steps turns,
 groan still deepens, combat burns.
 
now shield shield, helmet helmet closed,
 armour armour, lance lance opposed,
 host host shadowy squadrons drew,
 sounding darts iron tempests flew,
 victors vanquish’d join’d promiscuous cries,
 shrilling shouts dying groans arise;
 streaming blood slippery fields dyed,
 slaughter’d heroes swell dreadful tide.
 
torrents roll, increased numerous rills,
 rage impetuous, echoing hills
 rush vales, pour’d along plain,
 roar thousand channels main:
 distant shepherd trembling hears sound;
 mix hosts, cries rebound.
 
bold antilochus slaughter led,
 first struck valiant trojan dead:
 great echepolus lance arrives,
 razed high crest, helmet drives;
 warm’d brain brazen weapon lies,
 shades eternal settle o’er eyes.
 sinks tower, long assaults stood
 force fire, walls besmear’d blood.
 him, bold leader abantian throng,[140]
 seized despoil, dragg’d corpse along:
 strove tug inserted dart,
 agenor’s javelin reach’d hero’s heart.
 flank, unguarded ample shield,
 admits lance: falls, spurns field;
 nerves, unbraced, support limbs more;
 soul comes floating tide gore.
 trojans greeks now gather round slain;
 war renews, warriors bleed again:
 o’er prey rapacious wolves engage,
 man dies man, blood rage.
 
blooming youth fair simoisius fell,
 sent great ajax shades hell;
 fair simoisius, mother bore
 amid flocks silver simois’ shore:
 nymph descending hills ide,
 seek parents flowery side,
 brought forth babe, common care joy,
 thence simois named lovely boy.
 short date! dreadful ajax slain,
 falls, renders cares vain!
 falls poplar, watery ground
 raised high head, stately branches crown’d,
 (fell’d artist shining steel,
 shape circle bending wheel,)
 cut lies, tall, smooth, largely spread,
 beauteous honours head
 there, left subject wind rain,
 scorch’d suns, withers plain
 thus pierced ajax, simoisius lies
 stretch’d shore, thus neglected dies.
 
ajax, antiphus javelin threw;
 pointed lance erring fury flew,
 leucus, loved wise ulysses, slew.
 drops corpse simoisius slain,
 sinks breathless carcase plain.
 saw ulysses, grief enraged,
 strode foremost foes engaged;
 arm’d spear, meditates wound,
 act throw; cautious look’d around,
 struck sight trojans backward drew,
 trembling heard javelin flew.
 chief stood nigh, abydos came,
 old priam’s son, democoon name.
 weapon entered close ear,
 cold temples glides whizzing spear;[141]
 piercing shrieks youth resigns breath,
 eye-balls darken shades death;
 ponderous falls; clanging arms resound,
 broad buckler rings ground.
 
seized affright boldest foes appear;
 e’en godlike hector seems fear;
 slow gave way, rest tumultuous fled;
 greeks shouts press on, spoil dead:
 phœbus now ilion’s towering height
 shines forth reveal’d, animates fight.
 “trojans, bold, force force oppose;
 foaming steeds urge headlong foes!
 bodies rocks, ribb’d steel;
 weapons enter, strokes feel.
 ye forgot seem’d dread before?
 great, fierce achilles fights more.”
 
apollo thus ilion’s lofty towers,
 array’d terrors, roused trojan powers:
 war’s fierce goddess fires grecian foe,
 shouts thunders fields below.
 great diores fell, doom divine,
 vain valour illustrious line.
 broken rock force pyrus threw,
 (who cold Ænus led thracian crew,)[142]
 full ankle dropp’d ponderous stone,
 burst strong nerves, crash’d solid bone.
 supine tumbles crimson sands,
 helpless friends, native bands,
 spreads aid unavailing hands.
 foe rush’d furious pants breath,
 navel drove pointed death:
 gushing entrails smoked upon ground,
 warm life came issuing wound.
 
lance bold thoas conqueror sent,
 deep breast pap went,
 amid lungs fix’d winged wood,
 quivering heaving bosom stood:
 till dying chief, approaching near,
 Ætolian warrior tugg’d weighty spear:
 sudden waved flaming falchion round,
 gash’d belly ghastly wound;
 corpse now breathless bloody plain,
 spoil arms victor strove vain;
 thracian bands victor press’d,
 grove lances glitter’d breast.
 stern thoas, glaring revengeful eyes,
 sullen fury slowly quits prize.
 
thus fell two heroes; one pride thrace,
 one leader epeian race;
 death’s sable shade o’ercast eyes,
 dust vanquish’d victor lies.
 copious slaughter fields red,
 heap’d growing mountains dead.
 
brave chief martial scene beheld,
 pallas guarded dreadful field;
 might darts bid turn points away,
 swords around innocently play;
 war’s whole art wonder seen,
 counted heroes counted men.
 
fought host, thirst glory fired,
 crowds crowds triumphantly expired.

acts diomed.
 

diomed, assisted pallas, performs wonders day’s battle.
 pandarus wounds arrow, goddess cures him, enables
 discern gods mortals, prohibits contending
 former, excepting venus. Æneas joins pandarus oppose
 him; pandarus killed, Æneas great danger the
 assistance venus; who, removing fight, is
 wounded hand diomed. apollo seconds rescue, at
 length carries Æneas troy, healed temple of
 pergamus. mars rallies trojans, assists hector make stand.
 meantime Æneas restored field, overthrow
 several greeks; among rest tlepolemus slain sarpedon.
 juno minerva descend resist mars; latter incites diomed to
 go god; wounds him, sends groaning heaven.
 first battle continues book. scene same
 former.
 

pallas now tydides’ soul inspires,[143]
 fills force, warms fires,
 greeks deathless fame raise,
 crown hero distinguish’d praise.
 high helm celestial lightnings play,
 beamy shield emits living ray;
 unwearied blaze incessant streams supplies,
 like red star fires autumnal skies,
 fresh rears radiant orb sight,
 and, bathed ocean, shoots keener light.
 glories pallas chief bestow’d,
 such, arms, fierce effulgence flow’d:
 onward drives him, furious engage,
 fight burns, thickest rage.
 
sons dares first combat sought,
 wealthy priest, rich without fault;
 vulcan’s fane father’s days led,
 sons toils glorious battle bred;
 singled troops fight maintain,
 these, steeds, tydides plain.
 fierce renown brother-chiefs draw near,
 first bold phegeus cast sounding spear,
 o’er warrior’s shoulder took course,
 spent empty air erring force.
 so, tydides, flew thy lance vain,
 pierced breast, stretch’d plain.
 seized unusual fear, idæus fled,
 left rich chariot, brother dead.
 vulcan lent celestial aid,
 sunk death’s eternal shade;
 smoky cloud god fire
 preserved son, pity sire.
 steeds chariot, navy led,
 increased spoils gallant diomed.
 
struck amaze shame, trojan crew,
 slain, fled, sons dares view;
 blood-stain’d hand minerva press’d
 god battles, speech address’d:
 
“stern power war! mighty fall,
 bathe blood, shake lofty wall!
 let brave chiefs glorious toils divide;
 whose conquest, mighty jove decide:
 interdicted fields retire,
 tempt wrath heaven’s avenging sire.”
 
words allay impetuous warrior’s heat,
 god arms martial maid retreat;
 removed fight, xanthus’ flowery bounds
 sat, listen’d dying sounds.
 
meantime, greeks trojan race pursue,
 bold chieftain every leader slew:
 first odius falls, bites bloody sand,
 death ennobled atrides’ hand:
 
flight wheeling car address’d,
 speedy javelin drove back breast.
 dust mighty halizonian lay,
 arms resound, spirit wings way.
 
thy fate next, phæstus! doom’d feel
 great idomeneus’ protended steel;
 borus sent (his joy)
 fruitful tarne fields troy.
 cretan javelin reach’d afar,
 pierced shoulder mounts car;
 back car tumbles ground,
 everlasting shades eyes surround.
 
died scamandrius, expert chase,
 woods wilds wound savage race;
 diana taught sylvan arts,
 bend bow, aim unerring darts:
 vainly diana’s arts tries,
 fatal lance arrests flies;
 menelaus’ arm weapon sent,
 broad back heaving bosom went:
 sinks warrior thundering sound,
 brazen armour rings ground.
 
next artful phereclus untimely fell;
 bold merion sent realms hell.
 thy father’s skill, phereclus! thine,
 graceful fabric fair design;
 loved pallas, pallas impart
 shipwright’s builder’s art.
 beneath hand fleet paris rose,
 fatal cause country’s woes;
 he, mystic will heaven unknown,
 saw country’s peril, own.
 hapless artist, confused fled,
 spear merion mingled dead.
 right hip, forceful fury cast,
 bladder bone pass’d;
 prone knees falls fruitless cries,
 death lasting slumber seals eyes.
 
meges’ force swift pedaeus fled,
 antenor’s offspring foreign bed,
 whose generous spouse, theanor, heavenly fair,
 nursed young stranger mother’s care.
 vain cares! meges rear
 full nape infix’d fatal spear;
 swift crackling jaws weapon glides,
 cold tongue grinning teeth divides.
 
died hypsenor, generous divine,
 sprung brave dolopion’s mighty line,
 near adored scamander made abode,
 priest stream, honoured god.
 him, amidst flying numbers found,
 eurypylus inflicts deadly wound;
 broad shoulders fell forceful brand,
 thence glancing downwards, lopp’d holy hand,
 stain’d sacred blood blushing sand.
 sunk priest: purple hand death
 closed dim eye, fate suppress’d breath.
 
thus toil’d chiefs, different parts engaged.
 every quarter fierce tydides raged;
 amid greek, amid trojan train,
 rapt ranks thunders o’er plain;
 now here, now there, darts place place,
 pours rear, lightens face.
 thus high hills torrents swift strong
 deluge whole fields, sweep trees along,
 ruin’d moles rushing wave resounds,
 o’erwhelm’s bridge, bursts lofty bounds;
 yellow harvests ripen’d year,
 flatted vineyards, one sad waste appear![144]
 jove descends sluicy sheets rain,
 labours mankind vain.
 
raged tydides, boundless ire,
 drove armies back, made troy retire.
 grief leader lycian band
 saw wide waste destructive hand:
 bended bow chief drew;
 swift mark thirsty arrow flew,
 whose forky point hollow breastplate tore,
 deep shoulder pierced, drank gore:
 rushing stream brazen armour dyed,
 proud archer thus exulting cried:
 
“hither, ye trojans, hither drive steeds!
 lo! hand bravest grecian bleeds,
 long deathful dart can sustain;
 phœbus urged fields vain.”
 spoke he, boastful: winged dart
 stopp’d short life, mock’d shooter’s art.
 wounded chief, behind car retired,
 helping hand sthenelus required;
 swift seat leap’d upon ground,
 tugg’d weapon gushing wound;
 thus king guardian power address’d,
 purple current wandering o’er vest:
 
“o progeny jove! unconquer’d maid!
 e’er godlike sire deserved thy aid,
 e’er felt thee fighting field;
 now, goddess, now, thy sacred succour yield.
 give lance reach trojan knight,
 whose arrow wounds chief thou guard’st fight;
 lay boaster grovelling shore,
 vaunts eyes shall view light more.”
 
thus pray’d tydides, minerva heard,
 nerves confirm’d, languid spirits cheer’d;
 feels limb wonted vigour light;
 beating bosom claim’d promised fight.
 “be bold, (she cried), every combat shine,
 war thy province, thy protection mine;
 rush fight, every foe control;
 wake paternal virtue thy soul:
 strength swells thy boiling breast, infused me,
 thy godlike father breathes thee;
 yet more, mortal mists purge thy eyes,[145]
 set view warring deities.
 see thou shun, embattled plain;
 rashly strive human force vain.
 venus mingle martial band,
 shalt thou wound: pallas gives command.”
 
that, blue-eyed virgin wing’d flight;
 hero rush’d impetuous fight;
 tenfold ardour now invades plain,
 wild delay, enraged pain.
 fleecy flocks hunger calls,
 amidst field brindled lion falls;
 chance shepherd distant dart
 savage wound, rouses smart,
 foams, roars; shepherd dares stay,
 trembling leaves scattering flocks prey;
 heaps fall heaps; bathes blood ground,
 leaps victorious o’er lofty mound.
 less fury stern tydides flew;
 two brave leaders instant slew;
 astynous breathless fell, side,
 people’s pastor, good hypenor, died;
 astynous’ breast deadly lance receives,
 hypenor’s shoulder broad falchion cleaves.
 slain left, sprung noble rage
 abas polyidus engage;
 sons eurydamus, who, wise old,
 fate foresee, mystic dreams unfold;
 youths return’d doubtful plain,
 sad father tried arts vain;
 mystic dream make fates appear,
 though now determined tydides’ spear.
 
young xanthus next, thoon felt rage;
 joy hope phaenops’ feeble age:
 vast wealth, heirs
 labours life cares.
 cold death o’ertakes blooming years,
 leaves father unavailing tears:
 strangers now descends heapy store,
 race forgotten, name more.
 
two sons priam one chariot ride,
 glittering arms, combat side side.
 lordly lion seeks food
 grazing heifers range lonely wood,
 leaps amidst furious bound,
 bends strong necks, tears ground:
 seats brother chiefs torn,
 steeds chariot navy borne.
 
deep concern divine Æneas view’d
 foe prevailing, friends pursued;
 thick storm singing spears flies,
 exploring pandarus careful eyes.
 length found lycaon’s mighty son;
 chief venus’ race begun:
 
“where, pandarus, thy honours now,
 thy winged arrows unerring bow,
 thy matchless skill, thy yet unrivall’d fame,
 boasted glory lycian name?
 pierce mortal! mortal call
 wondrous force whole armies fall;
 god incensed, quits distant skies
 punish troy slighted sacrifice;
 (which, oh avert unhappy state!
 dreadful celestial hate)?
 whoe’er be, propitiate jove prayer;
 man, destroy; god, entreat spare.”
 
lycian: “whom eyes behold,
 right judge, diomed bold:
 coursers whirl o’er dusty field,
 towers helmet, flames shield.
 ’tis god, wears chief’s disguise:
 chief, guardian skies,
 involved clouds, protects fray,
 turns unseen frustrate dart away.
 wing’d arrow, idly fell,
 stroke fix’d gates hell;
 and, god, angry god withstands,
 fate due unerring hands.
 skill’d bow, foot sought war,
 join’d swift horses rapid car.
 ten polish’d chariots possess’d home,
 still grace lycaon’s princely dome:
 veil’d spacious coverlets stand;
 twice ten coursers wait lord’s command.
 good old warrior bade trust these,
 first troy sail’d sacred seas;
 fields, aloft, whirling car guide,
 ranks death triumphant ride.
 vain youth, yet thrift inclined,
 heard counsels unheedful mind,
 thought steeds (your large supplies unknown)
 might fail forage straiten’d town;
 took bow pointed darts hand
 left chariots native land.
 
“too late, friend! rashness deplore;
 shafts, fatal, carry death more.
 tydeus’ atreus’ sons points found,
 undissembled gore pursued wound.
 vain bleed: unavailing bow
 serves, slaughter, provoke foe.
 evil hour bended horns strung,

 cursed fate sent field
 without warrior’s arms, spear shield!
 e’er life quit trojan plain,
 e’er see spouse sire again,
 bow, unfaithful glorious aims,
 broke hand, shall feed blazing flames.”
 
leader dardan race:
 “be calm, phœbus’ honour’d gift disgrace.
 distant dart praised, though need
 rushing chariot bounding steed.
 yon hero let us bend course,
 and, hand hand, encounter force force.
 now mount seat, chariot’s height

 practised alike turn, stop, chase,

 secure these, fighting fields go;
 safe troy, jove assist foe.
 haste, seize whip, snatch guiding rein;
 warrior’s fury let arm sustain;

 take thou spear, chariot’s care mine.”
 
“o prince! (lycaon’s valiant replied)
 thine steeds, thine task guide.
 horses, practised lord’s command,

 these, victor’s prize, triumph led.
 thine guidance, then: spear shield

now heroes mount glittering car;

“o friend! two chiefs force immense see,

 save life, bulwark war.”
 
hero cast gloomy look,
 fix’d chief scorn; thus spoke:
 
“me dost thou bid shun coming fight?
 wouldst thou move base, inglorious flight?
 know, ’tis honest soul fear,
 tydides born tremble here.
 hate cumbrous chariot’s slow advance,

 nerves strong, force entire,

 pallas tells me, forbids fly.
 dooms, god withstand,

 wide world make glory known.”

said, shook ponderous lance, flung;

guard slaughter’d friend, Æneas flies,

 men live degenerate days:[147]

 brave chief, mighty numbers sway’d,

 much-loved arms throws,

chief thus answered mild: “immortal maid!
 thy presence, confess thy aid.
 fear, thou know’st, withholds plains,
 sloth hath seized me, thy word restrains:
 warring gods thou bad’st turn spear,
 venus found resistance here.
 hence, goddess! heedful thy high commands,
 loth gave way, warn’d argive bands:
 mars, homicide, eyes beheld,
 slaughter red, raging round field.”
 
thus minerva:—“brave tydides, hear!
 mars himself, aught immortal, fear.
 full god impel thy foaming horse:
 pallas commands, pallas lends thee force.
 rash, furious, blind, flies,
 every side wavering combat tries;
 large promise makes, breaks promise made:
 now gives grecians, now trojans aid.”[159]
 
said, steeds approaching near,
 drew seat martial charioteer.
 vigorous power trembling car ascends,
 fierce revenge; diomed attends:
 groaning axle bent beneath load;
 great hero, great god.
 snatch’d reins, lash’d force,
 full mars impelled foaming horse:
 first, hide heavenly visage, spread
 black orcus’ helmet o’er radiant head.
 

[illustration: ] diomed casting spear mars
 

just gigantic periphas lay slain,
 strongest warrior Ætolian train;
 god, slew him, leaves prostrate prize
 stretch’d fell, tydides flies.
 now rushing fierce, equal arms appear
 daring greek, dreadful god war!
 full chief, courser’s head,
 mars’s arm enormous weapon fled:
 pallas opposed hand, caused glance
 far car strong immortal lance.
 threw force tydeus’ warlike son;
 javelin hiss’d; goddess urged on:
 broad cincture girt armour round,
 pierced god: groin received wound.
 rent skin warrior tugs again
 smoking steel. mars bellows pain:
 loud roar encountering armies yield,
 shouting millions shake thundering field.
 armies start, trembling gaze around;
 earth heaven re-bellow sound.
 vapours blown auster’s sultry breath,
 pregnant plagues, shedding seeds death,
 beneath rage burning sirius rise,
 choke parch’d earth, blacken skies;
 cloud god combat driven,
 high o’er dusky whirlwind scales heaven.
 wild pain, sought bright abodes,
 sullen sat beneath sire gods,
 show’d celestial blood, groan
 thus pour’d plaints immortal throne:
 
“can jove, supine, flagitious facts survey,
 brook furies daring day?
 mortal men celestial powers engage,
 gods gods exert eternal rage:
 thee, father! ills bear,
 thy fell daughter shield spear;
 thou gavest fury realms light,
 pernicious, wild, regardless right.
 heaven beside reveres thy sovereign sway,
 thy voice hear, thy behests obey:
 ’tis offend, even offending share
 thy breast, thy counsels, thy distinguish’d care:
 boundless she, thou partial grown,
 well may deem wondrous birth thy own.
 now frantic diomed, command,
 immortals lifts raging hand:
 heavenly venus first fury found,
 next encountering, dared wound;
 vanquish’d fled; even i, god fight,
 mortal madness scarce saved flight.
 else hadst thou seen sink yonder plain,
 heap’d round, heaving loads slain!
 pierced grecian darts, ages lie,
 condemn’d pain, though fated die.”
 
thus upbraiding, wrathful look
 lord thunders view’d, stern bespoke:
 “to me, perfidious! lamenting strain?
 lawless force shall lawless mars complain?
 gods tread spangled skies,
 thou unjust, odious eyes!
 inhuman discord thy dire delight,
 waste slaughter, rage fight.
 bounds, law, thy fiery temper quells,
 thy mother thy soul rebels.
 vain threats, vain power use;
 gives example, pursues.
 yet long inflicted pangs thou shall mourn,
 sprung since thou art jove, heavenly-born.
 else, singed lightning, hadst thou hence thrown,
 chain’d burning rocks titans groan.”
 
thus shakes olympus nod;
 gave pæon’s care bleeding god.[160]
 gentle hand balm pour’d around,
 heal’d immortal flesh, closed wound.
 fig’s press’d juice, infused cream,
 curds coagulates liquid stream,
 sudden fluids fix parts combined;
 such, soon, ethereal texture join’d.
 cleansed dust gore, fair hebe dress’d
 mighty limbs immortal vest.
 glorious sat, majesty restored,
 fast throne heaven’s superior lord.
 juno pallas mount bless’d abodes,
 task perform’d, mix among gods.

book vi.
 

argument.
 

episodes glaucus diomed, hector andromache.
 

gods left field, grecians prevail. helenus, the
 chief augur troy, commands hector return city, order to
 appoint solemn procession queen trojan matrons the
 temple minerva, entreat remove diomed fight. the
 battle relaxing absence hector, glaucus diomed have
 interview two armies; where, coming knowledge, of
 friendship hospitality passed ancestors, they
 make exchange arms. hector, performed orders of
 helenus, prevails upon paris return battle, and, taking a
 tender leave wife andromache, hastens field.
 scene first field battle, rivers
 simois scamander, changes troy.
 

now heaven forsakes fight: immortals yield
 human force human skill field:
 dark showers javelins fly foes foes;
 now here, now there, tide combat flows;
 troy’s famed streams, bound deathful plain
 either side, run purple main.
 
great ajax first conquest led way,
 broke thick ranks, turn’d doubtful day.
 thracian acamas falchion found,
 hew’d enormous giant ground;
 thundering arm deadly stroke impress’d
 black horse-hair nodded o’er crest;
 fix’d front brazen weapon lies,
 seals endless shades swimming eyes.
 next teuthras’ distain’d sands blood,
 axylus, hospitable, rich, good:
 fair arisbe’s walls (his native place)[161]
 held seat! friend human race.
 fast road, ever-open door
 obliged wealthy, relieved poor.
 stern tydides now falls prey,
 friend guard dreadful day!
 breathless good man fell, side
 faithful servant, old calesius died.
 
great euryalus dresus slain,
 next laid opheltius plain.
 two twins near, bold, beautiful, young,
 fair naiad bucolion sprung:
 (laomedon’s white flocks bucolion fed,
 monarch’s first-born foreign bed;
 secret woods won naiad’s grace,
 two fair infants crown’d strong embrace:)
 dead lay youthful charms;
 ruthless victor stripp’d shining arms.
 
astyalus polypœtes fell;
 ulysses’ spear pidytes sent hell;
 teucer’s shaft brave aretaon bled,
 nestor’s laid stern ablerus dead;
 great agamemnon, leader brave,
 mortal wound rich elatus gave,
 held pedasus proud abode,[162]
 till’d banks silver satnio flow’d.
 melanthius eurypylus slain;
 phylacus leitus flies vain.
 
unbless’d adrastus next mercy lies
 beneath spartan spear, living prize.
 scared din tumult fight,
 headlong steeds, precipitate flight,
 rush’d tamarisk’s strong trunk, broke
 shatter’d chariot crooked yoke;
 wide o’er field, resistless wind,
 troy fly, leave lord behind.
 prone face sinks beside wheel:
 atrides o’er shakes vengeful steel;
 fallen chief suppliant posture press’d
 victor’s knees, thus prayer address’d:
 
“o spare youth, life owe
 large gifts price father shall bestow.
 fame shall tell, that, battle slain,
 thy hollow ships captive detain:
 rich heaps brass shall thy tent told,[163]
 steel well-temper’d, persuasive gold.”
 
said: compassion touch’d hero’s heart
 stood, suspended lifted dart:
 pity pleaded vanquish’d prize,
 stern agamemnon swift vengeance flies,
 and, furious, thus: “oh impotent mind![164]
 shall these, shall atrides’ mercy find?
 well hast thou known proud troy’s perfidious land,
 well natives merit thy hand!
 one race, sex, age,
 shall save trojan boundless rage:
 ilion shall perish whole, bury all;
 babes, infants breast, shall fall;[165]
 dreadful lesson exampled fate,
 warn nations, curb great!”
 
monarch spoke; words, warmth address’d,
 rigid justice steel’d brother’s breast.
 fierce knees hapless chief thrust;
 monarch’s javelin stretch’d dust,
 pressing foot panting heart,
 forth slain tugg’d reeking dart.
 old nestor saw, roused warrior’s rage;
 “thus, heroes! thus vigorous combat wage;
 mars descend, servile gains,
 touch booty, foe remains.
 behold yon glittering host, future spoil!
 first gain conquest, reward toil.”
 
now greece eternal fame acquired,
 frighted troy within walls, retired,
 sage helenus state redress’d,
 taught gods moved sacred breast.
 hector stood, great Æneas join’d,
 seer reveal’d counsels mind:
 
“ye generous chiefs! immortals lay
 cares glories doubtful day;
 aids, country’s hopes depend;
 wise consult, active defend!
 here, gates, brave efforts unite,
 turn back routed, forbid flight,
 ere yet wives’ soft arms cowards gain,
 sport insult hostile train.
 commands hearten’d every band,
 ourselves, fix’d, will make dangerous stand;
 press’d are, sore former fight,
 straits demand last remains might.
 meanwhile thou, hector, town retire,
 teach mother gods require:
 direct queen lead assembled train
 troy’s chief matrons minerva’s fane;[166]
 unbar sacred gates, seek power,
 offer’d vows, ilion’s topmost tower.
 largest mantle rich wardrobes hold,
 prized art, labour’d o’er gold,
 goddess’ honour’d knees spread,
 twelve young heifers altars led:
 power, atoned fervent prayer,
 wives, infants, city spare,
 far avert tydides’ wasteful ire,
 mows whole troops, makes troy retire;
 thus achilles taught hosts dread,
 sprung though mortal bed;
 thus resistless ruled stream fight,
 rage unbounded, unmatch’d might.”
 
hector obedient heard: and, bound,
 leap’d trembling chariot ground;
 host inspiring force flies,
 bids thunder battle rise.
 rage recruited bold trojans glow,
 turn tide conflict foe:
 fierce front shakes two dazzling spears;
 greece recedes, ’midst triumphs fears;
 god, thought, ruled fate wars,
 shot avenging vault stars.
 
thus aloud: “ye dauntless dardans, hear!
 distant nations send war!
 mindful strength fathers bore;
 still yourselves, hector asks more.
 one hour demands trojan wall,
 bid altars flame, victims fall:
 shall, trust, matrons’ holy train,
 reverend elders, seek gods vain.”
 
said, ample strides hero pass’d;
 shield’s large orb behind shoulder cast,
 neck o’ershading, ankle hung;
 march’d brazen buckler rung.
 
now paused battle (godlike hector gone),[167]
 daring glaucus great tydeus’ son
 armies met: chiefs far
 observed other, mark’d war.
 near drew, tydides thus began:
 
“what art thou, boldest race man?
 eyes till now aspect ne’er beheld,
 fame reap’d amid embattled field;
 yet far troops thou dar’st appear,
 meet lance fiercest heroes fear.
 unhappy they, born luckless sires,
 tempt fury minerva fires!
 heaven, celestial, thou descend,
 know immortals contend.
 long lycurgus view’d golden light,
 daring man mix’d gods fight.
 bacchus, bacchus’ votaries, drove,
 brandish’d steel, nyssa’s sacred grove:
 consecrated spears lay scatter’d round,
 curling vines twisted ivy bound;
 bacchus headlong sought briny flood,
 thetis’ arms received trembling god.
 fail’d crime immortals’ wrath move;
 (the immortals bless’d endless ease above;)
 deprived sight avenging doom,
 cheerless breathed, wander’d gloom,
 sunk unpitied dire abodes,
 wretch accursed, hated gods!
 brave heaven: fruits earth
 sustain thy life, human thy birth,
 bold thou art, prodigal breath,
 approach, enter dark gates death.”
 
“what, whence am, sire,
 (replied chief,) can tydeus’ inquire?
 like leaves trees race man found,
 now green youth, now withering ground;
 another race following spring supplies;
 fall successive, successive rise:
 generations course decay;
 flourish these, pass’d away.
 thou still persist search birth,
 hear tale fills spacious earth.
 
“a city stands argos’ utmost bound,
 (argos fair, warlike steeds renown’d,)
 Æolian sisyphus, wisdom bless’d,
 ancient time happy wall possess’d,
 call’d ephyre: glaucus son;
 great glaucus, father bellerophon,
 o’er sons men beauty shined,
 loved valour preserves mankind.
 mighty praetus argos’ sceptre sway’d,
 whose hard commands bellerophon obey’d.
 direful jealousy monarch raged,
 brave prince numerous toils engaged.
 antaea burn’d lawless flame,
 strove tempt paths fame:
 vain tempted relentless youth,
 endued wisdom, sacred fear, truth.
 fired scorn queen praetus fled,
 begg’d revenge insulted bed:
 incensed heard, resolving fate;
 hospitable laws restrain’d hate:
 lycia devoted youth sent,
 tablets seal’d, told dire intent.[168]
 now bless’d every power guards good,
 chief arrived xanthus’ silver flood:
 lycia’s monarch paid honours due,
 nine days feasted, nine bulls slew.
 tenth bright morning orient glow’d,
 faithful youth monarch’s mandate show’d:
 fatal tablets, till instant seal’d,
 deathful secret king reveal’d.
 first, dire chimaera’s conquest enjoin’d;
 mingled monster mortal kind!
 behind, dragon’s fiery tail spread;
 goat’s rough body bore lion’s head;
 pitchy nostrils flaky flames expire;
 gaping throat emits infernal fire.
 
“this pest slaughter’d, (for read skies,
 trusted heaven’s informing prodigies,)
 met arms solymæan crew,[169]
 (fiercest men,) warrior slew;
 next bold amazons’ whole force defied;
 conquer’d still, heaven side.
 
“nor ended toils: lycian foes,
 return, treacherous ambush rose,
 levell’d spears along winding shore:
 fell breathless, return’d more.
 
“at length monarch, repentant grief,
 confess’d gods, god-descended chief;
 daughter gave, stranger detain,
 half honours ample reign:
 lycians grant chosen space ground,
 woods, vineyards, harvests crown’d.
 long chief happy lot possess’d,
 two brave sons one fair daughter bless’d;
 (fair e’en heavenly eyes: fruitful love
 crown’d sarpedon’s birth embrace jove;)
 last, distracted mind,
 forsook heaven, forsaking humankind,
 wide o’er aleian field chose stray,
 long, forlorn, uncomfortable way![170]
 woes heap’d woes consumed wasted heart:
 beauteous daughter fell phoebe’s dart;
 eldest born raging mars slain,
 combat solymaean plain.
 hippolochus survived: came,
 honour’d author birth name;
 decree sought trojan town;
 instructions learn win renown,
 stand first worth command,
 add new honours native land,
 eyes mighty sires place,
 emulate glories race.”
 
spoke, transport fill’d tydides’ heart;
 earth generous warrior fix’d dart,
 friendly, thus lycian prince address’d:
 “welcome, brave hereditary guest!
 thus ever let us meet, kind embrace,
 stain sacred friendship race.
 know, chief, grandsires guests old;
 Œneus strong, bellerophon bold:
 ancient seat honour’d presence graced,
 twenty days genial rites pass’d.
 parting heroes mutual presents left;
 golden goblet thy grandsire’s gift;
 Œneus belt matchless work bestowed,
 rich tyrian dye refulgent glow’d.
 (this pledge learn’d, which, safely stored
 among treasures, still adorns board:
 tydeus left young, thebe’s wall
 beheld sons greece untimely fall.)
 mindful this, friendship let us join;
 heaven steps foreign lands incline,
 guest argos thou, lycia thine.
 enough trojans lance shall yield,
 full harvest yon ample field;
 enough greeks shall dye thy spear gore;
 thou diomed foes more.
 now change arms, prove either host
 guard friendship line boast.”
 
thus said, gallant chiefs alight,
 hands join, mutual faith plight;
 brave glaucus narrow thought resign’d,
 (jove warm’d bosom, enlarged mind,)
 diomed’s brass arms, mean device,
 nine oxen paid, (a vulgar price,)
 gave own, gold divinely wrought,[171]
 hundred beeves shining purchase bought.
 
meantime guardian trojan state,
 great hector, enter’d scæan gate.[172]
 beneath beech-tree’s consecrated shades,
 trojan matrons trojan maids
 around flock’d, press’d pious care
 husbands, brothers, sons, engaged war.
 bids train long procession go,
 seek gods, avert impending woe.
 now priam’s stately courts came,
 rais’d arch’d columns stupendous frame;
 o’er range marble structure runs,
 rich pavilions fifty sons,
 fifty chambers lodged: rooms state,[173]
 opposed those, priam’s daughters sate.
 twelve domes loved spouses shone,
 equal beauty, polish’d stone.
 hither great hector pass’d, pass’d unseen
 royal hecuba, mother-queen.
 (with laodice, whose beauteous face
 surpass’d nymphs troy’s illustrious race.)
 long strict embrace held son,
 press’d hand, tender thus begun:
 
“o hector! say, great occasion calls
 fight, greece surrounds walls;
 com’st thou supplicate almighty power
 lifted hands, ilion’s lofty tower?
 stay, till bring cup bacchus crown’d,
 jove’s high name, sprinkle ground,
 pay due vows gods around.
 plenteous draught refresh thy soul,
 draw new spirits generous bowl;
 spent thou art long laborious fight,
 brave defender thy country’s right.”
 
“far hence bacchus’ gifts; (the chief rejoin’d;)
 inflaming wine, pernicious mankind,
 unnerves limbs, dulls noble mind.
 let chiefs abstain, spare sacred juice
 sprinkle gods, better use.
 holy office profaned;
 ill fits me, human gore distain’d,
 pure skies horrid hands raise,
 offer heaven’s great sire polluted praise.
 you, matrons, go! spotless train,
 burn rich odours minerva’s fane.
 largest mantle full wardrobes hold,
 prized art, labour’d o’er gold,
 goddess’ honour’d knees spread,
 twelve young heifers altar led.
 may power, atoned fervent prayer,
 wives, infants, city spare;
 far avert tydides’ wasteful ire,
 mows whole troops, makes troy retire.
 this, mother, religious care:
 go rouse soft paris war;
 yet lost sense shame,
 recreant warrior hear voice fame.
 oh, kind earth hateful wretch embrace,
 pest troy, ruin race![174]
 deep dark abyss might descend,
 troy yet flourish, sorrows end.”
 
heard, gave command: summon’d came
 noble matron illustrious dame.
 phrygian queen rich wardrobe went,
 treasured odours breathed costly scent.
 lay vestures vulgar art,
 sidonian maids embroider’d every part,
 soft sidon youthful paris bore,
 helen touching tyrian shore.
 here, queen revolved careful eyes
 various textures various dyes,
 chose veil shone superior far,
 glow’d refulgent morning star.
 long procession leads;
 train majestically slow proceeds.
 soon ilion’s topmost tower come,
 awful reach high palladian dome,
 antenor’s consort, fair theano, waits
 pallas’ priestess, unbars gates.
 hands uplifted imploring eyes,
 fill dome supplicating cries.
 priestess shining veil displays,
 placed minerva’s knees, thus prays:
 
“oh awful goddess! ever-dreadful maid,
 troy’s strong defence, unconquer’d pallas, aid!
 break thou tydides’ spear, let fall
 prone dust trojan wall!
 twelve young heifers, guiltless yoke,
 shall fill thy temple grateful smoke.
 thou, atoned penitence prayer,
 ourselves, infants, city spare!”
 pray’d priestess holy fane;
 vow’d matrons, vow’d vain.
 
appear power prayers,
 hector paris’ lofty dome repairs.[175]
 mansion raised, every part
 assembling architects matchless art.
 near priam’s court hector’s palace stands
 pompous structure, town commands.
 spear hero bore wondrous strength,
 full ten cubits lance’s length,
 steely point golden ringlets join’d,
 brandish’d, motion shined
 thus entering, glittering rooms found
 brother-chief, whose useless arms lay round,
 eyes delighting splendid show,
 brightening shield, polishing bow.
 beside helen virgins stands,
 guides rich labours, instructs hands.
 
thus inactive, ardent look
 prince beheld, high-resenting spoke.
 “thy hate troy, time show?
 (o wretch ill-fated, thy country’s foe!)
 paris greece us conspire,
 thy close resentment, vengeful ire.
 thee great ilion’s guardian heroes fall,
 till heaps dead alone defend wall,
 thee soldier bleeds, matron mourns,
 wasteful war fury burns.
 ungrateful man! deserves thy care,
 troops hearten, toils share?
 rise, behold conquering flames ascend,
 phrygian glories end.”
 
“brother, ’tis just, (replied beauteous youth,)
 thy free remonstrance proves thy worth truth:
 yet charge absence less, generous chief!
 hate troy, conscious shame grief:
 here, hid human eyes, thy brother sate,
 mourn’d, secret, ilion’s fate.
 ’tis now enough; now glory spreads charms,
 beauteous helen calls chief arms.
 conquest to-day happier sword may bless,
 ’tis man’s fight, heaven’s give success.
 arm, contain thy ardent mind;
 go, paris shall lag behind.”
 

[illustration: ] hector chiding paris
 

said, answer’d priam’s warlike son;
 helen thus lowly grace begun:
 
“oh, generous brother! (if guilty dame
 caused woes deserve sister’s name!)
 heaven, ere dreadful deeds done,
 day show’d golden sun
 seen death! whirlwinds bear
 fatal infant fowls air?
 sunk beneath whelming tide,
 midst roarings waters died?
 heaven fill’d ills, accursed
 bore all, paris ills worst.
 helen least braver spouse might claim,
 warm’d virtue, regard fame!
 now tired toils, thy fainting limbs recline,
 toils, sustain’d paris’ sake mine
 gods link’d miserable doom,
 present woe, infamy come:
 wide shall spread, last ages long,
 example sad! theme future song.”
 
chief replied: “this time forbids rest;
 trojan bands, hostile fury press’d,
 demand hector, arm require;
 combat urges, soul’s fire.
 urge thou thy knight march glory calls,
 timely join me, ere leave walls.
 ere yet mingle direful fray,
 wife, infant, claim moment’s stay;
 day (perhaps last sees here)
 demands parting word, tender tear:
 day, god hates trojan land
 may vanquish hector grecian hand.”
 
said, pass’d sad presaging heart
 seek spouse, soul’s far dearer part;
 home sought her, sought vain;
 she, one maid menial train,
 hence retired; second joy,
 young astyanax, hope troy,
 pensive stood ilion’s towery height,
 beheld war, sicken’d sight;
 sad eyes vain lord explore,
 weep wounds bleeding country bore.
 
found soul desired,
 whose virtue charm’d beauty fired,
 stood gates, ask’d “what way bent
 parting step? fane went,
 late mourning matrons made resort;
 sought sisters trojan court?”
 “not court, (replied attendant train,)
 mix’d matrons minerva’s fane:
 ilion’s steepy tower bent way,
 mark fortunes doubtful day.
 troy fled, heard, grecian sword;
 heard, trembled absent lord:
 distracted surprise, seem’d fly,
 fear cheek, sorrow eye.
 nurse attended infant boy,
 young astyanax, hope troy.”
 
hector heard, return’d without delay;
 swift town trod former way,
 streets palaces, walks state;
 met mourner scæan gate.
 haste meet sprung joyful fair.
 blameless wife, aëtion’s wealthy heir
 (cilician thebe great aëtion sway’d,
 hippoplacus’ wide extended shade):
 nurse stood near, whose embraces press’d,
 hope hung smiling breast,
 soft charm early grace adorn,
 fair new-born star gilds morn.
 loved infant hector gave name
 scamandrius, scamander’s honour’d stream;
 astyanax trojans call’d boy,
 great father, defence troy.
 silent warrior smiled, pleased resign’d
 tender passions mighty mind;
 beauteous princess cast mournful look,
 hung hand, dejected spoke;
 bosom laboured boding sigh,
 big tear stood trembling eye.
 

[illustration: ] meeting hector andromache
 

“too daring prince! ah, whither dost thou run?
 ah, forgetful thy wife son!
 think’st thou wretched shall be,
 widow i, helpless orphan he?
 sure courage length life denies,
 thou must fall, thy virtue’s sacrifice.
 greece single heroes strove vain;
 now hosts oppose thee, thou must slain.
 grant me, gods, ere hector meets doom,
 can ask heaven, early tomb!
 shall days one sad tenor run,
 end sorrows first begun.
 parent now remains griefs share,
 father’s aid, mother’s tender care.
 fierce achilles wrapt walls fire,
 laid thebe waste, slew warlike sire!
 fate compassion victor bred;
 stern was, yet revered dead,
 radiant arms preserved hostile spoil,
 laid decent funeral pile;
 raised mountain bones burn’d,
 mountain-nymphs rural tomb adorn’d,
 jove’s sylvan daughters bade elms bestow
 barren shade, honour grow.
 
“by arm seven brave brothers fell;
 one sad day beheld gates hell;
 fat herds snowy flocks fed,
 amid fields hapless heroes bled!
 mother lived wear victor’s bands,
 queen hippoplacia’s sylvan lands:
 redeem’d late, scarce beheld again
 pleasing empire native plain,
 ah! oppress’d life-consuming woe,
 fell victim diana’s bow.
 
“yet hector still survives, see
 father, mother, brethren, all, thee:
 alas! parents, brothers, kindred, all
 will perish, hector fall,
 thy wife, thy infant, thy danger share:
 oh, prove husband’s father’s care!
 quarter skilful greeks annoy,
 yon wild fig-trees join wall troy;
 thou, tower defend important post;
 agamemnon points dreadful host,
 pass tydides, ajax, strive gain,
 vengeful spartan fires train.
 thrice bold foes fierce attack given,
 led hopes, dictated heaven.
 let others field arms employ,
 stay hector here, guard troy.”
 
chief replied: “that post shall care,
 alone, works war.
 sons troy, arms renown’d,
 troy’s proud dames, whose garments sweep ground
 attaint lustre former name,
 hector basely quit field fame?
 early youth bred martial pains,
 soul impels embattled plains!
 let foremost defend throne,
 guard father’s glories, own.
 
“yet come will, day decreed fates!
 (how heart trembles tongue relates!)
 day thou, imperial troy! must bend,
 see thy warriors fall, thy glories end.
 yet dire presage wounds mind,
 mother’s death, ruin kind,
 priam’s hoary hairs defiled gore,
 brothers gasping shore;
 thine, andromache! thy griefs dread:
 see thee trembling, weeping, captive led!
 argive looms battles design,
 woes, large part thine!
 bear victor’s hard commands, bring
 weight waters hyperia’s spring.
 groan beneath load life,
 cry, ‘behold mighty hector’s wife!’
 haughty greek, lives thy tears see,
 imbitters thy woes, naming me.
 thoughts glory past, present shame,
 thousand griefs shall waken name!
 may lie cold dreadful day,
 press’d load monumental clay!
 thy hector, wrapt everlasting sleep,
 shall neither hear thee sigh, see thee weep.”
 
thus spoke, illustrious chief troy
 stretch’d fond arms clasp lovely boy.
 babe clung crying nurse’s breast,
 scared dazzling helm, nodding crest.
 secret pleasure fond parent smiled,
 hector hasted relieve child,
 glittering terrors brows unbound,
 placed beaming helmet ground;
 kiss’d child, and, lifting high air,
 thus gods preferr’d father’s prayer:
 
“o thou! whose glory fills ethereal throne,
 ye deathless powers! protect son!
 grant him, like me, purchase just renown,
 guard trojans, defend crown,
 country’s foes war wage,
 rise hector future age!
 triumphant successful toils
 heroes slain bears reeking spoils,
 whole hosts may hail deserved acclaim,
 say, ‘this chief transcends father’s fame:’
 pleased amidst general shouts troy,
 mother’s conscious heart o’erflows joy.”
 
spoke, fondly gazing charms,
 restored pleasing burden arms;
 soft fragrant breast babe laid,
 hush’d repose, smile survey’d.
 troubled pleasure soon chastised fear,
 mingled smile tender tear.
 soften’d chief kind compassion view’d,
 dried falling drops, thus pursued:
 
“andromache! soul’s far better part,
 untimely sorrows heaves thy heart?
 hostile hand can antedate doom,
 till fate condemns silent tomb.
 fix’d term race earth;
 hard condition birth:
 force can resist, flight can save,
 sink alike, fearful brave.
 more—but hasten thy tasks home,
 guide spindle, direct loom:
 glory summons martial scene,
 field combat sphere men.
 heroes war, foremost place claim,
 first danger first fame.”
 
thus said, glorious chief resumes
 towery helmet, black shading plumes.
 princess parts prophetic sigh,
 unwilling parts, oft reverts eye
 stream’d every look; then, moving slow,
 sought palace, indulged woe.
 there, tears deplored godlike man,
 train soft infection ran;
 pious maids mingled sorrows shed,
 mourn living hector, dead.
 
now, longer deaf honour’s call,
 forth issues paris palace wall.
 brazen arms cast gleamy ray,
 swift town warrior bends way.
 wanton courser thus reins unbound[176]
 breaks stall, beats trembling ground;
 pamper’d proud, seeks wonted tides,
 laves, height blood shining sides;
 head now freed, tosses skies;
 mane dishevell’d o’er shoulders flies;
 snuffs females distant plain,
 springs, exulting, fields again.
 equal triumph, sprightly, bold, gay,
 arms refulgent god day,
 priam, glorying might,
 rush’d forth hector fields fight.
 
now, warriors passing way,
 graceful paris first excused stay.
 noble hector thus replied:
 “o chief! blood, now arms, allied!
 thy power war justice none contest;
 known thy courage, thy strength confess’d.
 pity sloth seize soul brave,
 godlike paris live woman’s slave!
 heart weeps blood trojans say,
 hopes thy deeds shall wipe stain away.
 haste then, glorious labours share,
 much suffer, thy sake, war.
 ills shall cease, whene’er jove’s decree
 crown bowl heaven liberty:
 proud foe frustrate triumphs mourns,
 greece indignant seas returns.”
