book vii.
 

argument
 

single combat hector ajax.
 

battle renewing double ardour upon return hector,
 minerva apprehensions greeks. apollo, seeing her
 descend olympus, joins near scæan gate. agree put
 general engagement day, incite hector challenge
 greeks single combat. nine princes accepting the
 challenge, lot cast falls upon ajax. heroes, after
 several attacks, parted night. trojans calling a
 council, antenor purposes delivery helen greeks, which
 paris will consent, offers restore riches. priam
 sends herald make offer, demand truce burning
 dead, last agreed agamemnon. the
 funerals performed, greeks, pursuant advice nestor,
 erect fortification protect fleet camp, flanked with
 towers, defended ditch palisades. neptune testifies his
 jealousy work, pacified promise jupiter. both
 armies pass night feasting jupiter disheartens trojans
 thunder, signs wrath.
 three twentieth day ends duel hector ajax,
 next day truce agreed; another taken the
 funeral rites slain one building the
 fortification ships. somewhat three days
 employed book. scene lies wholly field.
 

spoke guardian trojan state,
 rush’d impetuous scæan gate.
 paris follow’d dire alarms;
 breathing slaughter, resolved arms.
 sailors labouring main,
 long heaved weary oar vain,
 jove bids length expected gales arise;
 gales blow grateful, vessel flies.
 welcome troy’s desiring train,
 bands cheer’d, war awakes again.
 
bold paris first work death begun
 great menestheus, areithous’ son,
 sprung fair philomeda’s embrace,
 pleasing arnè native place.
 sunk eioneus shades below,
 beneath steely casque[177] felt blow
 full neck, hector’s weighty hand;
 roll’d, limbs relax’d, along land.
 glaucus’ spear bold iphinous bleeds,
 fix’d shoulder mounts steeds;
 headlong tumbles: slack nerves unbound,
 drop cold useless members ground.
 
now minerva saw argives slain,
 vast olympus gleaming plain
 fierce descends: apollo marked flight,
 shot less swift ilion’s towery height.
 radiant met, beneath beechen shade;
 thus apollo blue-eyed maid:
 
“what cause, daughter almighty jove!
 thus wings thy progress realms above?
 impetuous dost thou bend thy way,
 give greece long divided day?
 much troy already felt thy hate,
 now breathe thy rage, hush stern debate;
 day, business field suspend;
 war soon shall kindle, great ilion bend;
 since vengeful goddesses confederate join
 raze walls, though built hands divine.”
 
progeny jove replies:
 “i left, this, council skies:
 shall bid conflicting hosts forbear,
 art shall calm furious sons war?”
 god: “great hector’s soul incite
 dare boldest greek single fight,
 till greece, provoked, numbers show
 warrior worthy hector’s foe.”
 
agreed, heavenly powers withdrew;
 sage helenus secret counsels knew;
 hector, inspired, sought: address’d,
 thus told dictates sacred breast:
 “o priam! let thy faithful ear
 receive words: thy friend brother hear!
 go forth persuasive, engage
 warring nations suspend rage;
 dare boldest hostile train
 mortal combat listed plain.
 day shall end thy glorious date;
 gods spoke it, voice fate.”
 
said: warrior heard word joy;
 spear restrain’d youth troy,
 held midst athwart. either hand
 squadrons part; expecting trojans stand;
 great agamemnon bids greeks forbear:
 breathe, hush tumult war.
 athenian maid,[178] glorious god day,
 silent joy settling hosts survey:
 form vultures, beech’s height
 sit conceal’d, wait future fight.
 
thronging troops obscure dusky fields,
 horrid bristling spears, gleaming shields.
 general darkness veils main,
 (soft zephyr curling wide wat’ry plain,)
 waves scarce heave, face ocean sleeps,
 still horror saddens deeps;
 thus thick orders settling wide around,
 length composed sit, shade ground.
 great hector first amidst armies broke
 solemn silence, powers bespoke:
 
“hear, ye trojan, ye grecian bands,
 soul prompts, god commands.
 great jove, averse warfare compose,
 o’erwhelms nations new toils woes;
 war fiercer tide returns,
 till ilion falls, till yon navy burns.
 then, princes greeks! appear;
 ’tis hector speaks, calls gods hear:
 troops select boldest knight,
 him, boldest, hector dares fight.
 fall, chance battle slain,
 spoil, arms remain;
 let body, friends return’d,
 trojan hands trojan flames burn’d.
 apollo, whose aid trust,
 shall stretch daring champion dust;
 mine glory despoil foe;
 phœbus’ temple i’ll arms bestow:
 breathless carcase navy sent,
 greece shore shall raise monument;
 future mariner surveys,
 wash’d broad hellespont’s resounding seas,
 thus shall say, ‘a valiant greek lies there,
 hector slain, mighty man war,’
 stone shall tell vanquish’d hero’s name
 distant ages learn victor’s fame.”
 
fierce defiance greece astonish’d heard,
 blush’d refuse, accept fear’d.
 stern menelaus first silence broke,
 and, inly groaning, thus opprobrious spoke:
 
“women greece! scandal race,
 whose coward souls manly form disgrace,
 great shame, every age shall know
 grecian met noble foe!
 go then! resolve earth, whence ye grew,
 heartless, spiritless, inglorious crew!
 ye seem, unanimated clay,
 will dare danger day;
 ’tis man’s bold task generous strife try,
 hands god victory.”
 
words scarce spoke, generous ardour press’d,
 manly limbs azure arms dress’d.
 day, atrides! superior hand
 stretch’d thee breathless hostile strand;
 once, thy fury compose,
 kings greece, awful band, arose;
 even chief, great agamemnon, press’d
 thy daring hand, advice address’d:
 “whither, menelaus! wouldst thou run,
 tempt fate prudence bids thee shun?
 grieved though thou art, forbear rash design;
 great hector’s arm mightier far thine:
 even fierce achilles learn’d force fear,
 trembling met dreadful war.
 sit thou secure, amidst thy social band;
 greece cause shall arm powerful hand.
 mightiest warrior achaian name,
 though bold burning desire fame,
 content doubtful honour might forego,
 great danger, brave foe.”
 
said, turn’d brother’s vengeful mind;
 stoop’d reason, rage resign’d,
 longer bent rush certain harms;
 joyful friends unbrace azure arms.
 
whose lips divine persuasion flows,
 grave nestor, then, graceful act arose;
 thus kings spoke: “what grief, shame
 attend greece, grecian name!
 shall, alas! hoary heroes mourn
 sons degenerate, race scorn!
 tears shall thy silvery beard roll’d,
 peleus, old arms, wisdom old!
 joy generous prince hear
 every chief fought glorious war,
 participate fame, pleased inquire
 name, action, hero’s sire!
 gods! see warriors trembling stand,
 trembling one hostile hand;
 lift aged arms high,
 lament inglorious greece, beg die!
 oh! immortal powers above,
 minerva, phœbus, almighty jove!
 years might roll back, youth renew,
 give arm spring knew
 fierce war, jardan’s waters fall,
 led troops phea’s trembling wall,
 arcadian spears prowess tried,
 celadon rolls rapid tide.[179]
 ereuthalion braved us field,
 proud areithous’ dreadful arms wield;
 great areithous, known shore shore
 huge, knotted, iron mace bore;
 lance shook, bent twanging bow,
 broke, this, battle foe.
 manly force lycurgus slew,
 whose guileful javelin thicket flew,
 deep winding way breast assailed,
 aught warrior’s thundering mace avail’d.
 supine fell: arms mars before
 given vanquish’d, now victor bore:
 old age dimm’d lycurgus’ eyes,
 ereuthalion consign’d prize.
 furious crush’d levell’d bands,
 dared trial strongest hands;
 strongest hands fury stay:
 saw, fear’d, huge tempestuous sway
 till i, youngest host, appear’d,
 and, youngest, met army fear’d.
 fought chief: arms minerva crown’d:
 prone fell giant o’er length ground.
 was, nestor now!
 hector’s self want equal foe.
 but, warriors, youthful vigour boast,
 flower greece, examples host,
 sprung fathers, numbers sway,
 can stand trembling, desert day?”
 
warm reproofs listening kings inflame;
 nine, noblest grecian name,
 up-started fierce: far rest
 king men advanced dauntless breast:
 bold tydides, great arms, appear’d;
 next bulk gigantic ajax rear’d;
 oïleus follow’d; idomen there,[180]
 merion, dreadful god war:
 eurypylus thoas stand,
 wise ulysses closed daring band.
 these, alike inspired noble rage,
 demand fight. pylian sage:
 
“lest thirst glory brave souls divide,
 chief shall combat, let gods decide.
 heaven shall choose, chance raise
 country’s fame, immortal praise.”
 
lots produced, hero signs own:
 general’s helm fates thrown,[181]
 people pray, lifted eyes hands,
 vows like ascend bands:
 “grant, thou almighty! whose hand fate,
 worthy champion grecian state:
 task let ajax tydides prove,
 he, king kings, beloved jove.”
 old nestor shook casque. heaven inspired,
 leap’d forth lot, every greek desired.
 right left herald bears,
 held order grecian peers;
 rival yields mark unknown,
 till godlike ajax finds lot own;
 surveys inscription rejoicing eyes,
 casts him, transport cries:
 
“warriors! claim lot, arm joy;
 mine conquest chief troy.
 now brightest arms limbs invest,
 saturn’s vows address’d:
 pray secret, lest foes hear,
 deem prayers mean effect fear.
 said secret? no, vows declare
 voice fills earth air,
 lives chief ajax dread?
 ajax, toils battle bred!
 warlike salamis drew birth,
 and, born combats, fear force earth.”
 
said. troops elevated eyes,
 implore god whose thunder rends skies:
 “o father mankind, superior lord!
 lofty ida’s holy hill adored:
 highest heaven hast fix’d thy throne,
 supreme gods! unbounded alone:
 grant thou, telamon may bear away
 praise conquest doubtful day;
 or, illustrious hector thy care,
 may claim it, may share.”
 
now ajax braced dazzling armour on;
 sheathed bright steel giant-warrior shone:
 moves combat majestic pace;
 stalks arms grisly god thrace,[182]
 jove punish faithless men prepares,
 gives whole nations waste wars,
 thus march’d chief, tremendous god;
 grimly smiled; earth trembled strode:[183]
 massy javelin quivering hand,
 stood, bulwark grecian band.
 every argive heart new transport ran;
 troy stood trembling mighty man:
 even hector paused; new doubt oppress’d,
 felt great heart suspended breast:
 ’twas vain seek retreat, vain fear;
 challenged, foe drew near.
 
stern telamon behind ample shield,
 brazen tower, o’erlook’d field.
 huge orb, seven thick folds o’ercast,
 tough bull-hides; solid brass last,
 (the work tychius, hylè dwell’d
 arts armoury excell’d,)
 ajax bore manly breast,
 and, threatening, thus adverse chief address’d:
 
“hector! approach arm, singly know
 strength thou hast, grecian foe.
 achilles shuns fight; yet are,
 void soul, unskill’d war:
 let him, unactive sea-beat shore,
 indulge wrath, aid arms more;
 whole troops heroes greece yet boast,
 sends thee one, sample host,
 am, come prove thy might;
 more—be sudden, begin fight.”
 
“o telamon, thy country’s pride!
 (to ajax thus trojan prince replied)
 me, boy, woman, wouldst thou fright,
 new field, trembling fight?
 thou meet’st chief deserving thy arms,
 combat born, bred amidst alarms:
 know shift ground, remount car,
 turn, charge, answer every call war;
 right, left, dexterous lance wield,
 bear thick battle sounding shield/
 open fight, bold blow;
 steal conquest noble foe.”
 
said, rising, high field
 whirl’d long lance sevenfold shield.
 full brass descending above
 six bull-hides furious weapon drove,
 till seventh fix’d. ajax threw;
 hector’s shield forceful javelin flew,
 corslet enters, garment rends,
 glancing downwards, near flank descends.
 wary trojan shrinks, bending low
 beneath buckler, disappoints blow.
 bored shields chiefs javelins drew,
 close impetuous, charge renew;
 fierce mountain-lions bathed blood,
 foaming boars, terror wood.
 ajax, hector long lance extends;
 blunted point buckler bends;
 ajax, watchful foe drew near,
 drove trojan targe knotty spear;
 reach’d neck, matchless strength impell’d!
 spouts black gore, dims shining shield.
 yet ceased hector thus; stooping down,
 strong hand up-heaved flinty stone,
 black, craggy, vast: force bends;
 full brazen boss stone descends;
 hollow brass resounded shock:
 ajax seized fragment rock,
 applied nerve, swinging round high,
 force tempestuous, let ruin fly;
 huge stone thundering buckler broke:
 slacken’d knees received numbing stroke;
 great hector falls extended field,
 bulk supporting shatter’d shield:
 wanted heavenly aid: apollo’s might
 confirm’d sinews, restored fight.
 now heroes broad falchions drew
 flaming circles round heads flew;
 heralds’ voice word given.
 sacred ministers earth heaven:
 divine talthybius, greeks employ,
 sage idæus part troy,
 swords peaceful sceptres rear’d;
 first idæus’ awful voice heard:
 

[illustration: ] hector ajax separated heralds
 

“forbear, sons! force prove,
 dear men, beloved jove.
 either host matchless worth known,
 sounds praise, war own.
 now night extends awful shade;
 goddess parts you; night obey’d.”[184]
 
great ajax high soul express’d:
 “o sage! hector words address’d.
 let him, first provoked chiefs fight,
 let demand sanction night;
 first ask’d it, content obey,
 cease strife hector shows way.”
 
“o first greeks! (his noble foe rejoin’d)
 heaven adorns, superior thy kind,
 strength body, worth mind!
 now martial law commands us forbear;
 hereafter shall meet glorious war,
 future day shall lengthen strife,
 let gods decide death life!
 since, then, night extends gloomy shade,
 heaven enjoins it, night obey’d.
 return, brave ajax, thy grecian friends,
 joy nations thy arm defends;
 shall glad chief, trojan wife,
 wearies heaven vows hector’s life.
 let us, memorable day,
 exchange gift: greece troy may say,
 ‘not hate, glory, made chiefs contend;
 brave foe soul friend.’”
 
that, sword stars silver graced,
 baldric studded, sheath enchased,
 gave greek. generous greek bestow’d
 radiant belt rich purple glow’d.
 majestic grace quit plain;
 seeks grecian, phrygian train.
 
trojan bands returning hector wait,
 hail joy champion state;
 escaped great ajax, survey round,
 alive, unarm’d, vigorous wound;
 troy’s high gates godlike man bear
 present triumph, late despair.
 
ajax, glorying hardy deed,
 well-arm’d greeks agamemnon lead.
 steer sacrifice king design’d,
 full five years, nobler kind.
 victim falls; strip smoking hide,
 beast quarter, joints divide;
 spread tables, repast prepare,
 takes seat, receives share.
 king (an honorary sign)
 great ajax placed mighty chine.[185]
 now rage hunger removed,
 nestor, persuasive art approved,
 sage whose counsels long sway’d rest,
 words like prudent thought express’d:
 
“how dear, kings! fatal day cost,
 greeks perish’d! people lost!
 tides blood drench’d scamander’s shore!
 crowds heroes sunk rise more!
 hear me, chief! let morrow’s light
 awake thy squadrons new toils fight:
 space least permit war breathe,
 flames slaughter’d friends bequeath,
 red field scatter’d bodies bear,
 nigh fleet funeral structure rear;
 decent urns snowy bones may keep,
 pious children o’er ashes weep.
 here, one promiscuous pile blazed,
 high o’er general tomb raised;
 next, secure camp naval powers,
 raise embattled wall, lofty towers;
 space space ample gates around,
 passing chariots; trench profound.
 greece combat shall safety go,
 fear fierce incursions foe.”
 ’twas thus sage wholesome counsel moved;
 sceptred kings greece words approved.
 
meanwhile, convened priam’s palace-gate,
 trojan peers nightly council sate;
 senate void order, choice:
 hearts fearful, confused voice.
 antenor, rising, thus demands ear:
 “ye trojans, dardans, auxiliars, hear!
 ’tis heaven counsel breast inspires,
 move every god requires:
 let sparta’s treasures hour restored,
 argive helen ancient lord.
 ties faith, sworn alliance, broke,
 impious battles just gods provoke.
 advice ye practise, reject,
 hope success, dread dire effect.”
 
senior spoke sate. replied
 graceful husband spartan bride:
 “cold counsels, trojan, may become thy years
 sound ungrateful warrior’s ears:
 old man, void fallacy art,
 thy words express purpose thy heart,
 thou, thy time, sound advice hast given;
 wisdom date, assign’d heaven.
 hear me, princes trojan name!
 treasures i’ll restore, dame;
 treasures too, peace, will resign;
 bright possession ever mine.”
 
’twas then, growing discord compose,
 slow seat reverend priam rose:
 godlike aspect deep attention drew:
 paused, pacific words ensue:
 
“ye trojans, dardans, auxiliar bands!
 now take refreshment hour demands;
 guard well walls, relieve watch night.
 till new sun restores cheerful light.
 shall herald, atrides sent,
 ships proclaim son’s intent.
 next let truce ask’d, troy may burn
 slaughter’d heroes, bones inurn;
 done, fate war tried,
 whose conquest, mighty jove decide!”
 
monarch spoke: warriors snatch’d haste
 (each post arms) short repast.
 soon rosy morn waked day,
 black ships idæus bent way;
 there, sons mars, council found,
 raised voice: host stood listening round.
 
“ye sons atreus, ye greeks, give ear!
 words troy, troy’s great monarch, hear.
 pleased may ye hear (so heaven succeed prayers)
 paris, author war, declares.
 spoils treasures ilion bore
 (oh perish’d ere touch’d shore!)
 proffers injured greece: large increase
 added trojan wealth buy peace.
 restore beauteous bride again,
 greece demands, troy requests vain.
 next, ye chiefs! ask truce burn
 slaughter’d heroes, bones inurn.
 done, fate war tried,
 whose conquest, mighty jove decide!”
 
greeks gave ear, none silence broke;
 length tydides rose, rising spoke:
 “oh, take not, friends! defrauded fame,
 proffer’d wealth, even spartan dame.
 let conquest make ours: fate shakes wall,
 troy already totters fall.”
 
admiring chiefs, grecian name,
 general shouts return’d loud acclaim.
 thus king kings rejects peace:
 “herald! thou hear’st voice greece
 remains; let funeral flames fed
 heroes’ corps: war dead:
 go search slaughtered chiefs yonder plain,
 gratify manes slain.
 witness, jove, whose thunder rolls high!”
 said, rear’d sceptre sky.
 
sacred troy, princes lay
 wait event, herald bent way.
 came, standing midst, explain’d
 peace rejected, truce obtain’d.
 straight several cares trojans move,
 search plains, fell sounding grove:
 less greeks, descending shore,
 hew’d green forests, bodies bore.
 now forth chambers main,
 shed sacred light earth again,
 arose golden chariot day,
 tipp’d mountains purple ray.
 mingled throngs greek trojan train
 heaps carnage search’d mournful plain.
 scarce friend slaughter’d friend explore,
 dust dishonour’d, deformed gore.
 wounds wash’d, pious tears shed,
 and, laid along cars, deplored dead.
 sage priam check’d grief: silent haste
 bodies decent piles placed:
 melting hearts cold remains burn’d,
 and, sadly slow, sacred troy return’d.
 less greeks pious sorrows shed,
 decent pile dispose dead;
 cold remains consume equal care;
 slowly, sadly, fleet repair.
 now, ere morn streak’d reddening light
 doubtful confines day night,
 dying flames greeks appear’d,
 round pile general tomb rear’d.
 then, secure camp naval powers,
 raised embattled walls lofty towers:[186]
 space space ample gates around,
 passing chariots, trench profound
 large extent; deep earth below,
 strong piles infix’d stood adverse foe.
 
toil’d greeks: meanwhile gods above,
 shining circle round father jove,
 amazed beheld wondrous works man:
 he, whose trident shakes earth, began:
 
“what mortals henceforth shall power adore,
 fanes frequent, oracles implore,
 proud grecians thus successful boast
 rising bulwarks sea-beat coast?
 see long walls extending main,
 god consulted, victim slain!
 fame shall fill world’s remotest ends,
 wide morn golden beam extends;
 old laomedon’s divine abodes,
 radiant structures raised labouring gods,
 shall, razed lost, long oblivion sleep.”
 thus spoke hoary monarch deep.
 
almighty thunderer frown replies,
 clouds world, blackens half skies:
 “strong god ocean! thou, whose rage can make
 solid earth’s eternal basis shake!
 cause fear mortal works move[187]
 meanest subject realms above?
 where’er sun’s refulgent rays cast,
 thy power honour’d, thy fame shall last.
 yon proud work future age shall view,
 trace remain glory grew.
 sapp’d foundations thy force shall fall,
 and, whelm’d beneath waves, drop huge wall:
 vast drifts sand shall change former shore:
 ruin vanish’d, name more.”
 
thus heaven: while, o’er grecian train,
 rolling sun descending main
 beheld finish’d work. bulls slew;
 back tents savoury vapour flew.
 now fleet, arrived lemnos’ strands,
 bacchus’ blessings cheered generous bands.
 fragrant wines rich eunaeus sent
 thousant measures royal tent.
 (eunaeus, hypsipyle yore
 jason, shepherd people, bore,)
 rest purchased proper cost,
 well plenteous freight supplied host:
 each, exchange, proportion’d treasures gave;[188]
 some, brass iron; some, ox, slave.
 night feast, greek trojan powers:
 fields, within towers.
 jove averse signs wrath display’d,
 shot red lightnings gloomy shade:
 humbled stood; pale horror seized all,
 deep thunder shook aerial hall.
 pour’d jove bowl crown’d;
 large libations drench’d thirsty ground:
 late, refresh’d sleep toils fight,
 enjoy’d balmy blessings night.

book viii.
 

argument.
 

second battle, distress greeks.
 

jupiter assembles council deities, threatens the
 pains tartarus assist either side: minerva obtains of
 may direct greeks counsels. armies join
 battle: jupiter mount ida weighs balances fates both,
 affrights greeks thunders lightnings. nestor alone
 continues field great danger: diomed relieves him; whose
 exploits, hector, excellently described. juno
 endeavours animate neptune assistance greeks, in
 vain. acts teucer, length wounded hector, and
 carried off. juno minerva prepare aid grecians, are
 restrained iris, sent jupiter. night puts end the
 battle. hector continues field, (the greeks driven to
 fortifications ships,) gives orders keep the
 watch night camp, prevent enemy re-embarking and
 escaping flight. kindle fires fields, pass
 night arms.
 time seven twenty days employed opening of
 poem end book. scene (except the
 celestial machines) lies field towards seashore.
 

aurora now, fair daughter dawn,
 sprinkled rosy light dewy lawn;
 jove convened senate skies,
 high olympus’ cloudy tops arise,
 sire gods awful silence broke;
 heavens attentive trembled spoke:[189]
 
“celestial states! immortal gods! give ear,
 hear decree, reverence ye hear;
 fix’d decree heaven can move;
 thou, fate! fulfil it! and, ye powers, approve!
 god enters yon forbidden field,
 yields assistance, wills yield,
 back skies shame shall driven,
 gash’d dishonest wounds, scorn heaven;
 far, oh far, steep olympus thrown,
 low dark tartarean gulf shall groan,
 burning chains fix’d brazen floors,
 lock’d hell’s inexorable doors;
 deep beneath infernal centre hurl’d,[190]
 centre ethereal world.
 let tempts me, dread dire abodes:
 know, almighty god gods.
 league forces, then, ye powers above,
 join all, try omnipotence jove.
 let golden everlasting chain[191]
 whose strong embrace holds heaven, earth, main
 strive all, mortal immortal birth,
 drag, this, thunderer earth:
 ye strive vain! stretch hand,
 heave gods, ocean, land;
 fix chain great olympus’ height,
 vast world hangs trembling sight!
 reign, unbounded above;
 men, gods, compared jove.”
 
all-mighty spoke, durst powers reply:
 reverend horror silenced sky;
 trembling stood sovereign’s look;
 length best-beloved, power wisdom, spoke:
 
“o first greatest! god, gods adored
 thy might, father lord!
 but, ah! permit pity human state:
 help, least lament fate.
 fields forbidden submiss refrain,
 arms unaiding mourn argives slain;
 yet grant counsels still breasts may move,
 must perish wrath jove.”
 
cloud-compelling god suit approved,
 smiled superior best beloved;
 call’d coursers, chariot took;
 stedfast firmament beneath shook:
 rapt ethereal steeds chariot roll’d;
 brass hoofs, curling manes gold:
 heaven’s undrossy gold gods array,
 refulgent, flash’d intolerable day.
 high throne shines: coursers fly
 extended earth starry sky.
 ida’s topmost height came,
 (fair nurse fountains, savage game,)
 o’er pointed summits proudly raised,
 fane breathed odours, altar blazed:
 there, radiant car, sacred sire
 gods men released steeds fire:
 blue ambient mists immortal steeds embraced;
 high cloudy point seat placed;
 thence broad eye subject world surveys,
 town, tents, navigable seas.
 
now grecians snatch’d short repast,
 buckled shining arms haste.
 troy roused soon; dreadful day
 fate fathers, wives, infants lay.
 gates unfolding pour forth train;
 squadrons squadrons cloud dusky plain:
 men, steeds, chariots shake trembling ground,
 tumult thickens, skies resound;
 now shouts shocking armies closed,
 lances lances, shields shields opposed,
 host host shadowy legends drew,
 sounding darts iron tempests flew;
 victors vanquish’d join promiscuous cries,
 triumphant shouts dying groans arise;
 streaming blood slippery fields dyed,
 slaughter’d heroes swell dreadful tide.
 long morning beams, increasing bright,
 o’er heaven’s clear azure spread sacred light,
 commutual death fate war confounds,
 adverse battle gored equal wounds.
 sun height heaven ascends,
 sire gods golden scales suspends,[192]
 equal hand: explored fate
 greece troy, poised mighty weight:
 press’d load, grecian balance lies
 low sunk earth, trojan strikes skies.
 jove ida’s top horrors spreads;
 clouds burst dreadful o’er grecian heads;
 thick lightnings flash; muttering thunder rolls;
 strength withers, unmans souls.
 wrath trembling hosts retire;
 gods terrors, skies fire.
 great idomeneus sight bear,
 stern ajax, thunderbolts war:
 he, king war, alarm sustain’d
 nestor alone, amidst storm remain’d.
 unwilling remain’d, paris’ dart
 pierced courser mortal part;
 fix’d forehead, springing mane
 curl’d o’er brow, stung brain;
 mad anguish, begins rear,
 paw hoofs aloft, lash air.
 scarce falchion cut reins, freed
 encumber’d chariot dying steed,
 dreadful hector, thundering war,
 pour’d tumult whirling car.
 day stretch’d beneath matchless hand
 hoary monarch pylian band,
 diomed beheld; forth crowd
 rush’d, ulysses call’d aloud:
 
“whither, oh whither ulysses run?
 oh, flight unworthy great laertes’ son!
 mix’d vulgar shall thy fate found,
 pierced back, vile, dishonest wound?
 oh turn save hector’s direful rage
 glory greeks, pylian sage.”
 fruitless words lost unheard air,
 ulysses seeks ships, shelters there.
 bold tydides rescue goes,
 single warrior midst host foes;
 coursers sudden spring
 leap’d, anxious thus bespoke king:
 
“great perils, father! wait unequal fight;
 younger champions will oppress thy might.
 thy veins ancient vigour glow,
 weak thy servant, thy coursers slow.
 haste, ascend seat, car
 observe steeds tros, renown’d war.
 practised alike turn, stop, chase,
 dare fight, urge rapid race:
 late obey’d Æneas’ guiding rein;
 leave thou thy chariot faithful train;
 yon trojans will go,
 shall great hector want equal foe;
 fierce is, even may learn fear
 thirsty fury flying spear.”
 
thus said chief; nestor, skill’d war,
 approves counsel, ascends car:
 steeds left, trusty servants hold;
 eurymedon, sthenelus bold:
 reverend charioteer directs course,
 strains aged arm lash horse.
 hector face; unknowing fear,
 fierce drove on; tydides whirl’d spear.
 spear erring haste mistook way,
 plunged eniopeus’ bosom lay.
 opening hand death forsakes rein;
 steeds fly back: falls, spurns plain.
 great hector sorrows servant kill’d,
 yet unrevenged permits press field;
 till, supply place rule car,
 rose archeptolemus, fierce war.
 now death horror cover’d all;[193]
 like timorous flocks trojans wall
 inclosed bled: jove awful sound
 roll’d big thunder o’er vast profound:
 full tydides’ face lightning flew;
 ground flamed sulphur blue;
 quivering steeds fell prostrate sight;
 nestor’s trembling hand confess’d fright:
 dropp’d reins: and, shook sacred dread,
 thus, turning, warn’d intrepid diomed:
 
“o chief! daring thy friend’s defence
 retire advised, urge chariot hence.
 day, averse, sovereign skies
 assists great hector, palm denies.
 sun may see happier hour,
 greece shall conquer heavenly power.
 ’tis man fix’d decree move:
 great will glory submit jove.”
 
“o reverend prince! (tydides thus replies)
 thy years awful, thy words wise.
 ah, grief! haughty hector boast
 fled inglorious guarded coast.
 dire disgrace shall blast fame,
 o’erwhelm me, earth; hide warrior’s shame!”
 gerenian nestor thus replied:[194]
 “gods! can thy courage fear phrygian’s pride?
 hector may vaunt, shall heed boast?
 felt thy arm, dardan host,
 troy, yet bleeding heroes lost;
 even phrygian dame, dreads sword
 laid dust loved, lamented lord.”
 said, and, hasty, o’er gasping throng
 drives swift steeds: chariot smokes along;
 shouts trojans thicken wind;
 storm hissing javelins pours behind.
 voice shakes solid skies,
 pleased, hector braves warrior flies.
 “go, mighty hero! graced rest
 seats council sumptuous feast:
 now hope honours thy train;
 go less woman, form man!
 scale walls, wrap towers flames,
 lead exile fair phrygian dames,
 thy proud hopes, presumptuous prince! fled;
 arm shall reach thy heart, stretch thee dead.”
 
now fears dissuade him, now hopes invite.
 stop coursers, stand fight;
 thrice turn’d chief, thrice imperial jove
 ida’s summits thunder’d above.
 great hector heard; saw flashing light,
 (the sign conquest,) thus urged fight:
 
“hear, every trojan, lycian, dardan band,
 famed war, dreadful hand hand.
 mindful wreaths arms won,
 great forefathers’ glories, own.
 heard ye voice jove? success fame
 await troy, greece eternal shame.
 vain skulk behind boasted wall,
 weak bulwarks; destined arm fall.
 high o’er slighted trench steeds shall bound,
 pass victorious o’er levell’d mound.
 soon yon hollow ships stand,
 fight flames, toss blazing brand;
 till, proud navy wrapt smoke fires,
 greece, encompass’d, one blaze expires.”
 
furious said; bending o’er yoke,
 encouraged proud steeds, thus spoke:
 
“now, xanthus, Æthon, lampus, urge chase,
 thou, podargus! prove thy generous race;
 fleet, fearless, important day,
 master’s well-spent care repay.
 this, high-fed, plenteous stalls ye stand,
 served pure wheat, princess’ hand;
 spouse, great aëtion’s line,
 oft steep’d strengthening grain wine.
 now swift pursue, now thunder uncontroll’d:
 give seize rich nestor’s shield gold;
 tydeus’ shoulders strip costly load,
 vulcanian arms, labour god:
 gain, victory, ye powers!
 night, glorious night, fleet ours!”
 
heard, deep anguish stung saturnia’s soul;
 shook throne, shook starry pole:
 thus neptune: “thou, whose force can make
 stedfast earth foundations shake,
 seest thou greeks fates unjust oppress’d,
 swells thy heart immortal breast?
 yet Ægae, helicè, thy power obey,[195]
 gifts unceasing thine altars lay.
 deities greece combine,
 vain gloomy thunderer might repine:
 sole sit, scarce god friend,
 see trojans shades descend:
 scene idaean bower;
 ungrateful prospect sullen power!”
 
neptune wrath rejects rash design:
 “what rage, madness, furious queen! thine?
 war highest. above
 submit tremble hand jove.”
 
now godlike hector, whose matchless might
 jove gave glory destined fight,
 squadrons squadrons drives, fills fields
 close-ranged chariots, thicken’d shields.
 deep trench length extended lay,
 compacted troops stand wedged firm array,
 dreadful front! shake brands, threat
 long-destroying flames hostile fleet.
 king men, juno’s self inspired,
 toil’d tents, army fired.
 swift moved, lifted hand
 purple robe, bright ensign command.
 high midmost bark king appear’d:
 there, ulysses’ deck, voice heard:
 ajax achilles reach’d sound,
 whose distant ships guarded navy bound.
 “o argives! shame human race! (he cried:
 hollow vessels voice replied,)
 now glorious boasts yore,
 hasty triumphs lemnian shore?
 fearless hero dares hundred foes,
 feast lasts, goblet flows;
 meet one martial man found,
 fight rages, flames surround?
 mighty jove! sire distress’d!
 ever king like me, like oppress’d?
 power immense, justice arm’d vain;
 glory ravish’d, people slain!
 thee vows breathed every shore;
 altar smoked victims’ gore?
 fat bulls fed constant flame,
 ask’d destruction trojan name.
 now, gracious god! far humbler demand;
 give least ’scape hector’s hand,
 save relics grecian land!”
 
thus pray’d king, heaven’s great father heard
 vows, bitterness soul preferr’d:
 wrath appeased, happy signs declares,
 gives people monarch’s prayers.
 eagle, sacred bird heaven! sent,
 fawn talons truss’d, (divine portent!)
 high o’er wondering hosts soar’d above,
 paid vows panomphaean jove;
 let prey altar fall;
 greeks beheld, transport seized all:
 encouraged sign, troops revive,
 fierce troy doubled fury drive.
 tydides first, grecian force,
 o’er broad ditch impell’d foaming horse,
 pierced deep ranks, strongest battle tore,
 dyed javelin red trojan gore.
 young agelaus (phradmon sire)
 flying coursers shunn’d dreadful ire;
 struck back, phrygian fell oppress’d;
 dart drove on, issued breast:
 headlong quits car: arms resound;
 ponderous buckler thunders ground.
 forth rush tide greeks, passage freed;
 atridae first, ajaces next succeed:
 meriones, like mars arms renown’d,
 godlike idomen, now passed mound;
 evaemon’s next issues foe,
 last young teucer bended bow.
 secure behind telamonian shield
 skilful archer wide survey’d field,
 every shaft hostile victim slew,
 close beneath sevenfold orb withdrew:
 conscious infant so, fear alarms,
 retires safety mother’s arms.
 thus ajax guards brother field,
 moves moves, turns shining shield.
 first teucer’s mortal arrows bled?
 orsilochus; fell ormenus dead:
 godlike lycophon next press’d plain,
 chromius, daetor, ophelestes slain:
 bold hamopaon breathless sunk ground;
 bloody pile great melanippus crown’d.
 heaps fell heaps, sad trophies art,
 trojan ghost attending every dart.
 great agamemnon views joyful eye
 ranks grow thinner arrows fly:
 “o youth forever dear! (the monarch cried)
 thus, always thus, thy early worth tried;
 thy brave example shall retrieve host,
 thy country’s saviour, thy father’s boast!
 sprung alien’s bed thy sire grace,
 vigorous offspring stolen embrace:
 proud boy, own’d generous flame,
 brave repays cares fame.
 now hear monarch’s vow: heaven’s high powers
 give raze troy’s long-defended towers;
 whatever treasures greece design,
 next rich honorary gift thine:
 golden tripod, distinguished car,
 coursers dreadful ranks war:
 fair captive, thy eyes approve,
 shall recompense warrior’s toils love.”
 
chief: “with praise rest inspire,
 urge soul already fill’d fire.
 strength have, now battle tried,
 till every shaft phrygian blood dyed.
 since rallying wall forced foe,
 still aim’d hector bent bow:
 eight forky arrows hand fled,
 eight bold heroes points lie dead:
 sure god denies destroy
 fury field, dog troy.”
 
said, twang’d string. weapon flies
 hector’s breast, sings along skies:
 miss’d mark; pierced gorgythio’s heart,
 drench’d royal blood thirsty dart.
 (fair castianira, nymph form divine,
 offspring added king priam’s line.)
 full-blown poppies, overcharged rain,[196]
 decline head, drooping kiss plain;
 sinks youth: beauteous head, depress’d
 beneath helmet, drops upon breast.
 another shaft raging archer drew,
 shaft erring fury flew,
 (from hector, phœbus turn’d flying wound,)
 yet fell dry guiltless ground:
 thy breast, brave archeptolemus! tore,
 dipp’d feathers vulgar gore.
 headlong falls: sudden fall alarms
 steeds, startle sounding arms.
 hector grief charioteer beheld
 pale breathless sanguine field:
 bids cebriones direct rein,
 quits bright car, issues plain.
 dreadful shouts: earth stone took,
 rush’d teucer lifted rock.
 youth already strain’d forceful yew;
 shaft already shoulder drew;
 feather hand, just wing’d flight,
 touch’d neck hollow chest unite;
 there, juncture knits channel bone,
 furious chief discharged craggy stone:
 bow-string burst beneath ponderous blow,
 numb’d hand dismiss’d useless bow.
 fell: ajax broad shield display’d,
 screen’d brother mighty shade;
 till great alaster, mecistheus, bore
 batter’d archer groaning shore.
 
troy yet found grace olympian sire,
 arm’d hands, fill’d breasts fire.
 greeks repulsed, retreat behind wall,
 trench heaps confusedly fall.
 first foe, great hector march’d along,
 terror clothed, mortal strong.
 bold hound, gives lion chase,
 beating bosom, eager pace,
 hangs haunch, fastens heels,
 guards turns, circles wheels;
 thus oft grecians turn’d, still flew;
 thus following, hector still hindmost slew.
 flying pass’d trench profound,
 many chief lay gasping ground;
 ships desperate stand made,
 fired troops, called gods aid.
 fierce rattling chariot hector came:
 eyes like gorgon shot sanguine flame
 wither’d host: like mars stood:
 dire monster, dreadful god!
 strong distress wife jove survey’d;
 pensive thus, war’s triumphant maid:
 
“o daughter god, whose arm can wield
 avenging bolt, shake sable shield!
 now, moment last despair,
 shall wretched greece confess care,
 condemn’d suffer full force fate,
 drain dregs heaven’s relentless hate?
 gods! shall one raging hand thus level all?
 numbers fell! numbers yet shall fall!
 power divine shall hector’s wrath assuage?
 still swells slaughter, still grows rage!”
 
spake imperial regent skies;
 goddess azure eyes:
 
“long since hector stain’d fields gore,
 stretch’d argive native shore:
 above, sire heaven, withstands,
 mocks attempts, slights just demands;
 stubborn god, inflexible hard,
 forgets service deserved reward:
 saved i, this, favourite distress’d,
 stern eurystheus long labours press’d?
 begg’d, tears begg’d, deep dismay;
 shot heaven, gave arm day.
 oh wisdom known dire event,
 grim pluto’s gloomy gates went;
 triple dog never felt chain,
 styx cross’d, hell explored vain.
 averse heaven gods,
 thetis’ suit partial thunderer nods;
 grace gloomy, fierce, resenting son,
 hopes frustrate, greeks undone.
 future day, perhaps, may moved
 call blue-eyed maid best beloved.
 haste, launch thy chariot, yon ranks ride;
 will arm, thunder thy side.
 then, goddess! say, shall hector glory then?
 (that terror greeks, man men)
 juno’s self, pallas shall appear,
 dreadful crimson walks war!
 mighty trojan then, yonder shore,
 expiring, pale, terrible more,
 shall feast fowls, glut dogs gore?”
 
ceased, juno rein’d steeds care:
 (heaven’s awful empress, saturn’s heir:)
 pallas, meanwhile, various veil unbound,
 flowers adorn’d, art immortal crown’d;
 radiant robe sacred fingers wove
 floats rich waves, spreads court jove.
 father’s arms mighty limbs invest,
 cuirass blazes ample breast.
 vigorous power trembling car ascends:
 shook arm, massy javelin bends:
 huge, ponderous, strong! fury burns
 proud tyrants humbles, whole hosts o’erturns.
 
saturnia lends lash; coursers fly;
 smooth glides chariot liquid sky.
 heaven’s gates spontaneous open powers,
 heaven’s golden gates, kept winged hours.
 commission’d alternate watch stand,
 sun’s bright portals skies command;
 close, unfold, eternal gates day
 bar heaven clouds, roll clouds away.
 sounding hinges ring, clouds divide.
 prone steep heaven course guide.
 jove, incensed, ida’s top survey’d,
 thus enjoin’d many-colour’d maid.
 

[illustration: ] juno minerva going assist greeks
 

“thaumantia! mount winds, stop car;
 highest shall wage war?
 furious yet dare vain debate,
 thus spoke, speak fate:
 coursers crush’d beneath wheels shall lie,
 car fragments, scatter’d o’er sky:
 lightning rebellious shall confound,
 hurl flaming, headlong, ground,
 condemn’d ten revolving years weep
 wounds impress’d burning thunder deep.
 shall minerva learn fear ire,
 dare combat nature’s sire.
 juno, headstrong imperious still,
 claims title transgress will.”
 
swift wind, various-colour’d maid
 ida’s top golden wings display’d;
 great olympus’ shining gate flies,
 meets chariot rushing skies,
 restrains progress bright abodes,
 speaks mandate sire gods.
 
“what frenzy goddesses! rage can move
 celestial minds tempt wrath jove?
 desist, obedient high command:
 word; know word shall stand:
 lightning rebellion shall confound,
 hurl ye headlong, flaming, ground;
 horses crush’d beneath wheels shall lie,
 car fragments scatter’d o’er sky;
 condemn’d ten rolling years weep
 wounds impress’d burning thunder deep.
 shall minerva learn fear ire,
 dare combat nature’s sire.
 juno, headstrong imperious still,
 claims title transgress will:
 thee, desperate insolence driven
 lift thy lance king heaven?”
 
then, mounting pinions wind,
 flew; juno thus rage resign’d:
 
“o daughter god, whose arm can wield
 avenging bolt, shake saber shield!
 let beings superior birth
 contend jove low race earth;
 triumphant now, now miserably slain,
 breathe perish fates ordain:
 jove’s high counsels full effect shall find;
 and, ever constant, ever rule mankind.”
 
spoke, backward turn’d steeds light,
 adorn’d manes gold, heavenly bright.
 hours unloosed them, panting stood,
 heap’d mangers ambrosial food.
 tied, rest high celestial stalls;
 chariot propp’d crystal walls,
 pensive goddesses, abash’d, controll’d,
 mix gods, fill seats gold.
 

[illustration: ] hours taking horses juno’s car
 

now thunderer meditates flight
 ida’s summits olympian height.
 swifter thought, wheels instinctive fly,
 flame vast air, reach sky.
 ’twas neptune’s charge coursers unbrace,
 fix car immortal base;
 stood chariot, beaming forth rays,
 till snowy veil screen’d blaze.
 he, whose all-conscious eyes world behold,
 eternal thunderer sat, enthroned gold.
 high heaven footstool feet makes,
 wide beneath olympus shakes.
 trembling afar offending powers appear’d,
 confused silent, frown fear’d.
 saw soul, thus word imparts:
 “pallas juno! say, heave hearts?
 soon battle o’er: proud troy retired
 face, wrath expired.
 know, whoe’er almighty power withstand!
 unmatch’d force, unconquer’d hand:
 shall sovereign skies control?
 gods crown starry pole.
 hearts shall tremble, arms take,
 immortal nerve horror shake.
 thus speak, speak shall stand;
 power soe’er provokes lifted hand,
 hill shall hold place;
 cut off, exiled ethereal race.”
 
juno pallas grieving hear doom,
 feast souls ilion’s woes come.
 though secret anger swell’d minerva’s breast,
 prudent goddess yet wrath repress’d;
 juno, impotent rage, replies:
 “what hast thou said, tyrant skies!
 strength omnipotence invest thy throne;
 ’tis thine punish; grieve alone.
 greece grieve, abandon’d fate
 drink dregs thy unmeasured hate.
 fields forbidden submiss refrain,
 arms unaiding see argives slain;
 yet grant counsels still breasts may move,
 lest perish rage jove.”
 
goddess thus; thus god replies,
 swells clouds, blackens skies:
 
“the morning sun, awaked loud alarms,
 shall see almighty thunderer arms.
 heaps argives shall load plain,
 radiant eyes shall view, view vain.
 shall great hector cease rage fight,
 navy flaming, thy greeks flight,
 even till day certain fates ordain
 stern achilles (his patroclus slain)
 shall rise vengeance, lay waste plain.
 fate, canst thou turn course
 thy rage, thy rebel force.
 fly, thy wilt, earth’s remotest bound,
 utmost verge seas resound;
 cursed iapetus saturn dwell,
 fast brink, within streams hell;
 sun e’er gilds gloomy horrors there;
 cheerful gales refresh lazy air:
 arm bold titanian band;
 arm vain; will, shall stand.”
 
now deep ocean sunk lamp light,
 drew behind cloudy veil night:
 conquering trojans mourn beams decay’d;
 greeks rejoicing bless friendly shade.
 
victors keep field; hector calls
 martial council near navy walls;
 scamander’s bank apart led,
 thinly scatter’d lay heaps dead.
 assembled chiefs, descending ground,
 attend order, prince surround.
 massy spear bore mighty strength,
 full ten cubits lance’s length;
 point brass, refulgent behold,
 fix’d wood circling rings gold:
 noble hector lance reclined,
 and, bending forward, thus reveal’d mind:
 
“ye valiant trojans, attention hear!
 ye dardan bands, generous aids, give ear!
 day, hoped, wrap conquering flame
 greece ships, crown toils fame.
 darkness now, save cowards, falls,
 guards trembling wooden walls.
 obey night, use peaceful hours
 steeds forage, refresh powers.
 straight town sheep oxen sought,
 strengthening bread generous wine brought.
 wide o’er field, high blazing sky,
 let numerous fires absent sun supply,
 flaming piles plenteous fuel raise,
 till bright morn purple beam displays;
 lest, silence shades night,
 greece sable ships attempt flight.
 unmolested let wretches gain
 lofty decks, safely cleave main;
 hostile wound let every dart bestow,
 lasting token phrygian foe,
 wounds, long hence may ask spouses’ care.
 warn children trojan war.
 now circuit ilion wall,
 let sacred heralds sound solemn call;
 bid sires hoary honours crown’d,
 beardless youths, battlements surround.
 firm guard, distant lie powers,
 let matrons hang lights towers;
 lest, covert midnight shade,
 insidious foe naked town invade.
 suffice, to-night, orders obey;
 nobler charge shall rouse dawning day.
 gods, trust, shall give hector’s hand
 detested foes free land,
 plough’d, fates averse, watery way:
 trojan vultures predestined prey.
 common safety must now care;
 soon morning paints fields air,
 sheathed bright arms let every troop engage,
 fired fleet behold battle rage.
 then, shall hector tydides prove
 whose fates heaviest scales jove.
 to-morrow’s light (o haste glorious morn!)
 shall see bloody spoils triumph borne,
 keen javelin shall breast gored,
 prostrate heroes bleed around lord.
 certain this, oh! might days endure,
 age inglorious, black death secure;
 might life glory know bound,
 like pallas worshipp’d, like sun renown’d!
 next dawn, last shall enjoy,
 shall crush greeks, end woes troy.”
 
leader spoke. host around
 shouts applause along shores resound.
 yoke smoking steeds untied,
 fix’d headstalls chariot-side.
 fat sheep oxen town led,
 generous wine, all-sustaining bread,
 full hecatombs lay burning shore:
 winds heaven curling vapours bore.
 ungrateful offering immortal powers![197]
 whose wrath hung heavy o’er trojan towers:
 priam sons obtain’d grace;
 proud troy hated, guilty race.
 
troops exulting sat order round,
 beaming fires illumined ground.
 moon, refulgent lamp night,[198]
 o’er heaven’s pure azure spreads sacred light,
 breath disturbs deep serene,
 cloud o’ercasts solemn scene,
 around throne vivid planets roll,
 stars unnumber’d gild glowing pole,
 o’er dark trees yellower verdure shed,
 tip silver every mountain’s head:
 shine vales, rocks prospect rise,
 flood glory bursts skies:
 conscious swains, rejoicing sight,
 eye blue vault, bless useful light.
 many flames proud ilion blaze,
 lighten glimmering xanthus rays.
 long reflections distant fires
 gleam walls, tremble spires.
 thousand piles dusky horrors gild,
 shoot shady lustre o’er field.
 full fifty guards flaming pile attend,
 whose umber’d arms, fits, thick flashes send,
 loud neigh coursers o’er heaps corn,
 ardent warriors wait rising morn.

book ix.
 

argument.
 

embassy achilles.
 

agamemnon, last day’s defeat, proposes greeks quit
 siege, return country. diomed opposes this, nestor
 seconds him, praising wisdom resolution. orders guard to
 strengthened, council summoned deliberate measures are
 followed emergency. agamemnon pursues advice, and
 nestor prevails upon send ambassadors achilles, in
 order move reconciliation. ulysses ajax made choice
 of, accompanied old phœnix. make, them, very
 moving pressing speeches, rejected roughness by
 achilles, notwithstanding retains phœnix tent. the
 ambassadors return unsuccessfully camp, troops betake
 sleep.
 book, next following, take space one night,
 twenty-seventh beginning poem. the
 scene lies sea-shore, station grecian ships.
 

thus joyful troy maintain’d watch night;
 fear, pale comrade inglorious flight,[199]
 heaven-bred horror, grecian part,
 sat face, sadden’d every heart.
 cloudy dungeon issuing forth,
 double tempest west north
 swells o’er sea, thracia’s frozen shore,
 heaps waves waves, bids Ægean roar:
 way boiling deeps toss’d:
 various passions urged troubled host,
 great agamemnon grieved rest;
 superior sorrows swell’d royal breast;
 orders heralds bears,
 bid council grecian peers,
 bid whispers: surround chief,
 solemn sadness majestic grief.
 king amidst mournful circle rose:
 wan cheek briny torrent flows.
 silent fountains, rock’s tall head,
 sable streams soft-trickling waters shed.
 vulgar grief stood oppress’d;
 words, mix’d sighs, thus bursting breast:
 
“ye sons greece! partake leader’s care;
 fellows arms princes war!
 partial jove justly complain,
 heavenly oracles believed vain.
 safe return promised toils,
 conquest honour’d enrich’d spoils:
 now shameful flight alone can save host;
 wealth, people, glory lost.
 jove decrees, almighty lord all!
 jove, whose nod whole empires rise fall,
 shakes feeble props human trust,
 towers armies humbles dust.
 haste then, ever quit fatal fields,
 haste joys native country yields;
 spread canvas, oars employ,
 hope fall heaven-defended troy.”
 
said: deep silence held grecian band;
 silent, unmov’d dire dismay stand;
 pensive scene! till tydeus’ warlike son
 roll’d king eyes, thus begun:
 “when kings advise us renounce fame,
 first let speak first suffer’d shame.
 oppose thee, prince! thy wrath withhold,
 laws council bid tongue bold.
 thou first, thou alone, fields fight,
 durst brand courage, defame might:
 friend unkind reproach appear’d,
 greeks stood witness, army heard.
 gods, chief! honours spring,
 gods made thee halves king:
 gave thee sceptres, wide command;
 gave dominion o’er seas land;
 noblest power might world control
 gave thee not—a brave virtuous soul.
 general’s voice, suggest
 fears like every grecian breast?
 confiding want worth, stands;
 fly, ’tis king commands.
 go thou, inglorious! embattled plain;
 ships thou hast store, nearest main;
 noble care grecians shall employ,
 combat, conquer, extirpate troy.
 greece shall stay; or, greece retire,
 shall stay, till troy expire;
 myself, sthenelus, will fight fame;
 god bade us fight, ’twas god came.”
 
ceased; greeks loud acclamations raise,
 voice voice resounds tydides’ praise.
 wise nestor reverend figure rear’d;
 spoke: host still attention heard:[200]
 
“o truly great! gods join’d
 strength body force mind:
 conduct, courage, excel,
 still first act advise well.
 wholesome counsels thy wisdom moves,
 applauding greece common voice approves.
 kings thou canst blame; bold prudent youth:
 blame even kings praise, truth.
 yet years since thy birth run
 hardly style thee nestor’s youngest son.
 let add yet remains behind,
 thought unfinish’d generous mind;
 age bids speak! shall advice bring
 distaste people, offend king:
 
“cursed man, void law right,
 unworthy property, unworthy light,
 unfit public rule, private care,
 wretch, monster, delights war;
 whose lust murder, whose horrid joy,
 tear country, kind destroy!
 night, refresh fortify thy train;
 trench wall let guards remain:
 duty young bold;
 thou, king, council call old;
 great thy sway, weighty thy cares;
 thy high commands must spirit wars.
 thracian wines recruit thy honour’d guests,
 happy counsels flow sober feasts.
 wise, weighty counsels aid state distress’d,
 monarch can choose best.
 see blaze hostile tents aspires,
 near fleet approach trojan fires!
 can, unmoved, behold dreadful light?
 eye beholds them, can close to-night?
 dreadful interval determines all;
 to-morrow, troy must flame, greece must fall.”
 
thus spoke hoary sage: rest obey;
 swift gates guards direct way.
 first pass lofty mound,
 generous thrasymed, arms renown’d:
 next him, ascalaphus, iälmen, stood,
 double offspring warrior-god:
 deipyrus, aphareus, merion join,
 lycomed creon’s noble line.
 seven leaders nightly bands,
 bold chief hundred spears commands.
 fires light, short repasts fall,
 line trench, others man wall.
 
king men, public counsels bent,
 convened princes ample tent,
 seized portion kingly feast,
 stay’d hand thirst hunger ceased.
 nestor spoke, wisdom long approved,
 slowly rising, thus council moved.
 
“monarch nations! whose superior sway
 assembled states, lords earth obey,
 laws sceptres thy hand given,
 millions care thee heaven.
 king! counsels age attend;
 thee cares begin, thee must end.
 thee, prince! fits alike speak hear,
 pronounce judgment, regard give ear,
 see wholesome motion withstood,
 ratify best public good.
 nor, though meaner give advice, repine,
 follow it, make wisdom thine.
 hear thought, now conceived haste,
 present judgment past.
 pelides’ tent forced maid,
 first opposed, faithful, durst dissuade;
 bold soul, headlong fury fired,
 wronged man, men gods admired:
 now seek means fatal wrath end,
 prayers move him, gifts bend.”
 
king. “with justice hast thou shown
 prince’s faults, reason own.
 happy man, jove still honours most,
 armies, host.
 bless’d love, wondrous hero stands;
 heaven fights war, humbles bands.
 fain heart, err’d frantic rage,
 wrathful chief angry gods assuage.
 gifts immense mighty soul can bow,[201]
 hear, ye greeks, witness vow.
 ten weighty talents purest gold,
 twice ten vases refulgent mould:
 seven sacred tripods, whose unsullied frame
 yet knows office, felt flame;
 twelve steeds unmatch’d fleetness force,
 still victorious dusty course;
 (rich man whose ample stores exceed
 prizes purchased winged speed;)
 seven lovely captives lesbian line,
 skill’d art, unmatch’d form divine,
 chose vulgar charms,
 lesbos sank beneath hero’s arms:
 these, buy friendship, shall paid,
 join’d long-contested maid;
 charms, briseïs resign,
 solemn swear charms never mine;
 untouch’d stay’d, uninjured removes,
 pure arms, guiltless loves,[202]
 instant shall his; powers
 give arms proud ilion’s hostile towers,
 shall store (when greece spoil divides)
 gold brass loaded navy’s sides:
 besides, full twenty nymphs trojan race
 copious love shall crown warm embrace,
 will choose; yield none,
 yield helen’s heavenly charms alone.
 yet hear further: wars o’er,
 safe land argos’ fruitful shore,
 shall live son, honours share,
 orestes’ self divide care.
 yet more—three daughters court bred,
 well worthy royal bed;
 laodice iphigenia fair,[203]
 bright chrysothemis golden hair;
 let choose eyes approve,
 ask presents, reward love:
 will give dower; vast store
 never father gave child before.
 seven ample cities shall confess sway,
 enope, pheræ obey,
 cardamyle ample turrets crown’d,
 sacred pedasus vines renown’d;
 Æpea fair, pastures hira yields,
 rich antheia flowery fields:[204]
 whole extent pylos’ sandy plain,
 along verdant margin main.
 heifers graze, labouring oxen toil;
 bold men, generous soil;
 shall reign, power justice crown’d,
 rule tributary realms around.
 give, vengeance control,
 sure may move mighty soul.
 pluto, grisly god, never spares,
 feels mercy, hears prayers,
 lives dark dreadful deep hell’s abodes,
 mortals hate him, worst gods.
 great though be, fits obey,
 since years, sway.”
 

[illustration: ] pluto
 

monarch thus. reverend nestor then:
 “great agamemnon! glorious king men!
 thy offers prince may take,
 fits generous king make.
 let chosen delegates hour sent
 (myself will name them) pelides’ tent.
 let phœnix lead, revered hoary age,
 great ajax next, ithacus sage.
 yet sanctify word send,
 let hodius eurybates attend.
 now pray jove grant greece demands;
 pray deep silence,[205] purest hands.”[206]
 

[illustration: ] embassy achilles
 

said; approved. heralds bring
 cleansing water living spring.
 youth wine sacred goblets crown’d,
 large libations drench’d sands around.
 rite perform’d, chiefs thirst allay,
 royal tent take way;
 wise nestor turns careful eye,
 forbids offend, instructs apply;
 much advised all, ulysses most,
 deprecate chief, save host.
 still night march, hear roar
 murmuring billows sounding shore.
 neptune, ruler seas profound,
 whose liquid arms mighty globe surround,
 pour forth vows, embassy bless,
 calm rage stern Æacides.
 now, arrived, sandy bay
 myrmidonian tents vessels lay;
 amused ease, godlike man found,
 pleased solemn harp’s harmonious sound.
 (the well wrought harp conquered thebae came;
 polish’d silver costly frame.)
 soothes angry soul, sings
 immortal deeds heroes kings.
 patroclus royal train,
 placed tent, attends lofty strain:
 full opposite sat, listen’d long,
 silence waiting till ceased song.
 unseen grecian embassy proceeds
 high tent; great ulysses leads.
 achilles starting, chiefs spied,
 leap’d seat, laid harp aside.
 like surprise arose menoetius’ son:
 pelides grasp’d hands, thus begun:
 
“princes, hail! whatever brought here.
 strong necessity, urgent fear;
 welcome, though greeks! foes ye came;
 dear bear name.”
 
that, chiefs beneath roof led,
 placed seats purple carpets spread.
 thus—“patroclus, crown larger bowl,
 mix purer wine, open every soul.
 warriors yonder host can send,
 thy friend honours these, thy friend.”
 
said: patroclus o’er blazing fire
 heaps brazen vase three chines entire:
 brazen vase automedon sustains,
 flesh porker, sheep, goat contains.
 achilles genial feast presides,
 parts transfixes, skill divides.
 meanwhile patroclus sweats, fire raise;
 tent brighten’d rising blaze:
 then, languid flames length subside,
 strows bed glowing embers wide,
 coals smoking fragments turns
 sprinkles sacred salt lifted urns;
 bread glittering canisters load,
 round board menoetius’ bestow’d;
 himself, opposed ulysses full sight,
 portion parts, orders every rite.
 first fat offering immortals due,
 amidst greedy flames patroclus threw;
 each, indulging social feast,
 thirst hunger soberly repress’d.
 done, phœnix ajax gave sign:
 unperceived; ulysses crown’d wine
 foaming bowl, instant thus began,
 speech addressing godlike man.
 
“health achilles! happy thy guests!
 honour’d atrides feasts:
 though generous plenty crown thy loaded boards,
 that, agamemnon’s regal tent affords;
 greater cares sit heavy souls,
 eased banquets flowing bowls.
 scenes slaughter yon fields appear!
 dead mourn, living fear;
 greece brink fate doubtful stands,
 owns help thy saving hands:
 troy aids ready vengeance call;
 threatening tents already shade wall:
 hear shouts conquest proclaim,
 point every ship vengeful flame!
 father gods declares,
 omens, thunder theirs.
 see, full jove, avenging hector rise!
 see! heaven earth raging chief defies;
 fury breast, lightning eyes!
 waits morn, sink flame
 ships, greeks, grecian name.
 heavens! country’s woes distract mind,
 lest fate accomplish rage design’d!
 must we, gods! heads inglorious lay
 trojan dust, fatal day?
 return, achilles: oh return, though late,
 save thy greeks, stop course fate;
 heart grief courage lies,
 rise redeem; ah, yet conquer, rise!
 day may come, when, warriors slain,
 heart shall melt, courage rise vain:
 regard time, prince divinely brave!
 wholesome counsels thy father gave.
 peleus aged arms embraced
 parting son, accents last:
 
“‘my child! strength, glory, success,
 thy arms may juno minerva bless!
 trust heaven: thou, thy cares engage
 calm thy passions, subdue thy rage:
 gentler manners let thy glory grow,
 shun contention, sure source woe;
 young old may thy praise combine,
 virtues humanity thine—’
 now-despised advice thy father gave;
 ah! check thy anger; truly brave.
 thou wilt yield great atrides’ prayers,
 gifts worthy thee royal hand prepares;
 not—but hear me, number o’er
 proffer’d presents, exhaustless store.
 ten weighty talents purest gold,
 twice ten vases refulgent mould;
 seven sacred tripods, whose unsullied frame
 yet knows office, felt flame;
 twelve steeds unmatched fleetness force,
 still victorious dusty course;
 (rich man, whose ample stores exceed
 prizes purchased winged speed;)
 seven lovely captives lesbian line,
 skill’d art, unmatch’d form divine,
 chose vulgar charms,
 lesbos sank beneath thy conquering arms.
 these, buy thy friendship shall paid,
 and, join’d these, long-contested maid;
 charms, briseïs he’ll resign,
 solemn swear charms thine;
 untouch’d stay’d, uninjured removes,
 pure arms, guiltless loves.
 instant shall thine; powers
 give arms proud ilion’s hostile towers,
 shalt thou store (when greece spoil divides)
 gold brass thy loaded navy’s sides.
 besides, full twenty nymphs trojan race
 copious love shall crown thy warm embrace;
 thyself shall chose; yield none,
 yield helen’s heavenly charms alone.
 yet hear further: wars o’er,
 safe land argos’ fruitful shore,
 shalt thou live son, honour share,
 orestes’ self divide care.
 yet more—three daughters court bred,
 well worthy royal bed:
 laodice iphigenia fair,
 bright chrysothemis golden hair:
 shalt thou wed thy eyes approve;
 asks presents, reward love:
 will give dower; vast store
 never father gave child before.
 seven ample cities shall confess thy sway,
 enope pheræ thee obey,
 cardamyle ample turrets crown’d,
 sacred pedasus, vines renown’d:
 Æpea fair, pastures hira yields,
 rich antheia flowery fields;
 whole extent pylos’ sandy plain,
 along verdant margin main.
 heifers graze, labouring oxen toil;
 bold men, generous soil.
 shalt thou reign, power justice crown’d,
 rule tributary realms around.
 proffers day bring,
 repentance suppliant king.
 this, relentless, thou disdain,
 honour interest plead vain,
 yet redress suppliant greece afford,
 be, amongst guardian gods, adored.
 regard thy suffering country claim,
 hear thy glory, voice fame:
 now chief, whose unresisted ire
 made nations tremble, whole hosts retire,
 proud hector, now, unequal fight demands,
 triumphs deserve thy hands.”
 
thus goddess-born: “ulysses, hear
 faithful speech, knows art fear;
 secret soul understood,
 tongue shall utter, deeds make good.
 let greece know, purpose retain:
 new treaties vex peace vain.
 dares think one thing, another tell,
 heart detests gates hell.
 
“then thus short fix’d resolves attend,
 atrides greeks can bend;
 long toils, long perils cause bore,
 now unfruitful glories charm more.
 fight fight, like reward claim,
 wretch hero find prize same.
 alike regretted dust lies,
 yields ignobly, bravely dies.
 dangers, glorious pains,
 life labours, lo! fruit remains?
 bold bird helpless young attends,
 danger guards them, want defends;
 search prey wings spacious air,
 untasted food supplies care:
 thankless greece hardships braved,
 wives, infants, labours saved;
 long sleepless nights heavy arms stood,
 sweat laborious days dust blood.
 sack’d twelve ample cities main,[207]
 twelve lay smoking trojan plain:
 atrides’ haughty feet laid
 wealth gathered, spoils made.
 mighty monarch peace possess’d;
 soldiers had, rest.
 present, too, every prince paid;
 every prince enjoys gift made:
 must refund, train;
 see pre-eminence merits gain!
 spoil alone greedy soul delights:
 spouse alone must bless lustful nights:
 woman, let (as may) enjoy;
 what’s quarrel, then, greece troy?
 shores assembled nations draws,
 calls vengeance woman’s cause?
 fair endowments beauteous face
 beloved none atreus’ race?
 wife choice passion doth approve,
 sure every wise worthy man will love.
 fair one less distinction claim;
 slave was, soul adored dame.
 wrong’d love, proffers disdain;
 deceived once, trust kings again.
 ye answer—what remains do,
 king, ulysses, may consult you.
 needs defence arm can make?
 walls human force can shake?
 fenced guarded navy round
 piles, ramparts, trench profound?
 will (the wonders done)
 repel rage priam’s single son?
 time (’twas greece fought)
 hector’s prowess wonders wrought;
 kept verge troy, dared wait
 achilles’ fury scæan gate;
 tried once, scarce saved fate.
 now ancient enmities o’er;
 to-morrow favouring gods implore;
 shall see parting vessels crown’d,
 hear oars hellespont resound.
 third day hence shall pythia greet sails,[208]
 mighty neptune send propitious gales;
 pythia achilles shall restore
 wealth left detested shore:
 thither spoils long war shall pass,
 ruddy gold, steel, shining brass:
 beauteous captives thither i’ll convey,
 rests unravish’d prey.
 one valued gift tyrant gave,
 resumed—the fair lyrnessian slave.
 tell him: loud, greeks may hear,
 learn scorn wretch basely fear;
 (for arm’d impudence, mankind braves,
 meditates new cheats slaves;
 though shameless is, face eyes
 dares not: dares dies;)
 tell him, terms, commerce decline,
 share council, battle join;
 deceiv’d, his; twice mine,
 no—let stupid prince, jove deprives
 sense justice, run frenzy drives;
 gifts hateful: kings kind
 stand slaves noble mind,
 though proffer’d possess’d,
 rapine others wrest:
 golden tides wealth crown
 many-peopled orchomenian town;[209]
 proud thebes’ unrivall’d walls contain,
 world’s great empress egyptian plain
 (that spreads conquests o’er thousand states,
 pours heroes hundred gates,
 two hundred horsemen two hundred cars
 wide portal issuing wars);[210]
 though bribes heap’d bribes, number more
 dust fields, sands along shore;
 offers friendship call,
 ’tis offers, scorn all.
 atrides’ daughter never shall led
 (an ill-match’d consort) achilles’ bed;
 like golden venus though charm’d heart,
 vied pallas works art;
 greater greek let high nuptials grace,
 hate alliance tyrant’s race.
 heaven restore realms life,
 reverend peleus shall elect wife;
 thessalian nymphs form divine,
 kings sue mix blood mine.
 bless’d kind love, years shall glide away,
 content just hereditary sway;
 there, deaf ever martial strife,
 enjoy dear prerogative life.
 life bought heaps gold.
 apollo’s pythian treasures hold,
 troy held, peace pride sway,
 can bribe poor possession day!
 lost herds treasures arms regain,
 steeds unrivall’d dusty plain:
 lips vital spirit fled,
 returns wake silent dead.
 fates long since thetis disclosed,
 alternate, life fame, proposed;
 here, stay, trojan town,
 short date, deathless renown:
 return, quit immortal praise
 years years, long-extended days.
 convinced, though late, find fond mistake,
 warn greeks wiser choice make;
 quit shores, native seats enjoy,
 hope fall heaven-defended troy.
 jove’s arm display’d asserts skies!
 hearts strengthen’d, glories rise.
 go greece, report fix’d design;
 bid counsels, armies join,
 let forces, arts conspire,
 save ships, troops, chiefs, fire.
 one stratagem fail’d, others will:
 ye find, achilles unconquer’d still.
 go then—digest message ye may—
 night let reverend phœnix stay:
 tedious toils hoary hairs demand
 peaceful death pythia’s friendly land.
 whether remain sail me,
 age sacred, will free.”

peleus ceased: chiefs around

 (down white beard stream sorrow flows;)
 fate suffering greece mourn’d,

[illustration: ] proserpine
 

“divine achilles! wilt thou retire,
 leave hosts blood, fleets fire?
 wrath dreadful fill thy ruthless mind,
 shall thy friend, thy phœnix, stay behind?
 royal peleus, pythia’s coast
 sent thee early achaian host;
 thy youth sage debates unskill’d,
 new perils direful field:
 bade teach thee ways war,
 shine councils, camps dare.
 never, ah, never let leave thy side!
 time shall part us, fate divide,
 though god, breathed life, restore
 bloom boasted, port bore,
 greece old beheld youthful flames
 (delightful greece, land lovely dames),
 father faithless mother’s arms,
 old was, adored stranger’s charms.
 tried youth (at desire)
 win damsel, prevent sire.
 sire curses loads hated head,
 cries, ‘ye furies! barren bed.’
 infernal jove, vengeful fiends below,
 ruthless proserpine, confirm’d vow.
 despair grief distract labouring mind!
 gods! crime impious heart design’d!
 thought (but kind god thought suppress’d)
 plunge poniard father’s breast;
 meditate flight: friends vain
 prayers entreat me, force detain.
 fat rams, black bulls, brawny swine,
 daily feast, draughts fragrant wine;
 strong guards placed, watch’d nine nights entire;
 roofs porches flamed constant fire.
 tenth, forced gates, unseen all:
 and, favour’d night, o’erleap’d wall,
 travels thence spacious greece extend;
 phthia’s court last labours end.
 sire received me, caress’d,
 gifts enrich’d, possessions bless’d.
 strong dolopians thenceforth own’d reign,
 coast runs along main.
 love thee bounties repaid,
 early wisdom thy soul convey’d:
 great thou art, lessons made thee brave:
 child took thee, hero gave.
 thy infant breast like affection show’d;
 still arms (an ever-pleasing load)
 knee, phœnix wouldst thou stand;
 food grateful phœnix’ hand.[211]
 pass watchings o’er thy helpless years,
 tender labours, compliant cares,
 gods (i thought) reversed hard decree,
 phœnix felt father’s joys thee:
 thy growing virtues justified cares,
 promised comfort silver hairs.
 now thy rage, thy fatal rage, resign’d;
 cruel heart ill suits manly mind:
 gods (the great, wise)
 moved offerings, vows, sacrifice;
 offending man high compassion wins,
 daily prayers atone daily sins.
 prayers jove’s daughters, celestial race,
 lame feet, wrinkled face;
 humble mien, dejected eyes,
 constant follow, injustice flies.
 injustice swift, erect, unconfined,
 sweeps wide earth, tramples o’er mankind,
 prayers, heal wrongs, move slow behind.
 hears daughters almighty jove,
 mediate throne above:
 man rejects humble suit make,
 sire revenges daughters’ sake;
 jove commission’d, fierce injustice then
 descends punish unrelenting men.
 let headlong passion bear sway
 reconciling goddesses obey:
 due honours seed jove belong,
 due honours calm fierce, bend strong.
 paid thee terms bring,
 rage still harbour’d haughty king;
 greece fortunes engage
 thy friend plead just rage.
 since honour asks general sends,
 sends thy heart commends;
 best noblest grecian train;
 permit sue, sue vain!
 let (my son) ancient fact unfold,
 great example drawn times old;
 hear fathers were, praise,
 conquer’d revenge former days.
 
“where calydon rocky mountains stands[212]
 fought Ætolian curetian bands;
 guard those; conquer, advance;
 mutual deaths dealt mutual chance.
 silver cynthia bade contention rise,
 vengeance neglected sacrifice;
 Œneus fields sent monstrous boar,
 levell’d harvests, whole forests tore:
 beast (when many chief tusks slain)
 great meleager stretch’d along plain,
 then, spoils, new debate arose,
 neighbour nations thence commencing foes.
 strong were, bold curetes fail’d,
 meleager’s thundering arm prevail’d:
 till rage length inflamed lofty breast
 (for rage invades wisest best).
 
“cursed althaea, wrath yields,
 wife’s embrace forgets fields.
 (she marpessa sprung, divinely fair,
 matchless idas, man war:
 god day adored mother’s charms;
 god father bent arms:
 afflicted pair, sorrows proclaim,
 cleopatra changed daughter’s name,
 call’d alcyone; name show
 father’s grief, mourning mother’s woe.)
 chief retired stern debate,
 found peace fierce althaea’s hate:
 althaea’s hate unhappy warrior drew,
 whose luckless hand royal uncle slew;
 beat ground, call’d powers beneath
 wreak brother’s death;
 hell heard curses realms profound,
 red fiends walk nightly round.
 vain Ætolia deliverer waits,
 war shakes walls, thunders gates.
 sent ambassadors, chosen band,
 priests gods, elders land;
 besought chief save sinking state:
 prayers urgent, proffers great:
 (full fifty acres richest ground,
 half pasture green, half vineyards crown’d:)
 suppliant father, aged Œneus, came;
 sisters follow’d; even vengeful dame,
 althaea, sues; friends fall:
 stands relentless, rejects all.
 meanwhile victor’s shouts ascend skies;
 walls scaled; rolling flames arise;
 length wife (a form divine) appears,
 piercing cries, supplicating tears;
 paints horrors conquer’d town,
 heroes slain, palaces o’erthrown,
 matrons ravish’d, whole race enslaved:
 warrior heard, vanquish’d, saved.
 Ætolians, long disdain’d, now took turn,
 left chief broken faith mourn.
 learn hence, betimes curb pernicious ire,
 stay till yonder fleets ascend fire;
 accept presents; draw thy conquering sword;
 amongst guardian gods adored.”
 
thus he: stern achilles thus replied:
 “my second father, reverend guide:
 thy friend, believe me, gifts demands,
 asks honours mortal’s hands;
 jove honours me, favours designs;
 pleasure guides me, will confines;
 stay (if high behest)
 life’s warm spirit beats within breast.
 yet hear one word, lodge thy heart:
 molest atrides’ part:
 tears taught flow,
 sorrows? mortal foe?
 generous friendship cold medium knows,
 burns one love, one resentment glows;
 one interests passions be;
 friend must hate man injures me.
 this, phœnix, ’tis generous part;
 share realms, honours, heart.
 let return: voyage, stay,
 rest undetermined till dawning day.”
 
ceased; order’d sage’s bed
 warmer couch numerous carpets spread.
 that, stern ajax long silence broke,
 thus, impatient, ulysses spoke:
 
“hence let us go—why waste time vain?
 see effect low submissions gain!
 liked liked, words must relate,
 greeks expect them, heroes wait.
 proud is, iron heart retains
 stubborn purpose, friends disdains.
 stern unpitying! brother bleed,
 just atonement, remit deed;
 sire slaughter forgives;
 price blood discharged, murderer lives:
 haughtiest hearts length rage resign,
 gifts can conquer every soul thine.[213]
 gods unrelenting breast steel’d,
 cursed thee mind yield.
 one woman-slave ravish’d thy arms:
 lo, seven offer’d, equal charms.
 hear, achilles! better mind;
 revere thy roof, thy guests kind;
 know men grecian host,
 honour worth, prize thy valour most.”
 
“o soul battles, thy people’s guide!
 (to ajax thus first greeks replied)
 well hast thou spoke; tyrant’s name
 rage rekindles, soul’s flame:
 ’tis just resentment, becomes brave:
 disgraced, dishonour’d, like vilest slave!
 return, then, heroes! answer bear,
 glorious combat care;
 till, amidst yon sinking navy slain,
 blood greeks shall dye sable main;
 till flames, hector’s fury thrown,
 consume vessels, approach own;
 just there, impetuous homicide shall stand,
 cease battle, feel hand.”
 
said, prince double goblet crown’d,
 cast large libation ground;
 vessels, gloomy shades,
 chiefs return; divine ulysses leads.
 meantime achilles’ slaves prepared bed,
 fleeces, carpets, soft linen spread:
 there, till sacred morn restored day,
 slumber sweet reverend phœnix lay.
 inner tent, ampler space,
 achilles slept; warm embrace
 fair diomede lesbian race.
 last, patroclus couch prepared,
 whose nightly joys beauteous iphis shared;
 achilles friend consign’d charms
 scyros fell conquering arms.
 
now elected chiefs greece sent,
 pass’d hosts, reach’d royal tent.
 rising all, goblets hands,
 peers leaders achaian bands
 hail’d return: atrides first begun:
 
“say success? divine laertes’ son!
 achilles’ high resolves declare all:
 returns chief, must navy fall?”
 
“great king nations! (ithacus replied)
 fix’d wrath, unconquer’d pride;
 slights thy friendship, thy proposals scorns,
 and, thus implored, fiercer fury burns.
 save army, fleets free,
 care; left greece thee.
 eyes shall view, morning paints sky,
 beneath oars whitening billows fly;
 us bids oars sails employ,
 hope fall heaven-protected troy;
 jove o’ershades arm divine,
 inspires war, bids glory shine.
 word: declared,
 sacred heralds great ajax heard.
 phœnix tent chief retains,
 safe transport native plains
 morning dawns; decree,
 age sacred, choice free.”
 
ulysses ceased: great achaian host,
 sorrow seized, consternation lost,
 attend stern reply. tydides broke
 general silence, undaunted spoke.
 “why gifts proud achilles send,
 strive prayers haughty soul bend?
 country’s woes glories deride,
 prayers will burst swelling heart pride.
 fierce impulse rage obey’d,
 battles let desert aid;
 let arm jove think fit:
 that, madness, heaven commit:
 can, always ours;
 night, let due repast refresh powers;
 (for strength consists spirits blood,
 owed generous wine food;)
 rosy messenger day
 strikes blue mountains golden ray,
 ranged ships, let squadrons shine
 flaming arms, long-extended line:
 dread front let great atrides stand,
 first danger, high command.”
 
shouts acclaim listening heroes raise,
 heaven due libations pays;
 till sleep, descending o’er tents, bestows
 grateful blessings desired repose.[214]
