book x.
 

argument.
 

night-adventure diomed ulysses.
 

upon refusal achilles return army, distress of
 agamemnon described lively manner. takes rest that
 night, passes camp, awaking leaders, contriving
 possible methods public safety. menelaus, nestor, ulysses,
 diomed employed raising rest captains. call
 council war, determine send scouts enemies’ camp,
 learn posture, discover intentions. diomed
 undertakes hazardous enterprise, makes choice ulysses for
 companion. passage surprise dolon, hector had
 sent like design camp grecians. are
 informed situation trojan auxiliary forces, and
 particularly rhesus, thracians lately arrived. they
 pass success; kill rhesus, several officers, and
 seize famous horses prince, return in
 triumph camp.
 night continues; scene lies two camps.
 

night chiefs vessels lay,
 lost sleep labours day:
 king: various thoughts oppress’d,[215]
 country’s cares lay rolling breast.
 lightnings jove’s ethereal power
 foretels rattling hail, weighty shower,
 sends soft snows whiten shore,
 bids brazen throat war roar;
 fits one flash succeeds one expires,
 heaven flames thick momentary fires:
 bursting frequent atrides’ breast,
 sighs following sighs inward fears confess’d.
 now o’er fields, dejected, surveys
 thousand trojan fires mounting blaze;
 hears passing wind music blow,
 marks distinct voices foe.
 now looking backwards fleet coast,
 anxious sorrows endangered host.
 rends hair, sacrifice jove,
 sues ever lives above:
 inly groans; glory despair
 divide heart, wage double war.
 
thousand cares labouring breast revolves;
 seek sage nestor now chief resolves,
 him, wholesome counsels, debate
 yet remains save afflicted state.
 rose, first cast mantle round,
 next feet shining sandals bound;
 lion’s yellow spoils back conceal’d;
 warlike hand pointed javelin held.
 meanwhile brother, press’d equal woes,
 alike denied gifts soft repose,
 laments greece, cause before
 much suffer’d must suffer more.
 leopard’s spotted hide shoulders spread:
 brazen helmet glitter’d head:
 thus (with javelin hand) went
 wake atrides royal tent.
 already waked, atrides descried,
 armour buckling vessel’s side.
 joyful met; spartan thus begun:
 “why puts brother bright armour on?
 sends spy, amidst silent hours,
 try yon camp, watch trojan powers?
 say, hero shall sustain task?
 bold exploits uncommon courage ask;
 guideless, alone, night’s dark shade go,
 midst hostile camp explore foe.”
 
king: “in distress stand,
 vulgar counsel affairs demand;
 greece preserve, now easy part,
 asks high wisdom, deep design, art.
 jove, averse, humble prayer denies,
 bows head hector’s sacrifice.
 eye witness’d, ear believed,
 one great day, one great arm achieved,
 wondrous deeds hector’s hand done,
 beheld, last revolving sun?
 honours beloved jove adorn!
 sprung god, goddess born;
 yet acts, greeks unborn shall tell,
 curse battle fathers fell.
 
“now speed thy hasty course along fleet,
 call great ajax, prince crete;
 ourself hoary nestor will repair;
 keep guards duty care,
 (for nestor’s influence best quarter guides,
 whose merion, o’er watch presides.”)
 spartan: “these thy orders borne,
 say, shall stay, despatch return?”
 “there shall thou stay, (the king men replied,)
 else may miss meet, without guide,
 paths many, camp wide.
 still, voice slothful soldiers raise,
 urge fathers’ fame future praise.
 forget now state lofty birth;
 titles here, works, must prove worth.
 labour lot man below;
 jove gave us life, gave us woe.”
 
said, parted several cares:
 king nestor’s sable ship repairs;
 sage protector greeks found
 stretch’d bed arms around;
 various-colour’d scarf, shield rears,
 shining helmet, pointed spears;
 dreadful weapons warrior’s rage,
 that, old arms, disdain’d peace age.
 then, leaning hand watchful head,
 hoary monarch raised eyes said:
 
“what art thou, speak, designs unknown,
 others sleep, thus range camp alone;
 seek’st thou friend nightly sentinel?
 stand off, approach not, thy purpose tell.”
 
“o neleus, (thus king rejoin’d,)
 pride greeks, glory thy kind!
 lo, wretched agamemnon stands,
 unhappy general grecian bands,
 jove decrees daily cares bend,
 woes, life shall end!
 scarce can knees trembling limbs sustain,
 scarce heart support load pain.
 taste sleep heavy eyes known,
 confused, sad, wander thus alone,
 fears distracted, fix’d design;
 people’s miseries mine.
 aught use thy waking thoughts suggest,
 (since cares, like mine, deprive thy soul rest,)
 impart thy counsel, assist thy friend;
 now let us jointly trench descend,
 every gate fainting guard excite,
 tired toils day watch night;
 else may sudden foe works invade,
 near, favour’d gloomy shade.”
 
thus nestor: “trust powers above,
 think proud hector’s hopes confirm’d jove:
 ill agree views vain mankind,
 wise counsels eternal mind!
 audacious hector, gods ordain
 great achilles rise rage again,
 toils attend thee, woes remain!
 lo, faithful nestor thy command obeys;
 care next chiefs raise:
 ulysses, diomed, chiefly need;
 meges strength, oïleus famed speed.
 despatch’d nimbler feet,
 tall ships, remotest fleet,
 lie great ajax king crete.[216]
 rouse spartan decree;
 dear us, dear thee,
 yet must tax sloth, claims share
 great brother martial care:
 behoved every chief sue,
 preventing every part perform’d you;
 strong necessity toils demands,
 claims hearts, urges hands.”
 
king: “with reverence allow
 thy just rebukes, yet learn spare now:
 generous brother gentle kind,
 seems remiss, bears valiant mind;
 much deference sovereign sway,
 content follow lead way:
 now, ills industrious prevent,
 long ere rest rose, sought tent.
 chiefs named, already call,
 prepare meet us near navy-wall;
 assembling there, trench gates,
 near night-guards, chosen council waits.”
 
“then none (said nestor) shall rule withstand,
 great examples justify command.”
 that, venerable warrior rose;
 shining greaves manly legs enclose;
 purple mantle golden buckles join’d,
 warm softest wool, doubly lined.
 rushing tent, snatch’d haste
 steely lance, lighten’d pass’d.
 camp traversed sleeping crowd,
 stopp’d ulysses’ tent, call’d aloud.
 ulysses, sudden voice sent,
 awakes, starts up, issues tent.
 “what new distress, sudden cause fright,
 thus leads wandering silent night?”
 “o prudent chief! (the pylian sage replied)
 wise thou art, now thy wisdom tried:
 whatever means safety can sought,
 whatever counsels can inspire thought,
 whatever methods, fly fight;
 all, depend important night!”
 heard, return’d, took painted shield;
 join’d chiefs, follow’d field.
 without tent, bold diomed found,
 sheathed arms, brave companions round:
 sunk sleep, extended field,
 head reclining bossy shield.
 wood spears stood by, that, fix’d upright,
 shot flashing points quivering light.
 bull’s black hide composed hero’s bed;
 splendid carpet roll’d beneath head.
 then, foot, old nestor gently shakes
 slumbering chief, words awakes:
 
“rise, tydeus! brave strong
 rest seems inglorious, night long.
 sleep’st thou now, yon hill foe
 hangs o’er fleet, shades walls below?”
 
this, soft slumber eyelids fled;
 warrior saw hoary chief, said:
 “wondrous old man! whose soul respite knows,
 though years honours bid thee seek repose,
 let younger greeks sleeping warriors wake;
 ill fits thy age toils undertake.”
 “my friend, (he answered,) generous thy care;
 toils, subjects sons might bear;
 loyal thoughts pious love conspire
 ease sovereign relieve sire:
 now last despair surrounds host;
 hour must pass, moment must lost;
 single greek, conclusive strife,
 stands sharpest edge death life:
 yet, years thy kind regard engage,
 employ thy youth employ age;
 succeed cares, rouse rest;
 serves most, serves country best.”
 
said, hero o’er shoulders flung
 lion’s spoils, ankles hung;
 seized ponderous lance, strode along.
 meges bold, ajax famed speed,
 warrior roused, entrenchments lead.
 
now chiefs approach nightly guard;
 wakeful squadron, arms prepared:
 unwearied watch listening leaders keep,
 and, couching close, repel invading sleep.
 faithful dogs fleecy charge maintain,
 toil protected prowling train;
 gaunt lioness, hunger bold,
 springs mountains toward guarded fold:
 breaking woods rustling course hear;
 loud, loud, clamours strike ear
 hounds men: start, gaze around,
 watch every side, turn every sound.
 thus watch’d grecians, cautious surprise,
 voice, motion, drew ears eyes:
 step passing feet increased affright;
 hostile troy ever full sight.
 nestor joy wakeful band survey’d,
 thus accosted gloomy shade.
 “’tis well, sons! nightly cares employ;
 else must host become scorn troy.
 watch thus, greece shall live.” hero said;
 o’er trench following chieftains led.
 son, godlike merion, march’d behind
 (for princes council join’d).
 trenches pass’d, assembled kings around
 silent state consistory crown’d.
 place was, yet undefiled gore,
 spot hector stopp’d rage before;
 night descending, vengeful hand
 reprieved relics grecian band:
 (the plain beside mangled corps spread,
 progress mark’d heaps dead:)
 sat mournful kings: neleus’ son,
 council opening, words begun:
 
“is (said he) chief greatly brave,
 life hazard, country save?
 lives man, singly dares go
 yonder camp, seize straggling foe?
 favour’d night approach near,
 speech, counsels, designs hear?
 besiege navies prepare,
 troy must seat war?
 learn, peers recite,
 pass unharm’d dangers night;
 fame succeeding days,
 phœbus shines, men tongues praise!
 gifts grateful country bestow!
 must greece deliverer owe?
 sable ewe leader provide,
 sable lambkin side;
 every rite share increased,
 foremost honours feast.”
 
fear held mute: alone, untaught fear,
 tydides spoke—“the man seek here.
 yon black camps bend dangerous way,
 god within commands, obey.
 let chosen warrior join,
 raise hopes, second design.
 mutual confidence mutual aid,
 great deeds done, great discoveries made;
 wise new prudence wise acquire,
 one brave hero fans another’s fire.”
 
contending leaders word arose;
 generous breast emulation glows;
 brave task ajax strove share,
 bold merion strove, nestor’s valiant heir;
 spartan wish’d second place gain,
 great ulysses wish’d, wish’d vain.
 thus king men contest ends:
 “thou first warriors, thou best friends,
 undaunted diomed! chief join
 great enterprise, thine.
 just thy choice, without affection made;
 birth, office, respect paid;
 let worth determine here.” monarch spake,
 inly trembled brother’s sake.
 
“then thus (the godlike diomed rejoin’d)
 choice declares impulse mind.
 can doubt, great ulysses stands
 lend counsels assist hands?
 chief, whose safety minerva’s care;
 famed, dreadful, works war:
 bless’d conduct, aid require;
 wisdom like might pass flames fire.”
 
“it fits thee not, chiefs fame,
 (replied sage,) praise me, blame:
 praise friend, censure foe,
 lost hearers merits know.
 let us haste—night rolls hours away,
 reddening orient shows coming day,
 stars shine fainter ethereal plains,
 night’s empire third remains.”
 
thus spoke, generous ardour press’d,
 arms terrific huge limbs dress’d.
 two-edged falchion thrasymed brave,
 ample buckler, tydides gave:
 leathern helm cased head,
 short crest, plume o’erspread:
 (such youths unused arms worn:)
 spoils enrich it, studs adorn.
 next ulysses took shining sword,
 bow quiver, bright arrows stored:
 well-proved casque, leather braces bound,
 (thy gift, meriones,) temples crown’d;
 soft wool within; without, order spread,[217]
 boar’s white teeth grinn’d horrid o’er head.
 amyntor, rich ormenus’ son,
 autolycus fraudful rapine won,
 gave amphidamas; prize
 molus received, pledge social ties;
 helmet next merion possess’d,
 now ulysses’ thoughtful temples press’d.
 thus sheathed arms, council forsake,
 dark paths oblique progress take.
 just then, sign favour’d intent,
 long-wing’d heron great minerva sent:
 this, though surrounding shades obscured view,
 shrill clang whistling wings knew.
 right soar’d, ulysses pray’d,
 hail’d glad omen, address’d maid:
 
“o daughter god whose arm can wield
 avenging bolt, shake saber shield!
 thou! ever present way,
 motions, toils survey!
 safe may pass beneath gloomy shade,
 safe thy succour ships convey’d,
 let deed signal night adorn,
 claim tears trojans yet unborn.”
 
godlike diomed preferr’d prayer:
 “daughter jove, unconquer’d pallas! hear.
 great queen arms, whose favour tydeus won,
 thou defend’st sire, defend son.
 Æsopus’ banks banded powers
 greece left, sought theban towers,
 peace charge; received peaceful show,
 went legate, return’d foe:
 help’d thee, cover’d thy shield,
 fought numbers, made numbers yield.
 now present, celestial maid!
 still continue race thine aid!
 youthful steer shall fall beneath stroke,
 untamed, unconscious galling yoke,
 ample forehead, spreading horns,
 whose taper tops refulgent gold adorns.”
 heroes pray’d, pallas skies
 accords vow, succeeds enterprise.
 now, like two lions panting prey,
 dreadful thoughts trace dreary way,
 black horrors ensanguined plain,
 dust, blood, o’er arms, hills slain.
 
less bold hector, sons troy,
 high designs wakeful hours employ;
 assembled peers lofty chief enclosed;
 thus counsels breast proposed:
 
“what glorious man, high attempts prepared,
 dares greatly venture rich reward?
 yonder fleet bold discovery make,
 watch keep, resolves take?
 now subdued meditate flight,
 and, spent toil, neglect watch night?
 chariot shall please most,
 plunder vanquish’d host;
 fair steeds rest excel,
 glory served well.”
 
youth among tribes troy,
 dolon name, eumedes’ boy,
 (five girls beside reverend herald told.)
 rich brass, rich gold;
 bless’d nature charms face,
 swift foot, matchless race.
 “hector! (he said) courage bids meet
 high achievement, explore fleet:
 first exalt thy sceptre skies,
 swear grant demanded prize;
 immortal coursers, glittering car,
 bear pelides ranks war.
 encouraged thus, idle scout go,
 fulfil thy wish, whole intention know,
 even royal tent pursue way,
 counsels, aims betray.”
 
chief heaved golden sceptre high,
 attesting thus monarch sky:
 “be witness thou! immortal lord all!
 whose thunder shakes dark aerial hall:
 none dolon shall prize borne,
 alone immortal steeds adorn.”
 
thus hector swore: gods call’d vain,
 rash youth prepares scour plain:
 across back bended bow flung,
 wolf’s grey hide around shoulders hung,
 ferret’s downy fur helmet lined,
 hand pointed javelin shined.
 (never return) sought shore,
 trod path feet must tread more.
 scarce pass’d steeds trojan throng,
 (still bending forward coursed along,)
 when, hollow way, approaching tread
 ulysses mark’d, thus diomed;
 
“o friend! hear step hostile feet,
 moving way, hastening fleet;
 spy, perhaps, lurk beside main;
 nightly pillager strips slain.
 yet let pass, win little space;
 rush behind him, prevent pace.
 swift foot flies before,
 confine course along fleet shore,
 betwixt camp spears employ,
 intercept hoped return troy.”
 
stepp’d aside, stoop’d head,
 (as dolon pass’d,) behind heap dead:
 along path spy unwary flew;
 soft, just distance, chiefs pursue.
 distant they, space between,
 two teams mules divide green,
 (to hind like shares land allows,)
 now new furrows part approaching ploughs.
 now dolon, listening, heard pass’d;
 hector (he thought) sent, check’d haste,
 till scarce distance javelin’s throw,
 voice succeeding, perceived foe.
 two skilful hounds leveret wind;
 chase woods obscure trembling hind;
 now lost, now seen, intercept way,
 herd still turn flying prey:
 fast, fears, trojan flew;
 close, constant, bold greeks pursue.
 now almost fleet dastard falls,
 mingles guards watch walls;
 brave tydides stopp’d; gen’rous thought
 (inspired pallas) bosom wrought,
 lest foe forward greek advance,
 snatch glory lifted lance.
 thus aloud: “whoe’er thou art, remain;
 javelin else shall fix thee plain.”
 said, high air weapon cast,
 wilful err’d, o’er shoulder pass’d;
 fix’d earth. trembling wood
 wretch stood propp’d, quiver’d stood;
 sudden palsy seized turning head;
 loose teeth chatter’d, colour fled;
 panting warriors seize stands,
 unmanly tears life demands.
 
“o spare youth, breath owe,
 large gifts price father shall bestow:
 vast heaps brass shall ships told,
 steel well-temper’d refulgent gold.”
 
ulysses made wise reply:
 “whoe’er thou art, bold, fear die.
 moves thee, say, sleep closed sight,
 roam silent fields dead night?
 cam’st thou secrets camp find,
 hector prompted, thy daring mind?
 art wretch hopes plunder led,
 heaps carnage, despoil dead?”
 
thus pale dolon, fearful look:
 (still, spoke, limbs horror shook:)
 “hither came, hector’s words deceived;
 much promise, rashly believed:
 less bribe great achilles’ car,
 swift steeds sweep ranks war,
 urged me, unwilling, attempt make;
 learn counsels, resolves take:
 now subdued, fix hopes flight,
 and, tired toils, neglect watch night.”
 
“bold thy aim, glorious prize,
 (ulysses, scornful smile, replies,)
 far rulers proud steeds demand,
 scorn guidance vulgar hand;
 even great achilles scarce rage can tame,
 achilles sprung immortal dame.
 say, faithful, truth recite!
 lies encamp’d trojan chief to-night?
 stand coursers? quarter sleep
 princes? tell watch keep:
 say, since conquest, counsels are;
 combat, city far,
 back ilion’s walls transfer war?”
 
ulysses thus, thus eumedes’ son:
 “what dolon knows, faithful tongue shall own.
 hector, peers assembling tent,
 council holds ilus’ monument.
 certain guards nightly watch partake;
 where’er yon fires ascend, trojans wake:
 anxious troy, guard natives keep;
 safe cares, auxiliar forces sleep,
 whose wives infants, danger far,
 discharge souls half fears war.”
 
“then sleep aids among trojan train,
 (inquired chief,) scattered o’er plain?”
 spy: “their powers thus dispose
 paeons, dreadful bended bows,
 carians, caucons, pelasgian host,
 leleges, encamp along coast.
 distant far, lie higher land
 lycian, mysian, mæonian band,
 phrygia’s horse, thymbras’ ancient wall;
 thracians utmost, apart all.
 troy lately succour won,
 led rhesus, great eioneus’ son:
 saw coursers proud triumph go,
 swift wind, white winter-snow;
 rich silver plates shining car infold;
 solid arms, refulgent, flame gold;
 mortal shoulders suit glorious load,
 celestial panoply, grace god!
 let me, unhappy, fleet borne,
 leave here, captive’s fate mourn,
 cruel chains, till return reveal
 truth falsehood news tell.”
 
tydides, gloomy frown:
 “think live, though truth shown:
 shall dismiss thee, future strife
 risk bravely thy now forfeit life?
 camps thou may’st explore?
 no—once traitor, thou betray’st more.”
 
sternly spoke, wretch prepared
 humble blandishment stroke beard,
 like lightning swift wrathful falchion flew,
 divides neck, cuts nerves two;
 one instant snatch’d trembling soul hell,
 head, yet speaking, mutter’d fell.
 furry helmet brow tear,
 wolf’s grey hide, unbended bow spear;
 great ulysses lifting skies,
 favouring pallas dedicates prize:
 
“great queen arms, receive hostile spoil,
 let thracian steeds reward toil;
 thee, first heavenly host, praise;
 speed labours, direct ways!”
 said, spoils, dropping gore defaced,
 high spreading tamarisk placed;
 heap’d reeds gathered boughs plain,
 guide footsteps place again.
 
still night cross devious fields,
 slippery blood, o’er arms heaps shields,
 arriving thracian squadrons lay,
 eased sleep labours day.
 ranged three lines view prostrate band:
 horses yoked beside warrior stand.
 arms order ground reclined,
 brown shade fulgid weapons shined:
 amidst lay rhesus, stretch’d sleep profound,
 white steeds behind chariot bound.
 welcome sight ulysses first descries,
 points diomed tempting prize.
 “the man, coursers, car behold!
 described dolon, arms gold.
 now, brave tydides! now thy courage try,
 approach chariot, steeds untie;
 thy soul aspire fiercer deeds,
 urge thou slaughter, seize steeds.”
 
pallas (this said) hero’s bosom warms,
 breathed heart, strung nervous arms;
 where’er pass’d, purple stream pursued
 thirsty falchion, fat hostile blood,
 bathed footsteps, dyed fields gore,
 low groan remurmur’d shore.
 grim lion, nightly den,
 o’erleaps fences, invades pen,
 sheep goats, resistless way,
 falls, foaming rends guardless prey;
 stopp’d fury vengeful hand,
 till twelve lay breathless thracian band.
 ulysses following, partner slew,
 back foot slaughter’d warrior drew;
 milk-white coursers studious convey
 safe ships, wisely cleared way:
 lest fierce steeds, yet battles bred,
 start, tremble heaps dead.
 now twelve despatch’d, monarch last found;
 tydides’ falchion fix’d ground.
 just deathful dream minerva sent,
 warlike form appear’d tent,
 whose visionary steel bosom tore:
 dream’d monarch, awaked more.[218]
 
ulysses now snowy steeds detains,
 leads them, fasten’d silver reins;
 these, bow unbent, lash’d along;
 (the scourge forgot, rhesus’ chariot hung;)
 gave friend signal retire;
 him, new dangers, new achievements fire;
 doubtful stood, reeking blade
 send heroes infernal shade,
 drag car rhesus’ armour lay,
 heave manly force, lift away.
 unresolved tydeus stands,
 pallas appears, thus chief commands:
 
“enough, son; slaughter cease,
 regard thy safety, depart peace;
 haste ships, gotten spoils enjoy,
 tempt far hostile gods troy.”
 
voice divine confess’d martial maid;
 haste mounted, word obey’d;
 coursers fly ulysses’ bow,
 swift wind, white winter-snow.
 
unobserved pass’d: god light
 watch’d troy, mark’d minerva’s flight,
 saw tydeus’ heavenly succour bless’d,
 vengeful anger fill’d sacred breast.
 swift trojan camp descends power,
 wakes hippocoon morning-hour;
 (on rhesus’ side accustom’d attend,
 faithful kinsman, instructive friend;)
 rose, saw field deform’d blood,
 empty space late coursers stood,
 yet-warm thracians panting coast;
 wept, rhesus most:
 now rhesus’ name calls vain,
 gathering tumult spreads o’er plain;
 heaps trojans rush, wild affright,
 wondering view slaughters night.
 
meanwhile chiefs, arriving shade
 late spoils hector’s spy laid,
 ulysses stopp’d; tydides bore
 trophy, dropping yet dolon’s gore:
 mounts again; nimbler feet
 coursers ply, thunder towards fleet.
 

[illustration: ] diomed ulysses returning spoils rhesus
 

old nestor first perceived approaching sound,
 bespeaking thus grecian peers around:
 “methinks noise trampling steeds hear,
 thickening way, gathering ear;
 perhaps horses trojan breed
 (so may, ye gods! pious hopes succeed)
 great tydides ulysses bear,
 return’d triumphant prize war.
 yet much fear (ah, may fear vain!)
 chiefs outnumber’d trojan train;
 perhaps, even now pursued, seek shore;
 or, oh! perhaps heroes more.”
 
scarce spoke, when, lo! chiefs appear,
 spring earth; greeks dismiss fear:
 words friendship extended hands
 greet kings; nestor first demands:
 
“say thou, whose praises host proclaim,
 thou living glory grecian name!
 say whence coursers? chance bestow’d,
 spoil foes, present god?
 fair steeds, radiant gay,
 draw burning chariot day.
 old am, age scorn yield,
 daily mingle martial field;
 sure till now coursers struck sight
 like these, conspicuous ranks fight.
 god, deem, conferred glorious prize,
 bless’d ye are, favourites skies;
 care bids thunder roar,
 her, whose fury bathes world gore.”
 
“father! so, (sage ithacus rejoin’d,)
 gifts heaven nobler kind.
 thracian lineage steeds ye view,
 whose hostile king brave tydides slew;
 sleeping died, guards around,
 twelve beside lay gasping ground.
 spoils conquer’d dolon came,
 wretch, whose swiftness fame;
 hector sent forces explore,
 now lies headless sandy shore.”
 
o’er trench bounding coursers flew;
 joyful greeks loud acclaim pursue.
 straight tydides’ high pavilion borne,
 matchless steeds ample stalls adorn:
 neighing coursers new fellows greet,
 full racks heap’d generous wheat.
 dolon’s armour, ships convey’d,
 high painted stern ulysses laid,
 trophy destin’d blue-eyed maid.
 
now nocturnal sweat sanguine stain
 cleanse bodies neighb’ring main:
 polished bath, refresh’d toil,
 joints supple dissolving oil,
 due repast indulge genial hour,
 first pallas libations pour:
 sit, rejoicing aid divine,
 crown’d goblet foams floods wine.
 



book xi.
 

argument
 

third battle, acts agamemnon.
 

agamemnon, armed himself, leads grecians battle; hector
 prepares trojans receive them, jupiter, juno, minerva
 give signals war. agamemnon bears hector is
 commanded jupiter (who sends iris purpose) decline the
 engagement, till king shall wounded retire field.
 makes great slaughter enemy. ulysses diomed put a
 stop time latter, wounded paris, is
 obliged desert companion, encompassed trojans,
 wounded, utmost danger, till menelaus ajax rescue him.
 hector comes ajax, hero alone opposes multitudes, and
 rallies greeks. meantime machaon, wing the
 army, pierced arrow paris, carried fight in
 nestor’s chariot. achilles (who overlooked action ship)
 sent patroclus inquire greeks wounded that
 manner; nestor entertains tent account the
 accidents day, long recital former wars he
 remembered, tending put patroclus upon persuading achilles fight
 countrymen, least permit it, clad in
 achilles’ armour. patroclus, return, meets eurypylus also
 wounded, assists distress.
 book opens eight-and-twentieth day poem, and
 day, various actions adventures extended
 twelfth, thirteenth, fourteenth, fifteenth, sixteenth,
 seventeenth, part eighteenth books. scene lies in
 field near monument ilus.
 

saffron morn, early blushes spread,[219]
 now rose refulgent tithonus’ bed;
 new-born day gladden mortal sight,
 gild courts heaven sacred light:
 baleful eris, sent jove’s command,
 torch discord blazing hand,
 red skies bloody sign extends,
 and, wrapt tempests, o’er fleet descends.
 high ulysses’ bark horrid stand
 took, thunder’d seas land.
 
even ajax achilles heard sound,
 whose ships, remote, guarded navy bound,
 thence black fury grecian throng
 horror sounds loud orthian song:
 navy shakes, dire alarms
 bosom boils, warrior starts arms.
 sigh, inglorious return,
 breathe revenge, combat burn.
 

[illustration: ] descent discord
 

king men hardy host inspires
 loud command, great example fires!
 first rose, rest
 mighty limbs radiant armour dress’d,
 first cased manly legs around
 shining greaves silver buckles bound;
 beaming cuirass next adorn’d breast,
 king cinyras possess’d:
 (the fame greece assembled host
 reach’d monarch cyprian coast;
 ’twas then, friendship chief gain,
 glorious gift sent, sent vain:)
 ten rows azure steel work infold,
 twice ten tin, twelve ductile gold;
 three glittering dragons gorget rise,
 whose imitated scales skies
 reflected various light, arching bow’d,
 like colour’d rainbows o’er showery cloud
 (jove’s wondrous bow, three celestial dies,
 placed sign man amidst skies).
 radiant baldric, o’er shoulder tied,
 sustain’d sword glitter’d side:
 gold hilt, silver sheath encased
 shining blade, golden hangers graced.
 buckler’s mighty orb next display’d,
 round warrior cast dreadful shade;
 ten zones brass ample brim surround,
 twice ten bosses bright convex crown’d:
 tremendous gorgon frown’d upon field,
 circling terrors fill’d expressive shield:
 within concave hung silver thong,
 mimic serpent creeps along,
 azure length easy waves extends,
 till three heads embroider’d monster ends.
 last o’er brows fourfold helm placed,
 nodding horse-hair formidably graced;
 hands two steely javelins wields,
 blaze heaven, lighten fields.
 
instant juno, martial maid,
 happy thunders promised greece aid;
 high o’er chief clash’d arms air,
 and, leaning clouds, expect war.
 
close limits trench mound,
 fiery coursers chariots bound
 squires restrain’d: foot, wield
 lighter arms, rush forward field.
 second these, close array combined,
 squadrons spread sable wings behind.
 now shouts tumults wake tardy sun,
 light warriors’ toils begun.
 even jove, whose thunder spoke wrath, distill’d
 red drops blood o’er fatal field;[220]
 woes men unwilling survey,
 slaughters must stain day.
 
near ilus’ tomb, order ranged around,
 trojan lines possess’d rising ground:
 wise polydamas hector stood;
 Æneas, honour’d guardian god;
 bold polybus, agenor divine;
 brother-warriors antenor’s line:
 youthful acamas, whose beauteous face
 fair proportion match’d ethereal race.
 great hector, cover’d spacious shield,
 plies troops, orders field.
 red star now shows sanguine fires
 dark clouds, now night retires,
 thus ranks appear’d godlike man,
 plunged rear, blazing van;
 streamy sparkles, restless flies,
 flash arms, lightning skies.
 sweating reapers wealthy field,
 ranged two bands, crooked weapons wield,
 bear furrows, till labours meet;
 thick fall heapy harvests feet:
 greece troy field war divide,
 falling ranks strow’d every side.
 none stoop’d thought base inglorious flight;[221]
 horse horse, man man fight,
 rabid wolves fierce contest prey;
 wounds, bleeds, none resign day.
 discord joy scene death descries,
 drinks large slaughter sanguine eyes:
 discord alone, immortal train,
 swells red horrors direful plain:
 gods peace golden mansions fill,
 ranged bright order olympian hill:
 general murmurs told griefs above,
 accused partial will jove.
 meanwhile apart, superior, alone,
 eternal monarch, awful throne,
 wrapt blaze boundless glory sate;
 fix’d, fulfill’d just decrees fate.
 earth turn’d all-considering eyes,
 mark’d spot ilion’s towers arise;
 ships, fields armies spread,
 victor’s rage, dying, dead.
 
thus morning-beams, increasing bright,
 o’er heaven’s pure azure spread glowing light,
 commutual death fate war confounds,
 adverse battle gored equal wounds.
 now (what time sequester’d vale
 weary woodman spreads sparing meal,
 tired arms refuse axe rear,
 claim respite sylvan war;
 till half prostrate forests lay
 stretch’d long ruin, exposed day)
 then, till then, greeks’ impulsive might
 pierced black phalanx, let light.
 great agamemnon slaughter led,
 slew bienor people’s head:
 whose squire oïleus, sudden spring,
 leap’d chariot revenge king;
 front felt fatal wound,
 pierced brain, stretch’d ground.
 atrides spoil’d, left plain:
 vain youth, glittering armour vain:
 now soil’d dust, naked sky,
 snowy limbs beauteous bodies lie.
 
two sons priam next battle move,
 product, one marriage, one love:[222]
 car brother-warriors ride;
 took charge combat, guide:
 far task, wont keep,
 ida’s tops, father’s fleecy sheep.
 mountains achilles found,
 captive led, pliant osiers bound;
 sire ample sums restored;
 now perish atrides’ sword:
 pierced breast base-born isus bleeds:
 cleft head brother’s fate succeeds,
 swift spoil hasty victor falls,
 and, stript, features mind recalls.
 trojans see youths untimely die,
 helpless tremble themselves, fly.
 lion ranging o’er lawns,
 finds, grassy lair, couching fawns,
 bones cracks, reeking vitals draws,
 grinds quivering flesh bloody jaws;
 frighted hind beholds, dares stay,
 swift rustling thickets bursts way;
 drown’d sweat, panting mother flies,
 big tears roll trickling eyes.
 
amidst tumult routed train,
 sons false antimachus slain;
 bribes faithless counsels sold,
 voted helen’s stay paris’ gold.
 atrides mark’d, safety sought,
 slew children father’s fault;
 headstrong horse unable restrain,
 shook fear, dropp’d silken rein;
 chariot knees fall,
 thus lifted hands mercy call:
 
“o spare youth, life owe,
 antimachus shall copious gifts bestow:
 soon hears, that, battle slain,
 grecian ships captive sons detain,
 large heaps brass ransom shall told,
 steel well-tempered, persuasive gold.”
 
words, attended flood tears,
 youths address’d unrelenting ears:
 vengeful monarch gave stern reply:
 “if antimachus ye spring, ye die;
 daring wretch council stood
 shed ulysses’ brother’s blood,
 proffer’d peace! sues seed grace?
 no, die, pay forfeit race.”
 
said, pisander car cast,
 pierced breast: supine breathed last.
 brother leap’d earth; but, lay,
 trenchant falchion lopp’d hands away;
 sever’d head toss’d among throng,
 and, rolling, drew bloody train along.
 then, thickest fought, victor flew;
 king’s example greeks pursue.
 now foot flying foot slain,
 horse trod horse, lay foaming plain.
 dry fields thick clouds dust arise,
 shade black host, intercept skies.
 brass-hoof’d steeds tumultuous plunge bound,
 thick thunder beats labouring ground,
 still slaughtering on, king men proceeds;
 distanced army wonders deeds,
 winds raging flames conspire,
 o’er forests roll flood fire,
 blazing heaps grove’s old honours fall,
 one refulgent ruin levels all:
 atrides’ rage sinks foe,
 whole squadrons vanish, proud heads lie low.
 steeds fly trembling waving sword,
 many car, now lighted lord,
 wide o’er field guideless fury rolls,
 breaking ranks, crushing souls;
 keen falchion drinks warriors’ lives;
 grateful, now, vultures wives!
 
perhaps great hector found fate,
 jove destiny prolong’d date.
 safe darts, care heaven stood,
 amidst alarms, death, dust, blood.
 
now past tomb ancient ilus lay,
 mid field routed urge way:
 wild figs adjoining summit crown,
 path take, speed reach town.
 swift, atrides loud shouts pursued,
 hot toil, bathed hostile blood.
 now near beech-tree, scæan gates,
 hero halts, associates waits.
 meanwhile every side around plain,
 dispersed, disorder’d, fly trojan train.
 flies herd beeves, hear dismay’d
 lion’s roaring midnight shade;
 heaps tumble successless haste;
 savage seizes, draws, rends last.
 less fury stern atrides flew,
 still press’d rout, still hindmost slew;
 hurl’d cars bravest chiefs kill’d,
 rage, death, carnage load field.
 
now storms victor trojan wall;
 surveys towers, meditates fall.
 jove descending shook idaean hills,
 summits pour’d hundred rills:
 unkindled lightning hand took,
 thus many-coloured maid bespoke:
 
“iris, haste thy golden wings display,
 godlike hector word convey—
 agamemnon wastes ranks around,
 fights front, bathes blood ground,
 bid give way; issue forth commands,
 trust war less important hands:
 when, wounded spear dart,
 chief shall mount chariot, depart,
 jove shall string arm, fire breast,
 ships shall flying greece press’d,
 till main burning sun descend,
 sacred night awful shade extend.”
 
spoke, iris word obey’d;
 wings winds descends various maid.
 chief found amidst ranks war,
 close bulwarks, glittering car.
 goddess then: “o priam, hear!
 jove come, high mandate bear.
 agamemnon wastes ranks around,
 fights front, bathes blood ground,
 abstain fight; yet issue forth commands,
 trust war less important hands:
 when, wounded spear dart,
 chief shall mount chariot, depart,
 jove shall string thy arm, fire thy breast,
 ships shall flying greece press’d,
 till main burning sun descend,
 sacred night awful shade extend.”
 
said, vanish’d. hector, bound,
 springs chariot trembling ground,
 clanging arms: grasps either hand
 pointed lance, speeds band band;
 revives ardour, turns steps flight,
 wakes anew dying flames fight.
 stand arms: greeks onset dare,
 condense powers, wait coming war.
 new force, new spirit, breast returns;
 fight renew’d fiercer fury burns:
 king leads on: fix eye,
 learn conquer, die.
 
ye sacred nine! celestial muses! tell,
 faced first, prowess fell?
 great iphidamas, bold young,
 sage antenor theano sprung;
 youth grandsire cisseus bred,
 nursed thrace snowy flocks fed.
 scarce rosy cheeks invest,
 early honour warm generous breast,
 kind sire consign’d daughter’s charms
 (theano’s sister) youthful arms.
 call’d glory wars troy,
 leaves untasted first fruits joy;
 loved bride departs melting eyes,
 swift aid dearer country flies.
 twelve black ships reach’d percope’s strand,
 thence took long laborious march land.
 now fierce fame, ranks springs,
 towering arms, braves king kings.
 atrides first discharged missive spear;
 trojan stoop’d, javelin pass’d air.
 near corslet, monarch’s heart,
 strength, youth directs dart:
 broad belt, plates silver bound,
 point rebated, repell’d wound.
 encumber’d dart, atrides stands,
 till, grasp’d force, wrench’d hands;
 weighty sword discharged wound
 full neck, fell’d ground.
 stretch’d dust unhappy warrior lies,
 sleep eternal seals swimming eyes.
 oh worthy better fate! oh early slain!
 thy country’s friend; virtuous, though vain!
 youth shall join consort’s side,
 virgin, bride!
 presents embraces meet,
 lay spoils conquest feet,
 passion, lavish store,
 bestow’d much, vainly promised more!
 unwept, uncover’d, plain lay,
 proud victor bore arms away.
 
coon, antenor’s eldest hope, nigh:
 tears, sight, came starting eye,
 pierced grief much-loved youth view’d,
 pale features now deform’d blood.
 then, spear, unseen, time took,
 aim’d king, near elbow strook.
 thrilling steel transpierced brawny part,
 arm stood forth barbed dart.
 surprised monarch feels, yet void fear
 coon rushes lifted spear:
 brother’s corpse pious trojan draws,
 calls country assert cause;
 defends breathless sanguine field,
 o’er body spreads ample shield.
 atrides, marking unguarded part,
 transfix’d warrior brazen dart;
 prone brother’s bleeding breast lay,
 monarch’s falchion lopp’d head away:
 social shades dark journey go,
 join realms below.
 
vengeful victor rages round fields,
 every weapon art fury yields:
 long lance, sword, ponderous stone,
 whole ranks broken, whole troops o’erthrown.
 this, yet warm distill’d purple flood;
 wound grew stiff clotted blood,
 grinding tortures strong bosom rend,
 less keen darts fierce ilythiae send:
 (the powers cause teeming matron’s throes,
 sad mothers unutterable woes!)
 stung smart, all-panting pain,
 mounts car, gives squire rein;
 voice fury made strong,
 pain augmented, thus exhorts throng:
 
“o friends! greeks! assert honours won;
 proceed, finish arm begun:
 lo! angry jove forbids chief stay,
 envies half glories day.”
 
said: driver whirls lengthful thong;
 horses fly; chariot smokes along.
 clouds nostrils fierce coursers blow,
 sides foam descends snow;
 shot battle moment’s space,
 wounded monarch tent place.
 
sooner hector saw king retired,
 thus trojans aids fired:
 “hear, ye dardan, ye lycian race!
 famed close fight, dreadful face face:
 now call mind ancient trophies won,
 great forefathers’ virtues, own.
 behold, general flies! deserts powers!
 lo, jove declares conquest ours!
 now yon ranks impel foaming steeds;
 and, sure glory, dare immortal deeds.”
 
words like fiery chief alarms
 fainting host, every bosom warms.
 bold hunter cheers hounds tear
 brindled lion, tusky bear:
 voice hand provokes doubting heart,
 springs foremost lifted dart:
 godlike hector prompts troops dare;
 prompts alone, leads war.
 black body foe pours;
 cloud’s deep bosom, swell’d showers,
 sudden storm purple ocean sweeps,
 drives wild waves, tosses deeps.
 say, muse! jove trojan’s glory crown’d,
 beneath arm heroes bit ground?
 assaeus, dolops, autonous died,
 opites next added side;
 brave hipponous, famed many fight,
 opheltius, orus, sunk endless night;
 Æsymnus, agelaus; chiefs name;
 rest vulgar deaths unknown fame.
 western whirlwind, charged storms,
 dispels gather’d clouds notus forms:
 gust continued, violent strong,
 rolls sable clouds heaps heaps along;
 now skies foaming billows rears,
 now breaks surge, wide bottom bares:
 thus, raging hector, resistless hands,
 o’erturns, confounds, scatters bands.
 now last ruin whole host appals;
 now greece trembled wooden walls;
 wise ulysses call’d tydides forth,
 soul rekindled, awaked worth.
 “and stand deedless, eternal shame!
 till hector’s arm involve ships flame?
 haste, let us join, combat side side.”
 warrior thus, thus friend replied:
 
“no martial toil shun, danger fear;
 let hector come; wait fury here.
 jove conquest crowns trojan train:
 and, jove foe, human force vain.”
 
sigh’d; but, sighing, raised vengeful steel,
 car proud thymbraeus fell:
 molion, charioteer, pursued lord,
 death ennobled ulysses’ sword.
 slain, left eternal night,
 plunged amidst thickest ranks fight.
 two wild boars outstrip following hounds,
 swift revert, wounds return wounds.
 stern hector’s conquests middle plain
 stood check’d awhile, greece respired again.
 
sons merops shone amidst war;
 towering rode one refulgent car:
 deep prophetic arts father skill’d,
 warn’d children trojan field.
 fate urged on: father warn’d vain;
 rush’d fight, perish’d plain;
 breasts vital spirit warms;
 stern tydides strips shining arms.
 hypirochus great ulysses dies,
 rich hippodamus becomes prize.
 great jove ide slaughter fills sight,
 level hangs doubtful scale fight.
 tydeus’ lance agastrophus slain,
 far-famed hero pæonian strain;
 wing’d fears, foot strove fly,
 steeds distant, foe nigh:
 broken orders, swifter wind,
 fled, flying left life behind.
 hector sees, experienced eyes
 traverse files, rescue flies;
 shouts, pass’d, crystal regions rend,
 moving armies march attend.
 great diomed seized fear,
 thus bespoke brother war:
 
“mark way yon bending squadrons yield!
 storm rolls on, hector rules field:
 stand utmost force.”—the warrior said;
 swift word ponderous javelin fled;
 miss’d aim, plumage danced
 razed smooth cone, thence obliquely glanced.
 safe helm (the gift phœbus’ hands)
 without wound trojan hero stands;
 yet stunn’d, that, staggering plain.
 arm knee sinking bulk sustain;
 o’er dim sight misty vapours rise,
 short darkness shades swimming eyes.
 tydides followed regain lance;
 hector rose, recover’d trance,
 remounts car, herds amidst crowd:
 greek pursues him, exults aloud:
 “once thank phœbus thy forfeit breath,
 thank swiftness outstrips death.
 well apollo thy prayers repaid,
 oft partial power lent aid.
 thou shall long death deserved withstand,
 god assist tydides’ hand.
 fly then, inglorious! thy flight, day,
 whole hecatombs trojan ghosts shall pay,”
 
him, triumph’d, paris eyed far,
 (the spouse helen, fair cause war;)
 around fields feather’d shafts sent,
 ancient ilus’ ruin’d monument:
 behind column placed, bent bow,
 wing’d arrow unwary foe;
 just stoop’d, agastrophus’s crest
 seize, drew corslet breast,
 bowstring twang’d; flew shaft vain,
 pierced foot, nail’d plain.
 laughing trojan, joyful spring.
 leaps ambush, insults king.
 
“he bleeds! (he cries) god sped dart!
 god fix’d heart!
 troy, relieved wide-wasting hand,
 breathe slaughter combat stand:
 whose sons now tremble darted spear,
 scatter’d lambs rushing lion fear.”
 
dauntless thus: “thou conqueror fair,
 thou woman-warrior curling hair;
 vain archer! trusting distant dart,
 unskill’d arms act manly part!
 thou hast done boys women can;
 hands may wound, incense man.
 boast scratch thy feeble arrow gave,
 coward’s weapon never hurts brave.
 dart, thou may’st one day feel;
 fate wings flight, death steel:
 lights, noble life expires;
 touch makes orphans, bathes cheeks sires,
 steeps earth purple, gluts birds air,
 leaves objects distract fair.”
 ulysses hastens trembling heart,
 steps, bending draws dart:
 forth flows blood; eager pang succeeds;
 tydides mounts, navy speeds.
 
now field ulysses stands alone,
 greeks fled, trojans pouring on;
 stands collected himself, whole,
 questions thus unconquer’d soul:
 
“what subterfuge, hopes remain?
 shame, inglorious quit plain?
 danger, singly stand ground,
 friends scatter’d, foes around?
 yet wherefore doubtful? let truth suffice,
 brave meets danger, coward flies.
 die conquer, proves hero’s heart;
 and, knowing this, know soldier’s part.”
 
thoughts revolving careful breast,
 near, near, shady cohorts press’d;
 these, warrior, fate enclose;
 round deep steely circle grows.
 fares boar troop surrounds
 shouting huntsmen clamorous hounds;
 grinds ivory tusks; foams ire;
 sanguine eye-balls glare living fire;
 these, those, every part plied;
 red slaughter spreads every side.
 pierced shoulder, first deiopis fell;
 next ennomus thoon sank hell;
 chersidamas, beneath navel thrust,
 falls prone earth, grasps bloody dust.
 charops, hippasus, near;
 ulysses reach’d fatal spear;
 aid brother socus flies,
 socus brave, generous, wise.
 near drew, warrior thus began:
 
“o great ulysses! much-enduring man!
 deeper skill’d every martial sleight,
 worn toils, active fight!
 day two brothers shall thy conquest grace,
 end great hippasian race,
 thou beneath lance must press field.”
 said, forceful pierced spacious shield:
 strong brass ringing javelin thrown,
 plough’d half side, bared bone.
 pallas’ care, spear, though deep infix’d,
 stopp’d short life, entrails mix’d.
 
wound mortal wise ulysses knew,
 furious thus (but first steps withdrew):
 “unhappy man! whose death hands shall grace,
 fate calls thee hence finish’d thy race.
 longer check conquests foe;
 but, pierced this, endless darkness go,
 add one spectre realms below!”
 
spoke, socus, seized sudden fright,
 trembling gave way, turn’d back flight;
 shoulders pierced following dart,
 held passage panting heart:
 wide breast appear’d grisly wound;
 falls; armour rings ground.
 thus ulysses, gazing slain:
 “famed hippasus! press plain;
 ends thy narrow span assign’d fate,
 heaven owes ulysses yet longer date.
 ah, wretch! father shall thy corpse compose;
 thy dying eyes tender mother close;
 hungry birds shall tear balls away,
 hovering vultures scream around prey.
 greece shall honour, meet doom,
 solemn funerals lasting tomb.”
 
raging intolerable smart,
 writhes body, extracts dart.
 dart tide spouting gore pursued,
 gladden’d troy sight hostile blood.
 now troops troops fainting chief invade,
 forced recedes, loudly calls aid.
 thrice pitch lofty voice rears;
 well-known voice thrice menelaus hears:
 alarm’d, ajax telamon cried,
 shares labours, defends side:
 “o friend! ulysses’ shouts invade ear;
 distressed seems, assistance near;
 strong is, yet one opposed all,
 oppress’d multitudes, best may fall.
 greece robb’d must bid host despair,
 feel loss ages can repair.”
 
then, cry directs, course bends;
 great ajax, like god war, attends,
 prudent chief sore distress found,
 bands furious trojans compass’d round.[223]
 huntsman, flying spear,
 blind thicket wounds stately deer;
 cleft side, fresh blood distils,
 bounds aloft, scuds hills hills,
 till life’s warm vapour issuing wound,
 wild mountain-wolves fainting beast surround:
 just jaws prostrate limbs invade,
 lion rushes woodland shade,
 wolves, though hungry, scour dispersed away;
 lordly savage vindicates prey.
 ulysses thus, unconquer’d pains,
 single warrior half host sustains:
 soon ajax leaves tower-like shield,
 scattered crowds fly frighted o’er field;
 atrides’ arm sinking hero stays,
 and, saved numbers, car conveys.
 
victorious ajax plies routed crew;
 first doryclus, priam’s son, slew,
 strong pandocus next inflicts wound,
 lays lysander bleeding ground.
 torrent, swell’d wintry rains,
 pours mountains o’er deluged plains,
 pines oaks, foundations torn,
 country’s ruins! seas borne:
 fierce ajax thus o’erwhelms yielding throng;
 men, steeds, chariots, roll heaps along.
 
hector, scene slaughter far,
 raged left, ruled tide war:
 loud groans proclaim progress plain,
 deep scamander swells heaps slain.
 nestor idomeneus oppose
 warrior’s fury; battle glows;
 fierce foot, chariot’s height,
 sword deforms beauteous ranks fight.
 spouse helen, dealing darts around,
 pierced machaon distant wound:
 right shoulder broad shaft appear’d,
 trembling greece physician fear’d.
 nestor idomeneus begun:
 “glory greece, old neleus’ valiant son!
 ascend thy chariot, haste speed away,
 great machaon ships convey;
 wise physician skill’d wounds heal,
 armies public weal.”
 old nestor mounts seat; beside rode
 wounded offspring healing god.
 lends lash; steeds sounding feet
 shake dry field, thunder toward fleet.
 
now cebriones, hector’s car,
 survey’d various fortune war:
 “while (he cried) flying greeks slain,
 trojans trojans yonder load plain.
 great ajax see mingled throng
 men chariots driven heaps along!
 know well, distinguish’d o’er field
 broad glittering sevenfold shield.
 thither, hector, thither urge thy steeds,
 danger calls, combat bleeds;
 horse foot mingled deaths unite,
 groans slaughter mix shouts fight.”
 
thus spoke, driver’s lash resounds;
 swift ranks rapid chariot bounds;
 stung stroke, coursers scour fields,
 o’er heaps carcases, hills shields.
 horses’ hoofs bathed heroes’ gore,
 and, dashing, purple car before;
 groaning axle sable drops distils,
 mangled carnage clogs rapid wheels.
 hector, plunging thickest fight,
 broke dark phalanx, let light:
 (by long lance, sword, ponderous stone,
 ranks scatter’d troops o’erthrown:)
 ajax shuns, dire debate,
 fears arm whose force felt late.
 partial jove, espousing hector’s part,
 shot heaven-bred horror grecian’s heart;
 confused, unnerved hector’s presence grown,
 amazed stood, terrors own.
 o’er broad back moony shield threw,
 and, glaring round, tardy steps withdrew.
 thus grim lion retreat maintains,
 beset watchful dogs, shouting swains;
 repulsed numbers nightly stalls,
 though rage impels him, though hunger calls,
 long stands showering darts, missile fires;
 sourly slow indignant beast retires:
 turn’d stern ajax, whole hosts repell’d,
 swoln heart every step rebell’d.
 
slow beast, heavy strength endued,
 wide field troops boys pursued,
 though round sides wooden tempest rain,
 crops tall harvest, lays waste plain;
 thick hide hollow blows resound,
 patient animal maintains ground,
 scarce field efforts chased,
 stirs slowly stirs last:
 ajax thus weight trojans hung,
 strokes redoubled buckler rung;
 confiding now bulky strength stands,
 now turns, backward bears yielding bands;
 now stiff recedes, yet hardly seems fly,
 threats followers retorted eye.
 fix’d bar two warring powers,
 hissing darts descend iron showers:
 broad buckler many weapon stood,
 surface bristled quivering wood;
 many javelin, guiltless plain,
 marks dry dust, thirsts blood vain.
 bold eurypylus aid imparts,
 dauntless springs beneath cloud darts;
 whose eager javelin launch’d foe,
 great apisaon felt fatal blow;
 torn liver red current flow’d,
 slack knees desert dying load.
 victor rushing despoil dead,
 paris’ bow vengeful arrow fled;
 fix’d nervous thigh weapon stood,
 fix’d point, broken wood.
 back lines wounded greek retired,
 yet thus retreating, associates fired:
 
“what god, grecians! hearts dismay’d?
 oh, turn arms; ’tis ajax claims aid.
 hour stands mark hostile rage,
 last brave battle shall wage:
 haste, join forces; gloomy grave
 warrior rescue, country save.”
 thus urged chief: generous troop appears,
 spread bucklers, advance spears,
 guard wounded friend: thus stand
 pious care, great ajax joins band:
 takes new courage hero’s sight;
 hero rallies, renews fight.
 
thus raged armies like conflicting fires,
 nestor’s chariot far fight retires:
 coursers steep’d sweat, stain’d gore,
 greeks’ preserver, great machaon, bore.
 hour achilles, topmost height
 proud fleet, o’erlook’d fields fight;
 feasted eyes beheld around plain
 grecian rout, slaying, slain.
 friend machaon singled rest,
 transient pity touch’d vengeful breast.
 straight menoetius’ much-loved sent:
 graceful mars, patroclus quits tent;
 evil hour! fate decreed doom,
 fix’d date woes come.
 
“why calls friend? thy loved injunctions lay;
 whate’er thy will, patroclus shall obey.”
 
“o first friends! (pelides thus replied)
 still heart, ever side!
 time come, yon despairing host
 shall learn value man lost:
 now knees greeks shall pour moan,
 proud atrides tremble throne.
 go now nestor, taught
 wounded warrior late chariot brought:
 for, seen distance, seen behind,
 form recall’d machaon mind;
 i, yon cloud, discern face,
 coursers pass’d swift pace.”
 
hero said. friend obey’d haste,
 intermingled ships tents pass’d;
 chiefs descending car found:
 panting steeds eurymedon unbound.
 warriors standing breezy shore,
 dry sweat, wash away gore,
 paused moment, gentle gale
 convey’d freshness cool seas exhale;
 consult farther methods went,
 took seats beneath shady tent.
 draught prescribed, fair hecamede prepares,
 arsinous’ daughter, graced golden hairs:
 (whom aged arms, royal slave,
 greece, prize nestor’s wisdom gave:)
 table first azure feet placed;
 whose ample orb brazen charger graced;
 honey new-press’d, sacred flour wheat,
 wholesome garlic, crown’d savoury treat,
 next white hand antique goblet brings,
 goblet sacred pylian kings
 eldest times: emboss’d studs gold,
 two feet support it, four handles hold;
 bright handle, bending o’er brink,
 sculptured gold, two turtles seem drink:
 massy weight, yet heaved ease him,
 brisk nectar overlook’d brim.
 temper’d this, nymph form divine
 pours large portion pramnian wine;
 goat’s-milk cheese flavourous taste bestows,
 last flour smiling surface strows:
 wounded prince dame prepares:
 cordial beverage reverend nestor shares:
 salubrious draughts warriors’ thirst allay,
 pleasing conference beguiles day.
 
meantime patroclus, achilles sent,
 unheard approached, stood tent.
 old nestor, rising then, hero led
 high seat: chief refused said:
 
“’tis now season kind delays;
 great achilles impatience stays.
 great achilles respect owe;
 asks, hero, wounded foe,
 borne combat thy foaming steeds?
 grief see great machaon bleeds.
 report, hasty course bend;
 thou know’st fiery temper friend.”
 “can sons greece (the sage rejoin’d)
 excite compassion achilles’ mind?
 seeks sorrows host know?
 half story woe.
 tell him, great machaon bleeds alone,
 bravest heroes navy groan,
 ulysses, agamemnon, diomed,
 stern eurypylus, already bleed.
 but, ah! flattering hopes entertain!
 achilles heeds not, derides pain:
 even till flames consume fleet stays,
 waits rising fatal blaze.
 chief chief raging foe destroys;
 calm looks on, every death enjoys.
 now slow course all-impairing time
 unstrings nerves, ends manly prime;
 oh! still strength youth possess’d,
 bold arm epeian powers oppress’d,
 bulls elis glad triumph led,
 stretch’d great itymonaeus dead!
 fury fled trembling swains,
 plunder plains:
 fifty white flocks, full fifty herds swine,
 many goats, many lowing kine:
 thrice number unrivall’d steeds,
 teeming females, generous breeds.
 these, first essay arms, won;
 old neleus gloried conquering son.
 thus elis forced, long arrears restored,
 shares parted pylian lord.
 state pyle sunk last despair,
 proud elians first commenced war:
 neleus’ sons alcides’ rage slain;
 twelve bold brothers, alone remain!
 oppress’d, arm’d; now conquest gain’d,
 sire three hundred chosen sheep obtain’d.
 (that large reprisal might justly claim,
 prize defrauded, insulted fame,
 elis’ monarch, public course,
 detain’d chariot, victorious horse.)
 rest people shared; survey’d
 just partition, due victims paid.
 three days past, elis rose war,
 many courser, many car;
 sons actor army’s head
 (young were) vengeful squadrons led.
 high rock fair thryoessa stands,
 utmost frontier pylian lands:
 far streams famed alphaeus flow:
 stream pass’d, pitch’d tents below.
 pallas, descending shades night,
 alarms pylians commands fight.
 burns fame, swells martial pride,
 foremost; sire denied;
 fear’d youth, exposed stern alarms;
 stopp’d chariot, detain’d arms.
 sire denied vain: foot fled
 amidst chariots; goddess led.
 
“along fair arene’s delightful plain
 soft minyas rolls waters main:
 there, horse foot, pylian troops unite,
 sheathed arms, expect dawning light.
 thence, ere sun advanced noon-day flame,
 great alphaeus’ sacred source came.
 first jove solemn rites paid;
 untamed heifer pleased blue-eyed maid;
 bull, alphaeus; bull slain
 blue monarch watery main.
 arms slept, beside winding flood,
 round town fierce epeians stood.
 soon sun, all-revealing ray,
 flamed front heaven, gave day.
 bright scenes arms, works war appear;
 nations meet; pylos, elis here.
 first fell, beneath javelin bled;
 king augias’ son, spouse agamede:
 (she simples’ healing virtues knew,
 every herb drinks morning dew:)
 seized car, battle led;
 epeians saw, trembled, fled.
 foe dispersed, bravest warrior kill’d,
 fierce whirlwind now swept field:
 full fifty captive chariots graced train;
 two chiefs fell breathless plain.
 actor’s sons died, neptune shrouds
 youthful heroes veil clouds.
 o’er heapy shields, o’er prostrate throng,
 collecting spoils, slaughtering along,
 wide buprasian fields forced foes,
 o’er vales olenian rocks arose;
 till pallas stopp’d us alisium flows.
 even hindmost rear slay,
 arm led concludes day;
 back pyle triumphant take way.
 high jove public thanks assign’d,
 first gods; nestor, mankind.
 was, impell’d youthful blood;
 proved valour country’s good.
 
“achilles unactive fury glows,
 gives passion greece owes.
 shall grieve, eternal shade
 hosts shall sink, power aid!
 friend! memory recalls day,
 when, gathering aids along grecian sea,
 i, ulysses, touch’d phthia’s port,
 entered peleus’ hospitable court.
 bull jove slew sacrifice,
 pour’d libations flaming thighs.
 thyself, achilles, thy reverend sire
 menoetius, turn’d fragments fire.
 achilles sees us, feast invites;
 social sit, share genial rites.
 explained cause came,
 urged arms, found fierce fame.
 ancient fathers generous precepts gave;
 peleus said this:—‘my son! brave.’
 menoetius thus: ‘though great achilles shine
 strength superior, race divine,
 yet cooler thoughts thy elder years attend;
 let thy just counsels aid, rule thy friend.’
 thus spoke father thessalia’s court:
 words now forgot, though now vast import.
 ah! try utmost friend can say:
 gentle force fiercest minds obey;
 favouring god achilles’ heart may move;
 though deaf glory, may yield love.
 dire oracle breast alarm,
 aught heaven withhold saving arm,
 beam comfort yet greece may shine,
 thou lead myrmidonian line;
 clad achilles’ arms, thou appear,
 proud troy may tremble, desist war;
 press’d fresh forces, o’er-labour’d train
 shall seek walls, greece respire again.”
 
touch’d generous heart, tent
 along shore hasty strides went;
 soon came, where, crowded strand,
 public mart courts justice stand,
 tall fleet great ulysses lies,
 altars guardian gods arise;
 there, sad, met brave euaemon’s son,
 large painful drops members run;
 arrow’s head yet rooted wound,
 sable blood circles mark’d ground.
 faintly reeling confess’d smart,
 weak pace, dauntless heart.
 divine compassion touch’d patroclus’ breast,
 who, sighing, thus bleeding friend address’d:
 
“ah, hapless leaders grecian host!
 thus must ye perish barbarous coast?
 fate, glut dogs gore,
 far friends, native shore?
 say, great eurypylus! shall greece yet stand?
 resists yet raging hector’s hand?
 heroes doom’d die shame,
 period wars fame?”
 
eurypylus replies: “no more, friend;
 greece more! day glories end;
 even ships victorious troy pursues,
 force increasing toil renews.
 chiefs, used utmost rage meet,
 lie pierced wounds, bleeding fleet.
 but, thou, patroclus! act friendly part,
 lead ships, draw deadly dart;
 lukewarm water wash gore away;
 healing balms raging smart allay,
 sage chiron, sire pharmacy,
 taught achilles, achilles thee.
 two famed surgeons, podalirius stands
 hour surrounded trojan bands;
 great machaon, wounded tent,
 now wants succour oft lent.”
 
chief: “what remains do?
 event things gods alone can view.
 charged achilles’ great command fly,
 bear haste pylian king’s reply:
 thy distress instant claims relief.”
 said, arms upheld chief.
 slaves master’s slow approach survey’d,
 hides oxen floor display’d:
 stretch’d length wounded hero lay;
 patroclus cut forky steel away:
 hands bitter root bruised;
 wound wash’d, styptic juice infused.
 closing flesh instant ceased glow,
 wound torture, blood flow.

book xii.
 

argument.
 

battle grecian wall.
 

greeks retired intrenchments, hector attempts to
 force them; proving impossible pass ditch, polydamas
 advises quit chariots, manage attack foot. the
 trojans follow counsel; divided army five
 bodies foot, begin assault. upon signal eagle with
 serpent talons, appeared left hand the
 trojans, polydamas endeavours withdraw again. hector
 opposes, continues attack; which, many actions,
 sarpedon makes first breach wall. hector also, casting a
 stone vast size, forces open one gates, enters the
 head troops, victoriously pursue grecians even their
 ships.
 

thus hero’s pious cares attend
 cure safety wounded friend,
 trojans greeks clashing shields engage,
 mutual deaths dealt mutual rage.
 long trench lofty walls oppose;
 gods averse ill-fated works arose;
 powers neglected, victim slain,
 walls raised, trenches sunk vain.
 
without gods, short period stands
 proudest monument mortal hands!
 stood hector achilles raged,
 sacred troy warring hosts engaged;
 sons slain, city burn’d,
 survived greece greece return’d;
 neptune apollo shook shore,
 ida’s summits pour’d watery store;
 rhesus rhodius unite rills,
 caresus roaring stony hills,
 Æsepus, granicus, mingled force,
 xanthus foaming fruitful source;
 gulfy simois, rolling main[224]
 helmets, shields, godlike heroes slain:
 these, turn’d phœbus wonted ways,
 deluged rampire nine continual days;
 weight waters saps yielding wall,
 floating bulwarks fall.
 incessant cataracts thunderer pours,
 half skies descend sluicy showers.
 god ocean, marching stern before,
 huge trident wounds trembling shore,
 vast stones piles foundation heaves,
 whelms smoky ruin waves.
 now smooth’d sand, levell’d flood,
 fragment tells wonder stood;
 old bounds rivers roll again,
 shine ’twixt hills, wander o’er plain.[225]
 
gods later times perform;
 yet bulwark stood, braved storm;
 strokes yet echoed contending powers;
 war thunder’d gates, blood distain’d towers.
 smote arm jove dire dismay,
 close hollow ships grecians lay:
 hector’s approach every wind hear,
 hector’s fury every moment fear.
 he, like whirlwind, toss’d scattering throng,
 mingled troops, drove field along.
 ’midst dogs hunters’ daring bands,
 fierce might, boar lion stands;
 arm’d foes around dreadful circle form,
 hissing javelins rain iron storm:
 powers untamed, bold assault defy,
 turns rout disperse die:
 foams, glares, bounds all,
 falls, courage makes fall.
 equal rage encompass’d hector glows;
 exhorts armies, trenches shows.
 panting steeds impatient fury breathe,
 snort tremble gulf beneath;
 just brink neigh, paw ground,
 turf trembles, skies resound.
 eager view’d prospect dark deep,
 vast leap, headlong hung steep;
 bottom bare, (a formidable show!)
 bristled thick sharpen’d stakes below.
 foot alone strong defence force,
 try pass impervious horse.
 saw polydamas; who, wisely brave,
 restrain’d great hector, counsel gave:
 
“o thou, bold leader trojan bands!
 you, confederate chiefs foreign lands!
 entrance can cumbrous chariots find,
 stakes beneath, grecian walls behind?
 pass those, without thousand wounds,
 space combat yon narrow bounds.
 proud favours mighty jove shown,
 certain dangers rashly run:
 ’tis will haughty foes tame,
 oh may instant end grecian name!
 here, far argos, let heroes fall,
 one great day destroy bury all!
 turn, oppress train,
 hopes, methods retreat remain?
 wedged trench, troops confused,
 one promiscuous carnage crush’d bruised,
 troy must perish, arms prevail,
 shall trojan live tell tale.
 hear then, ye warriors! obey speed;
 back trenches let steeds led;
 alighting, wedged firm array,
 proceed foot, hector lead way.
 greece shall stoop conquering power,
 (if jove consent) fatal hour.”
 

[illustration: ] polydamas advising hector
 

counsel pleased: godlike hector sprung
 swift seat; clanging armour rung.
 chief’s example follow’d train,
 quits car, issues plain,
 orders strict charioteers enjoin’d
 compel coursers ranks behind.
 forces part five distinguish’d bands,
 obey several chiefs’ commands.
 best bravest first conspire,
 pant fight, threat fleet fire:
 great hector glorious these,
 polydamas, brave cebriones.
 next graceful paris shines,
 bold alcathous, agenor joins.
 sons priam third appear,
 deiphobus, helenas seer;
 arms mighty asius stood,
 drew hyrtacus noble blood,
 arisba’s yellow coursers bore,
 coursers fed sellè’s winding shore.
 antenor’s sons fourth battalion guide,
 great Æneas, born fountful ide.
 divine sarpedon last band obey’d,
 glaucus asteropaeus aid.
 next him, bravest, army’s head,
 brave hosts led.
 
now compacted shields close array,
 moving legions speed headlong way:
 already hopes fire fleet,
 see grecians gasping feet.
 
every trojan thus, every aid,
 advice wise polydamas obey’d,
 asius alone, confiding car,
 vaunted coursers urged meet war.
 unhappy hero! advised vain;
 wheels returning ne’er shall mark plain;
 coursers triumphant joy
 restore master gates troy!
 black death attends behind grecian wall,
 great idomeneus shall boast thy fall!
 fierce left drives, plain
 flying grecians strove ships gain;
 swift wall horse chariots pass’d,
 gates half-open’d receive last.
 thither, exulting force, flies:
 following host clamours rend skies:
 plunge grecians headlong main,
 proud hopes; hopes vain!
 
guard gates, two mighty chiefs attend,
 lapiths’ warlike race descend;
 polypœtes, great perithous’ heir,
 leonteus, like god war.
 two tall oaks, wall rise;
 roots earth, heads amidst skies:
 whose spreading arms leafy honours crown’d,
 forbid tempest, protect ground;
 high hills appears stately form,
 deep roots ever brave storm.
 graceful these, shock stand
 raging asius, furious band.
 orestes, acamas, front appear,
 Œnomaus thoon close rear:
 vain clamours shake ambient fields,
 vain around beat hollow shields;
 fearless brothers grecians call,
 guard navies, defend wall.
 even saw troy’s sable troops impend,
 greece tumultuous towers descend,
 forth portals rush’d intrepid pair,
 opposed breasts, stood war.
 two wild boars spring furious den,
 roused cries dogs voice men;
 every side crackling trees tear,
 root shrubs, lay forest bare;
 gnash tusks, fire eye-balls roll,
 till wide wound lets mighty soul.
 around heads whistling javelins sung,
 sounding strokes brazen targets rung;
 fierce fight, yet grecian powers
 maintain’d walls, mann’d lofty towers:
 save fleet last efforts try,
 stones darts mingled tempests fly.
 
sharp boreas blows abroad, brings
 dreary winter frozen wings;
 beneath low-hung clouds sheets snow
 descend, whiten fields below:
 fast darts either army pour,
 rampires rolls rocky shower:
 heavy, thick, resound batter’d shields,
 deaf echo rattles round fields.
 
shame repulsed, grief fury driven,
 frantic asius thus accuses heaven:
 “in powers immortal shall now believe?
 can flatter, can jove deceive?
 man doubt troy’s victorious power
 humble greece, fatal hour?
 like wasps hollow crannies drive,
 guard entrance common hive,
 darkening rock, unwearied wings
 strike assailants, infix stings;
 race determined, death contend:
 fierce greeks last retreats defend.
 gods! shall two warriors guard gates,
 repel army, defraud fates?”
 
empty accents mingled wind,
 moved great jove’s unalterable mind;
 godlike hector matchless might
 owed glory destined fight.
 like deeds arms forts tried,
 gates sustain’d equal tide;
 long walls stony showers heard,
 blaze flames, flash arms appear’d.
 spirit god breast inspire,
 raise act life, sing fire!
 greece unconquer’d kept alive war,
 secure death, confiding despair;
 guardian gods, deep dismay,
 unassisting arms deplored day.
 
even yet dauntless lapithae maintain
 dreadful pass, round heap slain.
 first damasus, polypœtes’ steel,
 pierced helmet’s brazen visor, fell;
 weapon drank mingled brains gore!
 warrior sinks, tremendous now more!
 next ormenus pylon yield breath:
 less leonteus strews field death;
 first belt hippomachus gored,
 sudden waved unresisted sword:
 antiphates, ranks broke,
 falchion struck, fate pursued stroke:
 iamenus, orestes, menon, bled;
 round rose monument dead.
 meantime, bravest trojan crew,
 bold hector polydamas, pursue;
 fierce impatience works fall,
 wrap rolling flames fleet wall.
 farther bank now stood gazed,
 heaven alarm’d, prodigies amazed:
 signal omen stopp’d passing host,
 martial fury wonder lost.
 jove’s bird sounding pinions beat skies;
 bleeding serpent enormous size,
 talons truss’d; alive, curling round,
 stung bird, whose throat received wound:
 mad smart, drops fatal prey,
 airy circles wings painful way,
 floats winds, rends heaven cries:
 amidst host fallen serpent lies.
 they, pale terror, mark spires unroll’d,
 jove’s portent beating hearts behold.
 first polydamas silence broke,
 long weigh’d signal, hector spoke:
 
“how oft, brother, thy reproach bear,
 words well meant, sentiments sincere?
 true counsels judge best,
 tell faithful dictates breast.
 speak thoughts every freeman’s right,
 peace, war, council, fight;
 move, deferring thy sway,
 tends raise power obey.
 hear words, may words vain!
 seek day grecian ships gain;
 sure, warn us, jove omen sent,
 thus mind explains clear event:
 victor eagle, whose sinister flight
 retards host, fills hearts fright,
 dismiss’d conquest middle skies,
 allow’d seize, possess prize;
 thus, though gird fires grecian fleet,
 though proud bulwalks tumble feet,
 toils unforeseen, fiercer, decreed;
 woes shall follow, heroes bleed.
 bodes soul, bids thus advise;
 thus skilful seer read skies.”
 
hector disdain return’d:
 (fierce spoke, eyes fury burn’d:)
 “are faithful counsels thy tongue?
 thy will partial, thy reason wrong:
 purpose thy heart thou vent,
 sure heaven resumes little sense lent.
 coward counsels thy madness move
 word, will reveal’d jove?
 leading sign, irrevocable nod,
 happy thunders favouring god,
 shall slight, guide wavering mind
 wandering birds flit every wind?
 ye vagrants sky! wings extend,
 suns arise, descend;
 right, left, unheeded take way,
 dictates high heaven obey.
 without sign sword brave man draws,
 asks omen country’s cause.
 should’st thou suspect war’s success?
 none fears more, none promotes less:
 though chiefs amidst yon ships expire,
 trust thy cowardice escape fire.
 troy sons may find general grave,
 thou canst live, thou canst slave.
 yet fears wary mind suggests
 spread cold poison soldiers’ breasts,
 javelin can revenge base part,
 free soul quivers thy heart.”
 
furious spoke, and, rushing wall,
 calls host; host obey call;
 ardour follow leader flies:
 redoubling clamours thunder skies.
 jove breathes whirlwind hills ide,
 drifts dust clouded navy hide;
 fills greeks terror dismay,
 gives great hector predestined day.
 strong themselves, stronger aid,
 close works rigid siege laid.
 vain mounds massy beams defend,
 undermine, rend;
 upheaved piles prop solid wall;
 heaps heaps smoky ruins fall.
 greece ramparts stands fierce alarms;
 crowded bulwarks blaze waving arms,
 shield touching shield, long refulgent row;
 whence hissing darts, incessant, rain below.
 bold ajaces fly tower tower,
 rouse, flame divine, grecian power.
 generous impulse every greek obeys;
 threats urge fearful; valiant, praise.
 
“fellows arms! whose deeds known fame,
 you, whose ardour hopes equal name!
 since alike endued force art;
 behold day may act part!
 day fire brave, warm cold,
 gain new glories, augment old.
 urge stand, faint, excite;
 drown hector’s vaunts loud exhorts fight;
 conquest, safety, fill thoughts all;
 seek fleet, sally wall;
 jove may drive routed train,
 troy lie trembling walls again.”
 
ardour kindles grecian powers;
 now stones descend heavier showers.
 high jove sharp artillery forms,
 opes cloudy magazine storms;
 winter’s bleak uncomfortable reign,
 snowy inundation hides plain;
 stills winds, bids skies sleep;
 pours silent tempest thick deep;
 first mountain-tops cover’d o’er,
 green fields, sandy shore;
 bent weight, nodding woods seen,
 one bright waste hides works men:
 circling seas, alone absorbing all,
 drink dissolving fleeces fall:
 side increased stony rain,
 white ruin rises o’er plain.
 
thus godlike hector troops contend
 force ramparts, gates rend:
 troy conquer, greeks yield,
 till great sarpedon tower’d amid field;
 mighty jove inspired martial flame
 matchless son, urged fame.
 arms shines, conspicuous afar,
 bears aloft ample shield air;
 within whose orb thick bull-hides roll’d,
 ponderous brass, bound ductile gold:
 two pointed javelins arm hands,
 majestic moves along, leads lycian bands.
 
press’d hunger, mountain’s brow
 descends lion flocks below;
 stalks lordly savage o’er plain,
 sullen majesty, stern disdain:
 vain loud mastiffs bay afar,
 shepherds gall iron war;
 regardless, furious, pursues way;
 foams, roars, rends panting prey.
 
resolved alike, divine sarpedon glows
 generous rage drives foes.
 views towers, meditates fall,
 sure destruction dooms aspiring wall;
 casting friend ardent look,
 fired thirst glory, thus spoke:
 
“why boast we, glaucus! extended reign,[226]
 xanthus’ streams enrich lycian plain,
 numerous herds range fruitful field,
 hills vines purple harvest yield,
 foaming bowls purer nectar crown’d,
 feasts enhanced music’s sprightly sound?
 shores joy survey’d,
 admired heroes, gods obey’d,
 unless great acts superior merit prove,
 vindicate bounteous powers above?
 ’tis ours, dignity give grace;
 first valour, first place;
 wondering eyes martial bands
 behold deeds transcending commands,
 such, may cry, deserve sovereign state,
 envy dare imitate!
 care elude gloomy grave,
 claims less fearful brave,
 lust fame vainly dare
 fighting fields, urge thy soul war.
 since, alas! ignoble age must come,
 disease, death’s inexorable doom,
 life, others pay, let us bestow,
 give fame nature owe;
 brave though fall, honour’d live,
 let us glory gain, glory give!”
 
said; words listening chief inspire
 equal warmth, rouse warrior’s fire;
 troops pursue leaders delight,
 rush foe, claim promised fight.
 menestheus high storm beheld
 threatening fort, blackening field:
 around walls gazed, view far
 aid appear’d avert approaching war,
 saw teucer ajaces stood,
 fight insatiate, prodigal blood.
 vain calls; din helms shields
 rings skies, echoes fields,
 brazen hinges fly, walls resound,
 heaven trembles, roar mountains, thunders ground.
 thus thoos: “hence speed (he said),
 urge bold ajaces aid;
 strength, united, best may help bear
 bloody labours doubtful war:
 hither lycian princes bend course,
 best bravest hostile force.
 fiercely foes contend,
 let telamon, least, towers defend,
 teucer haste unerring bow
 share danger, repel foe.”
 
swift, word, herald speeds along
 lofty ramparts, martial throng,
 finds heroes bathed sweat gore,
 opposed combat dusty shore.
 “ye valiant leaders warlike bands!
 aid (said thoos) peteus’ demands;
 strength, united, best may help bear
 bloody labours doubtful war:
 thither lycian princes bend course,
 best bravest hostile force.
 fiercely, here, foes contend,
 least, let telamon towers defend,
 teucer haste unerring bow
 share danger, repel foe.”
 
straight fort great ajax turn’d care,
 thus bespoke brothers war:
 “now, valiant lycomede! exert might,
 and, brave oïleus, prove force fight;
 trust fortune field,
 till arm foe shall repell’d:
 done, expect complete day.
 sevenfold shield strode away.”
 equal steps bold teucer press’d shore,
 whose fatal bow strong pandion bore.
 
high walls appear’d lycian powers,
 like black tempest gathering round towers:
 greeks, oppress’d, utmost force unite,
 prepared labour unequal fight:
 war renews, mix’d shouts groans arise;
 tumultuous clamour mounts, thickens skies.
 fierce ajax first advancing host invades,
 sends brave epicles shades,
 sarpedon’s friend. across warrior’s way,
 rent walls, rocky fragment lay;
 modern ages strongest swain
 heave unwieldy burden plain:
 poised, swung round; toss’d high,

 skilful divers airy steep
 headlong descend, shoot deep,
