 murmuring shades soul retires.
 
ramparts daring glaucus drew,
 teucer’s hand winged arrow flew;
 bearded shaft destined passage found,
 naked arm inflicts wound.
 chief, fear’d foe’s insulting boast
 might stop progress warlike host,
 conceal’d wound, and, leaping height
 retired reluctant unfinish’d fight.
 divine sarpedon regret beheld
 disabled glaucus slowly quit field;
 beating breast generous ardour glows,
 springs fight, flies upon foes.
 alcmaon first doom’d force feel;
 deep breast plunged pointed steel;
 yawning wound fury tore
 spear, pursued gushing streams gore:
 sinks warrior thundering sound,
 brazen armour rings ground.
 
swift battlement victor flies,
 tugs full force, every nerve applies:
 shakes; ponderous stones disjointed yield;
 rolling ruins smoke along field.
 mighty breach appears; walls lie bare;
 and, like deluge, rushes war.
 bold teucer draws twanging bow,
 ajax sends javelin foe;
 fix’d belt feather’d weapon stood,
 buckler drove trembling wood;
 jove present dire debate,
 shield offspring, avert fate.
 prince gave back, meditating flight,
 urging vengeance, severer fight;
 raised hope, fired glory’s charms,
 fainting squadrons new fury warms.
 “o where, ye lycians, strength boast?
 former fame ancient virtue lost!
 breach lies open, chief vain
 attempts alone guarded pass gain:
 unite, soon hostile fleet shall fall:
 force powerful union conquers all.”
 
just rebuke inflamed lycian crew;
 join, thicken, assault renew:
 unmoved embodied greeks fury dare,
 fix’d support weight war;
 greeks repel lycian powers,
 bold lycians force grecian towers.
 confines adjoining grounds,
 two stubborn swains blows dispute bounds;
 tug, sweat; neither gain, yield,
 one foot, one inch, contended field;
 thus obstinate death, fight, fall;
 can keep, can win wall.
 manly breasts pierced many wound,
 loud strokes heard, rattling arms resound;
 copious slaughter covers shore,
 high ramparts drip human gore.
 
two scales charged doubtful loads,
 side side trembling balance nods,
 (while laborious matron, just poor,
 nice exactness weighs woolly store,)
 till poised aloft, resting beam suspends
 equal weight; this, that, descends:[227]
 stood war, till hector’s matchless might,
 fates prevailing, turn’d scale fight.
 fierce whirlwind walls flies,
 fires host loud repeated cries.
 “advance, ye trojans! lend valiant hands,
 haste fleet, toss blazing brands!”
 hear, run; and, gathering call,
 raise scaling engines, ascend wall:
 around works wood glittering spears
 shoots up, rising host appears.
 ponderous stone bold hector heaved throw,
 pointed above, rough gross below:
 two strong men enormous weight raise,
 men live degenerate days:
 yet this, easy swain bear
 snowy fleece, toss’d, shook air;
 jove upheld, lighten’d load
 unwieldy rock, labour god.
 thus arm’d, folded gates came,
 massy substance, stupendous frame;
 iron bars brazen hinges strong,
 lofty beams solid timber hung:
 thundering planks forceful sway,
 drives sharp rock; solid beams give way,
 folds shatter’d; crackling door
 leap resounding bars, flying hinges roar.
 now rushing in, furious chief appears,
 gloomy night![228] shakes two shining spears:
 dreadful gleam bright armour came,
 eye-balls flash’d living flame.
 moves god, resistless course,
 seems match mortal force.
 pouring after, gaping space,
 tide trojans flows, fills place;
 greeks behold, tremble, fly;
 shore heap’d death, tumult rends sky.
 

[illustration: ] greek altar
 



book xiii.
 

argument.
 

fourth battle continued, neptune assists greeks: the
 acts idomeneus.
 

neptune, concerned loss grecians, upon seeing the
 fortification forced hector, (who entered gate near the
 station ajaces,) assumes shape calchas, inspires
 heroes oppose him: then, form one generals,
 encourages greeks retired vessels. the
 ajaces form troops close phalanx, put stop hector
 trojans. several deeds valour performed; meriones,
 losing spear encounter, repairs seek another tent
 idomeneus: occasions conversation two warriors,
 return together battle. idomeneus signalizes courage
 rest; kills othryoneus, asius, alcathous: deiphobus
 Æneas march him, length idomeneus retires. menelaus
 wounds helenus, kills pisander. trojans repulsed the
 left wing; hector still keeps ground ajaces, till,
 galled locrian slingers archers, polydamas advises to
 call council war: hector approves advice, goes first to
 rally trojans; upbraids paris, rejoins polydamas, meets ajax again,
 renews attack.
 eight-and-twentieth day still continues. scene between
 grecian wall sea-shore.
 

now thunderer sea-beat coast
 fix’d great hector conquering host,
 left fates, bloody fray
 toil struggle well-fought day.
 turn’d thracia field fight
 eyes shed insufferable light,
 mysians prove martial force,
 hardy thracians tame savage horse;
 far-famed hippomolgian strays,
 renown’d justice length days;[229]
 thrice happy race! that, innocent blood,
 milk, innoxious, seek simple food:
 jove sees delighted; avoids scene
 guilty troy, arms, dying men:
 aid, deems, either host given,
 high law suspends powers heaven.
 
meantime monarch watery main
 observed thunderer, observed vain.
 samothracia, mountain’s brow,
 whose waving woods o’erhung deeps below,
 sat; round cast azure eyes
 ida’s misty tops confusedly rise;
 below, fair ilion’s glittering spires seen;
 crowded ships sable seas between.
 there, crystal chambers main
 emerged, sat, mourn’d argives slain.
 jove incensed, grief fury stung,
 prone rocky steep rush’d along;
 fierce pass’d, lofty mountains nod,
 forest shakes; earth trembled trod,
 felt footsteps immortal god.
 realm realm three ample strides took,
 and, fourth, distant Ægae shook.
 
far bay shining palace stands,
 eternal frame! raised mortal hands:
 reach’d, brass-hoof’d steeds reins,
 fleet winds, deck’d golden manes.
 refulgent arms mighty limbs infold,
 immortal arms adamant gold.
 mounts car, golden scourge applies,
 sits superior, chariot flies:
 whirling wheels glassy surface sweep;
 enormous monsters rolling o’er deep
 gambol around watery way,
 heavy whales awkward measures play;
 subsiding spreads level plain,
 exults, owns monarch main;
 parting waves coursers fly;
 wondering waters leave axle dry.
 
deep liquid regions lies cave,
 tenedos surges lave,
 rocky imbrus breaks rolling wave:
 great ruler azure round
 stopp’d swift chariot, steeds unbound,
 fed ambrosial herbage hand,
 link’d fetlocks golden band,
 infrangible, immortal: stay:
 father floods pursues way:
 where, like tempest, darkening heaven around,
 fiery deluge devours ground,
 impatient trojans, gloomy throng,
 embattled roll’d, hector rush’d along:
 loud tumult barbarous cry
 heavens re-echo, shores reply:
 vow destruction grecian name,
 hopes fleets already flame.
 
neptune, rising seas profound,
 god whose earthquakes rock solid ground,
 now wears mortal form; like calchas seen,
 loud voice, manly mien;
 shouts incessant every greek inspire,
 ajaces, adding fire fire.
 

[illustration: ] neptune rising sea
 

“’tis yours, warriors, hopes raise:
 oh recollect ancient worth praise!
 ’tis save us, cease fear;
 flight, shameful, destructive here.
 works though troy fury fall,
 pour armies o’er batter’d wall:
 greece strength: this, part o’erthrown,
 strength vain; dread alone:
 hector rages like force fire,
 vaunts gods, calls high jove sire:
 yet heavenly power breast excite,
 breathe hearts, string arms fight,
 greece yet may live, threaten’d fleet maintain:
 hector’s force, jove’s aid, vain.”
 
sceptre, deep controls,
 touch’d chiefs, steel’d manly souls:
 strength, own, touch divine imparts,
 prompts light limbs, swells daring hearts.
 then, falcon rocky height,
 quarry seen, impetuous sight,
 forth-springing instant, darts high,
 shoots wing, skims along sky:
 such, swift, power ocean flew;
 wide horizon shut view.
 
inspiring god oïleus’ active son
 perceived first, thus telamon:
 
“some god, friend, god human form
 favouring descends, wills stand storm.
 calchas this, venerable seer;
 short turned, saw power appear:
 mark’d parting, steps trod;
 bright evidence reveals god.
 even now energy divine share,
 seem walk wings, tread air!”
 
“with equal ardour (telamon returns)
 soul kindled, bosom burns;
 new rising spirits force alarm,
 lift impatient limb, brace arm.
 ready arm, unthinking, shakes dart;
 blood pours back, fortifies heart:
 singly, methinks, yon towering chief meet,
 stretch dreadful hector feet.”
 
full god urged burning breast,
 heroes thus mutual warmth express’d.
 neptune meanwhile routed greeks inspired;
 who, breathless, pale, length labours tired,
 pant ships; troy conquest calls,
 swarms victorious o’er yielding walls:
 trembling impending storm lie,
 tears rage stand burning eye.
 greece sunk thought, fatal hour;
 breathe new courage feel power.
 teucer leitus first words excite;
 stern peneleus rises fight;
 thoas, deipyrus, arms renown’d,
 merion next, impulsive fury found;
 last nestor’s bold ardour takes,
 thus god martial fire awakes:
 
“oh lasting infamy, oh dire disgrace
 chiefs vigorous youth, manly race!
 trusted gods, you, see
 brave greece victorious, navy free:
 ah, no—the glorious combat disclaim,
 one black day clouds former fame.
 heavens! prodigy eyes survey,
 unseen, unthought, till amazing day!
 fly length troy’s oft-conquer’d bands?
 falls fleet inglorious hands?
 rout undisciplined, straggling train,
 born glories dusty plain;
 like frighted fawns hill hill pursued,
 prey every savage wood:
 shall these, late trembled name,
 invade camps, involve ships flame?
 change shameful, say, cause wrought?
 soldiers’ baseness, general’s fault?
 fools! will ye perish leader’s vice;
 purchase infamy, life price?
 ’tis cause, achilles’ injured fame:
 another’s crime, shame.
 grant chief offend rage lust,
 must cowards, king’s unjust?
 prevent evil, country save:
 small thought retrieves spirits brave.
 think, subdue! dastards dead fame
 waste anger, feel shame:
 you, pride, flower host,
 heart weeps blood see glory lost!
 deem day, battle, lose;
 day black, fate vile, ensues.
 let reflect, prizes fame breath,
 endless infamy, instant death:
 for, lo! fated time, appointed shore:
 hark! gates burst, brazen barriers roar!
 impetuous hector thunders wall;
 hour, spot, conquer, fall.”
 
words grecians’ fainting hearts inspire,
 listening armies catch godlike fire.
 fix’d post bold ajax found,
 well-ranged squadrons strongly circled round:
 close order, disposed fight,
 pallas’ self might view fix’d delight;
 god war inclined eyes,
 god war own’d just surprise.
 chosen phalanx, firm, resolved fate,
 descending hector battle wait.
 iron scene gleams dreadful o’er fields,
 armour armour lock’d, shields shields,
 spears lean spears, targets targets throng,
 helms stuck helms, man drove man along.
 floating plumes unnumber’d wave above,
 earthquake stirs nodding grove;
 levell’d skies pointing rays,
 brandish’d lances motion blaze.
 
thus breathing death, terrible array,
 close compacted legions urged way:
 fierce drove on, impatient destroy;
 troy charged first, hector first troy.
 mountain’s craggy forehead torn,
 rock’s round fragment flies, fury borne,
 (which stubborn stone torrent rends,)
 precipitate ponderous mass descends:
 steep steep rolling ruin bounds;
 every shock crackling wood resounds;
 still gathering force, smokes; urged amain,
 whirls, leaps, thunders down, impetuous plain:
 stops—so hector. whole force proved,[230]
 resistless raged, and, stopp’d, unmoved.
 
war bent, darts shed,
 falchions wave around head:
 repulsed stands, stand retires;
 repeated shouts army fires.
 “trojans! firm; arm shall make way
 yon square body, black array:
 stand, spear shall rout scattering power,
 strong seem, embattled like tower;
 juno’s heavenly bosom warms,
 first gods, day inspires arms.”
 
said; roused soul every breast:
 urged desire fame, beyond rest,
 forth march’d deiphobus; but, marching, held
 wary steps ample shield.
 bold merion aim’d stroke (nor aim’d wide);
 glittering javelin pierced tough bull-hide;
 pierced through: unfaithful hand,
 point broke short, sparkled sand.
 trojan warrior, touch’d timely fear,
 raised orb distance bore spear.
 greek, retreating, mourn’d frustrate blow,
 cursed treacherous lance spared foe;
 ships surly speed went,
 seek surer javelin tent.
 
meanwhile rising rage battle glows,
 tumult thickens, clamour grows.
 teucer’s arm warlike imbrius bleeds,
 mentor, rich generous steeds.
 ere yet troy sons greece led,
 fair pedaeus’ verdant pastures bred,
 youth dwelt, remote war’s alarms,
 blest bright medesicaste’s arms:
 (this nymph, fruit priam’s ravish’d joy,
 allied warrior house troy:)
 troy, glory call’d arms, came,
 match’d bravest chiefs fame:
 priam’s sons, guardian throne,
 lived, beloved honour’d own.
 teucer pierced throat ear:
 groans beneath telamonian spear.
 far-seen mountain’s airy crown,
 subdued steel, tall ash tumbles down,
 soils verdant tresses ground;
 falls youth; arms fall resound.
 teucer rushing despoil dead,
 hector’s hand shining javelin fled:
 saw, shunn’d death; forceful dart
 sung on, pierced amphimachus’s heart,
 cteatus’ son, neptune’s forceful line;
 vain courage, race divine!
 prostrate falls; clanging arms resound,
 broad buckler thunders ground.
 seize beamy helm victor flies,
 just fastened dazzling prize,
 ajax’ manly arm javelin flung;
 full shield’s round boss weapon rung;
 felt shock, doom’d feel,
 secure mail, sheath’d shining steel.
 repulsed yields; victor greeks obtain
 spoils contested, bear slain.
 leaders athenian line,
 (stichius brave, menestheus divine,)
 deplored amphimachus, sad object! lies;
 imbrius remains fierce ajaces’ prize.
 two grim lions bear across lawn,
 snatch’d devouring hounds, slaughter’d fawn.
 fell jaws high-lifting wood,
 sprinkling shrubs drops blood;
 these, chief: great ajax dead
 strips bright arms; oïleus lops head:
 toss’d like ball, whirl’d air away,
 hector’s feet gory visage lay.
 
god ocean, fired stern disdain,
 pierced sorrow grandson slain,
 inspires grecian hearts, confirms hands,
 breathes destruction trojan bands.
 swift whirlwind rushing fleet,
 finds lance-famed idomen crete,
 pensive brow generous care express’d
 wounded soldier touch’d breast,
 chance war javelin tore,
 sad comrades battle bore;
 surgeons camp sent:
 office paid, issued tent
 fierce fight: god begun,
 thoas’ voice, andræmon’s valiant son,
 ruled calydon’s white rocks arise,
 pleuron’s chalky cliffs emblaze skies:
 
“where’s now imperious vaunt, daring boast,
 greece victorious, proud ilion lost?”
 
king: “on greece blame thrown;
 arms trade, war own.
 hardy heroes well-fought plains
 fear withholds, shameful sloth detains:
 ’tis heaven, alas! jove’s all-powerful doom,
 far, far distant native home
 wills us fall inglorious! oh, friend!
 foremost fight, still prone lend
 arms counsels, now perform thy best,
 thou canst singly, urge rest.”
 
thus he: thus god whose force can make
 solid globe’s eternal basis shake:
 “ah! never may see native land,
 feed vultures hateful strand,
 seeks ignobly ships stay,
 dares combat signal day!
 this, behold! horrid arms shine,
 urge thy soul rival acts mine.
 together let us battle plain;
 two, worst; even succour vain:
 vain weakest, force unite;
 ours, bravest confess’d fight.”
 
said, rushes combat burns;
 swift tent cretan king returns:
 thence, two javelins glittering hand,
 clad arms lighten’d strand,
 fierce foe impetuous hero drove,
 like lightning bursting arm jove,
 pale man wrath heaven declares,
 terrifies offending world wars;
 streamy sparkles, kindling skies,
 pole pole trail glory flies:
 thus bright armour o’er dazzled throng
 gleam’d dreadful, monarch flash’d along.
 
him, near tent, meriones attends;
 thus questions: “ever best friends!
 say, every art battle skill’d,
 holds thy courage brave field?
 important message art thou bound,
 bleeds friend unhappy wound?
 inglorious here, soul abhors stay,
 glows prospects th’ approaching day.”
 
“o prince! (meriones replies) whose care
 leads forth embattled sons crete war;
 speaks grief: headless lance wield;
 rest lies rooted trojan shield.”
 
cretan: “enter, receive
 wonted weapons; tent can give;
 spears store, (and trojan lances all,)
 shed lustre round illumined wall,
 though i, disdainful distant war,
 trust dart, aim uncertain spear,
 yet hand hand fight, spoil slain;
 thence trophies, arms gain.
 enter, see heaps helmets roll’d,
 high-hung spears, shields flame gold.”
 
“nor vain (said merion) martial toils;
 can boast ignoble spoils:
 ship contains; whence distant far,
 fight conspicuous war,
 need more? greek be
 knows merion, appeal thee.”
 
this, idomeneus: “the fields fight
 proved thy valour, unconquer’d might:
 ambush foes design’d,
 even thy courage lag behind:
 sharp service, singled rest,
 fear each, valour, stands confess’d.
 force, firmness, pale coward shows;
 shifts place: colour comes goes:
 dropping sweat creeps cold every part;
 bosom beats quivering heart;
 terror death wild eye-balls stare;
 chattering teeth stands, stiffening hair,
 looks bloodless image despair!
 brave—still dauntless, still same,
 unchanged colour, unmoved frame:
 composed thought, determined eye,
 fix’d soul, conquer die:
 aught disturb tenour breast,
 ’tis wish strike rest.
 
“in assays thy blameless worth known,
 every art dangerous war thy own.
 chance fight whatever wounds bore,
 wounds glorious all, before;
 may teach, ’twas still thy brave delight
 t’oppose thy bosom thy foremost fight.
 why, like infants, cold honour’s charms,
 stand talk, glory calls arms?
 go—from conquer’d spears choicest take,
 owners send nobly back.”
 
swift word bold merion snatch’d spear
 and, breathing slaughter, follow’d war.
 mars armipotent invades plain,
 (the wide destroyer race man,)
 terror, best-beloved son, attends course,
 arm’d stern boldness, enormous force;
 pride haughty warriors confound,
 lay strength tyrants ground:
 thrace fly, call’d dire alarms
 warring phlegyans, ephyrian arms;
 invoked both, relentless dispose,
 glad conquest, murderous rout those.
 march’d leaders cretan train,
 bright arms shot horror o’er plain.
 
first spake merion: “shall join right,
 combat centre fight?
 left wonted succour lend?
 hazard fame parts alike attend.”
 
“not centre (idomen replied:)
 ablest chieftains main battle guide;
 godlike ajax makes post care,
 gallant teucer deals destruction there,
 skill’d shafts gall distant field,
 bear close battle sounding shield.
 can rage haughty hector tame:
 safe arms, navy fears flame,
 till jove descends, bolts shed,
 hurl blazing ruin head.
 great must be, human birth,
 feed like mortals fruits earth.
 neither rocks can crush, steel can wound,
 ajax fells ensanguined ground.
 standing fight mates achilles’ force,
 excell’d alone swiftness course.
 left ready arms apply,
 live glory, glory die.”
 
said: merion th’ appointed place,
 fierce god battles, urged pace.
 soon foe shining chiefs beheld
 rush like fiery torrent o’er field,
 force embodied tide pour;
 rising combat sounds along shore.
 warring winds, sirius’ sultry reign,
 different quarters sweep sandy plain;
 every side dusty whirlwinds rise,
 dry fields lifted skies:
 thus despair, hope, rage, together driven,
 met black hosts, and, meeting, darken’d heaven.
 dreadful glared iron face war,
 bristled upright spears, flash’d afar;
 dire gleam breastplates, helms, shields,
 polish’d arms emblazed flaming fields:
 tremendous scene! general horror gave,
 touch’d joy bosoms brave.
 
saturn’s great sons fierce contention vied,
 crowds heroes anger died.
 sire earth heaven, thetis won
 crown glory peleus’ godlike son,
 will’d destruction grecian powers,
 spared awhile destined trojan towers;
 neptune, rising azure main,
 warr’d king heaven stern disdain,
 breathed revenge, fired grecian train.
 gods one source, one ethereal race,
 alike divine, heaven native place;
 jove greater; first-born skies,
 men, gods, supremely wise.
 this, jove’s superior might afraid,
 neptune human form conceal’d aid.
 powers enfold greek trojan train
 war discord’s adamantine chain,
 indissolubly strong: fatal tie
 stretch’d both, close compell’d die.
 
dreadful arms, grown combats grey,
 bold idomeneus controls day.
 first hand othryoneus slain,
 swell’d false hopes, mad ambition vain;
 call’d voice war martial fame,
 high cabesus’ distant walls came;
 cassandra’s love sought, boasts power,
 promised conquest proffer’d dower.
 king consented, vaunts abused;
 king consented, fates refused.
 proud himself, imagined bride,
 field measured larger stride.
 stalk’d, cretan javelin found;
 vain breastplate repel wound:
 dream glory lost, plunged hell;
 arms resounded boaster fell.
 great idomeneus bestrides dead;
 “and thus (he cries) behold thy promise sped!
 help thy arms ilion bring,
 contract phrygian king!
 offers now, illustrious prince! receive;
 aid will argos give?
 conquer troy, thy forces join,
 count atrides’ fairest daughter thine.
 meantime, methods advise,
 come, follow fleet thy new allies;
 hear greece part say.”
 spoke, dragg’d gory corse away.
 asius view’d, unable contain,
 chariot warring plain:
 (his crowded coursers, squire consign’d,
 impatient panted neck behind:)
 vengeance rising sudden spring,
 hoped conquest cretan king.
 wary cretan, foe drew near,
 full throat discharged forceful spear:
 beneath chin point seen glide,
 glitter’d, extant side.
 mountain-oak, poplar tall,
 pine, fit mast great admiral,
 groans oft-heaved axe, many wound,
 spreads length ruin o’er ground:
 sunk proud asius dreadful day,
 stretch’d much-loved coursers lay.
 grinds dust distain’d streaming gore,
 and, fierce death, lies foaming shore.
 deprived motion, stiff stupid fear,
 stands aghast trembling charioteer,
 shuns foe, turns steeds away,
 falls transfix’d, unresisting prey:
 pierced antilochus, pants beneath
 stately car, labours breath.
 thus asius’ steeds (their mighty master gone)
 remain prize nestor’s youthful son.
 
stabb’d sight, deiphobus drew nigh,
 made, force, vengeful weapon fly.
 cretan saw; and, stooping, caused glance
 slope shield disappointed lance.
 beneath spacious targe, (a blazing round,
 thick bull-hides brazen orbits bound,
 raised arm two strong braces stay’d,)
 lay collected defensive shade.
 o’er safe head javelin idly sung,
 tinkling verge faintly rung.
 even spear vigorous arm confess’d,
 pierced, obliquely, king hypsenor’s breast:
 warm’d liver, ground bore
 chief, people’s guardian now more!
 
“not unattended (the proud trojan cries)
 unrevenged, lamented asius lies:
 thee, hell’s black portals stand display’d,
 mate shall joy thy melancholy shade.”
 
heart-piercing anguish, haughty boast,
 touch’d every greek, nestor’s most.
 grieved was, pious arms attend,
 broad buckler shields slaughter’d friend:
 till sad mecistheus alastor bore
 honour’d body tented shore.
 
yet fight idomeneus withdraws;
 resolved perish country’s cause,
 find foe, heaven shall doom
 wail fate death’s eternal gloom.
 sees alcathous front aspire:
 great Æsyetes hero’s sire;
 spouse hippodame, divinely fair,
 anchises’ eldest hope, darling care:
 charm’d parents’ husband’s heart
 beauty, sense, every work art:
 ilion’s youth loveliest boy,
 fairest fair troy.
 neptune now hapless hero dies,
 covers cloud beauteous eyes,
 fetters every limb: yet bent meet
 fate stands; shuns lance crete.
 fix’d column, deep-rooted oak,
 winds sleep; breast received stroke.
 ponderous stroke corslet yields,
 long used ward death fighting fields.
 riven armour sends jarring sound;
 labouring heart heaves strong bound,
 long lance shakes, vibrates wound;
 fast flowing source, prone lay,
 life’s purple tide impetuous gush’d away.
 
idomen, insulting o’er slain:
 “behold, deiphobus! vaunt vain:
 see! one greek three trojan ghosts attend;
 this, third victim, shades send.
 approaching now thy boasted might approve,
 try prowess seed jove.
 jove, enamour’d mortal dame,
 great minos, guardian country, came:
 deucalion, blameless prince, minos’ heir;
 first-born i, third jupiter:
 o’er spacious crete, bold sons, reign,
 thence ships transport main:
 lord host, o’er host shine,
 scourge thee, thy father, thy line.”
 
trojan heard; uncertain meet,
 alone, venturous arms king crete,
 seek auxiliar force; length decreed
 call hero partake deed,
 forthwith Æneas rises thought:
 troy’s remotest lines sought,
 he, incensed partial priam, stands,
 sees superior posts meaner hands.
 him, ambitious great aid,
 bold deiphobus approach’d, said:
 
“now, trojan prince, employ thy pious arms,
 e’er thy bosom felt fair honour’s charms.
 alcathous dies, thy brother thy friend;
 come, warrior’s loved remains defend.
 beneath cares thy early youth train’d,
 one table fed you, one roof contain’d.
 deed fierce idomeneus owe;
 haste, revenge th’ insulting foe.”
 
Æneas heard, space resign’d
 tender pity manly mind;
 rising rage, burns fight:
 greek awaits collected might.
 fell boar, rough mountain’s head,
 arm’d wild terrors, slaughter bred,
 loud rustics rise, shout far,
 attends tumult, expects war;
 o’er bent back bristly horrors rise;
 fires stream lightning sanguine eyes,
 foaming tusks dogs men engage;
 hunters rouse mighty rage:
 stood idomeneus, javelin shook,
 met trojan lowering look.
 antilochus, deipyrus, near,
 youthful offspring god war,
 merion, aphareus, field renown’d:
 warrior sent voice around.
 “fellows arms! timely aid unite;
 lo, great Æneas rushes fight:
 sprung god, mortal bold;
 fresh youth, arms grown old.
 else hand, hour decide strife,
 great dispute, glory, life.”
 
spoke, all, one soul, obey’d;
 lifted bucklers cast dreadful shade
 around chief. Æneas demands
 th’ assisting forces native bands;
 paris, deiphobus, agenor, join;
 (co-aids captains trojan line;)
 order follow th’ embodied train,
 like ida’s flocks proceeding o’er plain;
 fleecy care, erect bold,
 stalks proud ram, father bold.
 joy swain surveys them, leads
 cool fountains, well-known meads:
 joys Æneas, native band
 moves rank, stretches o’er land.
 
round dread alcathous now battle rose;
 every side steely circle grows;
 now batter’d breast-plates hack’d helmets ring,
 o’er heads unheeded javelins sing.
 rest, two towering chiefs appear,
 great idomeneus, Æneas here.
 like gods war, dispensing fate, stood,
 burn’d drench ground mutual blood.
 trojan weapon whizz’d along air;
 cretan saw, shunn’d brazen spear:
 sent arm strong, missive wood
 stuck deep earth, quiver’d stood.
 oenomas received cretan’s stroke;
 forceful spear hollow corslet broke,
 ripp’d belly ghastly wound,
 roll’d smoking entrails ground.
 stretch’d plain, sobs away breath,
 and, furious, grasps bloody dust death.
 victor breast weapon tears;
 spoils not, shower spears.
 though now unfit active war wage,
 heavy cumbrous arms, stiff cold age,
 listless limbs unable course,
 standing fight yet maintains force;
 till faint labour, foes repell’d,
 tired slow steps drags field.
 deiphobus beheld pass’d,
 and, fired hate, parting javelin cast:
 javelin err’d, held course along,
 pierced ascalaphus, brave young:
 mars fell gasping ground,
 gnash’d dust, bloody wound.
 
knew furious father fall;
 high-throned amidst great olympian hall,
 golden clouds th’ immortal synod sate;
 detain’d bloody war jove fate.
 
now, dust breathless hero lay,
 slain ascalaphus commenced fray,
 deiphobus seize helmet flies,
 temples rends glittering prize;
 valiant mars, meriones drew near,
 loaded arm discharged spear:
 drops weight, disabled pain;
 hollow helmet rings plain.
 swift vulture leaping prey,
 torn arm grecian rent away
 reeking javelin, rejoin’d friends.
 wounded brother good polites tends;
 around waist pious arms threw,
 rage battle gently drew:
 swift coursers, splendid car,
 rapt lessening thunder war;
 troy drove him, groaning shore,
 sprinkling, pass’d, sands gore.
 
meanwhile fresh slaughter bathes sanguine ground,
 heaps fall heaps, heaven earth resound.
 bold aphareus great Æneas bled;
 toward chief turn’d daring head,
 pierced throat; bending head, depress’d
 beneath helmet, nods upon breast;
 shield reversed o’er fallen warrior lies,
 everlasting slumber seals eyes.
 antilochus, thoon turn’d round,
 transpierced back dishonest wound:
 hollow vein, neck extends
 along chine, eager javelin rends:
 supine falls, social train
 spreads imploring arms, spreads vain.
 thv exulting victor, leaping lay,
 broad shoulders tore spoils away;
 time observed; closed foes around,
 sides thick peals arms resound.
 shield emboss’d ringing storm sustains,
 impervious untouch’d remains.
 (great neptune’s care preserved hostile rage
 youth, joy nestor’s glorious age.)
 arms intrepid, first fought,
 faced every foe, every danger sought;
 winged lance, resistless wind,
 obeys motion master’s mind!
 restless flies, impatient free,
 meditates distant enemy.
 asius, adamas, drew near,
 struck target brazen spear
 fierce front: neptune wards blow,
 blunts javelin th’ eluded foe:
 broad buckler half weapon stood,
 splinter’d earth flew half broken wood.
 disarm’d, mingled trojan crew;
 merion’s spear o’ertook flew,
 deep belly’s rim entrance found,
 sharp pang, mortal wound.
 bending fell, doubled ground,
 lay panting. thus ox fetters tied,
 death’s strong pangs distend labouring side,
 bulk enormous field displays;
 heaving heart beats thick ebbing life decays.
 spear conqueror body drew,
 death’s dim shadows swarm view.
 next brave deipyrus dust laid:
 king helenus waved high thracian blade,
 smote temples arm strong,
 helm fell off, roll’d amid throng:
 luckier greek rests prize;
 dark death godlike owner lies!
 raging grief, great menelaus burns,
 fraught vengeance, victor turns:
 shook ponderous lance, act throw;
 stood adverse bended bow:
 full breast trojan arrow fell,
 harmless bounded plated steel.
 ample barn’s well harden’d floor,
 (the winds collected open door,)
 broad fan force whirl’d around,
 light leaps golden grain, resulting ground:
 steel guards atrides’ heart,
 repell’d distance flies bounding dart.
 atrides, watchful unwary foe,
 pierced lance hand grasp’d bow.
 nailed yew: wounded hand
 trail’d long lance mark’d blood sand:
 good agenor gently wound
 spear solicits, bandage bound;
 sling’s soft wool, snatch’d soldier’s side,
 tent ligature supplied.
 
behold! pisander, urged fate’s decree,
 springs ranks fall, fall thee,
 great menelaus! enchance thy fame:
 high-towering front, warrior came.
 first sharp lance atrides thrown;
 lance far distant winds blown.
 pierced pisander atrides’ shield:
 pisander’s spear fell shiver’d field.
 discouraged, future blind,
 vain dreams conquest swell haughty mind;
 dauntless rushes spartan lord
 like lightning brandish’d far beaming sword.
 left arm high opposed shining shield:
 right beneath, cover’d pole-axe held;
 (an olive’s cloudy grain handle made,
 distinct studs, brazen blade;)
 helm discharged noble blow;
 plume dropp’d nodding plain below,
 shorn crest. atrides waved steel:
 deep front weighty falchion fell;
 crashing bones force gave way;
 dust blood groaning hero lay:
 forced ghastly orbs, spouting gore,
 clotted eye-balls tumble shore.
 fierce atrides spurn’d bled,
 tore arms, and, loud-exulting, said:
 
“thus, trojans, thus, length taught fear;
 race perfidious, delight war!
 already noble deeds ye perform’d;
 princess raped transcends navy storm’d:
 bold feats impious might approve,
 without th’ assistance, fear jove.
 violated rites, ravish’d dame;
 heroes slaughter’d ships flame,
 crimes heap’d crimes, shall bend glory down,
 whelm ruins yon flagitious town.
 thou, great father! lord earth skies,
 thought man, supremely wise!
 thy hand fates mortals flow,
 whence favour impious foe?
 godless crew, abandon’d unjust,
 still breathing rapine, violence, lust?
 best things, beyond measure, cloy;
 sleep’s balmy blessing, love’s endearing joy;
 feast, dance; whate’er mankind desire,
 even sweet charms sacred numbers tire.
 troy ever reaps dire delight
 thirst slaughter, lust fight.”
 
said, seized (while yet carcase heaved)
 bloody armour, train received:
 sudden mix’d among warring crew,
 bold pylæmenes slew.
 harpalion asia travell’d far,
 following martial father war:
 filial love left native shore,
 never, ah, never behold more!
 unsuccessful spear chanced fling
 target spartan king;
 thus lance disarm’d, death flies,
 turns around apprehensive eyes.
 him, hip transpiercing fled,
 shaft merion mingled dead.
 beneath bone glancing point descends,
 and, driving down, swelling bladder rends:
 sunk sad companions’ arms lay,
 short pantings sobb’d soul away;
 (like vile worm extended ground;)
 life’s red torrent gush’d wound.
 
car paphlagonian train
 slow procession bore plain.
 pensive father, father now more!
 attends mournful pomp along shore;
 unavailing tears profusely shed;
 and, unrevenged, deplored offspring dead.
 
paris far moving sight beheld,
 pity soften’d fury swell’d:
 honour’d host, youth matchless grace,
 loved paphlagonian race!
 full strength bent angry bow,
 wing’d feather’d vengeance foe.
 chief was, brave euchenor named,
 riches much, virtue famed.
 held seat corinth’s stately town;
 polydus’ son, seer old renown.
 oft father told early doom,
 arms abroad, slow disease home:
 climb’d vessel, prodigal breath,
 chose certain glorious path death.
 beneath ear pointed arrow went;
 soul came issuing narrow vent:
 limbs, unnerved, drop useless ground,
 everlasting darkness shades round.
 
knew great hector legions yield,
 (wrapp’d cloud tumult field:)
 wide left force greece commands,
 conquest hovers o’er th’ achaian bands;
 tide superior virtue sway’d,
 shakes solid earth gave aid.
 centre hector fix’d remain’d,
 first gates forced, bulwarks gain’d;
 there, margin hoary deep,
 (their naval station ajaces keep.
 low walls confine beating tides,
 whose humble barrier scarce foe divides;
 late fight foot horse engaged,
 thunder battle raged,)
 join’d, whole bœotian strength remains,
 proud iaonians sweeping trains,
 locrians phthians, th’ epaean force;
 join’d, repel hector’s fiery course.
 flower athens, stichius, phidas, led;
 bias great menestheus head:
 meges strong epaean bands controll’d,
 dracius prudent, amphion bold:
 phthians, medon, famed martial might,
 brave podarces, active fight.
 drew phylacus noble line;
 iphiclus’ son: (oïleus) thine:
 (young ajax’ brother, stolen embrace;
 dwelt far distant native place,
 fierce step-dame father’s reign
 expell’d exiled brother slain:)
 rule phthians, arms employ,
 mix’d bœotians, shores troy.
 
now side side, like unwearied care,
 ajax laboured field war:
 two lordly bulls, equal toil,
 force bright ploughshare fallow soil,
 join’d one yoke, stubborn earth tear,
 trace large furrows shining share;
 o’er huge limbs foam descends snow,
 streams sweat sour foreheads flow.
 train heroes followed field,
 bore turns great ajax’ sevenfold shield;
 whene’er breathed, remissive might,
 tired incessant slaughters fight.
 following troops brave associate grace:
 close engagement unpractised race,
 locrian squadrons javelin wield,
 bear helm, lift moony shield;
 skill’d far flying shaft wing,
 whirl sounding pebble sling,
 dexterous aim certain wound,
 fell distant warrior ground.
 thus telamonian train,
 throng’d bright arms, pressing fight maintain:
 far rear locrian archers lie,
 whose stones arrows intercept sky,
 mingled tempest foes pour;
 troy’s scattering orders open shower.
 
now greeks eternal fame acquired,
 gall’d ilians walls retired;
 sage polydamas, discreetly brave,
 address’d great hector, counsel gave:
 
“though great all, thou seem’st averse lend
 impartial audience faithful friend;
 gods men thy matchless worth known,
 every art glorious war thy own;
 cool thought counsel excel,
 widely differs warring well!
 content bounteous gods given,
 seek alone engross gifts heaven.
 powers bloody war belong,
 sweet music charm song;
 few, wondrous few, jove assign’d
 wise, extensive, all-considering mind;
 guardians these, nations round confess,
 towns empires safety bless.
 heaven lodged virtue breast,
 attend, hector! judge best,
 see, thou mov’st, dangers dangers spread,
 war’s whole fury burns around thy head.
 behold! distress’d within yon hostile wall,
 many trojans yield, disperse, fall!
 troops, out-number’d, scarce war maintain!
 brave heroes ships lie slain!
 cease thy fury: and, chiefs kings
 convoked council, weigh sum things.
 whether (the gods succeeding desires)
 yon tall ships bear trojan fires;
 quit fleet, pass unhurt away,
 contented conquest day.
 fear, fear, lest greece, yet undone,
 pay large debt last revolving sun;
 achilles, great achilles, yet remains
 yonder decks, yet o’erlooks plains!”
 
counsel pleased; hector, bound,
 leap’d chariot trembling ground;
 swift leap’d clanging arms resound.
 “to guard post (he cried) thy art employ,
 detain scatter’d youth troy;
 yonder heroes faint, bend way,
 hasten back end doubtful day.”
 
said, towering chief prepares go,
 shakes white plumes breezes flow,
 seems moving mountain topp’d snow.
 host, inspiring force, flies,
 bids anew martial thunder rise.
 panthus’ son, hector’s high command
 haste bold leaders trojan band:
 round battlements, round plain,
 many chief look’d, look’d vain;
 deiphobus, helenus seer,
 asius’ son, asius’ self appear:
 pierced many ghastly wound,
 cold death, groaning ground;
 low dust, (a mournful object) lay;
 high wall breathed souls away.
 
far left, amid throng found
 (cheering troops, dealing deaths around)
 graceful paris; whom, fury moved,
 opprobrious thus, th’ impatient chief reproved:
 
“ill-fated paris! slave womankind,
 smooth face fraudulent mind!
 deiphobus, asius gone?
 godlike father, th’ intrepid son?
 force helenus, dispensing fate;
 great othryoneus, fear’d late?
 black fate hang’s o’er thee th’ avenging gods,
 imperial troy foundations nods;
 whelm’d thy country’s ruin shalt thou fall,
 one devouring vengeance swallow all.”
 
paris thus: “my brother friend,
 thy warm impatience makes thy tongue offend,
 battles deserved thy blame,
 though deedless, unknown fame:
 since yon rampart thy arms lay low,
 scatter’d slaughter fatal bow.
 chiefs seek yonder shore lie slain;
 heroes, two alone remain;
 deiphobus, helenus seer,
 now disabled hostile spear.
 go then, successful, thy soul inspires:
 heart hand shall second thy fires:
 arm can, prepare know,
 till death death paid, blow blow.
 ’tis ours, forces own
 combat: strength gods alone.”
 words hero’s angry mind assuage:
 fierce mingle thickest rage.
 around polydamas, distain’d blood,
 cebrion, phalces, stern orthaeus stood,
 palmus, polypœtes divine,
 two bold brothers hippotion’s line
 (who reach’d fair ilion, ascania far,
 former day; next engaged war).
 gloomy clouds whirlwind springs,
 bears jove’s thunder dreadful wings,
 wide o’er blasted fields tempest sweeps;
 then, gather’d, settles hoary deeps;
 afflicted deeps tumultuous mix roar;
 waves behind impel waves before,
 wide rolling, foaming high, tumbling shore:
 thus rank rank, thick battalions throng,
 chief urged chief, man drove man along.
 far o’er plains, dreadful order bright,
 brazen arms reflect beamy light:
 full blazing great hector shined,
 like mars commission’d confound mankind.
 flaming enormous shield,
 like broad sun, illumined field;
 nodding helm emits streamy ray;
 piercing eyes battle stray,
 and, beneath targe flash’d along,
 shot terrors round, wither’d e’en strong.
 
thus stalk’d he, dreadful; death look:
 whole nations fear’d; argive shook.
 towering ajax, ample stride,
 advanced first, thus chief defied:
 
“hector! come on; thy empty threats forbear;
 ’tis thy arm, ’tis thundering jove fear:
 skill war us idly given,
 lo! greece humbled, troy, heaven.
 vain hopes haughty mind imparts,
 force fleet: greeks hands hearts.
 long ere flames lofty navy fall,
 boasted city, god-built wall,
 shall sink beneath us, smoking ground;
 spread long unmeasured ruin round.
 time shall come, when, chased along plain,
 even thou shalt call jove, call vain;
 even thou shalt wish, aid thy desperate course,
 wings falcons thy flying horse;
 shalt run, forgetful warrior’s fame,
 clouds friendly dust conceal thy shame.”
 
thus spoke, behold, open view,
 sounding wings dexter eagle flew.
 jove’s glad omen grecians rise,
 hail, shouts, progress skies:
 far-echoing clamours bound side side;
 ceased; thus chief troy replied:
 
“from whence menace, insulting strain?
 enormous boaster! doom’d vaunt vain.
 may gods hector life bestow,
 (not short life mortals lead below,
 jove’s high lineage born,
 blue-eyed maid, gilds morn,)
 decisive day shall end fame
 greece, argos name.
 thou, imperious! thy madness wait
 lance hector, thou shalt meet thy fate:
 giant-corse, extended shore,
 shall largely feast fowls fat gore.”
 
said; like lion stalk’d along:
 shouts incessant earth ocean rung,
 sent following host: grecian train
 answering thunders fill’d echoing plain;
 shout tore heaven’s concave, and, above,
 shook fix’d splendours throne jove.

argument.[231]
 

juno deceives jupiter girdle venus.
 

nestor, sitting table machaon, alarmed the
 increasing clamour war, hastens agamemnon; way he
 meets prince diomed ulysses, informs the
 extremity danger. agamemnon proposes make escape by
 night, ulysses withstands; diomed adds advice, that,

genial feast, flowing bowl,
 charm cares nestor’s watchful soul;
 startled ears increasing cries attend;
 thus, impatient, wounded friend:
 
“what new alarm, divine machaon, say,
 mix’d events attend mighty day?
 hark! shouts divide, meet,
 now come full, thicken fleet!
 cordial draught dispel thy care,
 let hecamede strengthening bath prepare,
 refresh thy wound, cleanse clotted gore;
 adventures day explore.”
 
said: and, seizing thrasymedes’ shield,
 (his valiant offspring,) hasten’d field;
 (that day father’s buckler bore;)
 snatch’d lance, issued door.
 soon prospect open’d view,
 wounded eyes scene sorrow knew;
 dire disarray! tumult fight,
 wall ruins, greeks flight.
 old ocean’s silent surface sleeps,
 waves just heaving purple deeps:
 yet expected tempest hangs high,
 weighs cloud, blackens sky,
 mass waters will wind obey;
 jove sends one gust, bids roll away.
 wavering counsels thus mind engage,
 fluctuates doubtful thought pylian sage,
 join host, general haste;
 debating long, fixes last:
 yet, moves, sight bosom warms,

 gleaming falchions flash, javelins fly;

him, march, wounded princes meet,
 tardy steps ascending fleet:
 king men, ulysses divine,
 tydeus owes noble line[232]
 (their ships distance battle stand,
 lines advanced along shelving strand:
 whose bay, fleet unable contain
 length; beside margin main,
 rank rank, crowded ships moor:
 landed first, lay highest shore.)
 supported spears, took way,
 unfit fight, anxious day.
 nestor’s approach alarm’d grecian breast,
 thus general host address’d:
 
“o grace glory achaian name;
 drives thee, nestor, field fame?
 shall proud hector see boast fulfill’d,
 fleets ashes, heroes kill’d?
 threat, ah! now soon made good,
 many grecian bosom writ blood.
 every heart inflamed equal rage
 king, will one chief engage?
 lived see mournful eyes
 every greek new achilles rise?”
 
gerenian nestor then: “so fate will’d;
 all-confirming time fate fulfill’d.
 thunders aerial bower,
 jove himself, upon past power.
 wall, late inviolable bound,
 best defence, lies smoking ground:
 even ships conquering arms extend,
 groans slaughter’d greeks heaven ascend.
 speedy measures employ thought
 distress! counsel profit aught:
 arms much: though mars souls incite,
 gaping wounds withhold us fight.”
 
monarch: “that army bends,
 troy triumphant high fleet ascends,
 rampart, late surest trust
 best defence, lies smoking dust;
 jove’s afflictive hand bear,
 who, far argos, wills ruin here.
 past days happier greece blest,
 favour, aid confess’d;
 now heaven averse, hands battle ties,
 lifts trojan glory skies.
 cease length waste blood vain,
 launch ships lie nearest main;
 leave anchor, till coming night:
 then, impetuous troy forbear fight,
 bring sea, hoist sail flight.
 better evils, well foreseen, run,
 perish danger may shun.”
 
thus he. sage ulysses thus replies,
 anger flash’d disdainful eyes:
 “what shameful words (unkingly thou art)
 fall trembling tongue timorous heart?
 oh thy sway curse meaner powers,
 thou shame host ours!
 host, jove endued martial might,
 taught conquer, fall fight:
 adventurous combats bold wars wage,
 employ’d youth, yet employs age.
 wilt thou thus desert trojan plain?
 whole streams blood spilt vain?
 base sentence thou couch thy fear,
 speak whispers, lest greek hear.
 lives man dead fame, dares
 think meanness, thought declares?
 comes even whose sovereign sway
 banded legions greece obey?
 general’s voice calls flight,
 war hangs doubtful, soldiers fight?
 troy? yet fate denies
 thou givest foe: greece becomes prize.
 troops (our hoisted sails view,
 abandon’d) shall fight pursue;
 thy ships flying, despair shall see;
 owe destruction prince like thee.”
 
“thy just reproofs (atrides calm replies)
 like arrows pierce me, thy words wise.
 unwilling lose host,
 force greece quit hateful coast;
 glad submit, whoe’er, young, old,
 aught, conducive weal, unfold.”
 
tydides cut short, thus began:
 “such counsel seek, behold man
 boldly gives it, shall say,
 young though be, disdain obey:
 youth, mighty tydeus springs,
 may speak councils assembled kings.
 hear great oenides’ son,
 whose honoured dust (his race glory run)
 lies whelm’d ruins theban wall;
 brave life, glorious fall.
 three bold sons generous prothous bless’d,
 pleuron’s walls calydon possess’d;
 melas agrius, (who far surpass’d
 rest courage) Œneus last.
 him, sire. calydon expell’d,
 pass’d argos, exile dwell’d;
 monarch’s daughter (so jove ordain’d)
 won, flourish’d adrastus reign’d;
 there, rich fortune’s gifts, acres till’d,
 beheld vines liquid harvest yield,
 numerous flocks whiten’d field.
 tydeus was, foremost fame!
 lives greece stranger name.
 then, common good thoughts inspire,
 attend, respect sire.
 though sore battle, though wounds oppress’d,
 let go forth, animate rest,
 advance glory share,
 though partaker, witness war.
 lest new wounds wounds o’erpower us quite,
 beyond missile javelin’s sounding flight,
 safe let us stand; and, tumult far,
 inspire ranks, rule distant war.”
 
added not: listening kings obey,
 slow moving on; atrides leads way.
 god ocean (to inflame rage)
 appears warrior furrowed o’er age;
 press’d own, general’s hand took,
 thus venerable hero spoke:
 
“atrides! lo! disdainful eye
 achilles sees country’s forces fly;
 blind, impious man! whose anger guide,
 glories unutterable pride.
 may perish, may jove disclaim
 wretch relentless, o’erwhelm shame!
 heaven forsakes thee: o’er yonder sands
 soon shall thou view scattered trojan bands
 fly diverse; proud kings, chiefs renown’d,
 driven heaps heaps, clouds involved around
 rolling dust, winged wheels employ
 hide ignominious heads troy.”
 
spoke, rush’d amid warrior crew,
 sent voice flew,
 loud, shout encountering armies yield
 twice ten thousand shake labouring field;
 voice, thundering sound
 whose trident rends solid ground.
 argive bosom beats meet fight,
 grisly war appears pleasing sight.
 
meantime saturnia olympus’ brow,
 high-throned gold, beheld fields below;
 joy glorious conflict survey’d,
 great brother gave grecians aid.
 placed aloft, ida’s shady height
 sees jove, trembles sight.
 jove deceive, methods shall try,
 arts, blind all-beholding eye?
 length trusts power; resolved prove
 old, yet still successful, cheat love;
 wisdom oppose charms,
 lull lord thunders arms.
 
swift bright apartment repairs,
 sacred dress beauty’s pleasing cares:
 skill divine vulcan form’d bower,
 safe access intruding power.
 touch’d secret key, doors unfold:
 self-closed, behind shut valves gold.
 first bathes; round body pours
 soft oils fragrance, ambrosial showers:
 winds, perfumed, balmy gale convey
 heaven, earth, aerial way:
 spirit divine! whose exhalation greets
 sense gods mortal sweets.
 thus breathed heaven, decent pride
 artful hands radiant tresses tied;
 part head shining ringlets roll’d,
 part o’er shoulders waved like melted gold.
 around next heavenly mantle flow’d,
 rich pallas’ labour’d colours glow’d:
 large clasps gold foldings gather’d round,
 golden zone swelling bosom bound.
 far-beaming pendants tremble ear,
 gem illumined triple star.
 o’er head cast veil white
 new-fallen snow, dazzling light.
 last fair feet celestial sandals grace.
 thus issuing radiant majestic pace,
 forth dome imperial goddess moves,
 calls mother smiles loves.
 
“how long (to venus thus apart cried)
 shall human strife celestial minds divide?
 ah yet, will venus aid saturnia’s joy,
 set aside cause greece troy?”
 
“let heaven’s dread empress (cytheraea said)
 speak request, deem will obey’d.”
 
“then grant (said queen) conquering charms,
 power, mortals immortals warms,
 love, melts mankind fierce desires,
 burns sons heaven sacred fires!
 
“for lo! haste remote abodes,
 great parents, (sacred source gods!)
 ocean tethys old empire keep,
 last limits land deep.
 kind arms tender years past;
 time old saturn, olympus cast,
 upper heaven jove resign’d reign,
 whelm’d huge mass earth main.
 strife, hear, made union cease,
 held long ancient pair peace.
 honour, love, shall obtain,
 compose fatal feuds again;
 minds mutual ties engage,
 and, youth owed, repay age!”
 
said. awe divine, queen love
 obey’d sister wife jove;
 fragrant breast zone embraced,[233]
 various skill high embroidery graced.
 every art, every charm,
 win wisest, coldest warm:
 fond love, gentle vow, gay desire,
 kind deceit, still-reviving fire,
 persuasive speech, persuasive sighs,
 silence spoke, eloquence eyes.
 hand cyprian goddess laid:
 “take this, thy wish;” said.
 smiles took charm; smiling press’d
 powerful cestus snowy breast.
 
venus courts jove withdrew;
 whilst olympus pleased saturnia flew.
 o’er high pieria thence course bore,
 o’er fair emathia’s ever-pleasing shore,
 o’er hemus’ hills snows eternal crown’d;
 flying foot approach’d ground.
 taking wing athos’ lofty steep,
 speeds lemnos o’er rolling deep,
 seeks cave death’s half-brother, sleep.[234]
 
“sweet pleasing sleep! (saturnia thus began)
 spread’st thy empire o’er god man;
 e’er obsequious thy juno’s will,
 power slumbers! hear, favour still.
 shed thy soft dews jove’s immortal eyes,
 sunk love’s entrancing joys lies.
 splendid footstool, throne, shine
 gold unfading, somnus, shall thine;
 work vulcan; indulge thy ease,
 wine feasts thy golden humours please.”
 
“imperial dame (the balmy power replies),
 great saturn’s heir, empress skies!
 o’er gods spread easy chain;
 sire all, old ocean, owns reign.
 hush’d waves lie silent main.
 how, unbidden, shall dare steep
 jove’s awful temples dew sleep?
 long since, venturous, thy bold command,
 eternal lids laid hand;
 time, deserting ilion’s wasted plain,
 conquering son, alcides, plough’d main.
 lo! deeps arise, tempests roar,
 drive hero coan shore:

 rising wrath, tumbled gods gods;
 chief sought, realms high
 hurl’d indignant nether sky,
 gentle night, fled aid,
 (the friend earth heaven,) wings display’d;
 impower’d wrath gods men tame,
 even jove revered venerable dame.”
 
“vain thy fears (the queen heaven replies,
 and, speaking, rolls large majestic eyes);
 think’st thou troy jove’s high favour won,
 like great alcides, all-conquering son?
 hear, obey mistress skies,
 deed expect vulgar prize;
 know, thy loved-one shall ever thine,
 youngest grace, pasithaë divine.”[235]
 
“swear (he said) tremendous floods
 roar hell, bind invoking gods:
 let great parent earth one hand sustain,
 stretch o’er sacred main:
 call black titans, chronos dwell,
 hear witness depths hell;
 she, loved-one, shall ever mine,
 youngest grace, pasithaë divine.”
 
queen assents, infernal bowers
 invokes sable subtartarean powers,
 rule inviolable floods,
 mortals name dread titanian gods.

now navy borne silent wings,

troops assent; martial arms change:

 terrors almighty hand!

dreadful spoke, toss’d head high;

 wife live honour’d, race succeed,

roused soul every trojan breast:

 mark flames approach, near fall,

 hands trusted fates;
 better far one decisive strife,

 keep hard-got inch barren sands,
 still press’d, press’d inglorious hands.”

 famed prowess well-fought field,
 pierced centre sounding shield:
 meges, phyleus’ ample breastplate wore,
 (well-known fight sellè’s winding shore;
 king euphetes gave golden mail,
 compact, firm many jointed scale)
 oft, cities storm’d, battles won,
 saved father, now saves son.
 full trojan’s head urged lance,
 high plumes helmet dance,
 new ting’d tyrian dye: dust below,
 shorn crest, purple honours glow.
 meantime fight spartan king survey’d,
 stood meges’ side sudden aid.
 dolops’ shoulder urged forceful dart,
 held passage panting heart,
 issued breast. thundering sound
 warrior falls, extended ground.
 rush conquering greeks spoil slain:
 hector’s voice excites kindred train;
 hero most, hicetaon sprung,
 fierce melanippus, gallant, brave, young.
 (ere troy grecians cross’d main)
 fed large oxen percotè’s plain;
 oppress’d, country claim’d care,
 return’d ilion, excell’d war;
 this, priam’s court, held place,
 beloved less priam’s royal race.
 hector singled, troops led,
 thus inflamed him, pointing dead.
 
“lo, melanippus! lo, dolops lies;
 thus royal kinsman dies?
 o’ermatch’d falls; two prey,
 lo! bear bloody arms away!
 come on—a distant war longer wage,
 hand hand thy country’s foes engage:
 till greece once, glory end;
 ilion towery height descend,
 heaved lowest stone; bury all
 one sad sepulchre, one common fall.”
 
hector (this said) rush’d forward foes:
 equal ardour melanippus glows:
 ajax thus—“o greeks! respect fame,
 respect yourselves, learn honest shame:
 let mutual reverence mutual warmth inspire,
 catch breast breast noble fire,
 valour’s side odds combat lie;
 brave live glorious, lamented die;
 wretch trembles field fame,
 meets death, worse death, eternal shame.”
 
generous sense vain imparts;
 sunk, rooted grecian hearts:
 join, throng, thicken call,
 flank navy brazen wall;
 shields touching shields, order blaze above,
 stop trojans, though impell’d jove.
 fiery spartan first, loud applause.
 warms bold nestor cause.
 “is (he said) arms youth like you,
 strong fight, active pursue?
 stand distant, attempt deed?
 lift bold lance, make trojan bleed.”
 
said; backward lines retired;
 forth rush’d youth martial fury fired,
 beyond foremost ranks; lance threw,
 round black battalions cast view.
 troops troy recede sudden fear,
 swift javelin hiss’d along air.
 advancing melanippus met dart
 bold breast, felt heart:
 thundering falls; falling arms resound,
 broad buckler rings ground.
 victor leaps upon prostrate prize:
 thus roe well-breath’d beagle flies,
 rends side, fresh-bleeding dart
 distant hunter sent heart.
 observing hector rescue flew;
 bold was, antilochus withdrew.
 savage, ranging o’er plain,
 torn shepherd’s dog, shepherd’s swain,
 conscious deed, glares around,
 hears gathering multitude resound,
 timely flies yet-untasted food,
 gains friendly shelter wood:
 fears youth; troy shouts pursue,
 stones darts mingled tempest flew;
 enter’d grecian ranks, turns
 manly breast, new fury burns.
 
now fleet tides trojans drove,
 fierce fulfil stern decrees jove:
 sire gods, confirming thetis’ prayer,
 grecian ardour quench’d deep despair;
 lifts glory troy’s prevailing bands,
 swells hearts, strengthens hands.
 ida’s top waits longing eyes,
 view navy blazing skies;
 then, till then, scale war shall turn,
 trojans fly, conquer’d ilion burn.
 fates revolved almighty mind,
 raises hector work design’d,
 bids mortal fury glow,
 drives him, like lightning, foe.
 mars, human crimes vengeance call,
 shakes huge javelin, whole armies fall.
 rage conflagration rolls,
 wraps vast mountains, involves poles.
 foams wrath; beneath gloomy brow
 like fiery meteors red eye-balls glow:
 radiant helmet temple burns,
 waves nods, lightens turns:
 jove splendour round chief thrown,
 cast blaze hosts one.
 unhappy glories! fate near,
 due stern pallas, pelides’ spear:
 yet jove deferr’d death pay,
 gave fate allow’d, honours day!
 
now fire fame, breast, eyes
 burn foe, single every prize;
 still closest ranks, thickest fight,
 points ardour, exerts might.
 grecian phalanx, moveless tower,
 sides batter’d, yet resists power:
 tall rock o’erhangs hoary main,[241]
 winds assail’d, billows beat vain,
 unmoved hears, above, tempest blow,
 sees watery mountains break below.
 girt surrounding flames, seems fall
 like fire jove, bursts upon all:
 bursts wave cloud impends,
 and, swell’d tempests, ship descends;
 white decks foam; winds aloud
 howl o’er masts, sing every shroud:
 pale, trembling, tired, sailors freeze fears;
 instant death every wave appears.
 pale greeks eyes hector meet,
 chief thunders, shakes fleet.
 
lion, rushing den,
 amidst plain wide-water’d fen,
 (where numerous oxen, ease feed,
 large expatiate o’er ranker mead)
 leaps herds herdsman’s eyes;
 trembling herdsman far distance flies;
 lordly bull (the rest dispersed fled)
 singles out; arrests, lays dead.
 thus rage jove-like hector flew
 greece heaps; one seized, slew:
 mycenian periphes, mighty name,
 wisdom great, arms well known fame;
 minister stern eurystheus’ ire
 alcides, copreus sire:
 redeem’d honours race,
 generous sire base;
 o’er country’s youth conspicuous far
 every virtue, peace war:
 doom’d hector’s stronger force yield!
 margin ample shield
 struck hasty foot: heels up-sprung;
 supine fell; brazen helmet rung.
 fallen chief invading trojan press’d,
 plunged pointed javelin breast.
 circling friends, strove guard late
 unhappy hero, fled, shared fate.
 
chased foremost line, grecian train
 now man next, receding toward main:
 wedged one body tents stand,
 wall’d round sterns, gloomy, desperate band.
 now manly shame forbids inglorious flight;
 now fear confines fight:
 man courage breathes man; nestor most
 (the sage preserver grecian host)
 exhorts, adjures, guard utmost shores;
 parents, implores.
 
“oh friends! men: generous breasts inflame
 mutual honour, mutual shame!
 think hopes, fortunes; care
 wives, infants, parents share:
 think living father’s reverend head;
 think ancestor glory dead;
 absent, speak, sue,
 ask safety, fame, you:
 gods fates one action lay,
 lost, desert day.”
 
spoke, round breathed heroic fires;
 minerva seconds sage inspires.
 mist darkness jove around threw
 clear’d, restoring war view;
 sudden ray shot beaming o’er plain,
 show’d shores, navy, main:
 hector saw, fly, fight,
 scene wide-opening blaze light,
 first field great ajax strikes eyes,
 port majestic, ample size:
 ponderous mace studs iron crown’d,
 full twenty cubits long, swings around;
 fights, like others, fix’d certain stands
 looks moving tower bands;
 high decks vast gigantic stride,
 godlike hero stalks side side.
 horseman watery mead
 (skill’d manage bounding steed)
 drives four fair coursers, practised obey,
 great city public way;
 safe art, side side run,
 shifts seat, vaults one one;
 now this, now flies;
 admiring numbers follow eyes.
 
ship ship thus ajax swiftly flew,
 less wonder warring crew.
 furious, hector thunder’d threats aloud,
 rush’d enraged trojan crowd;
 swift invades ships, whose beaky prores
 lay rank’d contiguous bending shores;
 strong eagle airy height,
 marks swans’ cranes’ embodied flight,
 stoops impetuous, light food,
 and, stooping, darkens wings flood.
 jove leads almighty hand,
 breathes fierce spirits following band.
 warring nations meet, battle roars,
 thick beats combat sounding prores.
 thou wouldst thought, furious fire,
 force tame them, toil tire;
 new vigour new fights won,
 long battle begun.
 greece, yet unconquer’d, kept alive war,
 secure death, confiding despair:
 troy proud hopes already view’d main
 bright blaze, red heroes slain:
 like strength felt hope, despair,
 contends, war.
 
’twas thou, bold hector! whose resistless hand
 first seized ship contested strand;
 dead protesilaüs bore,[242]
 first touch’d unhappy trojan shore:
 arms warring nations stood,
 bathed generous breasts mutual blood.
 room poise lance bend bow;
 hand hand, man man, grow:
 wounded, wound; seek other’s hearts
 falchions, axes, swords, shorten’d darts.
 falchions ring, shields rattle, axes sound,
 swords flash air, glitter ground;
 streaming blood slippery shores dyed,
 slaughter’d heroes swell dreadful tide.
 
still raging, hector ample hand
 grasps high stern, gives loud command:
 

[illustration: ] ajax defending greek ships
 

“haste, bring flames! toil ten long years
 finished; day desired appears!
 happy day acclamations greet,
 bright destruction yon hostile fleet.
 coward-counsels timorous throng
 reverend dotards check’d glory long:
 long jove lull’d us lethargic charms,
 now peals thunder calls arms:
 great day crowns full desires,
 wakes force, seconds fires.”
 
spoke—the warriors fierce command
 pour new deluge grecian band.
 even ajax paused, (so thick javelins fly,)
 stepp’d back, doubted live die.
 yet, oars placed, stands wait
 chief approaching dares attempt fate:
 even last naval charge defends,
 now shakes spear, now lifts, now protends;
 even yet, greeks piercing shouts inspires,
 amidst attacks, deaths, darts, fires.
 
“o friends! heroes! names ever dear,
 sons mars, thunderbolts war!
 ah! yet mindful old renown,
 great forefathers’ virtues own.
 aids expect utmost strait?
 bulwarks rising fate?
 aids, bulwarks retreat attend,
 friends help, city defend.
 spot have, lose keep;
 stand trojans, rolls deep.
 ’tis hostile ground tread; native lands
 far, far hence: fates hands.”
 
raging spoke; wastes breath,
 turns javelin work death.
 whate’er bold trojan arm’d daring hands,
 sable ships, flaming brands,
 well chief naval weapon sped,
 luckless warrior stern lay dead:
 full twelve, boldest, moment fell,
 sent great ajax shades hell.

book xvi.
 

argument
 

sixth battle, acts death patroclus
 

patroclus (in pursuance request nestor eleventh book)
 entreats achilles suffer go assistance greeks
 achilles’ troops armour. agrees it, time
 charges content rescuing fleet, without further
 pursuit enemy. armour, horses, soldiers, officers are
 described. achilles offers libation success friend,
 patroclus leads myrmidons battle. trojans, at
 sight patroclus achilles’ armour, taking hero,
 cast uttermost consternation; beats the
 vessels, hector flies, sarpedon killed, though jupiter was
 averse fate. several particulars battle are
 described; heat which, patroclus, neglecting orders of
 achilles, pursues foe walls troy, apollo repulses
 disarms him, euphorbus wounds him, hector kills him, which
 concludes book.
 

warr’d armies ensanguined shore,
 black vessels smoked human gore.
 meantime patroclus achilles flies;
 streaming tears fall copious eyes.
 faster, trickling plains below,
 tall rock sable waters flow.
 divine pelides, compassion moved.
 thus spoke, indulgent, best beloved:[243]
 
“patroclus, say, grief thy bosom bears,
 flows fast unmanly tears?
 girl, infant mother keeps
 loved breast, fonder passion weeps;
 mother’s soul, infant warms,
 clung knees, reaching arms,
 thou hast mine! oh tell me, end
 thy melting sorrows thus pursue thy friend?
 
“griev’st thou me, martial band?
 come sad tidings native land?
 fathers live (our first, tender care),
 thy good menoetius breathes vital air,
 hoary peleus yet extends days;
 pleased age hear children’s praise.
 may meaner cause thy pity claim?
 perhaps yon relics grecian name,
 doom’d ships sink fire sword,
 pay forfeit haughty lord?
 whate’er cause, reveal thy secret care,
 speak sorrows friend share.”
 sigh instant bosom broke,
 another follow’d, patroclus spoke:
 
“let greece length pity touch thy breast,
 thyself greek; and, once, greeks best!
 lo! every chief might fate prevent,
 lies pierced wounds, bleeding tent:
 eurypylus, tydides, atreus’ son,
 wise ulysses, navy groan,
 country’s wounds own.
 pain soft arts pharmacy can ease,
 thy breast alone lenitives appease.
 may never rage like thine soul enslave,
 great vain! unprofitably brave!
 thy country slighted last distress,
 friend, man, thee shall hope redress?
 no—men unborn, ages yet behind,
 shall curse fierce, unforgiving mind.
 
“o man unpitying! man thy race;
 sure thou spring’st soft embrace,
 ever amorous hero caused thy birth,
 ever tender goddess brought thee forth:
 rugged rock’s hard entrails gave thee form,
 raging seas produced thee storm,
 soul well suiting tempestuous kind,
 rough thy manners, untamed thy mind.
 
“if dire oracle thy breast alarm,
 aught jove, thetis, stop thy arm,
 beam comfort yet greece may shine,
 lead myrmidonian line:
 clad thy dreadful arms appear,
 proud troy shall tremble, desert war;
 without thy person greece shall win day,
 thy mere image chase foes away.
 press’d fresh forces, o’erlabour’d train
 shall quit ships, greece respire again.”
 thus, blind fate! supplicating breath,
 thou begg’st arms, arms thy death.
 unfortunately good! boding sigh
 thy friend return’d; it, reply:
 “patroclus! thy achilles knows fears;
 words jove oracles hears;
 aught mother’s caution can suggest;
 tyrant’s pride lies rooted breast.
 wrongs, wrongs, constant thought engage,
 those, sole oracles, inspire rage:
 made tyrant: gave power wrong
 even me: felt it; shall feel long.
 maid, black-eyed maid, forced away,
 due toils many well-fought day;
 due conquest father’s reign;
 due votes grecian train.
 forced her; me, bold brave,
 disgraced, dishonour’d, like meanest slave.
 bear this—the wrongs grieve past;
 ’tis time fury relent last:
 fix’d date; day wish’d appears:
 hector ships battle bears,
 flames eyes, shouts invade ears.
 go then, patroclus! court fair honour’s charms
 troy’s famed fields, achilles’ arms:
 lead forth martial myrmidons fight,
 go save fleets, conquer right.
 see thin relics baffled band
 last edge yon deserted land!
 behold ilion ships descends;
 cloud blackens, storm impends!
 thus, when, sight amazed,
 troy saw trembled, helmet blazed:
 injurious king friendship lost,
 yon ample trench buried half host.
 camps, bulwarks now trojans fear,
 dreadful, achilles there;
 longer flames lance tydeus’ son;
 general calls heroes on:
 hector, alone, hear; dreadful breath
 commands slaughter, proclaims death.
 yet now, patroclus, issue plain:
 now save ships, rising fires restrain,
 give greeks visit greece again.
 heed words, mark friend’s command,
 trusts fame honours thy hand,
 thy deeds expects achaian host
 shall render back beauteous maid lost:
 rage uncontroll’d hostile crew,
 touch hector, hector due.
 though jove thunder command war,
 just, consult glory, forbear.
 fleet saved, desist chase,
 lead ilion’s walls grecian race;
 adverse god thy rashness may destroy;
 god, like phœbus, ever kind troy.
 let greece, redeem’d destructive strait,
 work; leave rest fate.
 o! immortal powers above,
 apollo, pallas, almighty jove!
 one trojan might left alive,
 greek race survive:
 might vast destruction shun,
 destroy accursed town!”
 conference held chiefs; strand
 great jove conquest crown’d trojan band.
 ajax sounding storm sustain’d,
 thick darts iron tempest rain’d:
 tired arm weighty buckler hung;
 hollow helm falling javelins rung;
 breath, quick short pantings, comes goes;
 painful sweat members flows.
 spent o’erpower’d, barely breathes most;
 yet scarce army stirs post;
 dangers dangers around glow,
 toil toil, woe succeeds woe.
 
say, muses, throned starry frame,
 first navy blazed trojan flame?
 
stern hector waved sword, standing near,
 furious ajax plied ashen spear,
 full lance stroke justly sped,
 broad falchion lopp’d brazen head;
 pointless spear warrior shakes vain;
 brazen head falls sounding plain.
 great ajax saw, own’d hand divine;
 confessing jove, trembling sign,
 warn’d retreats. swift sides pour
 hissing brands; thick streams fiery shower;
 o’er high stern curling volumes rise,
 sheets rolling smoke involve skies.
 
divine achilles view’d rising flames,
 smote thigh, thus aloud exclaims:
 “arm, arm, patroclus! lo, blaze aspires!
 glowing ocean reddens fires.
 arm, ere vessels catch spreading flame;
 arm, ere grecians name;
 haste bring troops.”—the hero said;
 friend ardour joy obey’d.
 
cased limbs brass; first around
 manly legs, silver buckles bound
 clasping greaves; breast applies

 whose son’s great arm alone weapon wields,

brave automedon (an honour’d name,

 words—now, warriors! grieve more,

joyful heard, kindling spoke,
