 loud o’er rout heard victor’s cry,
 war bleeds, thickest die,
 horse arms, chariots lie o’erthrown,
 bleeding heroes axles groan.
 stop, check, steeds peleus knew:
 bank bank immortal coursers flew.
 high-bounding o’er fosse, whirling car
 smokes ranks, o’ertakes flying war,
 thunders hector; hector flies,
 patroclus shakes lance; fate denies.
 less noise, less impetuous force,
 tide trojans urge desperate course,
 autumn jove fury pours,
 earth loaden incessant showers;
 (when guilty mortals break eternal laws,
 judges, bribed, betray righteous cause;)
 deep beds bids rivers rise,
 opens flood-gates skies:
 impetuous torrents hills obey,
 whole fields drown’d, mountains swept away;
 loud roars deluge till meets main;
 trembling man sees labours vain!
 
now chief (the foremost troops repell’d)
 back ships destined progress held,
 bore half troy resistless way,
 forced routed ranks stand day.
 space silver simois flows,
 lay fleets, rampires rose,
 grim dust blood patroclus stands,
 turns slaughter conquering bands.
 first pronous died beneath fiery dart,
 pierced shield valiant heart.
 thestor next, saw chief appear,
 fell victim coward fear;
 shrunk sat, wild haggard eye,
 stood combat, force fly;
 patroclus mark’d shunn’d war,
 unmanly tremblings shook car,
 dropp’d flowing reins. ’twixt jaws,
 javelin sticks, chariot draws.
 rock overhangs main,
 angler, studious line cane,
 mighty fish draws panting shore:
 less ease barbed javelin bore
 gaping dastard; spear shook,
 fell, life heartless breast forsook.
 
next eryalus flies; stone,
 large rock, fury thrown:
 full crown ponderous fragment flew,
 burst helm, cleft head two:
 prone ground breathless warrior fell,
 death involved shades hell.
 low dust epaltes, echius, lie;
 ipheas, evippus, polymelus, die;
 amphoterus erymas succeed;
 last tlepolemus pyres bleed.
 where’er moves, growing slaughters spread
 heaps heaps monument dead.
 
now sarpedon brave friends beheld
 grovelling dust, gasping field,
 reproach flying host warms:
 “oh stain honour! oh disgrace arms!
 forsake, inglorious, contended plain;
 hand unaided shall war sustain:
 task mine hero’s strength try,
 mows whole troops, makes army fly.”
 
spake: and, speaking, leaps car:
 patroclus lights, sternly waits war.
 two vultures mountain’s height
 stoop resounding pinions fight;
 cuff, tear, raise screaming cry;
 desert echoes, rocks reply:
 warriors thus opposed arms, engage
 equal clamours, equal rage.
 
jove view’d combat: whose event foreseen,
 thus bespoke sister queen:
 “the hour draws on; destinies ordain,[245]
 godlike shall press phrygian plain:
 already verge death stands,
 life owed fierce patroclus’ hands,
 passions parent’s breast debate!
 say, shall snatch impending fate,
 send safe lycia, distant far
 dangers toils war;
 doom bravest offspring yield,
 fatten, celestial blood, field?”
 
thus goddess radiant eyes:
 “what words these, sovereign skies!
 short date prescribed mortal man;
 shall jove one extend narrow span,
 whose bounds fix’d race began?
 many sons gods, foredoom’d death,
 proud ilion must resign breath!
 thine exempt, debate rise above,
 murmuring powers condemn partial jove.
 give bold chief glorious fate fight;
 ascending soul wing’d flight,
 let sleep death convey, thy command,
 breathless body native land.
 friends people, future praise,
 marble tomb pyramid shall raise,
 lasting honours ashes give;
 fame (’tis dead can have) shall live.”
 
said: cloud-compeller, overcome,
 assents fate, ratifies doom.
 touch’d grief, weeping heavens distill’d
 shower blood o’er fatal field:
 god, eyes averting plain,
 laments son, predestined slain,
 far lycian shores, happy native reign.
 now met arms, combatants appear;
 heaved shield, poised lifted spear;
 strong patroclus’ hand javelin fled,
 pass’d groin valiant thrasymed;
 nerves unbraced bulk sustain,
 falls, falling bites bloody plain.
 two sounding darts lycian leader threw:
 first aloof erring fury flew,
 next transpierced achilles’ mortal steed,
 generous pedasus theban breed:
 fix’d shoulder’s joint, reel’d around,
 roll’d bloody dust, paw’d slippery ground.
 sudden fall entangled harness broke;
 axle crackled, chariot shook:
 bold automedon, disengage
 starting coursers, restrain rage,
 divides traces sword, freed
 encumbered chariot dying steed:
 rest move on, obedient rein:
 car rolls slowly o’er dusty plain.
 
towering chiefs fiercer fight advance:
 first sarpedon whirl’d weighty lance,
 o’er warrior’s shoulder took course,
 spent empty air dying force.
 patroclus’ never-erring dart;
 aim’d breast pierced mortal part,
 strong fibres bind solid heart.
 mountain oak, poplar tall,
 pine (fit mast great admiral)
 nods axe, till groaning sound
 sinks, spreads honours ground,
 thus fell king; laid earth supine,
 chariot stretch’d form divine:
 grasp’d dust distain’d streaming gore,
 and, pale death, lay groaning shore.
 lies bull beneath lion’s paws,
 grim savage grinds foamy jaws
 trembling limbs, sucks smoking blood;
 deep groans, hollow roars, rebellow wood.
 
leader lycian band
 dying chief address’d last command;
 “glaucus, bold; thy task first dare
 glorious dangers destructive war,
 lead troops, combat head,
 incite living, supply dead.
 tell them, charged latest breath
 unrevenged bear sarpedon’s death.
 grief, shame, must glaucus undergo,
 spoil’d arms adorn grecian foe!
 friend, warrior fight;
 defend body, conquer right:
 that, taught great examples, may try
 like thee vanquish, like die.”
 ceased; fates suppress’d labouring breath,
 eyes darken’d shades death.
 insulting victor disdain bestrode
 prostrate prince, bosom trod;
 drew weapon panting heart,
 reeking fibres clinging dart;
 wide wound gush’d stream blood,
 soul issued purple flood.
 flying steeds myrmidons detain,
 unguided now, mighty master slain.
 all-impotent aid, transfix’d grief,
 unhappy glaucus heard dying chief:
 painful arm, yet useless smart
 inflicted late teucer’s deadly dart,
 supported better hand stay’d:
 phœbus (’twas could) pray’d:
 
“all-seeing monarch! whether lycia’s coast,
 sacred ilion, thy bright presence boast,
 powerful alike ease wretch’s smart;
 hear me! god every healing art!
 lo! stiff clotted blood, pierced pain,
 thrills arm, shoots every vein,
 stand unable sustain spear,
 sigh, distance glorious war.
 low dust great sarpedon laid,
 jove vouchsafed hapless offspring aid;
 thou, god health! thy succour lend,
 guard relics slaughter’d friend:
 thou, though distant, canst restore might,
 head lycians, support fight.”
 
apollo heard; and, suppliant stood,
 heavenly hand restrain’d flux blood;
 drew dolours wounded part,
 breathed spirit rising heart.
 renew’d art divine, hero stands,
 owns assistance immortal hands.
 first fight native troops warms,
 loudly calls troy’s vindictive arms;
 ample strides stalks place place;
 now fires agenor, now polydamas:
 Æneas next, hector accosts;
 inflaming thus rage hosts.
 
“what thoughts, regardless chief! thy breast employ?
 oh forgetful friends troy!
 generous friends, who, country far,
 breathe brave souls another’s war.
 see! dust great sarpedon lies,
 action valiant, council wise,
 guarded right, kept people free;
 lycians lost, lost thee!
 stretch’d patroclus’ arm yonder plains,
 save hostile rage loved remains!
 ah let greece conquer’d trophies boast,
 corse revenge heroes lost!”
 
spoke: leader grief partook:
 troy, loss, legions shook.
 transfix’d deep regret, view o’erthrown
 country’s pillar, own;
 chief, led troy’s beleaguer’d wall
 host heroes, outshined all.
 fired, rush on; first hector seeks foes,
 superior vengeance greatly glows.
 
o’er dead fierce patroclus stands,
 rousing ajax, roused listening bands:
 
“heroes, men; before;
 weigh great occasion, more.
 chief taught lofty walls yield,
 lies pale death, extended field.
 guard body troy numbers flies;
 ’tis half glory maintain prize.
 haste, strip arms, slaughter round spread,
 send living lycians dead.”
 
heroes kindle fierce command;
 martial squadrons close either hand:
 troy lycia charge loud alarms,
 thessalia there, greece, oppose arms.
 horrid shouts circle round slain;
 clash armour rings o’er plain.
 great jove, swell horrors fight,
 o’er fierce armies pours pernicious night,
 round confounds warring hosts,
 fate ennobling crowd ghosts.
 
now greece gives way, great epigeus falls;
 agacleus’ son, budium’s lofty walls;
 chased murder thence suppliant came
 peleus, silver-footed dame;
 now sent troy, achilles’ arms aid,
 pays due vengeance kinsman’s shade.
 soon luckless hand touch’d dead,
 rock’s large fragment thunder’d head;
 hurl’d hectorean force cleft twain
 shatter’d helm, stretch’d o’er slain.
 
fierce fight patroclus came,
 and, like eagle darting game,
 sprung trojan lycian band.
 grief thy heart, fury urged thy hand,
 generous greek! full vigour thrown,
 sthenelaus flew weighty stone,
 sunk dead: troy, near
 arm, drew back; hector learn’d fear.
 far able hand lance can throw,
 lists, fighting foe;
 far trojans lines retired;
 till glaucus, turning, rest inspired.
 bathyclaeus fell beneath rage,
 hope chalcon’s trembling age;
 wide o’er land stretch’d large domain,
 stately seats, riches blest vain:
 him, bold youth, eager pursue
 flying lycians, glaucus met slew;
 pierced bosom sudden wound,
 fell, falling made fields resound.
 achaians sorrow heroes slain;
 conquering shouts trojans shake plain,
 crowd spoil dead: greeks oppose;
 iron circle round carcase grows.
 
brave laogonus resign’d breath,
 despatch’d merion shades death:
 ida’s holy hill made abode,
 priest jove, honour’d like god.
 jaw ear javelin went;
 soul, exhaling, issued vent.
 spear Æneas victor threw,
 stooping forward death withdrew;
 lance hiss’d harmless o’er covering shield,
 trembling struck, rooted field;
 yet scarce spent, quivers plain,
 sent great Æneas’ arm vain.
 “swift thou art (the raging hero cries)
 skill’d dancing dispute prize,
 spear, destined passage found,
 fix’d thy active vigour ground.”
 
“o valiant leader dardan host!
 (insulted merion thus retorts boast)
 strong are, ’tis mortal force trust,
 arm strong may stretch thee dust.
 lance thy fate given,
 vain thy vaunts; success still heaven:
 this, instant, sends thee pluto’s coast;
 mine glory, thy parting ghost.”
 
“o friend (menoetius’ answer gave)
 words combat, ill befits brave;
 empty boasts sons troy repel,
 swords must plunge shades hell.
 speak, beseems council; dare
 glorious action, task war.”
 
said, patroclus battle flies;
 great merion follows, new shouts arise:
 shields, helmets rattle, warriors close;
 thick heavy sounds storm blows.
 shrilling vale, mountain ground,
 labours woodman’s axe resound;
 blows following blows heard re-echoing wide,
 crackling forests fall every side:
 thus echoed fields loud alarms,
 fell warriors, rung arms.
 
now great sarpedon sandy shore,
 heavenly form defaced dust gore,
 stuck darts warring heroes shed,
 lies undistinguish’d vulgar dead.
 long-disputed corse chiefs enclose,
 every side busy combat grows;
 thick beneath shepherd’s thatch’d abode
 (the pails high foaming milky flood)
 buzzing flies, persevering train,
 incessant swarm, chased return again.
 
jove view’d combat stern survey,
 eyes flash’d intolerable day.
 fix’d field sight, breast debates
 vengeance due, meditates fates:
 whether urge prompt effect, call
 force hector patroclus’ fall,
 instant see short-lived trophies won,
 stretch breathless slaughter’d son;
 yet, many soul’s untimely flight,
 augment fame horror fight.
 crown achilles’ valiant friend praise
 length dooms; and, last days
 shall set glory, bids drive foe;
 unattended see shades below.
 hector’s mind fills dire dismay;
 mounts car, calls hosts away;
 sunk troy’s heavy fates, sees decline
 scales jove, pants awe divine.
 
then, before, hardy lycians fled,
 left monarch common dead:
 around, heaps heaps, dreadful wall
 carnage rises, heroes fall.
 (so jove decreed!) length greeks obtain
 prize contested, despoil slain.
 radiant arms patroclus borne;
 patroclus’ ships glorious spoils adorn.
 
thus phœbus, realms above,
 spoke throne cloud-compelling jove:
 “descend, phœbus! phrygian plain,
 fight convey sarpedon slain;
 bathe body crystal flood,
 dust dishonour’d, deform’d blood;
 o’er limbs ambrosial odours shed,
 celestial robes adorn dead.
 rites discharged, sacred corse bequeath
 soft arms silent sleep death.
 friends immortal charge shall bear;
 friends tomb pyramid shall rear:
 honour mortals death receive,
 unavailing honours may give!”
 

[illustration: ] sleep death conveying body sarpedon to
 lycia
 

apollo bows, mount ida’s height,
 swift field precipitates flight;
 thence war breathless hero bore,
 veil’d cloud, silver simois’ shore;
 bathed honourable wounds, dress’d
 manly members immortal vest;
 perfumes sweet ambrosial dews
 restores freshness, form renews.
 sleep death, two twins winged race,
 matchless swiftness, silent pace,
 received sarpedon, god’s command,
 moment reach’d lycian land;
 corse amidst weeping friends laid,
 endless honours wait sacred shade.
 
meanwhile patroclus pours along plains,
 foaming coursers, loosen’d reins.
 fierce trojan lycian crew,
 ah blind fate! thy headlong fury flew:
 fate powerful jove ordain,
 vain thy friend’s command, thy courage vain.
 he, god, whose counsels uncontroll’d
 dismay mighty, confound bold;
 god gives, resumes, orders all,
 urged thee on, urged thee fall.
 
first, brave hero! arm slain,
 last beneath thy vengeance press’d plain;
 heaven thy fatal fury led,
 call’d fill number dead?
 adrestus first; autonous succeeds;
 echeclus follows; next young megas bleeds,
 epistor, melanippus, bite ground;
 slaughter, elasus mulius crown’d:
 sunk pylartes eternal night;
 rest, dispersing, trust fates flight.
 
now troy stoop’d beneath matchless power,
 flaming phœbus kept sacred tower.
 thrice battlements patroclus strook;[246]
 blazing ægis thrice apollo shook;
 tried fourth; when, bursting cloud,
 mortal voice heard aloud.
 
“patroclus! cease; heaven-defended wall
 defies thy lance; fated yet fall;
 thy friend, thy greater far, shall withstand,
 troy shall stoop even achilles’ hand.”
 
spoke god darts celestial fires;
 greek obeys him, awe retires.
 hector, checking scæan gates
 panting coursers, breast debates,
 field forces employ,
 draw troops within walls troy.
 thus thought, beside phœbus stood,
 asius’ shape, reigned sangar’s flood;
 (thy brother, hecuba! dymas sprung,
 valiant warrior, haughty, bold, young;)
 thus accosts him. “what shameful sight!
 god! hector forbears fight?
 thine vigour successful spear
 soon convince thee false fear.
 turn thee, ah turn thee field fame,
 patroclus’ blood efface thy shame.
 perhaps apollo shall thy arms succeed,
 heaven ordains thy lance bleed.”
 
spoke inspiring god; took flight,
 plunged amidst tumult fight.
 bids cebrion drive rapid car;
 lash resounds, coursers rush war.
 god grecians’ sinking souls depress’d,
 pour’d swift spirits trojan breast.
 patroclus lights, impatient fight;
 spear left, stone employs right:
 nerves drives foe.
 pointed above, rough gross below:
 falling ruin crush’d cebrion’s head,
 lawless offspring king priam’s bed;
 front, brows, eyes, one undistinguish’d wound:
 bursting balls drop sightless ground.
 charioteer, yet held rein,
 struck car, falls headlong plain.
 dark shades soul unwilling glides,
 proud victor thus fall derides.
 
“good heaven! active feats yon artist shows!
 skilful divers phrygian foes!
 mark ease sink sand!
 pity practice land!”
 
rushing sudden prostrate prize,
 spoil carcase fierce patroclus flies:
 swift lion, terrible bold,
 sweeps field, depopulates fold;
 pierced dauntless heart, tumbles slain,
 fatal courage finds bane.
 bold hector leaping car,
 defends body, provokes war.
 thus slaughter’d hind, equal rage,
 two lordly rulers wood engage;
 stung fierce hunger, prey invades,
 echoing roars rebellow shades.
 stern hector fastens warrior’s head,
 foot patroclus drags dead:
 around, confusion, rage, fright,
 mix contending hosts mortal fight.
 pent hills, wild winds roar aloud
 deep bosom gloomy wood;
 leaves, arms, trees, aloft air blown,
 broad oaks crackle, sylvans groan;
 way that, rattling thicket bends,
 whole forest one crash descends.
 less noise, less tumultuous rage,
 dreadful shock mingled hosts engage.
 darts shower’d darts, now round carcase ring;
 now flights arrows bounding string:
 stones follow stones; clatter fields,
 hard, heavy, shake sounding shields.
 rising whirlwind clouds plains,
 sunk soft dust mighty chief remains,
 and, stretch’d death, forgets guiding reins!
 
now flaming zenith, sol driven
 fervid orb half vault heaven;
 host equal tempests fell
 showering darts, numbers sank hell.
 evening wheels o’erhung main,
 glad conquest rested grecian train.
 amidst tumult alarms,
 draw conquer’d corse radiant arms.
 rash patroclus new fury glows,
 breathing slaughter, pours amid foes.
 thrice press like mars flew,
 thrice three heroes onset slew.
 ends thy glory! fates untwine
 last, black remnant bright line:
 apollo dreadful stops thy middle way;
 death calls, heaven allows longer day!
 
lo! god dusky clouds enshrined,
 approaching dealt staggering blow behind.
 weighty shock neck shoulders feel;
 eyes flash sparkles, stunn’d senses reel
 giddy darkness; far distance flung,
 bounding helmet champaign rung.
 achilles’ plume stain’d dust gore;
 plume never stoop’d earth before;
 long used, untouch’d, fighting fields shine,
 shade temples mad divine.
 jove dooms now hector’s helm nod;
 long—for fate pursues him, god.
 
spear shivers falls; ample shield
 drops arm: baldric strows field:
 corslet astonish’d breast forsakes:
 loose joint; nerve horror shakes;
 stupid stares, all-assistless stands:
 force mortal hands!
 
dardan youth was, well known fame,
 panthus sprung, euphorbus name;
 famed manage foaming horse,
 skill’d dart, matchless course:
 full twenty knights tumbled car,
 yet learn’d rudiments war.
 venturous spear first drew hero’s gore;
 struck, wounded, durst more.
 nor, though disarm’d, patroclus’ fury stood:
 swift withdrew long-protended wood.
 turn’d short, herded crowd.
 thus, arm divine, mortal spear,
 wounded, once, patroclus yields fear,
 retires succour social train,
 flies fate, heaven decreed, vain.
 stern hector, bleeding chief views,
 breaks ranks, retreat pursues:
 lance arrests mortal wound;
 falls, earth thunders, arms resound.
 greece sunk; moment all
 yet-surviving heroes seem’d fall.
 so, scorch’d heat, along desert score,
 roaming lion meets bristly boar,
 fast spring; dispute flood,
 flaming eyes, jaws besmear’d blood;
 length sovereign savage wins strife;
 torn boar resigns thirst life.
 patroclus thus, many chiefs o’erthrown,
 many lives effused, expires own.
 dying now hector’s feet lies,
 sternly views him, triumphant cries:
 
“lie there, patroclus! thee, joy
 thy pride promised, subverting troy;
 fancied scenes ilion wrapt flames,
 thy soft pleasures served captive dames.
 unthinking man! fought towers free,
 guard beauteous race lords like thee:
 thou prey vultures shalt made;
 thy achilles lend thee aid;
 though much parting great chief might say,
 much enjoin thee, important day.
 
‘return not, brave friend (perhaps said),
 without bloody arms hector dead.’
 spoke, patroclus march’d, thus sped.”
 
supine, wildly gazing skies,
 faint, expiring breath, chief replies:
 
“vain boaster! cease, know powers divine!
 jove’s apollo’s deed, thine;
 heaven owed whate’er call,
 heaven disarm’d ere fall.
 twenty mortals, thy match might,
 opposed fairly, sunk fight:
 fate phœbus first o’erthrown,
 euphorbus next; third mean part thy own.
 thou, imperious! hear latest breath;
 gods inspire it, sounds thy death:
 insulting man, thou shalt soon i;
 black fate o’erhangs thee, thy hour draws nigh;
 even now life’s last verge see thee stand,
 see thee fall, achilles’ hand.”
 
faints: soul unwilling wings way,
 (the beauteous body left load clay)
 flits lone, uncomfortable coast;
 naked, wandering, melancholy ghost!
 
hector pausing, eyes fed
 pale carcase, thus address’d dead:
 
“from whence boding speech, stern decree
 death denounced, denounced me?
 well achilles’ fate given
 hector’s lance? knows will heaven?”
 
pensive said; pressing lay
 breathless bosom, tore lance away;
 upwards cast corse: reeking spear
 shakes, charges bold charioteer.
 swift automedon loosen’d reins
 rapt chariot o’er distant plains,
 far rage immortal coursers drove;
 immortal coursers gift jove.
 

[illustration: ] Æsculapius
 



book xvii.
 

argument.
 

seventh battle, body patroclus.—the acts menelaus.
 

menelaus, upon death patroclus, defends body enemy:
 euphorbus, attempts it, slain. hector advancing, menelaus
 retires; soon returns ajax, drives off. this, glaucus
 objects hector flight, thereupon puts armour had
 won patroclus, renews battle. greeks give way, till
 ajax rallies them: Æneas sustains trojans. Æneas hector attempt
 chariot achilles, borne automedon. horses of
 achilles deplore loss patroclus: jupiter covers body a
 thick darkness: noble prayer ajax occasion. menelaus
 sends antilochus achilles, news patroclus’ death: then
 returns fight, where, though attacked utmost fury, he
 meriones, assisted ajaces, bear body ships.
 time evening eight-and-twentieth day. scene
 lies fields troy.
 

cold earth divine patroclus spread,
 lies pierced wounds among vulgar dead.
 great menelaus, touch’d generous woe,
 springs front, guards foe.
 thus round new-fallen young heifer moves,
 fruit throes, first-born loves;
 anxious (helpless lies, bare)
 turns, re-turns her, mother’s care,
 opposed near carcase came,
 broad shield glimmers, lances flame.
 
panthus, skill’d dart send,
 eyes dead hero, insults friend.
 “this hand, atrides, laid patroclus low;
 warrior! desist, tempt equal blow:
 spoils prowess won, resign:
 depart life, leave glory mine.”
 
trojan thus: spartan monarch burn’d
 generous anguish, scorn return’d:
 “laugh’st thou not, jove! thy superior throne,
 mortals boast prowess own?
 thus lion glories might,
 panther braves spotted foe fight,
 thus boar (those terrors plain;)
 man vaunts force, vaunts vain.
 far vainest boastful kind,
 sons panthus vent haughty mind.
 yet ’twas late, beneath conquering steel
 boaster’s brother, hyperenor, fell;
 arm rashly defied,
 vain vigour, vain pride.
 eyes beheld dust expire,
 cheer spouse, glad sire.
 presumptuous youth! like shall thy doom,
 go, wait thy brother stygian gloom;
 or, thou may’st, avoid threaten’d fate;
 fools stay feel it, wise late.”
 
unmoved, euphorbus thus: “that action known,
 come, brother’s blood repay thy own.
 weeping father claims thy destined head,
 spouse, widow bridal bed.
 thy conquer’d spoils shall bestow,
 soothe consort’s parent’s woe.
 longer defer glorious strife,
 let heaven decide fortune, fame, life.”
 
swift word missile lance flings;
 well-aim’d weapon buckler rings,
 blunted brass, innoxious falls.
 jove father great atrides calls,
 flies javelin arm vain,
 pierced throat, bent plain;
 wide neck appears grisly wound,
 prone sinks warrior, arms resound.
 shining circlets golden hair,
 even graces might proud wear,
 instarr’d gems gold, bestrow shore,
 dust dishonour’d, deform’d gore.
 
young olive, sylvan scene,
 crown’d fresh fountains eternal green,
 lifts gay head, snowy flowerets fair,
 plays dances gentle air;
 lo! whirlwind high heaven invades
 tender plant, withers shades;
 lies uprooted genial bed,
 lovely ruin now defaced dead:
 thus young, thus beautiful, euphorbus lay,
 fierce spartan tore arms away.
 proud deed, glorious prize,
 affrighted troy towering victor flies:
 flies, mountain lion’s ire
 village curs trembling swains retire,
 o’er slaughter’d bull hear roar,
 see jaws distil smoking gore:
 pale fear, distance scatter’d round,
 shout incessant, vales resound.
 
meanwhile apollo view’d envious eyes,
 urged great hector dispute prize;
 (in mentes’ shape, beneath whose martial care
 rough ciconians learn’d trade war;)[247]
 “forbear (he cried) fruitless speed chase
 achilles’ coursers, ethereal race;
 stoop not, these, mortal man’s command,
 stoop none great achilles’ hand.
 long amused pursuit vain,
 turn, behold brave euphorbus slain;
 sparta slain! ever now suppress’d
 fire burn’d undaunted breast!”
 
thus spoke, apollo wing’d flight,
 mix’d mortals toils fight:
 words infix’d unutterable care
 deep great hector’s soul: war
 darts anxious eye; and, instant, view’d
 breathless hero blood imbued,
 (forth welling wound, prone lay)
 victor’s hands shining prey.
 sheath’d bright arms, cleaving ranks flies,
 sends voice thunder skies:
 fierce flood flame vulcan sent,
 flew, fired nations went.
 atrides voice storm divined,
 thus explored unconquer’d mind:
 
“then shall quit patroclus plain,
 slain cause, honour slain!
 desert arms, relics, friend?
 singly, hector troops attend?
 sure partial favour heaven bestow’d,
 brave hero brave god:
 forgive me, greece, quit field;
 ’tis hector, heaven yield.
 yet, god, heaven, give fear,
 voice ajax reach ear:
 still turn, still battle plains,
 give achilles yet remains
 patroclus—” this, more
 time allow’d: troy thicken’d shore.
 sable scene! terrors hector led.
 slow recedes, sighing quits dead.
 
fold unwilling lion parts,
 forced loud clamours, storm darts;
 flies indeed, threatens flies,
 heart indignant retorted eyes.
 now enter’d spartan ranks, turn’d
 manly breast, new fury burn’d;
 o’er black battalions sent view,
 cloud godlike ajax knew;
 labouring left warrior stood,
 grim arms, cover’d o’er blood;
 breathing courage, god day
 sunk heart terror dismay.
 
king: “oh ajax, oh friend!
 haste, patroclus’ loved remains defend:
 body achilles restore
 demands care; alas, can more!
 naked now, despoiled arms, lies;
 hector glories dazzling prize.”
 said, touch’d heart. raging pair
 pierced thick battle, provoke war.
 already stern hector seized head,
 doom’d trojan gods unhappy dead;
 soon ajax rear’d tower-like shield,
 sprung car, measured back field,
 train troy radiant armour bear,
 stand trophy fame war.
 
meanwhile great ajax (his broad shield display’d)
 guards dead hero dreadful shade;
 now before, now behind stood:
 thus centre gloomy wood,
 many step, lioness surrounds
 tawny young, beset men hounds;
 elate heart, rousing powers,
 dark o’er fiery balls hanging eyebrow lours.
 fast side generous spartan glows
 great revenge, feeds inward woes.
 
glaucus, leader lycian aids,
 hector frowning, thus flight upbraids:
 
“where now hector shall hector find?
 manly form, without manly mind.
 this, chief! hero’s boasted fame?
 vain, without merit, name!
 since battle renounced, thy thoughts employ
 methods may preserve thy troy:
 ’tis time try ilion’s state can stand
 thee alone, ask foreign hand:
 mean, empty boast! shall lycians stake
 lives you? lycians forsake?
 thy thankless arms can expect?
 thy friend sarpedon proves thy base neglect;
 say, shall slaughter’d bodies guard walls,
 unreveng’d great sarpedon falls?
 even died troy, left there,
 feast dogs, fowls air.
 command lycian wait,
 hence let march, give troy fate.
 spirit gods impart
 impel one trojan hand trojan heart,
 (such burn every soul draws
 sword glory, country’s cause)
 even yet mutual arms might employ,
 drag yon carcase walls troy.
 oh! patroclus ours, might obtain
 sarpedon’s arms honour’d corse again!
 greece achilles’ friend repaid,
 thus due honours purchased shade.
 words vain—let ajax appear,
 hector trembles recedes fear;
 thou dar’st meet terrors eye;
 lo! already thou prepar’st fly.”
 
trojan chief fix’d resentment eyed
 lycian leader, sedate replied:
 
“say, just, friend, hector’s ear
 warrior speech hear?
 deem’d thee wisest thy kind,
 ill insult suits prudent mind.
 shun great ajax? desert train?
 ’tis mine prove rash assertion vain;
 joy mingle battle bleeds,
 hear thunder sounding steeds.
 jove’s high will ever uncontroll’d,
 strong withers, confounds bold;
 now crowns fame mighty man, now
 strikes fresh garland victor’s brow!
 come, yon squadrons let us hew way,
 thou witness, fear to-day;
 yet greek sight hector dread,
 yet hero dare defend dead.”
 
turning martial hosts, cries:
 “ye trojans, dardans, lycians, allies!
 men, friends, action name,
 yet mindful ancient fame.
 hector proud achilles’ arms shall shine,
 torn friend, right conquest mine.”
 
strode along field, thus said:
 (the sable plumage nodded o’er head:)
 swift spacious plain sent look;
 one instant saw, one instant overtook
 distant band, sandy shore
 radiant spoils sacred ilion bore.
 mail unbraced field bestrow’d;
 train troy convey’d massy load.
 now blazing immortal arms stands;
 work present celestial hands;
 aged peleus achilles given,
 first peleus court heaven:
 father’s arms long achilles wears,
 forbid fate reach father’s years.
 
him, proud triumph, glittering afar,
 god whose thunder rends troubled air
 beheld pity; apart sat,
 and, conscious, look’d scene fate.
 shook sacred honours head;
 olympus trembled, godhead said;
 “ah, wretched man! unmindful thy end!
 moment’s glory; fates attend!
 heavenly panoply divinely bright
 thou stand’st, armies tremble thy sight,
 achilles’ self! beneath thy dart
 lies slain great achilles’ dearer part.
 thou mighty dead arms hast torn,
 greatest mankind worn.
 yet live! give thee one illustrious day,
 blaze glory ere thou fad’st away.
 ah! andromache shall come
 joyful tears welcome hector home;
 officious, endearing charms,
 thy tired limbs unbrace pelides’ arms!”
 
sable brow gave nod
 seals word; sanction god.
 stubborn arms (by jove’s command disposed)
 conform’d spontaneous, around closed:
 fill’d god, enlarged members grew,
 veins sudden vigour flew,
 blood brisker tides began roll,
 mars came rushing soul.
 exhorting loud field strode,
 look’d, moved, achilles, god.
 now mesthles, glaucus, medon, inspires,
 now phorcys, chromius, hippothous fires;
 great thersilochus like fury found,
 asteropaeus kindled sound,
 ennomus, augury renown’d.
 
“hear, ye hosts, hear, unnumber’d bands
 neighbouring nations, distant lands!
 ’twas state summon’d far,
 boast numbers, pomp war:
 ye came fight; valiant foe chase,
 save present, future race.
 this, wealth, products, enjoy,
 glean relics exhausted troy.
 now then, conquer die prepare;
 die conquer terms war.
 whatever hand shall win patroclus slain,
 whoe’er shall drag trojan train,
 hector’s self shall equal honours claim;
 hector part spoil, share fame.”
 
fired words, troops dismiss fears,
 join, thicken, protend spears;
 full greeks drive firm array,
 ajax hopes glorious prey:
 vain hope! numbers shall field o’erspread,
 victims perish round mighty dead!
 
great ajax mark’d growing storm far,
 thus bespoke brother war:
 “our fatal day, alas! come, friend;
 wars glories end!
 ’tis corse alone guard vain,
 condemn’d vultures trojan plain;
 must yield: sad fate must fall
 thee, me, perhaps, friend, all.
 see tempest direful hector spreads,
 lo! bursts, thunders heads!
 call greeks, hear call,
 bravest greeks: hour demands all.”
 
warrior raised voice, wide around
 field re-echoed distressful sound.
 “o chiefs! princes, whose hand given
 rule men; whose glory heaven!
 due honours atrides grace:
 ye guides guardians argive race!
 all, well-known voice shall reach far,
 all, see cloud war;
 come all! let generous rage arms employ,
 save patroclus dogs troy.”
 
oilean ajax first voice obey’d,

 next idomeneus, slow age,
 merion, burning hero’s rage.
 long-succeeding numbers can name?
 greeks, eager fame.
 fierce charge great hector led throng;
 whole troy embodied rush’d shouts along.
 thus, mountain billow foams raves,
 swoln river disembogues waves,
 full mouth stopp’d rushing tide,
 boiling ocean works side side,
 river trembles utmost shore,
 distant rocks re-bellow roar.

 him, chief hosts contend
 lived hateful, lived friend:
 dead protects superior care.
 dooms carcase birds air.

greece, close order, collected might,

 yet ’tis given troy ravage o’er

 thalia, glauce (every watery name),
 nesaea mild, silver spio came:
 cymothoe cymodoce nigh,
 blue languish soft alia’s eye.
 locks actaea limnoria rear,
 proto, doris, panope appear,
 thoa, pherusa, doto, melita;
 agave gentle, amphithoe gay:
 next callianira, callianassa show
 sister looks; dexamene slow,
 swift dynamene, now cut tides:
 iaera now verdant wave divides:
 nemertes apseudes lifts head,
 bright galatea quits pearly bed;
 orythia, clymene, attend,
 maera, amphinome, train extend;
 black janira, janassa fair,
 amatheia amber hair.
 these, deep ocean held
 sacred seats, glimmering grotto fill’d;
 beat ivory breast silent woe,
 till thetis’ sorrows thus began flow:
 
“hear me, judge, ye sisters main!
 just cause thetis complain!
 wretched, mortal, fate!
 wretched immortal state!
 sprung bed godlike hero came,
 bravest far ever bore name;
 like fair olive, careful hand
 grew, flourish’d adorn’d land!
 troy sent him: fates ordain
 never, never must return again.
 short space light heaven view,
 short, alas! fill’d anguish too!
 hear sorrows echo shore!
 ease them, must deplore;
 go least bear tender part,
 mourn loved-one mother’s heart.”
 
said, left caverns main,
 bathed tears; melancholy train
 attend way. wide-opening part tides,
 long pomp silver wave divides.
 approaching now, touch’d trojan land;
 then, two two, ascended strand.
 immortal mother, standing close beside
 mournful offspring, sighs replied;
 along coast mingled clamours ran,
 thus silver-footed dame began:
 
“why mourns son? thy late preferr’d request
 god granted, greeks distress’d:
 mourns son? thy anguish let share,
 reveal cause, trust parent’s care.”
 
he, deeply groaning—“to cureless grief,
 even thunderer’s favour brings relief.
 patroclus—ah!—say, goddess, can boast
 pleasure now? revenge lost;
 patroclus, loved martial train,
 beyond mankind, beyond slain!
 lost arms gods bestow’d
 peleus; hector bears glorious load.
 cursed day, powers above
 thy charms submitted mortal love:
 hadst thou still, sister main,
 pursued pleasures watery reign:
 happier peleus, less ambitious, led
 mortal beauty equal bed!
 ere sad fruit thy unhappy womb
 caused sorrows past, woes come.
 soon, alas! wretched offspring slain,
 new woes, new sorrows, shall create again.
 ’tis fate alternate now give;
 patroclus dead, achilles hates live.
 let revenge proud hector’s heart,
 let last spirit smoke upon dart;
 conditions will breathe: till then,
 blush walk among race men.”
 
flood tears, this, goddess shed:
 “ah then, see thee dying, see thee dead!
 hector falls, thou diest.”—“let hector die,
 let fall! (achilles made reply)
 far lies patroclus native plain!
 fell, falling, wish’d aid vain.
 ah then, since miserable day
 cast hope return away;
 since, unrevenged, hundred ghosts demand
 fate hector achilles’ hand;
 since here, brutal courage far renown’d,
 live idle burden ground,
 (others council famed nobler skill,
 useful preserve, kill,)
 let me—but oh! ye gracious powers above!
 wrath revenge men gods remove:
 far, far dear every mortal breast,
 sweet soul, honey taste:
 gathering like vapours noxious kind
 fiery blood, darkening mind.
 agamemnon urged deadly hate;
 ’tis past—i quell it; resign fate.
 yes—i will meet murderer friend;
 (if gods ordain it) meet end.
 stroke fate strongest shun:
 great alcides, jove’s unequall’d son,
 juno’s hate, length resign’d breath,
 sunk victim all-conquering death.
 shall achilles fall! stretch’d pale dead,
 grecian hope, trojan dread!
 let me, instant, rush fields,
 reap glory life’s short harvest yields.
 shall force widow’d dame tear
 frantic hands long dishevell’d hair?
 shall force breast heave sighs,
 soft tears trickle eyes?
 yes, shall give fair mournful charms—
 vain hold me—hence! arms! arms!—
 soon shall sanguine torrent spread wide,
 shall know achilles swells tide.”
 
“my (coerulean thetis made reply,
 fate submitting secret sigh,)
 host succour, thy friends save,
 worthy thee; duty brave.
 canst thou, naked, issue plains?
 thy radiant arms trojan foe detains.
 insulting hector bears spoils high,
 vainly glories, fate nigh.
 yet, yet awhile thy generous ardour stay;
 assured, meet thee dawn day,
 charged refulgent arms (a glorious load),
 vulcanian arms, labour god.”
 
turning daughters main,
 goddess thus dismiss’d azure train:
 
“ye sister nereids! deeps descend;
 haste, father’s sacred seat attend;
 go find architect divine,
 vast olympus’ starry summits shine:
 tell hoary sire”—this charge gave:
 sea-green sisters plunge beneath wave:
 thetis ascends bless’d abodes,
 treads brazen threshold gods.
 

[illustration: ] thetis ordering nereids descend sea
 

now greeks furious hector’s force,
 urge broad hellespont headlong course;
 yet chiefs patroclus’ body bore
 safe tempest tented shore.
 horse, foot, equal fury join’d,
 pour’d rear, thunder’d close behind:
 like flame fields ripen’d corn,
 rage hector o’er ranks borne.
 thrice slain hero foot drew;
 thrice skies trojan clamours flew:
 oft ajaces assault sustain;
 check’d, turns; repuls’d, attacks again.
 fiercer shouts lingering troops fires,
 yields step, post retires:
 watchful shepherds strive force, vain,
 hungry lion carcase slain.
 even yet patroclus borne away,
 glories extended day,
 high juno realms air,
 secret, despatch’d trusty messenger.
 various goddess showery bow,
 shot whirlwind shore below;
 great achilles ships came,
 thus began many-colour’d dame:
 
“rise, peleus! rise, divinely brave!
 assist combat, patroclus save:
 slaughter fleet spread,
 fall mutual wounds around dead.
 drag back troy foe contends:
 death rage hector ends:
 prey dogs dooms corse lie,
 marks place fix head high.
 rise, prevent (if yet think fame)
 thy friend’s disgrace, thy eternal shame!”
 
“who sends thee, goddess, ethereal skies?”
 achilles thus. iris thus replies:
 
“i come, pelides! queen jove,
 immortal empress realms above;
 unknown sits remote high,
 unknown synod sky.”
 “thou comest vain (he cries, fury warm’d);
 arms none, can fight unarm’d?
 unwilling am, force stay,
 till thetis bring dawn day
 vulcanian arms: can wield,
 except mighty telamonian shield?
 that, friend’s defence, ajax spread,
 strong lance around heaps dead:
 gallant chief defends menoetius’ son,
 achilles done.”
 
“thy want arms (said iris) well know;
 though unarm’d, yet clad terrors, go!
 let achilles o’er yon trench appear,
 proud troy shall tremble, consent fear;
 greece one glance tremendous eye
 shall take new courage, disdain fly.”
 
spoke, pass’d air. hero rose:
 ægis pallas o’er shoulder throws;
 around brows golden cloud spread;
 stream glory flamed head.
 beleaguer’d town arise
 smokes, high curling shaded skies;
 (seen island, o’er main afar,
 men distress’d hang sign war;)
 soon sun ocean hides rays,
 thick hills flaming beacons blaze;
 long-projected beams seas bright,
 heaven’s high arch reflects ruddy light:
 achilles’ head splendours rise,
 reflecting blaze blaze skies.
 forth march’d chief, distant crowd,
 high rampart raised voice aloud;
 shout minerva swells sound;
 troy starts astonish’d, shores rebound.
 loud trumpet’s brazen mouth far
 shrilling clangour sounds alarm war,
 struck walls, echoes float high,
 round bulwarks thick towers reply;
 high brazen voice hero rear’d:
 hosts dropp’d arms, trembled heard:
 back chariots roll, coursers bound,
 steeds men lie mingled ground.
 aghast see living lightnings play,
 turn eyeballs flashing ray.
 thrice trench dreadful voice raised,
 thrice fled, confounded amazed.
 twelve tumult wedged, untimely rush’d
 spears, chariots crush’d:
 while, shielded darts, greeks obtain
 long-contended carcase slain.
 
lofty bier breathless warrior bears:
 around, sad companions melt tears.
 chief achilles, bending head,
 pours unavailing sorrows o’er dead,
 late triumphant, steeds car,
 sent refulgent field war;
 (unhappy change!) now senseless, pale, found,
 stretch’d forth, gash’d many gaping wound.
 
meantime, unwearied heavenly way,
 ocean’s waves unwilling light day
 quench’d red orb, juno’s high command,
 labours eased achaian band.
 frighted trojans (panting war,
 steeds unharness’d weary car)
 sudden council call’d: chief appear’d
 haste, standing; sit fear’d.
 ’twas now season prolong’d debate;
 saw achilles, fate.
 silent stood: polydamas last,
 skill’d discern future past,
 panthus, thus express’d fears
 (the friend hector, equal years;
 self-same night gave,
 one wise council, one action brave):
 

[illustration: ] juno commanding sun set
 

“in free debate, friends, sentence speak;
 me, move, morning break,
 raise camp: dangerous post,
 far troy walls, naked coast.
 deem’d greece dreadful, engaged
 mutual feuds king hero raged;
 then, hoped armies might prevail
 boldly camp’d beside thousand sail.
 dread pelides now: rage mind
 long continues shores confined,
 fields, long equal fray
 contending nations won lost day;
 troy, troy, shall henceforth strife,
 hard contest fame, life.
 haste ilion, favouring night
 detains terrors, keeps arm fight.
 morrow’s sun behold us here,
 arm, terrors, shall feel, fear;
 hearts now disdain, shall leap joy,
 heaven permit enter troy.
 let fatal prophecy true,
 tremble think, ensue.
 whatever fate, yet let us try
 force thought reason can supply;
 let us counsel guard depend;
 town gates bulwarks shall defend.
 morning dawns, well-appointed powers,
 array’d arms, shall line lofty towers.
 let fierce hero, then, fury calls,
 vent mad vengeance rocky walls,
 fetch thousand circles round plain,
 till spent coursers seek fleet again:
 may rage tired, labour’d down!
 dogs shall tear ere sack town.”
 
“return! (said hector, fired stern disdain)
 what! coop whole armies walls again?
 was’t enough, ye valiant warriors, say,
 nine years imprison’d towers ye lay?
 wide o’er world ilion famed old
 brass exhaustless, mines gold:
 inglorious walls stay’d,
 sunk treasures, stores decay’d;
 phrygians now scatter’d spoils enjoy,
 proud mæonia wastes fruits troy.
 great jove length arms conquest calls,
 shuts grecians wooden walls,
 darest thou dispirit gods incite?
 flies trojan? shall stop flight.
 better counsel attention lend;
 take due refreshment, watch attend.
 one whose riches cost care,
 forth let bring troops share;
 ’tis better generously bestow’d those,
 left plunder country’s foes.
 soon morn purple orient warms,
 fierce yon navy will pour arms.
 great achilles rise might,
 danger: shall stand fight.
 honour, ye gods! let gain give;
 live glorious, whosoe’er shall live!
 mars common lord, alike all;
 oft victor triumphs, fall.”
 
shouting host loud applauses join’d;
 pallas robb’d many mind;
 sense condemn’d, left choose
 worst advice, better refuse.
 
long night extends sable reign,
 around patroclus mourn’d grecian train.
 stern superior grief pelides stood;
 slaughtering arms, used bathe blood,
 now clasp clay-cold limbs: gushing start
 tears, sighs burst swelling heart.
 lion thus, dreadful anguish stung,
 roars desert, demands young;
 grim savage, rifled den
 late returning, snuffs track men,
 o’er vales o’er forest bounds;
 clamorous grief bellowing wood resounds.
 grieves achilles; and, impetuous, vents
 myrmidons loud laments.
 
“in vain promise, gods! engage,
 console menoetius’ feeble age,
 vowed much-loved offspring restore,
 charged rich spoils, fair opuntia’s shore?[252]
 mighty jove cuts short, just disdain,
 long, long views poor designing man!
 one fate warrior friend shall strike,
 troy’s black sands must drink blood alike:
 wretched mother shall deplore,
 aged father never see more!
 yet, patroclus! yet space stay,
 swift pursue thee darksome way.
 ere thy dear relics grave laid,
 shall hector’s head offer’d thy shade;
 that, arms, shall hang thy shrine;
 twelve, noblest trojan line,
 sacred vengeance, hand expire;
 lives effused around thy flaming pyre.
 thus let lie till then! thus, closely press’d,
 bathe thy cold face, sob upon thy breast!
 trojan captives thy mourners stay,
 weep night murmur day:
 spoils arms, thine; when, wasting wide,
 swords kept time, conquer’d side side.”
 
spoke, bade sad attendants round
 cleanse pale corse, wash honour’d wound.
 massy caldron stupendous frame
 brought, placed o’er rising flame:
 heap’d lighted wood; flame divides
 beneath vase, climbs around sides:
 wide womb pour rushing stream;
 boiling water bubbles brim.
 body bathe pious toil,
 embalm wounds, anoint limbs oil,
 high bed state extended laid,
 decent cover’d linen shade;
 last o’er dead milk-white veil threw;
 done, sorrows sighs renew.
 
meanwhile juno, realms above,
 (his wife sister,) spoke almighty jove.
 “at last thy will prevails: great peleus’ son
 rises arms: grace thy greeks won.
 say (for know not), race divine,
 thou mother martial line?”
 
“what words these? (the imperial dame replies,
 anger flash’d majestic eyes)
 succour like mortal arm might lend,
 success mere human wit attend:
 shall i, second power above,
 heaven’s queen, consort thundering jove,
 say, shall one nation’s fate command,
 wreak vengeance one guilty land?”
 

[illustration: ] tripod
 

they. meanwhile silver-footed dame
 reach’d vulcanian dome, eternal frame!
 high-eminent amid works divine,
 heaven’s far-beaming brazen mansions shine.
 lame architect goddess found,
 obscure smoke, forges flaming round,
 bathed sweat fire fire flew;
 puffing loud, roaring billows blew.
 day common task labour claim’d:
 full twenty tripods hall framed,
 placed living wheels massy gold,
 (wondrous tell,) instinct spirit roll’d
 place place, around bless’d abodes
 self-moved, obedient beck gods:
 fair handles now, o’erwrought flowers,
 moulds prepared, glowing ore pours.
 just responsive thought frame
 stood prompt move, azure goddess came:
 charis, spouse, grace divinely fair,
 (with purple fillets round braided hair,)
 observed entering; soft hand press’d,
 and, smiling, thus watery queen address’d:
 
“what, goddess! unusual favour draws?
 hail, welcome! whatsoe’er cause;
 till now stranger, happy hour
 approach, taste dainties bower.”
 

[illustration: ] thetis eurynome receiving infant vulcan
 

high throne, stars silver graced,
 various artifice, queen placed;
 footstool feet: calling, said,
 “vulcan, draw near, ’tis thetis asks aid.”
 “thetis (replied god) powers may claim,
 ever-dear, ever-honour’d name!
 proud mother hurl’d sky,
 (my awkward form, seems, displeased eye,)
 she, eurynome, griefs redress’d,
 soft received silver breast.
 even arts employ’d infant thought:
 chains, bracelets, pendants, toys, wrought.
 nine years kept secret dark abode,
 secure lay, conceal’d man god:
 deep cavern’d rock days led;
 rushing ocean murmur’d o’er head.
 now, since presence glads mansion, say,
 desert service can pay?
 vouchsafe, thetis! board share
 genial rites, hospitable fare;
 labours forge forego,
 bid roaring bellows cease blow.”
 
anvil lame artist rose;
 wide distorted legs oblique goes,
 stills bellows, (in order laid)
 locks chests instruments trade.
 sponge sooty workman dress’d
 brawny arms embrown’d, hairy breast.
 huge sceptre graced, red attire,
 came halting forth sovereign fire:
 monarch’s steps two female forms uphold,
 moved breathed animated gold;
 voice, sense, science given
 works divine (such wonders heaven!)
 supported, unequal gait,
 reach’d throne pensive thetis sate;
 placed beside shining frame,
 thus address’d silver-footed dame:
 
“thee, welcome, goddess! occasion calls
 (so long stranger) honour’d walls?
 ’tis thine, fair thetis, command lay,
 vulcan’s joy duty obey.”
 

[illustration: ] vulcan charis receiving thetis
 

mournful mother thus replies:
 (the crystal drops stood trembling eyes:)
 “o vulcan! say, ever breast divine
 pierced sorrows, o’erwhelm’d mine?
 goddesses, jove prepare
 thetis weight care?
 i, i, watery race
 force subjected man’s embrace,
 who, sinking now age sorrow, pays
 mighty fine imposed length days.
 sprung bed, godlike hero came,
 bravest sure ever bore name;
 like fair plant beneath careful hand
 grew, flourish’d, adorn’d land!
 troy sent him! native shore
 never, ah never, shall receive more;
 (even lives, wastes secret woe;)
 i, goddess, can retard blow!
 robb’d prize grecian suffrage gave,
 king nations forced royal slave:
 grieved; and, till greeks oppress’d
 required arm, sorrow’d unredress’d.
 large gifts promise, elders send;
 vain—he arms not, permits friend
 arms, steeds, forces employ:
 marches, combats, almost conquers troy:
 slain phœbus (hector name)
 resigns armour, life, fame.
 thou, pity, prayer won:
 grace immortal arms short-lived son,
 field martial pomp restore,
 shine glory, till shines more!”
 
artist-god: “thy griefs resign,
 secure, vulcan can, ever thine.
 hide fates, well,
 hands cruel stroke repel,
 shall forge envied arms, gaze
 wondering ages, world’s amaze!”
 
thus said, father fires
 black labours forge retires.
 soon bade blow, bellows turn’d
 iron mouths; furnace burn’d,
 resounding breathed: blast expires,
 twenty forges catch fires;
 just god directs, now loud, now low,
 raise tempest, gently blow;
 hissing flames huge silver bars roll’d,
 stubborn brass, tin, solid gold;
 before, deep fix’d, eternal anvils stand;
 ponderous hammer loads better hand,
 left tongs turns vex’d metal round,
 thick, strong strokes, doubling vaults rebound.
 
first form’d immense solid shield;
 rich various artifice emblazed field;
 utmost verge threefold circle bound;[253]
 silver chain suspends massy round;
 five ample plates broad expanse compose,
 godlike labours surface rose.
 shone image master-mind:
 earth, heaven, ocean design’d;
 unwearied sun, moon completely round;
 starry lights heaven’s high convex crown’d;
 pleiads, hyads, northern team;
 great orion’s refulgent beam;
 which, around axle sky,
 bear, revolving, points golden eye,
 still shines exalted ethereal plain,
 bathes blazing forehead main.
 
two cities radiant shield appear,
 image one peace, one war.
 sacred pomp genial feast delight,
 solemn dance, hymeneal rite;
 along street new-made brides led,
 torches flaming, nuptial bed:
 youthful dancers circle bound
 soft flute, cithern’s silver sound:
 fair streets matrons row
 stand porches, enjoy show.
 
forum swarm numerous train;
 subject debate, townsman slain:
 one pleads fine discharged, one denied,
 bade public laws decide:
 witness produced either hand:
 this, that, partial people stand:
 appointed heralds still noisy bands,
 form ring, sceptres hands:
 seats stone, within sacred place,[254]
 reverend elders nodded o’er case;
 alternate, attesting sceptre took,
 rising solemn, sentence spoke.
 two golden talents lay amidst, sight,
 prize best adjudged right.
 
another part (a prospect differing far)[255]
 glow’d refulgent arms, horrid war.
 two mighty hosts leaguer’d town embrace,
 one pillage, one burn place.
 meantime townsmen, arm’d silent care,
 secret ambush foe prepare:
 wives, children, watchful band
 trembling parents, turrets stand.
 march; pallas mars made bold:
 gold gods, radiant garments gold,
 gold armour: squadron led,
 august, divine, superior head!
 place ambush fit found, stood,
 cover’d shields, beside silver flood.
 two spies distance lurk, watchful seem
 sheep oxen seek winding stream.
 soon white flocks proceeded o’er plains,
 steers slow-moving, two shepherd swains;
 behind piping reeds go,
 fear ambush, suspect foe.
 arms glittering squadron rising round
 rush sudden; hills slaughter heap ground;
 whole flocks herds lie bleeding plains,
 and, amidst them, dead, shepherd swains!
 bellowing oxen besiegers hear;
 rise, take horse, approach, meet war,
 fight, fall, beside silver flood;
 waving silver seem’d blush blood.
 tumult, contention stood confess’d;
 one rear’d dagger captive’s breast;
 one held living foe, freshly bled
 new-made wounds; another dragg’d dead;
 now here, now there, carcases tore:
 fate stalk’d amidst them, grim human gore.
 whole war came out, met eye;
 bold figure seem’d live die.
 
field deep furrow’d next god design’d,[256]
 third time labour’d sweating hind;
 shining shares full many ploughmen guide,
 turn crooked yokes every side.
 still either end wheel around,
 master meets goblet crown’d;
 hearty draught rewards, renews toil,
 back turning ploughshares cleave soil:
 behind, rising earth ridges roll’d;
 sable look’d, though form’d molten gold.
 
another field rose high waving grain;
 bended sickles stand reaper train:
 stretched ranks levell’d swarths found,
 sheaves heap’d sheaves thicken ground.
 sweeping stroke mowers strow lands;
 gatherers follow, collect bands;
 last children, whose arms borne
 (too short gripe them) brown sheaves corn.
 rustic monarch field descries,
 silent glee, heaps around rise.
 ready banquet turf laid,
 beneath ample oak’s expanded shade.
 victim ox sturdy youth prepare;
 reaper’s due repast, woman’s care.
 
next, ripe yellow gold, vineyard shines,
 bent ponderous harvest vines;
 deeper dye dangling clusters show,
 curl’d silver props, order glow:
 darker metal mix’d intrench’d place;
 pales glittering tin inclosure grace.
 this, one pathway gently winding leads,
 march train baskets heads,
 (fair maids blooming youths,) smiling bear
 purple product autumnal year.
 youth awakes warbling strings,
 whose tender lay fate linus sings;
 measured dance behind move train,
 tune soft voice, answer strain.
 
herds oxen march, erect bold,
 rear high horns, seem low gold,
 speed meadows whose sounding shores
 rapid torrent rushes roars:
 four golden herdsmen guardians stand,
 nine sour dogs complete rustic band.
 two lions rushing wood appear’d;
 seized bull, master herd:
 roar’d: vain dogs, men withstood;
 tore flesh, drank sable blood.
 dogs (oft cheer’d vain) desert prey,
 dread grim terrors, distance bay.
 
next this, eye art vulcan leads
 deep fair forests, length meads,
 stalls, folds, scatter’d cots between;
 fleecy flocks, whiten scene.
 
figured dance succeeds; seen
 lofty gnossus cretan queen,
 form’d daedalean art; comely band
 youths maidens, bounding hand hand.
 maids soft simars linen dress’d;
 youths graceful glossy vest:
 locks flowery wreath inroll’d;
 sides adorn’d swords gold,
 glittering gay, silver belts depend.
 now rise, descend,
 well-taught feet: now shape oblique ways,
 confusedly regular, moving maze:
 now forth once, swift sight, spring,
 undistinguish’d blend flying ring:
 whirls wheel, giddy circle toss’d,
 and, rapid runs, single spokes lost.
 gazing multitudes admire around:
 two active tumblers centre bound;
 now high, now low, pliant limbs bend:
 general songs sprightly revel end.
 
thus broad shield complete artist crown’d
 last hand, pour’d ocean round:
 living silver seem’d waves roll,
 beat buckler’s verge, bound whole.
 
done, whate’er warrior’s use requires
 forged; cuirass outshone fires,
 greaves ductile tin, helm impress’d
 various sculpture, golden crest.
 thetis’ feet finished labour lay:
 she, falcon cuts aerial way,
 swift olympus’ snowy summit flies,
 bears blazing present skies.[257]
 



book xix.
 

argument.
 

reconciliation achilles agamemnon.
 

thetis brings armour made vulcan. preserves the
 body friend corruption, commands assemble the
 army, declare resentment end. agamemnon achilles are
 solemnly reconciled: speeches, presents, ceremonies that
 occasion. achilles great difficulty persuaded refrain from
 battle till troops refreshed advice of
 ulysses. presents conveyed tent achilles, where
 briseïs laments body patroclus. hero obstinately
 refuses repast, gives lamentations his
 friend. minerva descends strengthen him, order jupiter. he
 arms fight: appearance described. addresses to
 horses, reproaches death patroclus. one of
 miraculously endued voice, inspired prophesy his
 fate: hero, astonished prodigy, rushes fury to
 combat.
 thirtieth day. scene sea-shore.
 

soon aurora heaved orient head
 waves, blush’d early red,
 (with new-born day gladden mortal sight,
 gild courts heaven sacred light,)
 immortal arms goddess-mother bears
 swift son: finds tears
 stretch’d o’er patroclus’ corse; rest
 sovereign’s sorrows express’d.
 ray divine heavenly presence shed,
 thus, hand soft touching, thetis said:
 
“suppress, son, rage grief, know
 man, heaven, gave blow;
 behold arms vulcan bestow’d,
 arms worthy thee, fit grace god.”
 
drops radiant burden ground;
 clang strong arms, ring shores around;
 back shrink myrmidons dread surprise,
 broad effulgence turn eyes.
 unmoved hero kindles show,
 feels rage divine bosom glow;
 fierce eyeballs living flames expire,
 flash incessant like stream fire:
 turns radiant gift: feeds mind
 immortal artist design’d.
 
“goddess! (he cried,) glorious arms, shine
 matchless art, confess hand divine.
 now bloody battle let bend:
 ah! relics slaughter’d friend!
 wide wounds spirit fled,
 shall flies, worms obscene, pollute dead?”
 
“that unavailing care laid aside,
 (the azure goddess replied,)
 whole years untouch’d, uninjured shall remain,
 fresh life, carcase slain.
 go, achilles, affairs require,
 grecian peers renounce thine ire:
 uncontroll’d boundless war engage,
 heaven strength supply mighty rage!”
 

[illustration: ] thetis bringing armour achilles
 

nostrils slain pour’d
 nectareous drops, rich ambrosia shower’d
 o’er corse. flies forbid prey,
 untouch’d rests, sacred decay.
 achilles strand obedient went:
 shores resounded voice sent.
 heroes heard, naval train
 tend ships, guide o’er main,
 alarm’d, transported, well-known sound,
 frequent full, great assembly crown’d;
 studious see terror plain,
 long lost battle, shine arms again.
 tydides ulysses first appear,
 lame wounds, leaning spear;
 sacred seats council placed,
 king men, atrides, came last:
 sore wounded agenor’s son.
 achilles (rising midst) begun:
 
“o monarch! better far fate
 thee, me, grecian state,
 (ere day mad passion sway’d,
 rash contended black-eyed maid)
 preventing dian despatch’d dart,
 shot shining mischief heart!
 many hero press’d shore,
 troy’s glad fields fatten’d gore.
 long, long shall greece woes caused bewail,
 sad posterity repeat tale.
 this, subject debate,
 past, forgotten, resign’d fate.
 should, alas, mortal man, i,
 burn fury can never die?
 anger ends: let war succeed,
 even greece bled, let ilion bleed.
 now call hosts, try sight
 troy yet shall dare camp second night!
 deem, mightiest, arm knows,
 shall ’scape transport, joy repose.”
 
said: finish’d wrath loud acclaim
 greeks accept, shout pelides’ name.
 thus, rising lofty throne,
 state unmoved, king men begun:
 
“hear me, ye sons greece! silence hear!
 grant monarch impartial ear:
 awhile loud, untimely joy suspend,
 let rash, injurious clamours end:
 unruly murmurs, ill-timed applause,
 wrong best speaker, justest cause.
 charge me, ye greeks, dire debate:
 know, angry jove, all-compelling fate,
 fell erinnys, urged wrath day
 achilles’ arms forced prey.
 will heaven?
 myself, vengeful ate driven;
 she, jove’s dread daughter, fated infest
 race mortals, enter’d breast.
 ground haughty fury treads,
 prints lofty footsteps heads
 mighty men; inflicting goes
 long-festering wounds, inextricable woes!
 old, stalk’d amid bright abodes;
 jove himself, sire men gods,
 world’s great ruler, felt venom’d dart;
 deceived juno’s wiles, female art:
 alcmena’s nine long months run,
 jove expected immortal son,
 gods goddesses unruly joy
 show’d, vaunted matchless boy:
 ‘from us, (he said) day infant springs,
 fated rule, born king kings.’
 saturnia ask’d oath, vouch truth,
 fix dominion favour’d youth.
 thunderer, unsuspicious fraud,
 pronounced solemn words bind god.
 joyful goddess, olympus’ height,
 swift achaian argos bent flight:
 scarce seven moons gone, lay sthenelus’s wife;
 push’d lingering infant life:
 charms alcmena’s coming labours stay,
 stop babe, just issuing day.
 bids saturnius bear oath mind;
 ‘a youth (said she) jove’s immortal kind
 day born: sthenelus springs,
 claims thy promise king kings.’
 grief seized thunderer, oath engaged;
 stung soul, sorrow’d, raged.
 ambrosial head, perch’d sate,
 snatch’d fury-goddess debate,
 dread, irrevocable oath swore,
 immortal seats ne’er behold more;
 whirl’d headlong down, ever driven
 bright olympus starry heaven:
 thence nether world fury fell;
 ordain’d man’s contentious race dwell.
 full oft god son’s hard toils bemoan’d,
 cursed dire fury, secret groan’d.[258]
 even thus, like jove himself, misled,
 raging hector heap’d camps dead.
 can errors rage atone?
 martial troops, treasures thy own:
 instant navy shall sent
 whate’er ulysses promised thy tent:
 thou! appeased, propitious prayer,
 resume thy arms, shine war.”
 
“o king nations! whose superior sway
 (returns achilles) hosts obey!
 keep send presents, thy care;
 us, ’tis equal: ask war.
 yet talk, instant shun
 fight, glorious work remains undone.
 let every greek, sees spear confound
 trojan ranks, deal destruction round,
 emulation, act survey,
 learn thence business day.”
 
peleus thus; thus replies
 great councils, ithacus wise:
 “though, godlike, thou art toils oppress’d,
 least armies claim repast rest:
 long laborious must combat be,
 gods inspired, led thee.
 strength derived spirits blood,
 augment generous wine food:
 boastful war, without stay,
 can last hero single day?
 courage may prompt; but, ebbing strength,
 mere unsupported man must yield length;
 shrunk dry famine, toils declined,
 drooping body will desert mind:
 built anew strength-conferring fare,
 limbs soul untamed, tires war.
 dismiss people, then, give command,
 strong repast hearten every band;
 let presents achilles made,
 full assembly greece laid.
 king men shall rise public sight,
 solemn swear (observant rite)
 that, spotless, came, maid removes,
 pure arms, guiltless loves.
 done, sumptuous banquet shall made,
 full price injured honour paid.
 stretch henceforth, prince! thy sovereign might
 beyond bounds reason right;
 ’tis chief praise e’er kings belong’d,
 right justice power wrong’d.”
 
monarch: “just thy decree,
 thy words give joy, wisdom breathes thee.
 due atonement gladly prepare;
 heaven regard justly swear!
 awhile let greece assembled stay,
 great achilles grudge short delay.
 till fleet presents convey’d,
 jove attesting, firm compact made.
 train noble youths charge shall bear;
 select, ulysses, thy care:
 order rank’d let gifts appear,
 fair train captives close rear:
 talthybius shall victim boar convey,
 sacred jove, yon bright orb day.”
 
“for (the stern Æacides replies)
 less important season may suffice,
 stern fury war o’er,
 wrath, extinguish’d, burns breast more.
 hector slain, faces sky,
 grim gaping wounds, heroes lie:
 call war! might voice incite,
 now, now, instant, shall commence fight:
 then, day’s complete, let generous bowls,
 copious banquets, glad weary souls.
 let palate know taste food,
 till insatiate rage cloy’d blood:
 pale lies friend, wounds disfigured o’er,
 cold feet pointed door.
 revenge soul! meaner care,
 interest, thought, room harbour there;
 destruction feast, mortal wounds,
 scenes blood, agonizing sounds.”
 
“o first greeks, (ulysses thus rejoin’d,)
 best bravest warrior kind!
 thy praise dreadful camps shine,
 old experience calm wisdom mine.
 hear counsel, reason yield,
 bravest soon satiate field;
 though vast heaps strow crimson plain,
 bloody harvest brings little gain:
 scale conquest ever wavering lies,
 great jove turns it, victor dies!
 great, bold, thousands daily fall,
 endless grief, weep all.
 eternal sorrows avails shed?
 greece honours solemn fasts dead:
 enough, death demands brave, pay
 tribute melancholy day.
 one chief patience grave resign’d,
 care devolves others left behind.
 let generous food supplies strength produce,
 let rising spirits flow sprightly juice,
 let warm heads scenes battle glow,
 pour new furies feebler foe.
 yet short interval, none shall dare
 expect second summons war;
 waits that, dire effects shall find,
 trembling ships lags behind.
 embodied, battle let us bend,
 haughty troy descend.”
 
now delegates ulysses sent,
 bear presents royal tent:
 sons nestor, phyleus’ valiant heir,
 thias merion, thunderbolts war,
 lycomedes creiontian strain,
 melanippus, form’d chosen train.
 swift word given, youths obey’d:
 twice ten bright vases midst laid;
 row six fair tripods succeeds;
 twice number high-bounding steeds:
 seven captives next lovely line compose;
 eighth briseïs, like blooming rose,
 closed bright band: great ithacus, before,
 first train, golden talents bore:
 rest public view chiefs dispose,
 splendid scene! agamemnon rose:
 boar talthybius held: grecian lord
 drew broad cutlass sheath’d beside sword:
 stubborn bristles victim’s brow
 crops, offering meditates vow.
 hands uplifted attesting skies,
 heaven’s broad marble roof fixed eyes.
 solemn words deep attention draw,
 greece around sat thrill’d sacred awe.
 
“witness thou first! thou greatest power above,
 all-good, all-wise, all-surveying jove!
 mother-earth, heaven’s revolving light,
 ye, fell furies realms night,
 rule dead, horrid woes prepare
 perjured kings, falsely swear!
 black-eyed maid inviolate removes,
 pure unconscious manly loves.
 false, heaven vengeance shed,
 levell’d thunder strike guilty head!”
 
that, weapon deep inflicts wound;
 bleeding savage tumbles ground;
 sacred herald rolls victim slain
 (a feast fish) foaming main.
 
thus achilles: “hear, ye greeks! know
 whate’er feel, ’tis jove inflicts woe;
 else atrides rage inflame,
 arms, unwilling, force dame.
 ’twas jove’s high will alone, o’erruling all,
 doom’d strife, doom’d greeks fall.
 go then, ye chiefs! indulge genial rite;
 achilles waits ye, expects fight.”
 
speedy council word adjourn’d:
 black vessels greeks return’d.
 achilles sought tent. train before
 march’d onward, bending gifts bore.
 tents squires industrious spread:
 foaming coursers stalls led;
 new seats female captives move.
 briseïs, radiant queen love,
 slow pass’d, beheld sad survey
 where, gash’d cruel wounds, patroclus lay.
 prone body fell heavenly fair,
 beat sad breast, tore golden hair;
 beautiful grief, humid eyes
 shining tears lifts, thus cries:
 
“ah, youth ever dear, ever kind,
 tender friend distracted mind!
 left thee fresh life, beauty gay;
 now find thee cold, inanimated clay!
 woes wretched race life attend!
 sorrows sorrows, never doom’d end!
 first loved consort virgin bed
 eyes fatal battle bled:
 three brave brothers one mournful day
 trod dark, irremeable way:
 thy friendly hand uprear’d plain,
 dried sorrows husband slain;
 achilles’ care promised prove,
 first, dearest partner love;
 rites divine ratify band,
 make empress native land.
 accept grateful tears! thee flow,
 thee, ever felt another’s woe!”
 
sister captives echoed groan groan,
 mourn’d patroclus’ fortunes, own.
 leaders press’d chief every side;
 unmoved heard them, sighs denied.
 
“if yet achilles friend, whose care
 bent please him, request forbear;
 till yonder sun descend, ah, let pay
 grief anguish one abstemious day.”
 
spoke, warriors turn’d face:
 yet still brother-kings atreus’ race.
 nestor, idomeneus, ulysses sage,
 phœnix, strive calm grief rage:
 rage calm not, grief control;
 groans, raves, sorrows soul.
 
“thou too, patroclus! (thus heart vents)
 spread inviting banquet tents:
 thy sweet society, thy winning care,
 stay’d achilles, rushing war.
 now, alas! death’s cold arms resign’d,
 banquet revenge can glad mind?
 greater sorrow afflict breast,
 hoary peleus deceased?
 now, perhaps, phthia dreads hear
 son’s sad fate, drops tender tear.
 more, neoptolemus brave,
 offspring, sink grave?
 yet offspring lives; (i distant far,
 neglectful, wage hateful war.)
 this, cruel stroke attend;
 fate claim’d achilles, might spare friend.
 hoped patroclus might survive, rear
 tender orphan parent’s care,
 scyros’ isle conduct o’er main,
 glad eyes paternal reign,
 lofty palace, large domain.
 peleus breathes vital air;
 drags wretched life age care,
 till news sad fate invades
 hastening soul, sinks shades.”
 
sighing said: grief heroes join’d,
 stole tear left behind.
 mingled grief sire heaven survey’d,
 thus pity blue-eyed maid:
 
“is achilles now thy care,
 dost thou thus desert great war?
 lo, yon sails canvas wings extend,
 comfortless sits, wails friend:
 ere thirst want forces oppress’d,
 haste infuse ambrosia breast.”
 
spoke; sudden, word jove,
 shot descending goddess above.
 swift ether shrill harpy springs,
 wide air floating ample wings,
 great achilles flight address’d,
 pour’d divine ambrosia breast,[259]
 nectar sweet, (refection gods!)
 then, swift ascending, sought bright abodes.
 
now issued ships warrior-train,
 like deluge pour’d upon plain.
 piercing blasts boreas blow,
 scatter o’er fields driving snow;
 dusky clouds fleecy winter flies,
 whose dazzling lustre whitens skies:
 helms succeeding helms, shields shields,
 catch quick beams, brighten fields;
 broad glittering breastplates, spears pointed rays,
 mix one stream, reflecting blaze blaze;
 thick beats centre coursers bound;
 splendour flame skies, laugh fields around,
 
full midst, high-towering o’er rest,
 limbs arms divine achilles dress’d;
 arms father fire bestow’d,
 forged eternal anvils god.
 grief revenge furious heart inspire,
 glowing eyeballs roll living fire;
 grinds teeth, furious delay
 o’erlooks embattled host, hopes bloody day.
 
silver cuishes first thighs infold;
 o’er breast braced hollow gold;
 brazen sword various baldric tied,
 that, starr’d gems, hung glittering side;
 and, like moon, broad refulgent shield
 blazed long rays, gleam’d athwart field.
 
night-wandering sailors, pale fears,
 wide o’er watery waste, light appears,
 far-seen mountain blazing high,
 streams lonely watch-tower sky:
 mournful eyes gaze, gaze again;
 loud howls storm, drives o’er main.
 
next, high head helmet graced; behind
 sweepy crest hung floating wind:
 like red star, flaming hair
 shakes diseases, pestilence, war;
 stream’d golden honours head,
 trembled sparkling plumes, loose glories shed.
 chief beholds wondering eyes;
 arms poises, motions tries;
 buoy’d inward force, seems swim,
 feels pinion lifting every limb.
 
now shakes great paternal spear,
 ponderous huge, greek rear,
 pelion’s cloudy top ash entire
 old chiron fell’d, shaped sire;
 spear stern achilles wields,
 death heroes, dread fields.
 
automedon alcimus prepare
 immortal coursers, radiant car;
 (the silver traces sweeping side;)
 fiery mouths resplendent bridles tied;
 ivory-studded reins, return’d behind,
 waved o’er backs, chariot join’d.
 charioteer whirl’d lash around,
 swift ascended one active bound.
 bright heavenly arms, squire
 achilles mounts, sets field fire;
 brighter phœbus ethereal way
 flames chariot, restores day.
 high o’er host, terrible stands,
 thunders steeds dread commands:
 
“xanthus balius! podarges’ strain,
 (unless ye boast heavenly race vain,)
 swift, mindful load ye bear,
 learn make master care:
 falling squadrons bear slaughtering sword,
 nor, ye left patroclus, leave lord.”
 
generous xanthus, words said,
 seem’d sensible woe, droop’d head:
 trembling stood golden wain,
 bow’d dust honours mane.
 when, strange tell! (so juno will’d) broke
 eternal silence, portentous spoke.
 “achilles! yes! day least bear
 thy rage safety files war:
 come will, fatal time must come,
 fault, god decrees thy doom.
 crime, slowness course,
 fell thy patroclus, heavenly force;
 bright far-shooting god gilds day
 (confess’d saw him) tore arms away.
 no—could swiftness o’er winds prevail,
 beat pinions western gale,
 vain—the fates thy death demand,
 due mortal immortal hand.”
 
ceased ever, furies tied,
 fateful voice. intrepid chief replied
 unabated rage—“so let be!
 portents prodigies lost me.
 know fate: die, see more
 much-loved parents, native shore—
 enough—when heaven ordains, sink night:
 now perish troy!” said, rush’d fight.

book xx.
 

argument.
 

battle gods, acts achilles.
 

jupiter, upon achilles’ return battle, calls council the
 gods, permits assist either party. terrors the
 combat described, deities engaged. apollo encourages Æneas
 meet achilles. long conversation, two heroes
 encounter; Æneas preserved assistance neptune.
 achilles falls upon rest trojans, upon point of
 killing hector, apollo conveys away cloud. achilles
 pursues trojans great slaughter.
 day continues. scene field troy.
 

thus round pelides breathing war blood
 greece, sheathed arms, beside vessels stood;
 near impending neighbouring height,
 troy’s black battalions wait shock fight.
 jove themis gives command, call
 gods council starry hall:
 swift o’er olympus’ hundred hills flies,
 summons senate skies.
 shining on, long procession come
 jove’s eternal adamantine dome.
 one absent, rural power
 haunts verdant gloom, rosy bower;
 fair-hair’d dryad shady wood,
 azure sister silver flood;
 old ocean, hoary sire! keeps
 ancient seat beneath sacred deeps.
 marble thrones, lucid columns crown’d,
 (the work vulcan,) sat powers around.
 even whose trident sways watery reign
 heard loud summons, forsook main,
 assumed throne amid bright abodes,
 question’d thus sire men gods:
 
“what moves god heaven earth commands,
 grasps thunder awful hands,
 thus convene whole ethereal state?
 greece troy subject debate?
 already met, louring hosts appear,
 death stands ardent edge war.”
 
“’tis true (the cloud-compelling power replies)
 day call council skies
 care human race; even jove’s eye
 sees regret unhappy mortals die.
 far olympus’ top secret state
 ourself will sit, see hand fate
 work will. celestial powers! descend,
 minds direct, succour lend
 either host. troy soon must lie o’erthrown,
 uncontroll’d achilles fights alone:
 troops lately durst meet eyes;
 can now, rage rise?
 assist them, gods! ilion’s sacred wall
 may fall day, though fate forbids fall.”
 said, fired heavenly breasts rage.
 
adverse parts warring gods engage:
 heaven’s awful queen; whose azure round
 girds vast globe; maid arms renown’d;
 hermes, profitable arts sire;
 vulcan, black sovereign fire:
 fleet repair instant flight;
 vessels tremble gods alight.
 aid troy, latona, phœbus came,
 mars fiery-helm’d, laughter-loving dame,
 xanthus, whose streams golden currents flow,
 chaste huntress silver bow.
 ere yet gods various aid employ,
 argive bosom swell’d manly joy,
 great achilles (terror plain),
 long lost battle, shone arms again.
 dreadful stood front host;
 pale troy beheld, seem’d already lost;
 bravest heroes pant inward fear,
 trembling see another god war.
 
powers descending swell’d fight,
 tumult rose: fierce rage pale affright
 varied face: discord sounds alarms,
 earth echoes, nations rush arms.
 now trembling shores minerva calls,
 now thunders grecian walls.
 mars hovering o’er troy, terror shrouds
 gloomy tempests, night clouds:
 now trojan heart fury pours
 voice divine, ilion’s topmost towers:
 now shouts simois, beauteous hill;
 mountain shook, rapid stream stood still.
 
above, sire gods thunder rolls,
 peals peals redoubled rend poles.
 beneath, stern neptune shakes solid ground;
 forests wave, mountains nod around;
 summits tremble ida’s woods,
 sources boil hundred floods.
 troy’s turrets totter rocking plain,
 toss’d navies beat heaving main.
 deep dismal regions dead,[260]
 infernal monarch rear’d horrid head,
 leap’d throne, lest neptune’s arm lay
 dark dominions open day,
 pour light pluto’s drear abodes,
 abhorr’d men, dreadful even gods.[261]
 

[illustration: ] gods descending battle
 

war immortals wage; horrors rend
 world’s vast concave, gods contend.
 first silver-shafted phœbus took plain
 blue neptune, monarch main.
 god arms giant bulk display’d,
 opposed pallas, war’s triumphant maid.
 latona march’d may.
 quiver’d dian, sister day,
 (her golden arrows sounding side,)
 saturnia, majesty heaven, defied.
 fiery vulcan last battle stands
 sacred flood rolls golden sands;
 xanthus name heavenly birth,
 called scamander sons earth.
 
thus gods various league engage,
 achilles glow’d mortal rage:
 hector sought; search hector turn’d
 eyes around, hector burn’d;
 burst like lightning ranks, vow’d
 glut god battles blood.
 
Æneas first dared stay;
 apollo wedged warrior’s way,
 swell’d bosom undaunted might,
 half-forced half-persuaded fight.
 like young lycaon, royal line,
 voice aspect, seem’d power divine;
 bade chief reflect, late scorn
 distant threats braved goddess-born.
 
thus hero anchises’ strain:
 “to meet pelides persuade vain:
 already met, void fear
 observed fury flying spear;
 ida’s woods chased us field,
 force scattered, herds kill’d;
 lyrnessus, pedasus ashes lay;
 (jove assisting) survived day:
 else sunk oppress’d fatal fight
 fierce achilles minerva’s might.
 where’er moved, goddess shone before,
 bathed brazen lance hostile gore.
 mortal man achilles can sustain?
 immortals guard dreadful plain,
 suffer dart fall vain.
 god aid, arm check power,
 though strong battle brazen tower.”
 
jove: “that god implore,
 great achilles before.
 heavenly venus thou deriv’st thy strain,
 sister main;
 aged sea-god father line;
 jove sacred source thine.
 lift thy weapon noble blow,
 fear vaunting mortal foe.”
 
said, spirit breathed breast,
 thick troops embolden’d hero press’d:
 venturous act white-arm’d queen survey’d,
 thus, assembling powers, said:
 
“behold action, gods! claims care,
 great Æneas rushing war!
 pelides directs course,
 phœbus impels, phœbus gives force.
 restrain bold career; least, attend
 favour’d hero, let power descend.
 guard life, add renown,
 we, great armament heaven, came down.
 hereafter let fall, fates design,
 spun short life’s illustrious line:[262]
 lest adverse god now cross way,
 give know powers assist day:
 shall mortal stand dire alarms,
 heaven’s refulgent host appear arms?”[263]
 
thus she; thus god whose force can make
 solid globe’s eternal basis shake:
 “against might man, feeble known,
 celestial powers exert own?
 suffice yonder mount view scene,
 leave war fates mortal men.
 armipotent, god light,
 obstruct achilles, commence fight,
 thence gods troy swift descend:
 full soon, doubt not, shall conflict end;
 these, ruin confusion hurl’d,
 yield conquering arms lower world.”
 
thus said, tyrant sea,
 coerulean neptune, rose, led way.
 advanced upon field stood mound
 earth congested, wall’d, trench’d around;
 elder times guard alcides made,
 (the work trojans, minerva’s aid,)
 time vengeful monster main
 swept wide shore, drove plain.
 
neptune gods greece repair,
 clouds encompass’d, veil air:
 adverse powers, around apollo laid,
 crown fair hills silver simois shade.
 circle close heavenly party sat,
 intent form future scheme fate;
 mix yet fight, though jove high
 gives loud signal, heavens reply.
 
meanwhile rushing armies hide ground;
 trampled centre yields hollow sound:
 steeds cased mail, chiefs armour bright,
 gleaming champaign glows brazen light.
 amid hosts (a dreadful space) appear,
 great achilles; bold Æneas, here.
 towering strides Æneas first advanced;
 nodding plumage helmet danced:
 spread o’er breast fencing shield bore,
 and, moved, javelin flamed before.
 pelides; furious engage,
 rush’d impetuous. lion’s rage,
 viewing first foes scornful eyes,
 though arms peopled city rise,
 stalks careless on, unregarding pride;
 till length, brave youth defied,
 bold spear savage turns alone,
 murmurs fury hollow groan;
 grins, foams, rolls eyes around,
 lash’d tail heaving sides resound;
 calls rage; grinds teeth,
 resolved vengeance, resolved death.
 fierce achilles Æneas flies;
 stands Æneas, force defies.
 ere yet stern encounter join’d, begun
 seed thetis thus venus’ son:
 
“why comes Æneas ranks far?
 seeks meet achilles’ arm war,
 hope realms priam enjoy,
 prove merits throne troy?
 grant beneath thy lance achilles dies,
 partial monarch may refuse prize;
 sons many; thy pride may quell:
 ’tis fault love sons well,
 or, reward thy victorious hand,
 troy proposed spacious tract land,
 ample forest, fair domain,
 hills vines, arable grain?
 even this, perhaps, will hardly prove thy lot.
 can achilles soon forgot?
 (as think) saw brandish’d spear,
