 great Æneas seem’d fear:
 hearty haste ida’s mount fled,
 nor, till reach’d lyrnessus, turn’d head.
 lofty walls long progress stay’d;
 those, pallas, jove, we, ruins laid:
 grecian chains captive race cast;
 ’tis true, great Æneas fled fast.
 defrauded conquest before,
 lost, gods day restore.
 go; thou may’st, avoid threaten’d fate;
 fools stay feel it, wise late.”
 
anchises’ son: “such words employ
 one fears thee, unwarlike boy;
 disdain; best may defied
 mean reproaches, unmanly pride;
 unworthy high race came
 proclaim’d loudly voice fame:
 illustrious fathers draws line;
 goddess-born; half human, half divine.
 thetis’ day, venus’ offspring dies,
 tears shall trickle celestial eyes:
 two heroes, thus derived, contend,
 ’tis words glorious strife can end.
 yet thou seek learn birth
 (a tale resounded spacious earth)
 hear glorious origin prove
 ancient dardanus, first jove:
 dardania’s walls raised; ilion, then,
 (the city since many-languaged men,)
 not. natives content till
 shady foot ida’s fountful hill.[264]
 dardanus great erichthonius springs,
 richest, once, asia’s wealthy kings;
 three thousand mares spacious pastures bred,
 three thousand foals beside mothers fed.
 boreas, enamour’d sprightly train,
 conceal’d godhead flowing mane,
 voice dissembled loves neigh’d,
 coursed dappled beauties o’er mead:
 hence sprung twelve others unrivall’d kind,
 swift mother mares, father wind.
 lightly skimming, swept plain,
 plied grass, bent tender grain;
 along level seas flew,[265]
 scarce surface curl’d briny dew.
 erichthonius was: came
 sacred tros, trojan name.
 three sons renown’d adorn’d nuptial bed,
 ilus, assaracus, ganymed:
 matchless ganymed, divinely fair,
 heaven, enamour’d, snatch’d upper air,
 bear cup jove (ethereal guest,
 grace glory ambrosial feast).
 two remaining sons line divide:
 first rose laomedon ilus’ side;
 tithonus, now cares grown old,
 priam, bless’d hector, brave bold;
 clytius lampus, ever-honour’d pair;
 hicetaon, thunderbolt war.
 great assaracus sprang capys, he
 begat anchises, anchises me.
 race: ’tis fortune gives us birth,
 jove alone endues soul worth:
 he, source power might! boundless sway,
 human courage gives, takes away.
 long field words may contend,
 reproach infinite, knows end,
 arm’d truth falsehood, right wrong;
 voluble weapon tongue;
 wounded, wound; neither side can fail,
 every man equal strength rail:
 women alone, streets jar,
 perhaps excel us wordy war;
 like us stand, encompass’d crowd,
 vent anger impotent loud.
 cease then—our business field fight
 question, prove might.
 insults thou hast offer’d here,
 receive answer: ’tis flying spear.”
 
spoke. force javelin flung,
 fix’d deep, loudly buckler rung.
 far outstretch’d arm, pelides held
 (to meet thundering lance) dreadful shield,
 trembled stuck; void fear
 saw, ere fell, immeasurable spear.
 fears vain; impenetrable charms
 secured temper ethereal arms.
 two strong plates point passage held,
 stopp’d, rested, third repell’d.
 five plates various metal, various mould,
 composed shield; brass outward fold,
 tin inward, middle gold:
 stuck lance. rising ere threw,
 forceful spear great achilles flew,
 pierced dardan shield’s extremest bound,
 shrill brass return’d sharper sound:
 thin verge pelean weapon glides,
 slight covering expanded hides.
 Æneas contracted body bends,
 o’er high riven targe extends,
 sees, parting plates, upper air,
 back perceives quivering spear:
 fate near him, chills soul fright;
 swims eyes many-colour’d light.
 achilles, rushing dreadful cries,
 draws broad blade, Æneas flies:
 Æneas rousing foe came on,
 force collected, heaves mighty stone:
 mass enormous! modern days
 two earth’s degenerate sons raise.
 ocean’s god, whose earthquakes rock ground
 saw distress, moved powers around:
 
“lo! brink fate Æneas stands,
 instant victim achilles’ hands;
 phœbus urged; phœbus bestow’d
 aid vain: man o’erpowers god.
 can ye see righteous chief atone
 guiltless blood vices own?
 gods constant vows paid;
 sure, though wars troy, claims aid.
 fate wills this; thus can jove resign
 future father dardan line:[266]
 first great ancestor obtain’d grace,
 still love descends race:
 priam now, priam’s faithless kind,
 length odious all-seeing mind;
 great Æneas shall devolve reign,
 sons succeeding sons lasting line sustain.”
 
great earth-shaker thus: replies
 imperial goddess radiant eyes:
 “good is, immolate spare
 dardan prince, neptune! thy care;
 pallas i, gods can bind,
 sworn destruction trojan kind;
 even instant protract fate,
 save one member sinking state;
 till last flame quench’d last gore,
 even crumbling ruins more.”
 
king ocean fight descends,
 whistling darts course bends,
 swift interposed warrior flies,
 casts thick darkness o’er achilles’ eyes.[267]
 great Æneas’ shield spear drew,
 master’s feet weapon threw.
 done, force divine snatch’d high
 dardan prince, bore sky,
 smooth-gliding without step, heads
 warring heroes, bounding steeds:
 till battle’s utmost verge light,
 slow caucans close rear fight.
 godhead (his heavenly form confess’d)
 words like panting chief address’d:
 
“what power, prince! force inferior far,
 urged thee meet achilles’ arm war?
 henceforth beware, antedate thy doom,
 defrauding fate thy fame come.
 day decreed (for come must)
 shall lay dreadful hero dust,
 let furies arm known,
 secure grecian force transcends thy own.”
 
that, left wondering lay,
 achilles chased mist away:
 sudden, returning stream light,
 scene war came rushing sight.
 thus, amazed; “what wonders strike mind!
 spear, parted wings wind,
 laid me! dardan lord,
 fell instant, vanish’d sword!
 thought alone mortals contend,
 powers celestial sure foe defend.
 great is, arms scarce will try,
 content once, gods, fly.
 now let others bleed.” said, aloud
 vents fury inflames crowd:
 “o greeks! (he cries, every rank alarms)
 join battle, man man, arms arms!
 ’tis me, though favour’d sky,
 mow whole troops, make whole armies fly:
 god can singly host engage,
 mars himself, great minerva’s rage.
 whatsoe’er achilles can inspire,
 whate’er active force, acting fire;
 whate’er heart can prompt, hand obey;
 all, achilles, greeks! to-day.
 yon wide host arm shall scatter fear,
 thin squadrons single spear.”
 
said: less elate martial joy,
 godlike hector warm’d troops troy:
 “trojans, war! think, hector leads on;
 dread vaunts peleus’ haughty son.
 deeds must decide fate. e’en words
 insult brave, tremble swords:
 weakest atheist-wretch heaven defies,
 shrinks shudders thunder flies.
 yon boaster shall chief retire,
 though heart steel, hands fire;
 fire, steel, hector withstand,
 brave vengeful heart, dreadful hand.”
 
thus (breathing rage all) hero said;
 wood lances rises round head,
 clamours clamours tempest air,
 join, throng, thicken war.
 phœbus warns high heaven shun
 single fight thetis’ godlike son;
 safe combat mingled band,
 tempt near terrors hand.
 hears, obedient god light,
 and, plunged within ranks, awaits fight.
 
fierce achilles, shouting skies,
 troy’s whole force boundless fury flies.
 first falls iphytion, army’s head;
 brave chief, brave host led;
 great otrynteus derived blood,
 mother nais, flood;
 beneath shades tmolus, crown’d snow,
 hyde’s walls ruled lands below.
 fierce springs, sword head divides:
 parted visage falls equal sides:
 loud-resounding arms strikes plain;
 thus achilles glories o’er slain:
 
“lie there, otryntides! trojan earth
 receives thee dead, though gygae boast thy birth;
 beauteous fields hyllus’ waves roll’d,
 plenteous hermus swells tides gold,
 thine more.”—the insulting hero said,
 left sleeping eternal shade.
 rolling wheels greece body tore,
 dash’d axles vulgar gore.
 
demoleon next, antenor’s offspring, laid
 breathless dust, price rashness paid.
 impatient steel full-descending sway
 forced brazen helm furious way,
 resistless drove batter’d skull before,
 dash’d mingled brains gore.
 sees hippodamas, seized fright,
 deserts chariot swifter flight:
 lance arrests him: ignoble wound
 panting trojan rivets ground.
 groans away soul: louder roars,
 neptune’s shrine helicè’s high shores,
 victim bull; rocks re-bellow round,
 ocean listens grateful sound.
 fell polydore vengeful rage,[268]
 youngest hope priam’s stooping age:
 (whose feet swiftness race surpass’d:)
 sons, dearest, last.
 forbidden field takes flight,
 first folly youthful knight,
 vaunt swiftness wheels around plain,
 vaunts long, swiftness slain:
 struck crossing belts unite behind,
 golden rings double back-plate join’d
 forth navel burst thrilling steel;
 knees piercing shrieks fell;
 rushing entrails pour’d upon ground
 hands collect; darkness wraps round.
 hector view’d, ghastly gore,
 thus sadly slain unhappy polydore,
 cloud sorrow overcast sight,
 soul longer brook’d distant fight:
 full achilles’ dreadful front came,
 shook javelin like waving flame.
 peleus sees, joy possess’d,
 heart high-bounding rising breast.
 “and, lo! man black fates attend;
 man, slew achilles, friend!
 shall hector’s pelides’ spear
 turn walks war.”—
 revengeful eyes scann’d o’er:
 “come, receive thy fate!” spake more.
 
hector, undaunted, thus: “such words employ
 one dreads thee, unwarlike boy:
 give, defying defied,
 mean intercourse obloquy pride!
 know thy force mine superior far;
 heaven alone confers success war:
 mean am, gods may guide dart,
 give entrance braver heart.”
 
parts lance: pallas’ heavenly breath
 far achilles wafts winged death:
 bidden dart hector flies,
 feet great master lies.
 achilles closes hated foe,
 heart eyes flaming fury glow:
 present aid, apollo shrouds
 favour’d hero veil clouds.
 thrice struck pelides indignant heart,
 thrice impassive air plunged dart;
 spear fourth time buried cloud.
 foams fury, exclaims aloud:
 
“wretch! thou hast ’scaped again; thy flight
 saved thee, partial god light.
 long thou shalt thy just fate withstand,
 power assist achilles’ hand.
 fly inglorious! thy flight day
 whole hecatombs trojan ghosts shall pay.”
 
that, gluts rage numbers slain:
 dryops tumbled ensanguined plain,
 pierced neck: left panting there,
 stopp’d demuchus, great philetor’s heir.
 gigantic chief! deep gash’d enormous blade,
 soul ample passage made.
 laoganus dardanus expire,
 valiant sons unhappy sire;
 one instant chariot hurl’d,
 sunk one instant nether world:
 difference sad fates afford
 one spear destroy’d, one sword.
 
less unpitied, young alastor bleeds;
 vain youth, vain beauty pleads;
 vain begs thee, suppliant’s moan,
 spare form, age like thy own!
 unhappy boy! prayer, moving art,
 e’er bent fierce, inexorable heart!
 yet trembled knees, cried,
 ruthless falchion oped tender side;
 panting liver pours flood gore
 drowns bosom till pants more.
 
mulius’ head drove impetuous spear:
 warrior falls, transfix’d ear ear.
 thy life, echeclus! next sword bereaves,
 deep though front ponderous falchion cleaves;
 warm’d brain smoking weapon lies,
 purple death comes floating o’er eyes.
 brave deucalion died: dart flung
 knit nerves pliant elbow strung;
 dropp’d arm, unassisting weight,
 stood impotent, expecting fate:
 full neck falling falchion sped,
 broad shoulders hew’d crested head:
 forth bone spinal marrow flies,
 and, sunk dust, corpse extended lies.
 rhigmas, whose race fruitful thracia came,
 (the pierus, illustrious name,)
 succeeds fate: spear belly rends;
 prone car thundering chief descends.
 squire, saw expiring ground
 prostrate master, rein’d steeds around;
 back, scarce turn’d, pelian javelin gored,
 stretch’d servant o’er dying lord.
 flame winding valley fills,
 runs crackling shrubs hills;
 o’er stubble mountain flies,
 fires high woods, blazes skies,
 way that, spreading torrent roars:
 sweeps hero wasted shores;
 around wide, immense destruction pours
 earth deluged sanguine showers,
 autumnal harvests cover’d o’er,
 thick bestrewn, lies ceres’ sacred floor;
 round round, never-wearied pain,
 trampling steers beat unnumber’d grain:
 fierce coursers, chariot rolls,
 tread whole ranks, crush heroes’ souls,
 dash’d hoofs o’er dead fly,
 black, bloody drops smoking chariot dye:
 spiky wheels heaps carnage tore;
 thick groaning axles dropp’d gore.
 high o’er scene death achilles stood,
 grim dust, horrible blood:
 yet still insatiate, still rage flame;
 lust never-dying fame!
 

[illustration: ] centaur
 



book xxi.
 

argument.
 

battle river scamander.[269]
 

trojans fly achilles, towards town, others the
 river scamander: falls upon latter great slaughter: takes
 twelve captives alive, sacrifice shade patroclus; and
 kills lycaon asteropeus. scamander attacks waves:
 neptune pallas assist hero: simois joins scamander: length
 vulcan, instigation juno, almost dries river. this
 combat ended, gods engage other. meanwhile achilles
 continues slaughter, drives rest troy: agenor makes a
 stand, conveyed away cloud apollo; (to delude
 achilles) takes upon agenor’s shape, pursues in
 disguise, gives trojans opportunity retiring their
 city.
 day continues. scene banks stream
 scamander.
 

now xanthus’ gliding stream drove,
 xanthus, immortal progeny jove.
 river divides flying train,
 part town fly diverse o’er plain,
 late troops triumphant bore fight,
 now chased, trembling ignoble flight:
 (these gathered mist saturnia shrouds,
 rolls behind rout heap clouds:)
 part plunge stream: old xanthus roars,
 flashing billows beat whiten’d shores:
 cries promiscuous banks resound,
 here, there, eddies whirling round,
 flouncing steeds shrieking warriors drown’d.
 scorch’d locusts fields retire,
 fast behind runs blaze fire;
 driven land smoky cloud,
 clustering legions rush flood:
 so, plunged xanthus achilles’ force,
 roars resounding surge men horse.
 bloody lance hero casts aside,
 (which spreading tamarisks margin hide,)
 then, like god, rapid billows braves,
 arm’d sword, high brandish’d o’er waves:
 now plunges, now whirls round,
 deep groan’d waters dying sound;
 repeated wounds reddening river dyed,
 warm purple circled tide.
 swift foamy flood trojans fly,
 close rocks winding caverns lie:
 huge dolphin tempesting main,
 shoals fly scaly train,
 confusedly heap’d seek inmost caves,
 pant heave beneath floating waves.
 now, tired slaughter, trojan band
 twelve chosen youths drags alive land;
 rich belts captive arms restrains
 (late proud ornaments, now chains).
 attendants ships convey’d,
 sad victims destined patroclus’ shade;
 
then, plunged amid flood,
 young lycaon passage stood;
 priam; hero’s hand
 late made captive father’s land
 (as sycamore, sounding steel
 lopp’d green arms spoke chariot wheel)
 lemnos’ isle sold royal slave,
 jason’s price demanded gave;
 kind eetion, touching shore,
 ransom’d prince fair arisbe bore.
 ten days past, since father’s reign
 felt sweets liberty again;
 next, god men vain withstand
 gives youth conquering hand
 now never return! doom’d go
 sadder journey shades below.
 well-known face great achilles eyed,
 (the helm visor cast aside
 wild affright, dropp’d upon field
 useless lance unavailing shield,)
 trembling, panting, stream fled,
 knock’d faltering knees, hero said:
 “ye mighty gods! wonders strike view!
 vain conquering arms subdue?
 sure shall see yon heaps trojans kill’d
 rise shades, brave field;
 now captive, late bound
 sold lemnos, stalks trojan ground!
 sea’s unmeasured deeps detain,
 bar numbers native plain;
 lo! returns. try, then, flying spear!
 try, grave can hold wanderer;
 earth, length active prince can seize,
 earth, whose strong grasp held hercules.”
 
thus spoke, trojan pale fears
 approach’d, sought knees suppliant tears
 loth yield youthful breath,
 soul shivering approach death.
 achilles raised spear, prepared wound;
 kiss’d feet, extended ground:
 while, above, spear suspended stood,
 longing dip thirsty point blood,
 one hand embraced close, one stopp’d dart,
 thus melting words attempt heart:
 
“thy well-known captive, great achilles! see,
 lycaon trembles thy knee.
 pity suppliant’s name afford,
 shared gifts ceres thy board;
 late thy conquering arm lemnos bore,
 far father, friends, native shore;
 hundred oxen price day,
 now sums immense thy mercy shall repay.
 scarce respited woes yet appear,
 scarce twelve morning suns seen here;
 lo! jove submits thy hands,
 again, victim cruel fate demands!
 sprang priam, laothoe fair,
 (old altes’ daughter, lelegia’s heir;
 held pedasus famed abode,
 ruled fields silver satnio flow’d,)
 two sons (alas! unhappy sons) bore;
 ah! one spear shall drink brother’s gore,
 succeed slaughter’d polydore.
 arm terror shall fly?
 demon urges! ’tis doom die!
 ever yet soft pity touch’d thy mind,
 ah! think much hector’s kind!
 mother gave thy suppliant breath,
 his, wrought thy loved patroclus’ death.”
 
words, attended shower tears,
 youth address’d unrelenting ears:
 “talk life, ransom (he replies):
 patroclus dead, whoever meets me, dies:
 vain single trojan sues grace;
 least, sons priam’s hateful race.
 die then, friend! boots deplore?
 great, good patroclus more!
 he, far thy better, foredoom’d die,
 thou, dost thou bewail mortality?
 seest thou me, nature’s gifts adorn,
 sprung hero, goddess born?
 day shall come (which nothing can avert)
 spear, arrow, dart,
 night, day, force, design,
 impending death certain fate mine!
 die then,”—he said; word spoke,
 fainting stripling sank stroke:
 hand forgot grasp, left spear,
 trembling frame confess’d fear:
 sudden, achilles broad sword display’d,
 buried neck reeking blade.
 prone fell youth; panting land,
 gushing purple dyed thirsty sand.
 victor stream carcase gave,
 thus insults him, floating wave:
 
“lie there, lycaon! let fish surround
 thy bloated corpse, suck thy gory wound:
 sad mother shall thy funerals weep,
 swift scamander roll thee deep,
 whose every wave watery monster brings,
 feast unpunish’d fat kings.
 perish troy, trojan line!
 ruin theirs, compassion mine.
 boots ye now scamander’s worshipp’d stream,
 earthly honours, immortal name?
 vain immolated bulls slain,
 living coursers glut gulfs vain!
 thus rewards you, bitter fate;
 thus, till grecian vengeance complete:
 thus atoned patroclus’ honour’d shade,
 short absence achilles paid.”
 
boastful words provoked raging god;
 fury swells violated flood.
 means divine may yet power employ
 check achilles, rescue troy?
 meanwhile hero springs arms, dare
 great asteropeus mortal war;
 pelagon, whose lofty line
 flows source axius, stream divine!
 (fair peribaea’s love god crown’d,
 refluent waters circled round:)
 achilles rush’d; fearless stood,
 shook two spears, advancing flood;
 flood impell’d him, pelides’ head
 avenge waters choked heaps dead.
 near drew, achilles thus began:
 
“what art thou, boldest race man?
 who, whence? unhappy sire
 whose encounters resistless ire.”
 
“o peleus! avails trace
 (replied warrior) illustrious race?
 rich paeonia’s valleys command,
 arm’d protended spears, native band;
 now shines tenth bright morning since came
 aid ilion fields fame:
 axius, swells neighbouring rills,
 wide around floated region fills,
 begot sire, whose spear much glory won:
 now lift thy arm, try hero’s son!”
 
threatening said: hostile chiefs advance;
 asteropeus discharged lance,
 (for dexterous hands lance wield,)
 one struck, pierced not, vulcanian shield;
 one razed achilles’ hand; spouting blood
 spun forth; earth fasten’d weapon stood.
 like lightning next pelean javelin flies:
 erring fury hiss’d along skies;
 deep swelling bank driven spear,
 even middle earth; quiver’d there.
 side sword pelides drew,
 foe double fury flew.
 foe thrice tugg’d, shook rooted wood;
 repulsive might weapon stood:
 fourth, tries break spear vain;
 bent stands, tumbles plain;
 belly open’d ghastly wound,
 reeking entrails pour upon ground.
 beneath hero’s feet panting lies,
 eye darkens, spirit flies;
 proud victor thus triumphing said,
 radiant armour tearing dead:
 
“so ends thy glory! fate prove,
 strive presumptuous sons jove!
 sprung river, didst thou boast thy line?
 great saturnius source mine.
 durst thou vaunt thy watery progeny?
 peleus, Æacus, jove, i.
 race superior far those,
 thunders stream flows.
 rivers can, scamander might shown;
 jove dreads, wars son.
 even achelous might contend vain,
 roaring billows main.
 eternal ocean, whose fountains flow
 seas, rivers, springs below,
 thundering voice jove abhors hear,
 deep abysses shakes fear.”
 
said: bank javelin tore,
 left breathless warrior gore.
 floating tides bloody carcase lave,
 beat it, wave succeeding wave;
 till, roll’d banks, lies food
 curling eels, fishes flood.
 scatter’d round stream (their mightiest slain)
 amazed pæonians scour along plain;
 vents fury flying crew,
 thrasius, astyplus, mnesus slew;
 mydon, thersilochus, Ænius, fell;
 numbers lance plunged hell,
 bottom gulfs profound
 scamander spoke; shores return’d sound.
 
“o first mortals! (for gods thine)
 valour matchless, force divine!
 jove given thee every trojan head,
 ’tis thy rage heap dead.
 see! choked streams course can keep,
 roll wonted tribute deep.
 turn then, impetuous! injured flood;
 content, thy slaughters amaze god.”
 
human form, confess’d eyes,
 river thus; thus chief replies:
 “o sacred stream! thy word shall obey;
 till troy destined vengeance pay,
 till within towers perjured train
 shall pant, tremble arms again;
 till proud hector, guardian wall,
 stain lance, see achilles fall.”
 
said; drove fury foe.
 godhead silver bow
 yellow flood began: “o jove!
 mandate sire above
 full express, phœbus employ
 sacred arrows defence troy,
 make conquer, till hyperion’s fall
 awful darkness hide face all?”
 
spoke vain—the chief without dismay
 ploughs boiling surge desperate way.
 rising rage shores,
 deep bellowing river roars,
 huge heaps slain disgorges coast,
 round banks ghastly dead toss’d.
 before, billows ranged high,
 (a watery bulwark,) screen bands fly.
 now bursting head thundering sound,
 falling deluge whelms hero round:
 loaded shield bends rushing tide;
 feet, upborne, scarce strong flood divide,
 sliddering, staggering. border stood
 spreading elm, overhung flood;
 seized bending bough, steps stay;
 plant uprooted weight gave way.[270]
 heaving bank, undermining all;
 loud flash waters rushing fall
 thick foliage. large trunk display’d
 bridged rough flood across: hero stay’d
 weight, raised upon hand,
 leap’d channel, regain’d land.
 blacken’d wild waves: murmur rose:
 god pursues, huger billow throws,
 bursts bank, ambitious destroy
 man whose fury fate troy.
 like warlike eagle speeds pace
 (swiftest strongest aerial race);
 far spear can fly, achilles springs;
 every bound clanging armour rings:
 now here, now there, turns every side,
 winds course following tide;
 waves flow after, wheresoe’er wheels,
 gather fast, murmur heels.
 peasant garden brings
 soft rills water bubbling springs,
 calls floods high, bless bowers,
 feed pregnant streams plants flowers:
 soon clears whate’er passage stay’d,
 marks future current spade,
 swift o’er rolling pebbles, hills,
 louder louder purl falling rills;
 scattering, prevent pains,
 shine mazy wanderings o’er plains.
 
still flies achilles, eyes
 still swift scamander rolls where’er flies:
 speed escapes rapid floods;
 first men, match gods.
 oft turn’d torrent oppose,
 bravely try powers foes;
 oft surge, watery mountains spread,
 beats back, bursts upon head.
 yet dauntless still adverse flood braves,
 still indignant bounds waves.
 tired tides, knees relax toil;
 wash’d beneath slides slimy soil;
 thus (his eyes heaven’s expansion thrown)
 forth bursts hero angry groan:
 
“is god achilles befriend,
 power avert miserable end?
 prevent, jove! ignominious date,[271]
 make future life sport fate.
 heaven’s oracles believed vain,
 thetis must complain;
 phœbus’ darts prophesied fall,
 glorious arms trojan wall.
 oh! died fields battle warm,
 stretch’d like hero, hero’s arm!
 might hector’s spear dauntless bosom rend,
 swift soul o’ertake slaughter’d friend.
 ah no! achilles meets shameful fate,
 oh unworthy brave great!
 like vile swain, rainy day,
 crossing ford, torrent sweeps away,
 unregarded carcase sea.”
 
neptune pallas haste relief,
 thus human form address’d chief:
 power ocean first: “forbear thy fear,
 peleus! lo, thy gods appear!
 behold! jove descending thy aid,
 propitious neptune, blue-eyed maid.
 stay, furious flood shall cease rave
 ’tis thy fate glut angry wave.
 thou, counsel heaven suggests, attend!
 breathe combat, thy sword suspend,
 till troy receive flying sons, till all
 routed squadrons pant behind wall:
 hector alone shall stand fatal chance,
 hector’s blood shall smoke upon thy lance.
 thine glory doom’d.” thus spake gods:
 swift ascended bright abodes.
 
stung new ardour, thus heaven impell’d,
 springs impetuous, invades field:
 o’er expanded plain waters spread;
 heaved bounding billows danced dead,
 floating ’midst scatter’d arms; casques gold
 turn’d-up bucklers glitter’d roll’d.
 high o’er surging tide, leaps bounds,
 wades, mounts; parted wave resounds.
 whole river stops hero’s course,
 pallas fills immortal force.
 equal rage, indignant xanthus roars,
 lifts billows, o’erwhelms shores.
 
thus simois! “haste, brother flood;
 check mortal controls god;
 bravest heroes else shall quit fight,
 ilion tumble towery height.
 call thy subject streams, bid roar,
 thy fountains swell thy watery store,
 broken rocks, load dead,
 charge black surge, pour head.
 mark resistless floods goes,
 boldly bids warring gods foes!
 force, form divine sight,
 shall aught avail him, rage unite:
 whelm’d dark gulfs arms shall lie,
 blaze dreadful trojan eye;
 deep beneath sandy mountain hurl’d,
 immersed remain terror world.
 ponderous ruin shall confound place,
 greeks shall e’er perish’d relics grace,
 hand bones shall gather, inhume;
 cold rites, watery tomb.”
 

[illustration: ] achilles contending rivers
 

said; chief descends amain,
 increased gore, swelling slain.
 then, murmuring beds, boils, raves,
 foam whitens purple waves:
 every step, achilles stood
 crimson surge, deluged blood.
 fear touch’d queen heaven: saw dismay’d,
 call’d aloud, summon’d vulcan’s aid.
 
“rise war! insulting flood requires
 thy wasteful arm! assemble thy fires!
 aid, command enjoin’d,
 rush swift eastern western wind:
 old ocean word shall blow,
 pour red torrent watery foe,
 corses arms one bright ruin turn,
 hissing rivers bottoms burn.
 go, mighty thy rage! display thy power,
 drink whole flood, crackling trees devour.
 scorch banks! (till voice reclaim)
 exert unwearied furies flame!”
 
power ignipotent word obeys:
 wide o’er plain pours boundless blaze;
 consumes dead, dries soil
 shrunk waters channel boil.
 autumnal boreas sweeps sky,
 instant blows water’d gardens dry:
 look’d field, whiten’d ground,
 vulcan breathed fiery blast around.
 swift sedgy reeds ruin preys;
 along margin winds running blaze:
 trees flaming rows ashes turn,
 flowering lotos tamarisk burn,
 broad elm, cypress rising spire;
 watery willows hiss fire.
 now glow waves, fishes pant breath,
 eels lie twisting pangs death:
 now flounce aloft, now dive scaly fry,
 or, gasping, turn bellies sky.
 length river rear’d languid head,
 thus, short-panting, god said:
 
“oh vulcan! oh! power resists thy might?
 faint, sink, unequal fight—
 yield—let ilion fall; fate decree—
 ah—bend thy fiery arms me!”
 
ceased; wide conflagration blazing round;
 bubbling waters yield hissing sound.
 flames beneath cauldron rise,[272]
 melt fat rich sacrifice,
 amid fierce embrace circling fires
 waters foam, heavy smoke aspires:
 boils imprison’d flood, forbid flow,
 choked vapours feels bottom glow.
 juno then, imperial queen air,
 burning river sends earnest prayer:
 
“ah why, saturnia; must thy engage
 me, me, wasteful rage?
 gods dreadful arm employ,
 mightier gods assert cause troy.
 submissive desist, thou command;
 ah! withdraw all-destroying hand.
 hear solemn oath, yield fate
 unaided ilion, destined state,
 till greece shall gird destructive flame,
 one ruin sink trojan name.”
 
warm entreaty touch’d saturnia’s ear:
 bade ignipotent rage forbear,
 recall flame, mortal cause
 infest god: obedient flame withdraws:
 branching streams begin spread,
 soft remurmur wonted bed.
 
juno’s will strife resign,
 warring gods fierce contention join:
 rekindling rage heavenly breast alarms:
 horrid clangour shock ethereal arms:
 heaven loud thunder bids trumpet sound;
 wide beneath groans rending ground.
 jove, sport, dreadful scene descries,
 views contending gods careless eyes.
 power battles lifts brazen spear,
 first assaults radiant queen war:
 
“what moved thy madness, thus disunite
 ethereal minds, mix heaven fight?
 wonder this, thy frantic mood
 thou drovest mortal insult god?
 thy impious hand tydides’ javelin bore,
 madly bathed celestial gore.”
 
spoke, smote long-resounding shield,
 bears jove’s thunder dreadful field:
 adamantine ægis sire,
 turns glancing bolt forked fire.
 
heaved goddess mighty hand
 stone, limit neighbouring land,
 fix’d eldest times; black, craggy, vast;
 heavenly homicide cast.
 thundering falls, mass monstrous size:
 seven broad acres covers lies.
 stunning stroke stubborn nerves unbound:
 loud o’er fields ringing arms resound:
 scornful dame conquest views smiles,
 and, glorying, thus prostrate god reviles:
 
“hast thou yet, insatiate fury! known
 far minerva’s force transcends thy own?
 juno, thou rebellious darest withstand,
 corrects thy folly thus pallas’ hand;
 thus meets thy broken faith just disgrace,
 partial aid troy’s perfidious race.”
 
goddess spoke, turn’d eyes away,
 that, beaming round, diffused celestial day.
 jove’s cyprian daughter, stooping land,
 lent wounded god tender hand:
 slowly rises, scarcely breathes pain,
 and, propp’d fair arm, forsakes plain.
 bright empress heavens survey’d,
 and, scoffing, thus war’s victorious maid:
 
“lo! aid mars’s side seen!
 smiles’ loves’ unconquerable queen!
 mark insolence, open view,
 moves: let pallas, dares, pursue.”
 
minerva smiling heard, pair o’ertook,
 slightly breast wanton strook:
 she, unresisting, fell (her spirits fled);
 earth together lay lovers spread.
 “and like heroes fate all
 (minerva cries) guard trojan wall!
 grecian gods let phrygian be,
 dread, fierce, venus me;
 lowest stone shall troy moved.”
 thus she, juno smile approved.
 
meantime, mix mortal fight,
 god ocean dares god light.
 “what sloth seized us, fields around
 ring conflicting powers, heaven returns sound:
 shall, ignominious, shame retire,
 deed perform’d, olympian sire?
 come, prove thy arm! first war wage,
 suits greatness, superior age:
 rash thou art prop trojan throne,
 (forgetful wrongs, thy own,)
 guard race proud laomedon!
 hast thou forgot, how, monarch’s prayer,
 shared lengthen’d labours year?
 troy walls raised (for jove’s commands),
 yon proud bulwarks grew beneath hands:
 thy task feed bellowing droves
 along fair ida’s vales pendant groves.
 circling seasons train
 brought back grateful day crown’d pain,
 menace stern fraudful king defied
 latent godhead, prize denied:
 mad was, threaten’d servile bands,
 doom’d us exiles far barbarous lands.[273]
 incensed, heavenward fled swiftest wing,
 destined vengeance perjured king.
 dost thou, this, afford proud ilion grace,
 not, like us, infest faithless race;
 like us, present, future sons destroy,
 deep foundations heave troy?”
 
apollo thus: “to combat mankind
 ill suits wisdom celestial mind;
 man? calamitous birth,
 owe life nourishment earth;
 like yearly leaves, now, beauty crown’d,
 smile sun; now, wither ground.
 hands commit frantic scene,
 mix immortals cause mean.”
 
turns face, far-beaming heavenly fires,
 senior power submiss retires:
 thus retreating, artemis upbraids,
 quiver’d huntress sylvan shades:
 
“and thus youthful phœbus flies,
 yields ocean’s hoary sire prize?
 vain martial pomp, dreadful show
 pointed arrows silver bow!
 now boast yon celestial bower,
 thy force can match great earth-shaking power.”
 
silent heard queen woods upbraid:
 saturnia bore vaunting maid:
 furious thus: “what insolence driven
 thy pride face majesty heaven?
 though jove female plague design’d,
 fierce feeble race womankind,
 wretched matron feels thy piercing dart;
 thy sex’s tyrant, tiger’s heart?
 though tremendous woodland chase
 thy certain arrows pierce savage race?
 dares thy rashness powers divine
 employ arms, match thy force mine?
 learn hence, unequal war wage—”
 said, seized wrists eager rage;
 left hand lock’d, right untied
 bow, quiver, plumy pride.
 temples flies busy bow;
 now here, now there, winds blow;
 scattering arrows, rattling case,
 drop round, idly mark dusty place.
 swift field baffled huntress flies,
 scarce restrains torrent eyes:
 so, falcon wings way above,
 cleft cavern speeds gentle dove;
 (not fated yet die;) safe retreats,
 yet still heart marble beats.
 
latona hastes tender care;
 hermes viewing, thus declines war:
 “how shall face dame, gives delight
 whose thunders blacken heaven night?
 go, matchless goddess! triumph skies,
 boast conquest, yield prize.”
 
spoke; pass’d: latona, stooping low,
 collects scatter’d shafts fallen bow,
 that, glittering dust, lay there
 dishonour’d relics diana’s war:
 swift pursued blest abode,
 where, confused, sought sovereign god;
 weeping, grasp’d knees: ambrosial vest
 shook sighs, panted breast.
 
sire superior smiled, bade show
 heavenly hand caused daughter’s woe?
 abash’d, names imperial spouse;
 pale crescent fades upon brows.
 
thus above: while, swiftly gliding down,
 apollo enters ilion’s sacred town;
 guardian-god now trembled wall,
 fear’d greeks, though fate forbade fall.
 back olympus, war’s alarms,
 return shining bands gods arms;
 proud triumph, rage fire;
 take thrones around ethereal sire.
 
blood, death, achilles still proceeds,
 o’er slaughter’d heroes, o’er rolling steeds.
 avenging flames fury driven
 guilty towns exert wrath heaven;
 pale inhabitants, fall, fly;
 red vapours purple sky:
 raged achilles: death dire dismay,
 toils, terrors, fill’d dreadful day.
 
high turret hoary priam stands,
 marks waste destructive hands;
 views, arm, trojans’ scatter’d flight,
 near hero rising sight!
 stop, check, aid! feeble pace,
 settled sorrow aged face,
 fast could, sighing quits walls;
 thus descending, guards calls:
 
“you whose care city-gates belong,
 set wide portals flying throng:
 lo! comes, unresisted sway;
 comes, desolation marks way!
 within walls troops take breath,
 lock fast brazen bars, shut death.”
 thus charged reverend monarch: wide flung
 opening folds; sounding hinges rung.
 phœbus rush’d forth, flying bands meet;
 struck slaughter back, cover’d retreat,
 heaps trojans crowd gain gate,
 gladsome see last escape fate.
 thither, parch’d thirst, heartless train,
 hoary dust, beat hollow plain:
 gasping, panting, fainting, labour on
 heavier strides, lengthen toward town.
 enraged achilles follows spear;
 wild revenge, insatiable war.
 
greeks eternal praise acquired,
 troy inglorious walls retired;
 he, god darts ethereal flame,
 shot save her, redeem fame:
 young agenor force divine gave;
 (antenor’s offspring, haughty, bold, brave;)
 aid him, beside beech sate,
 wrapt clouds, restrain’d hand fate.
 now generous youth achilles spies,
 thick beats heart, troubled motions rise.
 (so, ere storm, waters heave roll.)
 stops, questions thus mighty soul;
 
“what, shall fly terror plain!
 like others fly, like others slain?
 vain hope! shun self-same road
 yon line slaughter’d trojans lately trod.
 no: common heap scorn fall—
 pass’d trojan wall,
 decline yonder path, leads
 ida’s forests surrounding shades?
 may reach, conceal’d, cooling flood,
 tired body wash dirt blood,
 soon night dusky veil extends,
 return safety trojan friends.
 if?—but wherefore vain debate?
 stand doubt, within reach fate?
 even now perhaps, ere yet turn wall,
 fierce achilles sees me, fall:
 swiftness, ’tis vain fly,
 valour, stands must die.
 howe’er ’tis better, fighting state,
 here, public view, meet fate.
 yet sure mortal; may feel
 (like sons earth) force steel.
 one soul informs dreadful frame:
 jove’s sole favour gives fame.”
 
said, stood, collected, might;
 beating bosom claim’d fight.
 deep-grown wood panther starts,
 roused thicket storm darts:
 untaught fear fly, hears sounds
 shouting hunters, clamorous hounds;
 though struck, though wounded, scarce perceives pain;
 barb’d javelin stings breast vain:
 whole war, untamed, savage flies;
 tears hunter, beneath dies.
 less resolved, antenor’s valiant heir
 confronts achilles, awaits war,
 disdainful retreat: high held before,
 shield (a broad circumference) bore;
 graceful stood, act throw
 lifted javelin, thus bespoke foe:
 
“how proud achilles glories fame!
 hopes day sink trojan name
 beneath ruins! know, hope vain;
 thousand woes, thousand toils remain.
 parents children just arms employ,
 strong many sons troy.
 great thou art, even thou may’st stain gore
 phrygian fields, press foreign shore.”
 
said: matchless force javelin flung
 smote knee; hollow cuishes rung
 beneath pointed steel; safe harms
 stands impassive ethereal arms.
 fiercely rushing daring foe,
 lifted arm prepares fatal blow:
 but, jealous fame, apollo shrouds
 god-like trojan veil clouds.
 safe pursuit, shut mortal view,
 dismiss’d fame, favoured youth withdrew.
 meanwhile god, cover escape,
 assumes agenor’s habit, voice shape,
 flies furious chief disguise;
 furious chief still follows flies.
 now o’er fields stretch lengthen’d strides,
 now urge course swift scamander glides:
 god, now distant scarce stride before,
 tempts pursuit, wheels shore;
 flying troops speed employ,
 pour heaps walls troy:
 stop, stay; thought ask, tell,
 ’scaped flight, battle fell.
 ’twas tumult all, violence flight;
 sudden joy confused, mix’d affright.
 pale troy achilles shuts gate:
 nations breathe, deliver’d fate.
 



book xxii.
 

argument.
 

death hector.
 

trojans safe within walls, hector stays oppose
 achilles. priam struck approach, tries persuade his
 re-enter town. hecuba joins entreaties, vain.
 hector consults within measures take; the
 advance achilles, resolution fails him, flies. achilles
 pursues thrice round walls troy. gods debate concerning
 fate hector; length minerva descends aid achilles.
 deludes hector shape deiphobus; stands combat, and
 slain. achilles drags dead body chariot sight of
 priam hecuba. lamentations, tears, despair. cries
 reach ears andromache, who, ignorant this, retired into
 inner part palace: mounts walls, beholds
 dead husband. swoons spectacle. excess grief and
 lamentation.
 thirtieth day still continues. scene lies walls,
 battlements troy.
 

thus bulwarks, smit panic fear,
 herded ilians rush like driven deer:
 safe wipe briny drops away,
 drown bowls labours day.
 close walls, advancing o’er fields
 beneath one roof well-compacted shields,
 march, bending on, greeks’ embodied powers,
 far stretching shade trojan towers.
 great hector singly stay’d: chain’d fate
 fix’d stood scæan gate;
 still bold arms determined employ,
 guardian still long-defended troy.
 
apollo now tired achilles turns:
 (the power confess’d glory burns:)
 “and (he cries) peleus’ view,
 mortal speed godhead pursue?
 thee know gods given,
 unskill’d trace latent marks heaven.
 boots thee now, troy forsook plain?
 vain thy past labour, thy present vain:
 safe walls now troops bestow’d,
 thy frantic rage attacks god.”
 
chief incensed—“too partial god day!
 check conquests middle way:
 ilion else refuge found!
 gasping numbers now bit ground!
 thou robb’st glory justly mine,
 powerful godhead, fraud divine:
 mean fame, alas! one heavenly strain,
 cheat mortal repines vain.”
 
city, terrible strong,
 high haughty steps tower’d along,
 proud courser, victor prize,
 near goal double ardour flies.
 him, blazing shot across field,
 careful eyes priam first beheld.
 half dreadful rises sight,[274]
 thick gloom tempestuous night,
 orion’s dog (the year autumn weighs),
 o’er feebler stars exerts rays;
 terrific glory! burning breath
 taints red air fevers, plagues, death.
 flamed fiery mail. wept sage:
 strikes reverend head, now white age;
 lifts wither’d arms; obtests skies;
 calls much-loved feeble cries:
 son, resolved achilles’ force dare,
 full scæan gates expects war;
 sad father rampart stands,
 thus adjures extended hands:
 
“ah stay not, stay not! guardless alone;
 hector! loved, dearest, bravest son!
 methinks already behold thee slain,
 stretch’d beneath fury plain.
 implacable achilles! might’st thou be
 gods dearer me!
 thee, vultures wild scatter round shore,
 bloody dogs grow fiercer thy gore.
 many valiant sons late enjoy’d,
 valiant vain! thy cursed arm destroy’d:
 or, worse slaughtered, sold distant isles
 shameful bondage, unworthy toils.
 two, speak, eyes vain explore,
 two one mother sprung, polydore,
 loved lycaon; now perhaps more!
 oh! yonder hostile camp live,
 heaps gold, treasures give!
 (their grandsire’s wealth, right birth own,
 consign’d daughter lelegia’s throne:)
 (which heaven forbid) already lost,
 pale wander stygian coast;
 sorrows must sad mother know,
 anguish i? unutterable woe!
 yet less anguish, less her, me,
 less troy, deprived thee.
 yet shun achilles! enter yet wall;
 spare thyself, thy father, spare us all!
 save thy dear life; or, soul brave
 neglect thought, thy dearer glory save.
 pity, yet live, silver hairs;
 yet thy father feels woes bears,
 yet cursed sense! wretch, rage
 (all trembling verge helpless age)
 great jove placed, sad spectacle pain!
 bitter dregs fortune’s cup drain:
 fill scenes death closing eyes,
 number days miseries!
 heroes slain, bridal bed o’erturn’d,
 daughters ravish’d, city burn’d,
 bleeding infants dash’d floor;
 yet see, perhaps yet more!
 perhaps even i, reserved angry fate,
 last sad relic ruin’d state,
 (dire pomp sovereign wretchedness!) must fall,
 stain pavement regal hall;
 famish’d dogs, late guardians door,
 shall lick mangled master’s spatter’d gore.
 yet sons thank ye, gods! ’tis well;
 well perish’d, fight fell.
 dies youth vigour, dies best,
 struck wounds, honest breast.
 fates, fulness rage,
 spurn hoar head unresisting age,
 dust reverend lineaments deform,
 pour dogs life-blood scarcely warm:
 this, misery! last, worse,
 man can feel! man, fated cursed!”
 
said, acting words say,
 rent head silver locks away.
 mournful mother bears part;
 yet sorrows turn hector’s heart.
 zone unbraced, bosom display’d;
 thus, fast-falling salt tears, said:
 
“have mercy me, son! revere
 words age; attend parent’s prayer!
 ever thee fond arms press’d,
 still’d thy infant clamours breast;
 ah thus helpless years forego,
 but, walls secured, repel foe.
 rage singly thou proceed,
 should’st thou, (but heaven avert it!) should’st thou bleed,
 must thy corse lie honour’d bier,
 spouse, mother, grace thee tear!
 far pious rites dear remains
 must feast vultures naked plains.”
 
they, cheeks torrents roll;
 fix’d remains purpose soul;
 resolved stands, fiery glance
 expects hero’s terrible advance.
 so, roll’d den, swelling snake
 beholds traveller approach brake;
 fed noxious herbs turgid veins
 gather’d half poisons plains;
 burns, stiffens collected ire,
 red eyeballs glare living fire.
 beneath turret, shield reclined,
 stood, question’d thus mighty mind:[275]
 
“where lies way? enter wall?
 honour shame ungenerous thought recall:
 shall proud polydamas gate
 proclaim, counsels obey’d late,
 timely follow’d former night,
 numbers saved hector’s flight?
 wise advice rejected disdain,
 feel folly people slain.
 methinks suffering country’s voice hear,
 worthless sons insult ear,
 rash courage charge chance war,
 blame virtues share.
 no—if e’er return, return must
 glorious, country’s terror laid dust:
 perish, let see fall
 field least, fighting wall.
 yet suppose measures forego,
 approach unarm’d, parley foe,
 warrior-shield, helm, lance, lay down,
 treat terms peace save town:
 wife withheld, treasure ill-detain’d
 (cause war, grievance land)
 honourable justice restore:
 add half ilion’s yet remaining store,
 troy shall, sworn, produce; injured greece
 may share wealth, leave walls peace.
 thought? unarm’d go,
 hope mercy vengeful foe,
 woman-like fall, fall without blow?
 greet here, man conversing man,
 met oak, journeying o’er plain;
 season now calm familiar talk,
 like youths maidens evening walk:
 war business, given
 die, triumph, that, determine heaven!”
 
thus pondering, like god greek drew nigh;
 dreadful plumage nodded high;
 pelian javelin, better hand,
 shot trembling rays glitter’d o’er land;
 breast beamy splendour shone,
 like jove’s lightning, rising sun.
 hector sees, unusual terrors rise,
 struck god, fears, recedes, flies.
 leaves gates, leaves wall behind:
 achilles follows like winged wind.
 thus panting dove falcon flies
 (the swiftest racer liquid skies),
 just holds, thinks holds prey,
 obliquely wheeling aerial way,
 open beak shrilling cries springs,
 aims claws, shoots upon wings:
 less fore-right rapid chase held,
 one urged fury, one fear impell’d:
 now circling round walls course maintain,
 high watch-tower overlooks plain;
 now fig-trees spread umbrage broad,
 (a wider compass,) smoke along road.
 next scamander’s double source bound,
 two famed fountains burst parted ground;
 hot scorching clefts seen rise,
 exhalations steaming skies;
 green banks summer’s heat o’erflows,
 like crystal clear, cold winter snows:
 gushing fount marble cistern fills,
 whose polish’d bed receives falling rills;
 trojan dames (ere yet alarm’d greece)
 wash’d fair garments days peace.[276]
 pass’d, one chasing, one flight:
 (the mighty fled, pursued stronger might:)
 swift course; vulgar prize play,
 vulgar victim must reward day:
 (such races crown speedy strife:)
 prize contended great hector’s life.
 hero’s funerals decreed
 grateful honour mighty dead;
 high rewards vigorous youth inflame
 (some golden tripod, lovely dame)
 panting coursers swiftly turn goal,
 turns raised spectator’s soul:
 thus three times round trojan wall fly.
 gazing gods lean forward sky;
 whom, eager chase look,
 sire mortals immortals spoke:
 
“unworthy sight! man beloved heaven,
 behold, inglorious round yon city driven!
 heart partakes generous hector’s pain;
 hector, whose zeal whole hecatombs slain,
 whose grateful fumes gods received joy,
 ida’s summits, towers troy:
 now see flying; fears resign’d,
 fate, fierce achilles, close behind.
 consult, ye powers! (’tis worthy debate)
 whether snatch impending fate,
 let bear, stern pelides slain,
 (good is) lot imposed man.”
 
pallas thus: “shall whose vengeance forms
 forky bolt, blackens heaven storms,
 shall prolong one trojan’s forfeit breath?
 man, mortal, pre-ordain’d death!
 will murmurs fill courts above?
 gods indignant blame partial jove?”
 
“go (return’d sire) without delay,
 exert thy will: give fates way.”
 swift mandate pleased tritonia flies,
 stoops impetuous cleaving skies.
 
forest, o’er vale lawn,
 well-breath’d beagle drives flying fawn,
 vain tries covert brakes,
 deep beneath trembling thicket shakes;
 sure vapour tainted dews,
 certain hound various maze pursues.
 thus step step, where’er trojan wheel’d,
 swift achilles compass’d round field.
 oft reach dardan gates bends,
 hopes assistance pitying friends,
 (whose showering arrows, coursed below,
 high turrets might oppress foe,)
 oft achilles turns plain:
 eyes city, eyes vain.
 men slumbers seem speedy pace,
 one pursue, one lead chase,
 sinking limbs fancied course forsake,
 can fly, can overtake:
 less labouring heroes pant strain:
 flies, pursues vain.
 
god, muse, assisted hector’s force
 fate long hold course?
 phœbus was; who, latest hour,
 endued knees strength, nerves power:
 great achilles, lest greek’s advance
 snatch glory lifted lance,
 sign’d troops yield foe way,
 leave untouch’d honours day.
 
jove lifts golden balances, show
 fates mortal men, things below:
 contending hero’s lot tries,
 weighs, equal hand, destinies.
 low sinks scale surcharged hector’s fate;
 heavy death sinks, hell receives weight.
 
phœbus left him. fierce minerva flies
 stern pelides, triumphing, cries:
 “o loved jove! day labours cease,
 conquest blazes full beams greece.
 great hector falls; hector famed far,
 drunk renown, insatiable war,
 falls thy hand, mine! force, flight,
 shall avail him, god light.
 see, vain supplicates above,
 roll’d feet unrelenting jove;
 rest here: will lead trojan on,
 urge meet fate shun.”
 
voice divine chief joyful mind
 obey’d; rested, lance reclined
 like deiphobus martial dame
 (her face, gesture, arms same),
 show aid, hapless hector’s side
 approach’d, greets thus voice belied:
 
“too long, hector! borne sight
 distress, sorrow’d thy flight:
 fits us now noble stand make,
 here, brothers, equal fates partake.”
 
he: “o prince! allied blood fame,
 dearer brother’s name;
 hecuba priam bore,
 long tried, long loved: much loved, honoured more!
 since you, numerous race alone
 defend life, regardless own.”
 
goddess: “much father’s prayer,
 much mother’s, press’d forbear:
 friends embraced knees, adjured stay,
 stronger love impell’d, obey.
 come then, glorious conflict let us try,
 let steel sparkle, javelin fly;
 let us stretch achilles field,
 arm bloody trophies yield.”
 
fraudful said; swiftly march’d before:
 dardan hero shuns foe more.
 sternly met. silence hector broke:
 dreadful plumage nodded spoke:
 
“enough, peleus! troy view’d
 walls thrice circled, chief pursued.
 now god within bids try
 thine, fate: kill thee, die.
 yet verge battle let us stay,
 moment’s space suspend day;
 let heaven’s high powers call’d arbitrate
 just conditions stern debate,
 (eternal witnesses below,
 faithful guardians treasured vow!)
 swear; if, victor strife,
 jove hands shall shed thy noble life,
 vile dishonour shall thy corse pursue;
 stripp’d arms alone (the conqueror’s due)
 rest greece uninjured i’ll restore:
 now plight thy mutual oath, ask more.”
 
“talk oaths (the dreadful chief replies,
 anger flash’d disdainful eyes),
 detested thou art, be,
 oath pact achilles plights thee:
 pacts lambs rabid wolves combine,
 leagues men furious lions join,
 call gods! one constant state
 lasting rancour eternal hate:
 thought rage, never-ceasing strife,
 till death extinguish rage, thought, life.
 rouse thy forces important hour,
 collect thy soul, call forth thy power.
 subterfuge, chance;
 ’tis pallas, pallas gives thee lance.
 grecian ghost, thee deprived breath,
 now hovers round, calls thee thy death.”
 
spoke, launch’d javelin foe;
 hector shunn’d meditated blow:
 stoop’d, o’er head flying spear
 sang innocent, spent force air.
 minerva watch’d falling land,
 drew, gave great achilles’ hand,
 unseen hector, who, elate joy,
 now shakes lance, braves dread troy.
 
“the life boasted javelin given,
 prince! miss’d. fate depends heaven,
 thee, presumptuous thou art, unknown,
 must prove fortune, thy own.
 boasting art, fears blind,
 false terrors sink another’s mind.
 know, whatever fate try,
 dishonest wound shall hector die.
 shall fall fugitive least,
 soul shall bravely issue breast.
 first, try thou arm; may dart
 end country’s woes, deep buried thy heart.”
 
weapon flew, course unerring held,
 unerring, heavenly shield repell’d
 mortal dart; resulting bound
 ringing orb, struck ground.
 hector beheld javelin fall vain,
 lance, hope remain;
 calls deiphobus, demands spear—
 vain, deiphobus there.
 comfortless stands: then, sigh;
 “’tis so—heaven wills it, hour nigh!
 deem’d deiphobus heard call,
 secure lies guarded wall.
 god deceived me; pallas, ’twas thy deed,
 death black fate approach! ’tis must bleed.
 refuge now, succour above,
 great jove deserts me, jove,
 propitious once, kind! welcome fate!
 ’tis true perish, yet perish great:
 yet mighty deed shall expire,
 let future ages hear it, admire!”
 
fierce, word, weighty sword drew,
 and, collected, achilles flew.
 jove’s bold bird, high balanced air,
 stoops clouds truss quivering hare.
 less achilles fierce soul prepares:
 breast flaming shield bears,
 refulgent orb! fourfold cone
 gilded horse-hair sparkled sun.
 nodding every step: (vulcanian frame!)
 moved, figure seem’d flame.
 radiant hesper shines keener light,[277]
 far-beaming o’er silver host night,
 starry train emblaze sphere:
 shone point great achilles’ spear.
 right hand waves weapon round,
 eyes whole man, meditates wound;
 rich mail patroclus lately wore
 securely cased warrior’s body o’er.
 one space length spies, let fate,
 ’twixt neck throat jointed plate
 gave entrance: penetrable part
 furious drove well-directed dart:
 pierced windpipe yet, took power
 speech, unhappy! thy dying hour.
 prone field bleeding warrior lies,
 while, thus triumphing, stern achilles cries:
 
“at last hector stretch’d upon plain,
 fear’d vengeance patroclus slain:
 then, prince! fear’d, now feel;
 achilles absent achilles still:
 yet short space great avenger stayed,
 low dust thy strength glory laid.
 peaceful sleeps, rites adorn’d,
 ever honour’d, ever mourn’d:
 cast rage hostile power,
 thee birds shall mangle, gods devour.”
 
hector, fainting approach death:
 “by thy soul! gave thee breath!
 sacred prevalence prayer;
 ah, leave grecian dogs tear!
 common rites sepulture bestow,
 soothe father’s mother’s woe:
 let large gifts procure urn least,
 hector’s ashes country rest.”
 
“no, wretch accursed! relentless replies;
 (flames, spoke, shot flashing eyes;)
 gave breath bid spare,
 sacred prevalence prayer.
 bloody banquet join!
 no—to dogs carcase resign.
 troy, bribe me, bring forth store,
 giving thousands, offer thousands more;
 dardan priam, weeping dame,
 drain whole realm buy one funeral flame:
 hector pile see,
 rob vultures one limb thee.”
 
thus chief dying accents drew:
 “thy rage, implacable! well knew:
 furies relentless breast steel’d,
 cursed thee heart yield.
 yet think, day will come, fate’s decree
 angry gods shall wreak wrong thee;
 phœbus paris shall avenge fate,
 stretch thee scæan gate.”[278]
 
ceased. fates suppress’d labouring breath,
 eyes stiffen’d hand death;
 dark realm spirit wings way,
 (the manly body left load clay,)
 plaintive glides along dreary coast,
 naked, wandering, melancholy ghost!
 
achilles, musing roll’d eyes
 o’er dead hero, thus unheard, replies:
 “die thou first! jove heaven ordain,
 follow thee”—he said, stripp’d slain.
 forcing backward gaping wound
 reeking javelin, cast ground.
 thronging greeks behold wondering eyes
 manly beauty superior size;
 some, ignobler, great dead deface
 wounds ungenerous, taunts disgrace:
 
“how changed hector, like jove late
 sent lightning fleets, scatter’d fate!”
 
high o’er slain great achilles stands,
 begirt heroes surrounding bands;
 thus aloud, host attends:
 “princes leaders! countrymen friends!
 since now length powerful will heaven
 dire destroyer arm given,
 troy fallen already? haste, ye powers!
 see, already deserted towers
 left unmann’d; yet retain
 souls heroes, great hector slain.
 troy, glory me?
 reflects mind aught thee,
 divine patroclus! death hath seal’d eyes;
 unwept, unhonour’d, uninterr’d lies!
 can dear image soul depart,
 long vital spirit moves heart?
 melancholy shades below,
 flames friends lovers cease glow,
 yet mine shall sacred last; mine, undecay’d,
 burn death, animate shade.
 meanwhile, ye sons greece, triumph bring
 corpse hector, pæans sing.
 song, slow-moving toward shore,
 “hector dead, ilion more.””
 
fell soul thought vengeance bred;
 (unworthy himself, dead;)
 nervous ancles bored, feet bound
 thongs inserted double wound;
 fix’d high behind rolling wain,
 graceful head trail’d along plain.
 proud car insulting victor stood,
 bore aloft arms, distilling blood.
 smites steeds; rapid chariot flies;
 sudden clouds circling dust arise.
 now lost formidable air;
 face divine, long-descending hair,
 purple ground, streak sable sand;
 deform’d, dishonour’d, native land,
 given rage insulting throng,
 and, parents’ sight, now dragg’d along!
 
mother first beheld sad survey;
 rent tresses, venerable grey,
 cast, far off, regal veils away.
 piercing shrieks bitter fate moans,
 sad father answers groans groans,
 tears tears mournful cheeks o’erflow,
 whole city wears one face woe:
 less rage hostile fires,
 foundations curling spires,
 o’er proud citadel length rise,
 last blaze send ilion skies.
 wretched monarch falling state,
 distracted, presses dardan gate.
 scarce whole people stop desperate course,
 strong affliction gives feeble force:
 grief tears heart, drives fro,
 raging impotence woe.
 length roll’d dust, thus begun,
 imploring all, naming one one:
 “ah! let me, let go sorrow calls;
 i, i, will issue walls
 (guide companion, friends! ask ye none),
 bow murderer son.
 grief perhaps pity may engage;
 perhaps least may respect age.
 father too; man like me;
 one, exempt age misery
 (vigorous more, young embrace
 begot pest me, race).
 many valiant sons, early bloom,
 cursed hand sent headlong tomb!
 thee, hector! last: thy loss (divinely brave)
 sinks sad soul sorrow grave.
 thy gentle spirit pass’d peace,
 expiring sire’s embrace,
 thy parents wept fatal hour,
 and, bending o’er thee, mix’d tender shower!
 comfort been, sad relief,
 melt full satiety grief!”
 
thus wail’d father, grovelling ground,
 eyes ilion stream’d around.
 
amidst matrons hecuba appears:
 (a mourning princess, train tears;)
 “ah heaven prolong’d hated breath,
 patient horrors, behold thy death?
 hector! late thy parents’ pride joy,
 boast nations! defence troy!
 safety fame owed;
 chief, hero, almost god!
 fatal change! become one sad day
 senseless corse! inanimated clay!”
 
yet fatal news spread
 fair andromache, hector dead;
 yet messenger told fate,
 e’en stay without scæan gate.
 far close recesses dome,
 pensive plied melancholy loom;
 growing work employ’d secret hours,
 confusedly gay intermingled flowers.
 fair-haired handmaids heat brazen urn,
 bath preparing lord’s return
 vain; alas! lord returns more;
 unbathed lies, bleeds along shore!
 now walls clamours reach ear,
 members shake sudden fear:
 forth ivory hand shuttle falls,
 thus, astonish’d, maids calls:
 

[illustration: ] bath
 

“ah follow me! (she cried) plaintive noise
 invades ear? ’tis sure mother’s voice.
 faltering knees trembling frame desert,
 pulse unusual flutters heart;
 strange disaster, reverse fate
 (ye gods avert it!) threats trojan state.
 far omen thoughts suggest!
 much fear hector’s dauntless breast
 confronts achilles; chased along plain,
 shut walls! fear, fear slain!
 safe crowd ever scorn’d wait,
 sought glory jaws fate:
 perhaps noble heat cost breath,
 now quench’d ever arms death.”
 
spoke: furious, distracted pace,
 fears heart, anguish face,
 flies dome (the maids steps pursue),
 mounts walls, sends around view.
 soon eyes killing object found,
 godlike hector dragg’d along ground.
 sudden darkness shades swimming eyes:
 faints, falls; breath, colour flies.
 hair’s fair ornaments, braids bound,
 net held them, wreath crown’d,
 veil diadem flew far away
 (the gift venus bridal day).
 around train weeping sisters stands,
 raise sinking assistant hands.
 scarce verge death recall’d, again
 faints, recovers complain.
 

[illustration: ] andromache fainting wall
 

“o wretched husband wretched wife!
 born one fate, one unhappy life!
 sure one star baneful beam display’d
 priam’s roof, hippoplacia’s shade.
 different parents, different climes came.
 different periods, yet fate same!
 birth great aëtion owed,
 tender care bestow’d?
 never been!—o thou, ghost
 dead husband! miserably lost!
 thou dismal realms ever gone!
 abandon’d, desolate, alone!
 child, comfort pains,
 sad product now hapless love, remains!
 smile upon sire; friend
 help now! father defend!
 ’scape sword, common doom,
 wrongs attend him, griefs come!
 even paternal roof expell’d,
 stranger ploughs patrimonial field.
 day, shades father sends,
 robs sad orphan father’s friends:
 he, wretched outcast mankind! appears
 ever sad, ever bathed tears;
 amongst happy, unregarded, he
 hangs robe, trembles knee,
 father’s former bounty fed
 reach goblet, divide bread:
 kindest present wants allay,
 leave wretched succeeding day.
 frugal compassion! heedless, boast
 parents still, feel lost,
 shall cry, ‘begone! thy father feasts here:’
 wretch obeys, retiring tear.
 thus wretched, thus retiring tears,
 sad soul astyanax appears!
 forced repeated insults return,
 widow’d mother vainly mourn:
 he, who, tender delicacy bred,
 princes sported, dainties fed,
 still evening gave rest,
 sunk soft upon nurse’s breast,
 must—ah must not? ilion calls
 astyanax, well-guarded walls,[279]
 now name more, unhappy boy!
 since now thy father guards troy.
 thou, hector, liest exposed air,
 far thy parents’ thy consort’s care;
 whose hand vain, directed love,
 martial scarf robe triumph wove.
 now devouring flames prey,
 useless thee, accursed day!
 yet let sacrifice least paid,
 honour living, dead!”
 

spake mournful dame: matrons hear, sigh back sighs, and
 answer tear tear.
 



book xxiii.
 

argument.
 

funeral games honour patroclus.[280]
 

achilles myrmidons honours body patroclus. after
 funeral feast retires sea-shore, where, falling asleep,
 ghost friend appears him, demands rites of
 burial; next morning soldiers sent mules waggons
 fetch wood pyre. funeral procession, offering
 hair dead. achilles sacrifices several animals, lastly
 twelve trojan captives, pile; sets fire it. pays
 libations winds, (at instance iris) rise, raise
 flames. pile burned night, gather bones,
 place urn gold, raise tomb. achilles institutes
 funeral games: chariot-race, fight caestus, the
 wrestling, foot-race, single combat, discus, shooting
 arrows, darting javelin: various descriptions of
 which, various success several antagonists, make the
 greatest part book.
 book ends thirtieth day. night following, ghost
 patroclus appears achilles: one-and-thirtieth day is
 employed felling timber pile: two-and-thirtieth
 burning it; three-and-thirtieth games. scene
 generally sea-shore.
 

thus humbled dust, pensive train
 sad city mourn’d hero slain.
 body soil’d dust, black gore,
 lies broad hellespont’s resounding shore.
 grecians seek ships, clear strand,
 all, martial myrmidonian band:
 yet assembled great achilles holds,
 stern purpose mind unfolds:
 
“not yet, brave companions war,
 release smoking coursers car;
 but, chariot order led,
 perform due honours patroclus dead.
 ere yet rest food seek relief,
 rites remain, glut rage grief.”
 
troops obey’d; thrice order led[281]
 (achilles first) coursers round dead;
 thrice sorrows laments renew;
 tears bathe arms, tears sands bedew.
 warrior thetis aids woe,
 melts strong hearts, bids eyes flow.
 chief, pelides: thick-succeeding sighs
 burst heart, torrents eyes:
 slaughtering hands, yet red blood, laid
 dead friend’s cold breast, thus said:
 
“all hail, patroclus! let thy honour’d ghost
 hear, rejoice pluto’s dreary coast;
 behold! achilles’ promise complete;
 bloody hector stretch’d thy feet.
 lo! dogs carcase resign;
 twelve sad victims, trojan line,
 sacred vengeance, instant shall expire;
 lives effused around thy funeral pyre.”
 
gloomy said, (horrible view)
 bier bleeding hector threw,
 prone dust. myrmidons around
 unbraced armour, steeds unbound.
 achilles’ sable ship repair,
 frequent full, genial feast share.
 now well-fed swine black smokes aspire,
 bristly victims hissing o’er fire:
 huge ox bellowing falls; feebler cries
 expires goat; sheep silence dies.
 around hero’s prostrate body flow’d,
 one promiscuous stream, reeking blood.
 now band argive monarchs brings
 glorious victor king kings.
 dead friend pensive warrior went,
 steps unwilling, regal tent.
 attending heralds, office bound,
 kindled flames tripod-vase surround:
 cleanse conquering hands hostile gore,
 urged vain; chief refused, swore:[282]
 
“no drop shall touch me, almighty jove!
 first greatest gods above!
 till pyre place thee; till rear
 grassy mound, clip thy sacred hair.
 ease least pious rites may give,
 soothe sorrows, bear live.
 howe’er, reluctant am, stay
 share feast; dawn day,
 (o king men!) claims thy royal care,
 greece warrior’s funeral pile prepare,
 bid forests fall: (such rites paid
 heroes slumbering eternal shade:)
 then, earthly part shall mount fire,
 let leagued squadrons posts retire.”
 
spoke: hear him, word obey;
 rage hunger thirst allay,
 ease sleep labours day.
 great pelides, stretch’d along shore,
 where, dash’d rocks, broken billows roar,
 lies inly groaning; either hand
 martial myrmidons confusedly stand.
 along grass languid members fall,
 tired chase around trojan wall;
 hush’d murmurs rolling deep,
 length sinks soft arms sleep.
 lo! shade, closing eyes,
 sad patroclus rose, seem’d rise:
 robe living wore, came:
 stature, voice, pleasing look, same.
 form familiar hover’d o’er head,
 “and sleeps achilles? (thus phantom said:)
 sleeps achilles, patroclus dead?
 living, seem’d dearest, tenderest care,
 now forgot, wander air.
 let pale corse rites burial know,
 give entrance realms below:
 till spirit finds resting-place,
 unbodied spectres chase
 vagrant dead around dark abode,
 forbid cross irremeable flood.
 now give thy hand; farther shore
 pass, soul returns more:
 last funereal flames ascend,
 shall meet achilles friend;
 thoughts loved make known;
 quit dearest, converse alone.
 fate sever’d sons earth,
 fate fore-doom’d waited birth:
 thee waits; trojan wall
 even great godlike thou art doom’d fall.
 hear then; fate love join,
 ah suffer bones may rest thine!
 together lived; together bred,
 one house received us, one table fed;
 golden urn, thy goddess-mother gave,
 may mix ashes one common grave.”
 
“and thou? (he answers) sight[283]
 return’st thou realms night?
 brother! think office paid,
 whate’er can rest discontented shade;
 grant one last embrace, unhappy boy!
 afford least melancholy joy.”
 
said, longing arms essay’d
 vain grasp visionary shade!
 like thin smoke sees spirit fly,[284]
 hears feeble, lamentable cry.
 confused wakes; amazement breaks bands
 golden sleep, starting sands,
 pensive muses uplifted hands:
 
“’tis true, ’tis certain; man, though dead, retains
 part himself; immortal mind remains:
 form subsists without body’s aid,
 aerial semblance, empty shade!
 night friend, late battle lost,
 stood side, pensive, plaintive ghost:
 even now familiar, life, came;
 alas! different! yet like same!”
 
thus spoke, eye grew big tears:
 now rosy-finger’d morn appears,
 shows every mournful face tears o’erspread,
 glares pale visage dead.
 agamemnon, rites demand,
 mules waggons sends chosen band
 load timber, pile rear;
 charge consign’d merion’s faithful care.
 proper instruments take road,
 axes cut, ropes sling load.
 first march heavy mules, securely slow,
 o’er hills, o’er dales, o’er crags, o’er rocks go:[285]
 jumping, high o’er shrubs rough ground,
 rattle clattering cars, shock’d axles bound.
 arrived ida’s spreading woods,[286]
 (fair ida, water’d descending floods,)
 loud sounds axe, redoubling strokes strokes;
 sides round forest hurls oaks
 headlong. deep echoing groan thickets brown;
 rustling, crackling, crashing, thunder down.
 wood grecians cleave, prepared burn;
 slow mules rough road return.
 sturdy woodmen equal burdens bore
 (such charge given them) sandy shore;
 spot great achilles show’d,
 eased shoulders, disposed load;
 circling around place, times come
 shall view patroclus’ achilles’ tomb.
 hero bids martial troops appear
 high cars pomp war;
 refulgent arms limbs attires,
 mount chariots, combatants squires.
 chariots first proceed, shining train;
 clouds foot smoke along plain;
 next melancholy band appear;
 amidst, lay dead patroclus bier;
 o’er corse scattered locks throw;
 achilles next, oppress’d mighty woe,
 supporting hands hero’s head,
 bends o’er extended body dead.
 patroclus decent appointed ground
 place, heap sylvan pile around.
 great achilles stands apart prayer,
 head divides yellow hair;
 curling locks youth vow’d,[287]
 sacred grew, sperchius’ honour’d flood:
 sighing, deep locks cast,
 roll’d eyes around watery waste:
 
“sperchius! whose waves mazy errors lost
 delightful roll along native coast!
 vainly vow’d, return,
 locks fall, hecatombs burn:
 full fifty rams bleed sacrifice,
 day thy silver fountains rise,
 shade consecrated bowers
 thy altars stand, perfumed native flowers!
 vow’d father, vow’d vain;
 achilles sees native plain;
 vain hope hairs longer grow,
 patroclus bears shades below.”
 
thus o’er patroclus hero pray’d,
 cold hand sacred lock laid.
 afresh grecian sorrows flow:
 now sun set upon woe;
 king men thus spoke chief:
 “enough, atrides! give troops relief:
 permit mourning legions retire,
 let chiefs alone attend pyre;
 pious care ours, dead burn—”
 said: people ships return:
 deputed inter slain
 heap rising pyramid plain.[288]
 hundred foot length, hundred wide,
 growing structure spreads every side;
 high top manly corse lay,
 well-fed sheep sable oxen slay:
 achilles covered fat dead,
 piled victims round body spread;
 jars honey, fragrant oil,
 suspends around, low-bending o’er pile.
 four sprightly coursers, deadly groan
 pour forth lives, pyre thrown.
 nine large dogs, domestic board,
 fall two, selected attend lord,
 last all, horrible tell,
 sad sacrifice! twelve trojan captives fell.[289]
 rage fire victorious preys,
 involves joins one common blaze.
 smear’d bloody rites, stands high,
 calls spirit dreadful cry:[290]
 
“all hail, patroclus! let thy vengeful ghost
 hear, exult, pluto’s dreary coast.
 behold achilles’ promise fully paid,
 twelve trojan heroes offer’d thy shade;
 heavier fates hector’s corse attend,
 saved flames, hungry dogs rend.”
 
spake he, threatening: gods made vain
 threat, guard inviolate slain:
 celestial venus hover’d o’er head,
 roseate unguents, heavenly fragrance! shed:
 watch’d night day,
 drove bloodhounds destined prey.
 sacred phœbus less employ’d care;
 pour’d around veil gather’d air,
 kept nerves undried, flesh entire,
 solar beam sirian fire.
 

[illustration: ] funeral pile patroclus
 

yet pile, dead patroclus lies,
 smokes, yet sullen flames arise;
 but, fast beside, achilles stood prayer,
 invoked gods whose spirit moves air,
 victims promised, libations cast,
 gentle zephyr boreal blast:
 call’d aerial powers, along skies
 breathe, whisper fires rise.
 winged iris heard hero’s call,
 instant hasten’d airy hall,
 old zephyr’s open courts high,
 sat blustering brethren sky.
 shone amidst them, painted bow;
 rocky pavement glitter’d show.
 banquet rise, invites
 various goddess partake rites.
 “not (the dame replied), haste go
 sacred ocean, floods below:
 even now solemn hecatombs attend,
 heaven feasting world’s green end
 righteous ethiops (uncorrupted train!)
 far extremest limits main.
 peleus’ entreats, sacrifice,
 western spirit, north, rise!
 let patroclus’ pile blast driven,
 bear blazing honours high heaven.”
 
swift word vanish’d view;
 swift word winds tumultuous flew;
 forth burst stormy band thundering roar,
 heaps heaps clouds toss’d before.
 wide main stooping skies,
 heaving deeps watery mountains rise:
 troy feels blast along shaking walls,
 till pile gather’d tempest falls.
 structure crackles roaring fires,
 night plenteous flame aspires.
 night achilles hails patroclus’ soul,
 large libations golden bowl.
 poor father, helpless undone,
 mourns o’er ashes son,
 takes sad pleasure last bones burn,
 pours tears, ere yet close urn:
 stay’d achilles, circling round shore,
 watch’d flames, till now flame more.
 ’twas when, emerging shades night,
 morning planet told approach light;
 and, fast behind, aurora’s warmer ray
 o’er broad ocean pour’d golden day:
 sank blaze, pile longer burn’d,
 caves whistling winds return’d:
 across thracian seas course bore;
 ruffled seas beneath passage roar.
 
parting pile ceased weep,
 sank quiet embrace sleep,
 exhausted grief: meanwhile crowd
 thronging grecians round achilles stood;
 tumult waked him: eyes shook
 unwilling slumber, chiefs bespoke:
 
“ye kings princes achaian name!
 first let us quench yet remaining flame
 sable wine; then, rites direct,
 hero’s bones careful view select:
 (apart, easy known lie
 amidst heap, obvious eye:
 rest around margin will seen
 promiscuous, steeds immolated men:)
 wrapp’d double cauls fat, prepare;
 golden vase dispose care;
 let rest decent honour laid,
 till shall follow infernal shade.
 meantime erect tomb pious hands,
 common structure humble sands:
 hereafter greece nobler work may raise,
 late posterity record praise!”
 
greeks obey; yet embers glow,
 wide o’er pile sable wine throw,
 deep subsides ashy heap below.
 next white bones sad companions place,
 tears collected, golden vase.
 sacred relics tent bore;
 urn veil linen covered o’er.
 done, bid sepulchre aspire,
 cast deep foundations round pyre;
 high midst heap swelling bed
 rising earth, memorial dead.
 
swarming populace chief detains,
 leads amidst wide extent plains;
 placed round: ships proceeds
 train oxen, mules, stately steeds,
 vases tripods (for funeral games),
 resplendent brass, resplendent dames.
 first stood prizes reward force
 rapid racers dusty course:
 woman first, beauty’s bloom,
 skill’d needle, labouring loom;
 large vase, two bright handles rise,
 twenty measures capacious size.
 second victor claims mare unbroke,
 big mule, unknowing yoke:
 third, charger yet untouch’d flame;
 four ample measures held shining frame:
 two golden talents fourth placed:
 ample double bowl contents last.
 fair order ranged upon plain,
 hero, rising, thus address’d train:
 
“behold prizes, valiant greeks! decreed
 brave rulers racing steed;
 prizes none beside ourself gain,
 immortal coursers take plain;
 (a race unrivall’d, ocean’s god
 peleus received, bestow’d.)
 time vigour display;
 suit, them, games sad day:
 lost patroclus now, wont deck
 flowing manes, sleek glossy neck.
 sad, shared human grief, stand,
 trail graceful honours sand!
 let others noble task prepare,
 trust courser flying car.”
 
fired word rival racers rise;
 far first eumelus hopes prize,
 famed though pieria fleetest breed,
 skill’d manage high-bounding steed.
 equal ardour bold tydides swell’d,
 steeds tros beneath yoke compell’d
 (which late obey’d dardan chief’s command,
 scarce god redeem’d hand).
 menelaus podargus brings,
 famed courser king kings:
 rich echepolus (more rich brave),
 ’scape wars, agamemnon gave,
 (Æthe name) home end days;
 base wealth preferring eternal praise.
 next antilochus demands course
 beating heart, cheers pylian horse.
 experienced nestor gives reins,
 directs judgment, heat restrains;
 idly warns hoary sire, hears
 prudent unattending ears.
 
“my son! though youthful ardour fire thy breast,
 gods loved thee, arts bless’d;
 neptune jove thee conferr’d skill
 swift round goal turn flying wheel.
 guide thy conduct little precept needs;
 slow, past vigour, steeds.
 fear thy rivals, though swiftness known;
 compare rivals’ judgment thy own:
 strength, art, obtains prize,
 swift less wise.
 ’tis art force numerous strokes
 dexterous woodman shapes stubborn oaks;
 art pilot, boiling deep
 howling tempest, steers fearless ship;
 ’tis artist wins glorious course;
 trust chariots horse.
 vain, unskilful goal strive,
 short, wide, ungovern’d courser drive:
 sure skill, though inferior steeds,
 knowing racer end proceeds;
 fix’d goal eye foreruns course,
 hand unerring steers steady horse,
 now contracts, now extends rein,
 observing still foremost plain.
 mark goal, ’tis easy found;
 yon aged trunk, cubit ground;
 stately oak last remains,
 hardy fir, unperish’d rains:
 inclosed stones, conspicuous afar;
 round, circle wheeling car.
 (some tomb perhaps old, dead grace;
 then, now, limit race.)
 bear close this, warily proceed,
 little bending left-hand steed;
 urge right, give reins;
 thy strict hand fellow’s head restrains,
 turns short; till, doubling roll,
 wheel’s round naves appear brush goal.
 yet (not break car, lame horse)
 clear stony heap direct course;
 lest incaution failing, thou mayst be
 joy others, reproach me.
 shalt thou pass goal, secure mind,
 leave unskilful swiftness far behind:
 though thy fierce rival drove matchless steed
 bore adrastus, celestial breed;
 famed race, regions known,
 whirl’d car proud laomedon.”
 
thus (nought unsaid) much-advising sage
 concludes; sat, stiff unwieldy age.
 next bold meriones seen rise,
 last, least ardent prize.
 mount seats; lots place dispose
 (roll’d helmet, achilles throws).
 young nestor leads race: eumelus then;
 next brother king men:
 thy lot, meriones, fourth cast;
 and, far bravest, diomed, last.
 stand order, impatient train:
 pelides points barrier plain,
 sends old phœnix place,
 mark racers, judge race.
 coursers barrier bound;
 lifted scourges resound;
 heart, eyes, voice, send before;
 champaign thunder shore:
 thick, drive, dusty clouds arise,
 lost courser whirlwind flies;
 loose shoulders long manes reclined,
 float speed, dance upon wind:
 smoking chariots, rapid bound,
 now seem touch sky, now ground.
 hot fame, conquest care,
 (each o’er flying courser hung air,)
 erect ardour, poised upon rein,
 pant, stretch, shout along plain.
 now (the last compass fetch’d around goal)
 near prize gathers soul,
 burns double hope, double pain,
 tears shore, thunders toward main.
 first flew eumelus pheretian steeds;
 tros bold diomed succeeds:
 close eumelus’ back puff wind,
 seem just mounting car behind;
 full neck feels sultry breeze,
 and, hovering o’er, stretching shadows sees.
 lost, left doubtful prize;
 angry phœbus tydides flies,
 strikes hand scourge, renders vain
 matchless horses’ labour plain.
 rage fills eye anguish, survey
 snatch’d hope glories day.
 fraud celestial pallas sees pain,
 springs knight, gives scourge again,
 fills steeds vigour. stroke
 breaks rival’s chariot yoke:
 way startled horses held;
 car reversed came rattling field;
 shot headlong seat, beside wheel,
 prone dust unhappy master fell;
 batter’d face elbows strike ground;
 nose, mouth, front, one undistinguish’d wound:
 grief stops voice, torrent drowns eyes:
 far glad tydides flies;
 minerva’s spirit drives matchless pace,
 crowns victor labour’d race.
 
next, though distant, menelaus succeeds;
 thus young nestor animates steeds:
 “now, now, generous pair, exert force;
 hope match tydides’ horse,
 since great minerva wings rapid way,
 gives lord honours day;
 reach atrides! shall mare outgo
 swiftness? vanquish’d female foe?
 neglect, lagging plain
 last ignoble gift gain,
 shall nestor’s hand food supply,
 old man’s fury rises, ye die.
 haste then: yon narrow road, sight,
 presents occasion, use right.”
 
thus he. coursers master’s threat
 quicker steps sounding champaign beat.
 now antilochus nice survey
 observes compass hollow way.
 ’twas where, force wintry torrents torn,
 fast road precipice worn:
 here, one pass, shun throng
 spartan hero’s chariot smoked along.
 close venturous youth resolves keep,
 still edging near, bears toward steep.
 atrides, trembling, casts eye below,
 wonders rashness foe.
 “hold, stay steeds—what madness thus ride
 narrow way! take larger field (he cried),
 must fall.”—atrides cried vain;
 flies fast, throws rein.
 far able arm disk can send,
 youthful rivals full force extend,
 far, antilochus! thy chariot flew
 king: he, cautious, backward drew
 horse compell’d; foreboding fears
 rattling ruin clashing cars,
 floundering coursers rolling plain,
 conquest lost frantic haste gain.
 thus upbraids rival flies:
 “go, furious youth! ungenerous unwise!
 go, expect i’ll prize resign;
 add perjury fraud, make thine—”
 steeds force cries,
 “be swift, vigorous, regain prize!
 rivals, destitute youthful force,
 fainting knees shall labour course,
 yield glory yours.”—the steeds obey;
 already heels wing way,
 seem already retrieve day.
 
meantime grecians ring beheld
 coursers bounding o’er dusty field.
 first mark’d cretan king;
 high rising ground, ring,
