 monarch sat: whence sure survey
 well observed chief led way,
 heard far animating cries,
 saw foremost steed sharpen’d eyes;
 whose broad front blaze shining white,
 like full moon, stood obvious sight.
 saw; rising, greeks begun:
 “are yonder horse discern’d alone?
 can ye, all, another chief survey,
 steeds lately led way?
 those, though swiftest, god withheld,
 lie sure disabled middle field:
 for, since goal doubled, round plain
 search find them, search vain.
 perchance reins forsook driver’s hand,
 and, turn’d short, tumbled strand,
 shot chariot; coursers stray
 frantic fury destined way.
 rise other, inform sight,
 dim eyes, perhaps, discern right;
 yet sure seems, judge shape air,
 great Ætolian chief, renown’d war.”
 
“old man! (oïleus rashly thus replies)
 thy tongue hastily confers prize;
 view course, sharpest eyed,
 youngest, yet readiest decide.
 eumelus’ steeds, high bounding chase,
 still, first, unrivall’d lead race:
 well discern him, shakes rein,
 hear shouts victorious o’er plain.”
 
thus he. idomeneus, incensed, rejoin’d:
 “barbarous words! arrogant mind!
 contentious prince, greeks beside
 last merit, first pride!
 vile reproach answer can make?
 goblet tripod let us stake,
 king judge. unwise
 will learn rashness, pay price.”
 
said: ajax, mad passion borne,
 stern replied; fierce scorn enhancing scorn
 fell extremes. thetis’ godlike son
 awful amidst rose, thus begun:
 
“forbear, ye chiefs! reproachful contend;
 much ye blame, others thus offend:
 lo! approaching steeds contest end.”
 sooner spoke, thundering near,
 drives, stream dust, charioteer.
 high o’er head circling lash wields:
 bounding horses scarcely touch fields:
 car amidst dusty whirlwind roll’d,
 bright mingled blaze tin gold,
 refulgent cloud: eye find
 track flying wheels left behind:
 fierce coursers urged rapid pace
 swift, seem’d flight, race.
 now victor goal tydides stands,
 quits bright car, springs upon sands;
 hot steeds sweaty torrents stream;
 well-plied whip hung athwart beam:
 joy brave sthenelus receives prize,
 tripod-vase, dame radiant eyes:
 ships train triumphant leads,
 chief unyokes panting steeds.
 
young nestor follows (who art, force,
 o’erpass’d atrides) second course.
 behind, atrides urged race, near
 courser swift career
 following car, just touching heel
 brushing tail whirling wheel:
 such, narrow now space between
 rivals, late distant green;
 soon swift Æthe lost ground regain’d,
 one length, one moment, race obtain’d.
 
merion pursued, greater distance still,
 tardier coursers, inferior skill.
 last came, admetus! thy unhappy son;
 slow dragged steeds batter’d chariot on:
 achilles saw, pitying thus begun:
 
“behold! man whose matchless art surpass’d
 sons greece! ablest, yet last!
 fortune denies, justice bids us pay
 (since great tydides bears first away)
 second honours day.”
 
greeks consent loud-applauding cries,
 eumelus received prize,
 youthful nestor, jealous fame,
 award opposes, asserts claim.
 “think (he cries) tamely will resign,
 peleus’ son! mare justly mine.
 gods, skilful confound,
 thrown horse horseman ground?
 perhaps sought heaven sacrifice,
 vows omitted forfeited prize.
 yet (distinction thy friend show,
 please soul desirous bestow)
 gift must grace eumelus, view thy store
 beauteous handmaids, steeds, shining ore;
 ample present let thence receive,
 greece shall praise thy generous thirst give.
 prize never shall forego;
 this, touches, warriors! foe.”
 
thus spake youth; words offend;
 pleased well-turn’d flattery friend,
 achilles smiled: “the gift proposed (he cried),
 antilochus! shall ourself provide.
 plates brass corslet cover’d o’er,
 (the renown’d asteropaeus wore,)
 whose glittering margins raised silver shine,
 (no vulgar gift,) eumelus! shall thine.”
 
said: automedon command
 corslet brought, gave hand.
 distinguish’d friend, bosom glows
 generous joy: menelaus rose;
 herald placed sceptre hands,
 still’d clamour shouting bands.
 without cause incensed nestor’s son,
 inly grieving, thus king begun:
 
“the praise wisdom, thy youth obtain’d,
 act rash, antilochus! stain’d.
 robb’d glory just reward,
 you, grecians! wrong declared:
 leader shall conduct blame,
 judge envious rival’s fame.
 shall we, ourselves, truth maintain?
 needs appealing fact plain?
 greek shall blame me, bid thee rise,
 vindicate oath th’ ill-gotten prize?
 rise thou darest, thy chariot stand,
 driving scourge high-lifted thy hand;
 touch thy steeds, swear thy whole intent
 conquer, circumvent.
 swear god whose liquid arms surround
 globe, whose dread earthquakes heave ground!”
 
prudent chief calm attention heard;
 mildly thus: “excuse, youth err’d;
 superior thou art, forgive offence,
 thy equal, years, sense.
 thou know’st errors unripen’d age,
 weak counsels, headlong rage.
 prize quit, thou thy wrath resign;
 mare, aught thou ask’st, freely thine
 ere become (from thy dear friendship torn)
 hateful thee, gods forsworn.”
 
spoke antilochus; word
 mare contested king restored.
 joy swells soul: vernal grain
 lifts green ear springing plain,
 fields vegetable life renew,
 laugh glitter morning dew;
 joy spartan’s shining face o’erspread,
 lifted gay heart, thus said:
 
“still may souls, generous youth! agree
 ’tis now atrides’ turn yield thee.
 rash heat perhaps moment might control,
 break, settled temper thy soul.
 (my friend) ’tis still wiser way
 waive contention superior sway;
 ah! few, like thee offend,
 like thee, talents regain friend!
 plead indulgence, thy fault atone,
 suffice thy father’s merit thy own:
 generous alike, me, sire son
 greatly suffer’d, greatly done.
 yield; may know, soul can bend,
 pride preferr’d friend.”
 
said; pleased passion command,
 resign’d courser noemon’s hand,
 friend youthful chief: content,
 shining charger vessel sent.
 golden talents merion next obtain’d;
 fifth reward, double bowl, remain’d.
 achilles reverend nestor bears.
 thus purpose gift declares:
 “accept thou this, sacred sire! (he said)
 dear memorial patroclus dead;
 dead ever lost patroclus lies,
 ever snatch’d desiring eyes!
 take thou token grateful heart,
 though ’tis thine hurl distant dart,
 quoit toss, ponderous mace wield,
 urge race, wrestle field:
 thy pristine vigour age overthrown,
 left glory past thy own.”
 
said, placed goblet side;
 joy venerable king replied:
 
“wisely well, son, thy words proved
 senior honour’d, friend beloved!
 true is, deserted strength,
 wither’d arms limbs fail’d length.
 oh! now force felt yore,
 known buprasium pylian shore!
 victorious every solemn game,
 ordain’d amarynces’ mighty name;
 brave epeians gave glory way,
 Ætolians, pylians, resign’d day.
 quell’d clytomedes fights hand,
 backward hurl’d ancæus sand,
 surpass’d iphyclus swift career,
 phyleus polydorus spear.
 sons actor won prize horse,
 won numbers, art force:
 famed twins, impatient survey
 prize prize nestor borne away,
 sprung car; united pains
 one lash’d coursers, one ruled reins.
 was! now tasks succeeds
 younger race, emulate deeds:
 yield, alas! (to age must yield?)
 though foremost hero field.
 go thou, son! generous friendship led,
 martial honours decorate dead:
 pleased take gift thy hands present,
 (pledge benevolence, kind intent,)
 rejoiced, numerous greeks, see
 one honours sacred age me:
 due distinctions thou well canst pay,
 may just gods return another day!”
 
proud gift, thus spake full days:
 achilles heard him, prouder praise.
 
prizes next order’d field,
 bold champions caestus wield.
 stately mule, yet toils unbroke,
 six years’ age, unconscious yoke,
 circus led, firmly bound;
 next stands goblet, massy, large, round.
 achilles rising, thus: “let greece excite
 two heroes equal hardy fight;
 dare foe lifted arms provoke,
 rush beneath long-descending stroke.
 apollo shall palm bestow,
 greeks supreme conquest know,
 mule dauntless labours shall repay,
 vanquish’d bear massy bowl away.”
 
dreadful combat great epeüs chose;[291]
 high o’er crowd, enormous bulk! rose,
 seized beast, thus began say:
 “stand forth man, bear bowl away!
 (price ruin: dares deny
 mule right; undoubted victor i)
 others, ’tis own’d, fields battle shine,
 first honours fight mine;
 excels all? let foe
 draw near, first certain fortune know;
 secure hand shall whole frame confound,
 mash bones, body pound:
 let friends nigh, needful train,
 heave batter’d carcase plain.”
 
giant spoke; stupid gaze
 host beheld him, silent amaze!
 ’twas thou, euryalus! durst aspire
 meet might, emulate thy sire,
 great mecistheus; days yore
 theban games noblest trophy bore,
 (the games ordain’d dead oedipus grace,)
 singly vanquish cadmean race.
 great tydides urges contend,
 warm hopes conquest friend;
 officious cincture girds round;
 wrist gloves death bound.
 amid circle now champion stands,
 poises high air iron hands;
 clashing gauntlets now fiercely close,
 crackling jaws re-echo blows,
 painful sweat members flows.
 length epeus dealt weighty blow
 full cheek unwary foe;
 beneath ponderous arm’s resistless sway
 dropp’d he, nerveless, extended lay.
 large fish, winds waters roar,
 huge billow dash’d shore,
 lies panting; less batter’d wound,
 bleeding hero pants upon ground.
 rear fallen foe, victor lends,
 scornful, hand; gives friends;
 whose arms support him, reeling throng,
 dragging disabled legs along;
 nodding, head hangs shoulder o’er;
 mouth nostrils pour clotted gore;[292]
 wrapp’d round mists lies, lost thought;
 friends receive bowl, dearly bought.
 
third bold game achilles next demands,
 calls wrestlers level sands:
 massy tripod victor lies,
 twice six oxen reputed price;
 next, loser’s spirits restore,
 female captive, valued four.
 scarce chief vigorous strife propose
 tower-like ajax ulysses rose.
 amid ring nervous rival stands,
 embracing rigid implicit hands.
 close lock’d above, heads arms mix’d:
 below, planted feet distance fix’d;
 like two strong rafters builder forms,
 proof wintry winds howling storms,
 tops connected, wider space
 fix’d centre stands solid base.
 now grasp manly body bends;
 humid sweat every pore descends;
 bones resound blows: sides, shoulders, thighs
 swell gripe, bloody tumours rise.
 ulysses, art renown’d,
 o’erturn strength ajax ground;
 strength ajax overthrow
 watchful caution artful foe.
 long strife even tired lookers on,
 thus ulysses spoke great telamon:
 “or let lift thee, chief, lift thou me:
 prove force, jove rest decree.”
 
said; and, straining, heaved ground
 matchless strength; time ulysses found
 strength evade, nerves combine
 ankle struck: giant fell supine;
 ulysses, following, bosom lies;
 shouts applause run rattling skies.
 ajax lift ulysses next essays;
 barely stirr’d him, raise:
 knee lock’d fast, foe’s attempt denied;
 grappling close, tumbled side side.
 defiled honourable dust roll,
 still breathing strife, unsubdued soul:
 rage, combat rise;
 great achilles thus divides prize:
 
“your noble vigour, friends, restrain;
 weary generous strength vain.
 ye won: let others excel,
 now prove prowess proved well.”
 
hero’s words willing chiefs obey,
 tired bodies wipe dust away,
 and, clothed anew, following games survey.
 
now succeed gifts ordain’d grace
 youths contending rapid race:
 silver urn full six measures held,
 none weight workmanship excell’d:
 sidonian artists taught frame shine,
 elaborate, artifice divine;
 whence tyrian sailors prize transport,
 gave thoas lemnian port:
 descended, good eunaeus heir’d
 glorious gift; and, lycaon spared,
 brave patroclus gave rich reward:
 now, hero’s funeral rites grace,
 stands prize swiftness race.
 well-fed ox second placed;
 half talent must content last.
 achilles rising bespoke train:
 “who hope palm swiftness obtain,
 stand forth, bear prizes plain.”
 
hero said, starting place,
 oilean ajax rises race;
 ulysses next; whose speed surpass’d
 youthful equals, nestor’s son, last.
 ranged line ready racers stand;
 pelides points barrier hand;
 start once; oïleus led race;
 next ulysses, measuring pace pace;
 behind him, diligently close, sped,
 closely following running thread
 spindle follows, displays charms
 fair spinster’s breast moving arms:
 graceful motion thus, foe plies,
 treads footstep ere dust can rise;
 glowing breath upon shoulders plays:
 admiring greeks loud acclamations raise:
 give wishes, hearts, eyes,
 send souls flies.
 now three times turn’d prospect goal,
 panting chief pallas lifts soul:
 “assist, goddess!” thus thought pray’d!
 present thought descends maid.
 buoy’d heavenly force, seems swim,
 feels pinion lifting every limb.
 fierce, ready now prize gain,
 unhappy ajax stumbles plain
 (o’erturn’d pallas), slippery shore
 clogg’d slimy dung mingled gore.
 (the self-same place beside patroclus’ pyre,
 late slaughter’d victims fed fire.)
 besmear’d filth, blotted o’er clay,
 obscene sight, rueful racer lay;
 well-fed bull (the second prize) shared,
 left urn ulysses’ rich reward.
 then, grasping horn mighty beast,
 baffled hero thus greeks address’d:
 
“accursed fate! conquest forego;
 mortal i, goddess foe;
 urged favourite rapid way,
 pallas, ulysses, won day.”
 
thus sourly wail’d he, sputtering dirt gore;
 burst laughter echoed shore.
 antilochus, humorous rest,
 takes last prize, takes jest:
 
“why wiser elders strive?
 gods still love them, always thrive.
 ye see, ajax must yield prize:
 ulysses, still aged wise;
 (a green old age unconscious decays,
 proves hero born better days!)
 behold vigour active race!
 achilles boasts swifter pace:
 can match achilles? can,
 must yet hero, man.”
 
effect succeeds speech. pelides cries,
 “thy artful praise deserves better prize.
 greece vain shall hear thy friend extoll’d;
 receive talent purest gold.”
 youth departs content. host admire
 nestor, worthy sire.
 
next buckler, spear, helm, brings;
 cast plain, brazen burden rings:
 arms late divine sarpedon wore,
 great patroclus short triumph bore.
 “stand forth bravest host! (he cries)
 whoever dares deserve rich prize,
 now grace lists army’s sight,
 sheathed steel, provoke foe fight.
 first jointed armour shall explore,
 stain rival’s mail issuing gore,
 sword asteropaeus possess’d old,
 (a thracian blade, distinct studs gold,)
 shall pay stroke, grace striker’s side:
 arms common let chiefs divide:
 brave champion, combat ends,
 sumptuous banquet tents attends.”
 
fierce word uprose great tydeus’ son,
 huge bulk ajax telamon.
 clad refulgent steel, either hand,
 dreadful chiefs amid circle stand;
 louring meet, tremendous sight;
 argive bosom beats fierce delight.
 opposed arms long idly stood,
 thrice closed, thrice charge renew’d.
 furious pass spear ajax made
 broad shield, corslet stay’d.
 thus foe: javelin aim’d above
 buckler’s margin, neck drove.
 greece, now trembling hero’s life,
 bade share honours, surcease strife.
 yet still victor’s due tydides gains,
 sword studded belt remains.
 
hurl’d hero, thundering ground,
 mass iron (an enormous round),
 whose weight size circling greeks admire,
 rude furnace, shaped fire.
 mighty quoit aëtion wont rear,
 whirling arm dismiss air;
 giant achilles slain, stow’d
 among spoils memorable load.
 this, bids nervous artists vie,
 teach disk sound along sky.
 “let him, whose might can hurl bowl, arise;
 farthest hurls it, take prize;
 one enrich’d large domain
 downs flocks, arable grain,
 small stock iron needs man provide;
 hinds swains whole years shall supplied
 hence; ask neighbouring city’s aid
 ploughshares, wheels, rural trade.”
 
stern polypœtes stepp’d throng,
 great leonteus, mortal strong;
 whose force rival forces oppose,
 uprose great ajax; epeus rose.
 stood order: first epeus threw;
 high o’er wondering crowds whirling circle flew.
 leonteus next little space surpass’d;
 third, strength godlike ajax cast.
 o’er marks flew; till fiercely flung
 polypœtes’ arm discus sung:
 far swain whirling sheephook throws,
 distant falls among grazing cows,
 past rapid circle flies:
 friends, loud applauses shake skies,
 force conjoin’d heave weighty prize.
 
those, skilful archery contend,
 next invites twanging bow bend;
 twice ten axes casts amidst round,
 ten double-edged, ten singly wound
 mast, late first-rate galley bore,
 hero fixes sandy shore;
 tall top milk-white dove tie,
 trembling mark arrows fly.
 
“whose weapon strikes yon fluttering bird, shall bear
 two-edged axes, terrible war;
 single, whose shaft divides cord.”
 said: experienced merion took word;
 skilful teucer: helm threw
 lots inscribed, forth latter flew.
 swift string sounding arrow flies;
 flies unbless’d! grateful sacrifice,
 firstling lambs, unheedful! didst thou vow
 phœbus, patron shaft bow.
 this, thy well-aim’d arrow turn’d aside,
 err’d dove, yet cut cord tied:
 adown mainmast fell parted string,
 free bird heaven displays wing:
 sea, shores, skies, loud applause resound,
 merion eager meditates wound:
 takes bow, directs shaft above,
 following eye soaring dove,
 implores god speed skies,
 vows firstling lambs, grateful sacrifice,
 dove, airy circles wheels,
 amid clouds piercing arrow feels;
 quite point passage found,
 feet fell bloody ground.
 wounded bird, ere yet breathed last,
 flagging wings alighted mast,
 moment hung, spread pinions there,
 sudden dropp’d, left life air.
 pleased crowd new peals thunder rise,
 ships brave merion bears prize.
 
close funeral games, achilles last
 massy spear amid circle placed,
 ample charger unsullied frame,
 flowers high-wrought, blacken’d yet flame.
 bids heroes prove art,
 whose dexterous skill directs flying dart.
 great merion hopes noble prize;
 disdain’d king men rise.
 joy pelides saw honour paid,
 rose monarch, respectful said:
 
“thee first virtue, power supreme,
 king nations! thy greeks proclaim;
 every martial game thy worth attest,
 know thee greatest best.
 take prize, let brave merion bear
 beamy javelin thy brother’s war.”
 
pleased hero’s lips praise hear,
 king merion gives brazen spear:
 but, set apart sacred use, commands
 glittering charger talthybius’ hands.

book xxiv.
 

argument.
 

redemption body hector.
 

gods deliberate redemption hector’s body. jupiter
 sends thetis achilles, dispose restoring it, iris
 priam, encourage go person treat it. old
 king, notwithstanding remonstrances queen, makes ready for
 journey, encouraged omen jupiter. sets
 forth chariot, waggon loaded presents, the
 charge idæus herald. mercury descends shape young
 man, conducts pavilion achilles. conversation
 way. priam finds achilles table, casts his
 feet, begs body son: achilles, moved with
 compassion, grants request, detains one night tent, and
 next morning sends home body: trojans run to
 meet him. lamentations andromache, hecuba, helen, the
 solemnities funeral.
 time twelve days employed book, body of
 hector lies tent achilles; many spent in
 truce allowed interment. scene partly in
 achilles’ camp, partly troy.
 

now finish’d games grecian band
 seek black ships, clear crowded strand,
 stretch’d ease genial banquet share,
 pleasing slumbers quiet care.
 achilles: he, grief resign’d,
 friend’s dear image present mind,
 takes sad couch, unobserved weep;
 tastes gifts all-composing sleep.
 restless roll’d around weary bed,
 soul patroclus fed:
 form pleasing, heart kind,
 youthful vigour, manly mind,
 toils shared, martial works wrought,
 seas measured, fields fought;
 pass’d remembrance dear,
 thought follows thought, tear succeeds tear.
 now supine, now prone, hero lay,
 now shifts side, impatient day:
 starting up, disconsolate goes
 wide lonely beach vent woes.
 solitary mourner raves,
 ruddy morning rises o’er waves:
 soon rose, furious steeds join’d!
 chariot flies, hector trails behind.
 thrice, patroclus! round thy monument
 hector dragg’d, hurried tent.
 sleep last o’ercomes hero’s eyes;
 foul dust unhonour’d carcase lies,
 deserted pitying skies:
 phœbus watch’d superior care,
 preserved gaping wounds tainting air;
 and, ignominious swept field,
 spread o’er sacred corse golden shield.
 heaven moved, hermes will’d go
 stealth snatch insulting foe:
 neptune this, pallas denies,
 th’ unrelenting empress skies,
 e’er since day implacable troy,
 time young paris, simple shepherd boy,
 won destructive lust (reward obscene),
 charms rejected cyprian queen.
 tenth celestial morning broke,
 heaven assembled, thus apollo spoke:
 

[illustration: ] hector’s body car achilles
 

“unpitying powers! oft holy fane
 hector tinged blood victims slain?
 can ye still cold remains pursue?
 still grudge body trojans’ view?
 deny consort, mother, son, sire,
 last sad honours funeral fire?
 dire achilles care?
 iron heart, inflexibly severe;
 lion, man, slaughters wide,
 strength rage, impotence pride;
 hastes murder savage joy,
 invades around, breathes destroy!
 shame soul; understood,
 greatest evil greatest good.
 still one loss rages unresign’d,
 repugnant lot mankind;
 lose friend, brother, son,
 heaven dooms mortal, will done:
 awhile sorrow, dismiss care;
 fate gives wound, man born bear.
 insatiate, commission given
 fate exceeds, tempts wrath heaven:
 lo, rage dishonest drags along
 hector’s dead earth, insensible wrong!
 brave though be, yet reason awed,
 violates laws man god.”
 

[illustration: ] judgment paris
 

“if equal honours partial skies
 doom’d heroes, (juno thus replies,)
 thetis’ must distinction know,
 hear, ye gods! patron bow.
 hector boasts mortal claim,
 birth deriving mortal dame:
 achilles, ethereal race,
 springs goddess man’s embrace
 (a goddess ourself peleus given,
 man divine, chosen friend heaven)
 grace nuptials, bright abode
 present; minstrel-god,
 well pleased share feast, amid quire
 stood proud hymn, tune youthful lyre.”
 
thus thunderer checks imperial dame:
 “let thy wrath court heaven inflame;
 merits, honours, same.
 mine, every god’s peculiar grace
 hector deserves, trojan race:
 still shrines grateful offerings lay,
 (the honours men gods can pay,)
 ever smoking altar ceased
 pure libation, holy feast:
 howe’er stealth snatch corse away,
 will not: thetis guards night day.
 haste, summon courts above
 azure queen; let persuasion move
 furious priam receive
 proffer’d ransom, corse leave.”
 
added not: iris skies,
 swift whirlwind, message flies,
 meteorous face ocean sweeps,
 refulgent gliding o’er sable deeps.
 samos wide forests spreads,
 rocky imbrus lifts pointed heads,
 plunged maid; (the parted waves resound;)
 plunged instant shot dark profound.
 bearing death fallacious bait,
 bent angle sinks leaden weight;
 pass’d goddess closing wave,
 thetis sorrow’d secret cave:
 placed amidst melancholy train
 (the blue-hair’d sisters sacred main)
 pensive sat, revolving fates come,
 wept godlike son’s approaching doom.
 thus goddess painted bow:
 “arise, thetis! thy seats below,
 ’tis jove calls.”—“and (the dame replies)
 calls jove thetis hated skies?
 sad object heavenly sight!
 ah may sorrows ever shun light!
 howe’er, heaven’s almighty sire obey’d—”
 spake, veil’d head sable shade,
 which, flowing long, graceful person clad;
 forth paced, majestically sad.
 
world waters repair
 (the way fair iris led) upper air.
 deeps dividing, o’er coast rise,
 touch momentary flight skies.
 lightning’s blaze sire found,
 gods shining synod round.
 thetis approach’d anguish face,
 (minerva rising, gave mourner place,)
 even juno sought sorrows console,
 offer’d hand nectar-bowl:
 tasted, resign’d it: began
 sacred sire gods mortal man:
 
“thou comest, fair thetis, grief o’ercast;
 maternal sorrows; long, ah, long last!
 suffice, know partake thy cares;
 yield fate, hear jove declares.
 nine days past since court above
 hector’s cause moved ear jove;
 ’twas voted, hermes godlike foe
 stealth bear him, will’d so:
 will, thy corse restore,
 conquest add glory more.
 hie thee him, mandate bear:
 tell tempts wrath heaven far;
 let (our anger dread)
 vent mad vengeance sacred dead;
 yield ransom father’s prayer;
 mournful father, iris shall prepare
 gifts sue; offer hands
 whate’er honour asks, heart demands.”
 
word silver-footed queen attends,
 olympus’ snowy tops descends.
 arrived, heard voice loud lament,
 echoing groans shook lofty tent:
 friends prepare victim, dispose
 repast unheeded, vents woes;
 goddess seats pensive son,
 press’d hand, tender thus begun:
 
“how long, unhappy! shall thy sorrows flow,
 thy heart waste life-consuming woe:
 mindless food, love, whose pleasing reign
 soothes weary life, softens human pain?
 snatch moments yet within thy power;
 long live, indulge amorous hour!
 lo! jove (for jove’s command bear)
 forbids tempt wrath heaven far.
 longer (his fury thou dread)
 detain relics great hector dead;
 vent senseless earth thy vengeance vain,
 yield ransom, restore slain.”
 
achilles: “be ransom given,
 submit, since will heaven.”
 
thus communed, olympian bowers
 jove orders iris trojan towers:
 “haste, winged goddess! sacred town,
 urge monarch redeem son.
 alone ilian ramparts let leave,
 bear stern achilles may receive:
 alone, will; trojan near
 except, place dead decent care,
 aged herald, gentle hand
 may slow mules funeral car command.
 let death, let danger dread,
 safe foe protection led:
 hermes achilles shall convey,
 guard life, partner way.
 fierce is, achilles’ self shall spare
 age, touch one venerable hair:
 thought must soul brave,
 sense duty, desire save.”
 

[illustration: ] iris advises priam obtain body hector
 

bow winged iris drives,
 swift priam’s mournful court arrives:
 sad sons beside father’s throne
 sat bathed tears, answer’d groan groan.
 amidst lay hoary sire,
 (sad scene woe!) face wrapp’d attire
 conceal’d sight; frantic hands spread
 shower ashes o’er neck head.
 room room pensive daughters roam;
 whose shrieks clamours fill vaulted dome;
 mindful those, late pride joy,
 lie pale breathless round fields troy!
 king jove’s messenger appears,
 thus whispers greets trembling ears:
 
“fear not, father! ill news bear;
 jove come, jove makes thee still care;
 hector’s sake walls bids thee leave,
 bear stern achilles may receive;
 alone, wills; trojan near,
 except, place dead decent care,
 aged herald, gentle hand
 may slow mules funeral car command.
 shalt thou death, shalt thou danger dread:
 safe foe protection led:
 thee hermes pelides shall convey,
 guard thy life, partner thy way.
 fierce is, achilles’ self shall spare
 thy age, touch one venerable hair;
 thought must soul brave,
 sense duty, desire save.”
 
spoke, vanish’d. priam bids prepare
 gentle mules harness car;
 there, gifts, polish’d casket lay:
 pious sons king’s command obey.
 pass’d monarch bridal-room,
 cedar-beams lofty roofs perfume,
 treasures empire lay;
 call’d queen, thus began say:
 
“unhappy consort king distress’d!
 partake troubles thy husband’s breast:
 saw descend messenger jove,
 bids try achilles’ mind move;
 forsake ramparts, gifts obtain
 corse hector, yon navy slain.
 tell thy thought: heart impels go
 hostile camps, bears foe.”
 
hoary monarch thus. piercing cries
 sad hecuba renews, replies:
 “ah! whither wanders thy distemper’d mind?
 prudence now awed mankind?
 phrygia foreign regions known;
 now confused, distracted, overthrown!
 singly pass hosts foes! face
 (o heart steel!) murderer thy race!
 view deathful eye, wander o’er
 hands yet red hector’s noble gore!
 alas! lord! knows spare,
 mercy, thy slain sons declare;
 brave! many fallen! claim rage
 vain thy dignity, vain thy age.
 no—pent sad palace, let us give
 grief wretched days live.
 still, still hector let sorrows flow,
 born own, parents’ woe!
 doom’d hour luckless life begun,
 dogs, vultures, peleus’ son!
 oh! dearest blood might allay
 rage, barbarities repay!
 ah! hector merit thus, whose breath
 expired meanly, unactive death?
 poured latest blood manly fight,
 fell hero country’s right.”
 
“seek stay me, soul affright
 words omen, like bird night,
 (replied unmoved venerable man;)
 ’tis heaven commands me, urge vain.
 mortal voice injunction laid,
 augur, priest, seer, obey’d.
 present goddess brought high command,
 saw, heard her, word shall stand.
 go, ye gods! obedient call:
 yon camp powers doom’d fall,
 content—by hand let expire!
 add slaughter’d wretched sire!
 one cold embrace least may allow’d,
 last tears flow mingled blood!”
 
forth open’d stores, said, drew
 twelve costly carpets refulgent hue,
 many vests, many mantles told,
 twelve fair veils, garments stiff gold,
 two tripods next, twice two chargers shine,
 ten pure talents richest mine;
 last large well-labour’d bowl place,
 (the pledge treaties friendly thrace:)
 seem’d mean stores employ,
 one last look buy back troy!
 
lo! sad father, frantic pain,
 around furious drives menial train:
 vain slave duteous care attends,
 office hurts him, face offends.
 “what make ye here, officious crowds! (he cries):
 hence! obtrude anguish eyes.
 ye griefs home, fix ye there:
 object despair?
 become people’s common show,
 set jove spectacle woe?
 no, must feel too; must fall;
 stern god ruin gives all:
 great hector lost alone;
 sole defence, guardian power gone!
 see blood fields phrygia drown,
 see ruins smoking town!
 send me, gods! ere sad day shall come,
 willing ghost pluto’s dreary dome!”
 
said, feebly drives friends away:
 sorrowing friends frantic rage obey.
 next sons erring fury falls,
 polites, paris, agathon, calls;
 threats deiphobus dius hear,
 hippothous, pammon, helenes seer,
 generous antiphon: yet nine
 survived, sad relics numerous line.
 
“inglorious sons unhappy sire!
 hector’s cause expire?
 wretch am! bravest offspring slain.
 you, disgrace priam’s house, remain!
 mestor brave, renown’d ranks war,
 troilus, dreadful rushing car,[293]
 last great hector, man divine,
 sure seem’d terrestrial line!
 relentless mars untimely slew,
 left these, soft servile crew,
 whose days feast wanton dance employ,
 gluttons flatterers, contempt troy!
 teach ye rapid wheels run,
 speed journey redeem son?”
 
sons father’s wretched age revere,
 forgive anger, produce car.
 high seat cabinet bind:
 new-made car solid beauty shined;
 box yoke, emboss’d costly pains,
 hung ringlets receive reins;
 nine cubits long, traces swept ground:
 chariot’s polish’d pole bound.
 fix’d ring running reins guide,
 close beneath gather’d ends tied.
 next gifts (the price hector slain)
 sad attendants load groaning wain:
 last yoke well-matched mules bring,
 (the gift mysia trojan king.)
 fair horses, long darling care,
 received, harness’d car:
 grieved was, task denied;
 hoary herald help’d him, side.
 careful gentle coursers join’d,
 sad hecuba approach’d anxious mind;
 golden bowl foam’d fragrant wine,
 (libation destined power divine,)
 held right, steed stands,
 thus consigns monarch’s hands:
 
“take this, pour jove; safe harms
 grace restore thee roof arms.
 since victor thy fears, slighting mine,
 heaven, thy soul, inspires bold design;
 pray god, high ida’s brow
 surveys thy desolated realms below,
 winged messenger send high,
 lead thy way heavenly augury:
 let strong sovereign plumy race
 tower right yon ethereal space.
 sign beheld, strengthen’d above,
 boldly pursue journey mark’d jove:
 god augury denies,
 suppress thy impulse, reject advice.”
 
“’tis just (said priam) sire above
 raise hands; good jove?”
 spoke, bade attendant handmaid bring
 purest water living spring:
 (her ready hands ewer bason held:)
 took golden cup queen fill’d;
 mid pavement pours rosy wine,
 uplifts eyes, calls power divine:
 
“o first greatest! heaven’s imperial lord!
 lofty ida’s holy hill adored!
 stern achilles now direct ways,
 teach mercy father prays.
 thy will, despatch yonder sky
 thy sacred bird, celestial augury!
 let strong sovereign plumy race
 tower right yon ethereal space;
 shall thy suppliant, strengthen’d above,
 fearless pursue journey mark’d jove.”
 
jove heard prayer, throne high,
 despatch’d bird, celestial augury!
 swift-wing’d chaser feather’d game,
 known gods percnos’ lofty name.
 wide appears palace-gate display’d,
 broad, pinions stretch’d ample shade,
 stooping dexter resounding wings
 imperial bird descends airy rings.
 dawn joy every face appears:
 mourning matron dries timorous tears:
 swift car impatient monarch sprung;
 brazen portal passage rung;
 mules preceding draw loaded wain,
 charged gifts: idæus holds rein:
 king gentle steeds controls,
 surrounding friends chariot rolls.
 slow wheels following people wait,
 mourn step, give fate;
 hands uplifted eye pass’d,
 gaze upon gazed last.
 now forward fares father way,
 lone fields, back ilion they.
 great jove beheld cross’d plain,
 felt woes miserable man.
 thus hermes: “thou whose constant cares
 still succour mortals, attend prayers;
 behold object thy charge consign’d:
 ever pity touch’d thee mankind,
 go, guard sire: observing foe prevent,
 safe conduct achilles’ tent.”
 
god obeys, golden pinions binds,[294]
 mounts incumbent wings winds,
 high, fields air, flight sustain,
 o’er wide earth, o’er boundless main;
 grasps wand causes sleep fly,
 soft slumbers seals wakeful eye:
 thus arm’d, swift hermes steers airy way,
 stoops hellespont’s resounding sea.
 beauteous youth, majestic divine,
 seem’d; fair offspring princely line!
 now twilight veil’d glaring face day,
 clad dusky fields sober grey;
 time herald hoary king
 (their chariots stopping silver spring,
 circling ilus’ ancient marble flows)
 allow’d mules steeds short repose,
 dim shade herald first espies
 man’s approach, thus priam cries:
 “i mark foe’s advance: king! beware;
 hard adventure claims thy utmost care!
 much fear destruction hovers nigh:
 state asks counsel; best fly?
 old helpless, feet fall,
 two wretched suppliants, mercy call?”
 
afflicted monarch shiver’d despair;
 pale grew face, upright stood hair;
 sunk heart; colour went came;
 sudden trembling shook aged frame:
 hermes, greeting, touch’d royal hand,
 and, gentle, thus accosts kind demand:
 
“say whither, father! mortal sight
 seal’d sleep, thou wanderest night?
 roam thy mules steeds plains along,
 grecian foes, numerous strong?
 couldst thou hope, thy treasures view;
 these, endless hate thy race pursue?
 defence, alas! could’st thou provide;
 thyself young, weak old man thy guide?
 yet suffer thy soul sink dread;
 harm shall touch thy reverend head;
 greece i’ll guard thee too; lines
 living image father shines.”
 
“thy words, speak benevolence mind,
 true, son! (the godlike sire rejoin’d:)
 great hazards; gods survey
 steps, send thee, guardian way.
 hail, bless’d! scarce mortal kind
 appear thy form, thy feature, thy mind.”
 
“nor true thy words, erring wide;
 (the sacred messenger heaven replied;)
 say, convey’st thou lonely plains
 yet precious thy store remains,
 lodge safety friendly hand:
 prepared, perchance, leave thy native land?
 fliest thou now?—what hopes can troy retain,
 thy matchless son, guard glory, slain?”
 
king, alarm’d: “say what, whence thou art
 search sorrows parent’s heart,
 know well godlike hector died?”
 thus priam spoke, hermes thus replied:
 
“you tempt me, father, pity touch:
 sad subject inquire much.
 oft eyes godlike hector view’d
 glorious fight, grecian blood embrued:
 saw when, like jove, flames toss’d
 thousand ships, wither’d half host:
 saw, help’d not: stern achilles’ ire
 forbade assistance, enjoy’d fire.
 serve, myrmidonian race;
 one ship convey’d us native place;
 polyctor sire, honour’d name,
 old like thyself, unknown fame;
 seven sons, lot cast
 serve prince, fell me, last.
 watch quarter, adventure falls:
 morn greeks attack walls;
 sleepless sit, impatient engage,
 scarce rulers check martial rage.”
 
“if thou art stern pelides’ train,
 (the mournful monarch thus rejoin’d again,)
 ah tell truly, where, oh! laid
 son’s dear relics? befalls dead?
 dogs dismember’d (on naked plains),
 yet unmangled rest, cold remains?”
 
“o favour’d skies! (thus answered then
 power mediates god men)
 dogs vultures thy hector rent,
 whole lies, neglected tent:
 twelfth evening since rested there,
 untouch’d worms, untainted air.
 still aurora’s ruddy beam spread,
 round friend’s tomb achilles drags dead:
 yet undisfigured, limb face,
 fresh lies, every living grace,
 majestical death! stains found
 o’er corse, closed every wound,
 though many wound gave. heavenly care,
 hand divine, preserves ever fair:
 host heaven, led
 life grateful, still regard dead.”
 
thus spoke priam celestial guide,
 joyful thus royal sire replied:
 “blest man pays gods above
 constant tribute respect love!
 inhabit olympian bower
 forgot not, exalted power;
 heaven, every virtue bears mind,
 even ashes just kind.
 thou, generous youth! goblet take,
 pledge gratitude hector’s sake;
 favouring gods steps survey,
 safe pelides’ tent conduct way.”
 
latent god: “o king, forbear
 tempt youth, apt youth err.
 can i, absent prince’s sight,
 take gifts secret, must shun light?
 master’s interest thus draw,
 licensed theft ’scapes law.
 respecting him, soul abjures offence;
 crime, dread consequence.
 thee, far argos, pleased convey;
 guard thy life, partner thy way:
 thee attend, thy safety maintain,
 o’er pathless forests, roaring main.”
 
said, took chariot bound,
 snatch’d reins, whirl’d lash around:
 inspiring god urged on,
 coursers fly spirit own.
 now reach’d naval walls, found
 guards repasting, bowls go round;
 virtue wand tries,
 pours deep slumber watchful eyes:
 heaved massy gates, removed bars,
 o’er trenches led rolling cars.
 unseen, hostile camp went,
 now approach’d pelides’ lofty tent.
 firs roof raised, cover’d o’er
 reeds collected marshy shore;
 and, fenced palisades, hall state,
 (the work soldiers,) hero sat:
 large door, whose well-compacted strength
 solid pine-tree barr’d wondrous length:
 scarce three strong greeks lift mighty weight,
 great achilles singly closed gate.
 hermes (such power gods) set wide;
 swift alighted celestial guide,
 thus reveal’d—”hear, prince! understand
 thou ow’st thy guidance mortal hand:
 hermes am, descended above,
 king arts, messenger jove,
 farewell: shun achilles’ sight fly;
 uncommon favours sky,
 stand confess’d frail mortality.
 now fearless enter, prefer thy prayers;
 adjure father’s silver hairs,
 son, mother! urge bestow
 whatever pity stern heart can know.”
 
thus said, vanish’d eyes,
 moment shot skies:
 king, confirm’d heaven, alighted there,
 left aged herald car,
 solemn pace various rooms went,
 found achilles inner tent:
 sat hero: alcimus brave,
 great automedon, attendance gave:
 served person royal feast;
 around, awful distance, stood rest.
 
unseen these, king entry made:
 and, prostrate now achilles laid,
 sudden (a venerable sight!) appears;
 embraced knees, bathed hands tears;
 direful hands kisses press’d, embrued
 even best, dearest blood!
 
wretch (who, conscious crime,
 pursued murder, flies native clime)
 just gains frontier, breathless, pale, amazed,
 gaze, wonder: thus achilles gazed:
 thus stood attendants stupid surprise:
 mute, yet seem’d question eyes:
 look’d other, none silence broke,
 till thus last kingly suppliant spoke:
 
“ah think, thou favour’d powers divine![295]
 think thy father’s age, pity mine!
 father’s reverend image trace,
 silver hairs, venerable face;
 trembling limbs, helpless person, see!
 equal, misery!
 yet now, perhaps, turn human fate
 expels helpless peaceful state;
 think, powerful foe thou seest fly,
 beg protection feeble cry.
 yet still one comfort soul may rise;
 hears still lives glad eyes,
 and, hearing, still may hope better day
 may send thee, chase foe away.
 comfort griefs, hopes remain,
 best, bravest, sons slain!
 yet race! ere greece ilion came,
 pledge many loved loving dame:
 nineteen one mother bore—dead, dead!
 oft, alas! wretched priam bled!
 still one left loss recompense;
 father’s hope, country’s last defence.
 thy rage slain! beneath thy steel,
 unhappy country’s cause fell!
 
“for hostile camps bent way,
 thus prostrate thy feet lay;
 large gifts proportion’d thy wrath bear;
 hear wretched, gods revere!
 
“think thy father, face behold!
 see me, helpless old!
 though wretched: yields me,
 first men sovereign misery!
 thus forced kneel, thus grovelling embrace
 scourge ruin realm race;
 suppliant children’s murderer implore,
 kiss hands yet reeking gore!”
 
words soft pity chief inspire,
 touch’d dear remembrance sire.
 hand (as prostrate still lay)
 old man’s cheek gently turn’d away.
 now turns indulged gush woe;
 now mingled tides together flow:
 low earth, gently bending o’er;
 father one, one deplore:
 great achilles different passions rend,
 now sire mourns, now friend.
 infectious softness heroes ran;
 one universal solemn shower began;
 bore heroes, felt man.
 
satiate length unavailing woes,
 high throne divine achilles rose;
 reverend monarch hand raised;
 white beard form majestic gazed,
 unrelenting; serene began
 words soothe miserable man:
 
“alas, weight anguish hast thou known,
 unhappy prince! thus guardless alone
 pass foes, thus undaunted face
 man whose fury destroy’d thy race!
 heaven sure arm’d thee heart steel,
 strength proportion’d woes feel.
 rise, then: let reason mitigate care:
 mourn avails not: man born bear.
 is, alas! gods’ severe decree:
 they, blest, free.
 two urns jove’s high throne ever stood,
 source evil one, one good;
 thence cup mortal man fills,
 blessings these, distributes ill;
 mingles both: wretch decreed
 taste bad unmix’d, cursed indeed;
 pursued wrongs, meagre famine driven,
 wanders, outcast earth heaven.
 happiest taste happiness sincere;
 find cordial draught dash’d care.
 peleus shone wealth power
 stars concurring bless’d natal hour!
 realm, goddess, wishes given;
 graced gods gifts heaven.
 one evil yet o’ertakes latest day:
 race succeeding imperial sway;
 son; he, alas! ordain’d
 fall untimely foreign land.
 see him, troy, pious care decline
 weak age, live curse thine!
 thou too, old man, hast happier days beheld;
 riches once, children excell’d;
 extended phrygia own’d thy ample reign,
 fair lesbos’ blissful seats contain,
 wide hellespont’s unmeasured main.
 since god hand pleased turn,
 fill thy measure bitter urn,
 sees sun, hapless heroes’ falls?
 war, blood men, surround thy walls!
 must be, must be. bear thy lot, shed
 unavailing sorrows o’er dead;
 thou canst call stygian shore,
 thou, alas! may’st live suffer more!”
 
king: “o favour’d skies!
 let grow earth! since hector lies
 bare beach deprived obsequies.
 give hector! eyes restore
 corse, take gifts: ask more.
 thou, thou may’st, boundless stores enjoy;
 safe may’st thou sail, turn thy wrath troy;
 shall thy pity forbearance give
 weak old man see light live!”
 
“move more, (achilles thus replies,
 kindling anger sparkled eyes,)
 seek tears steady soul bend:
 yield thy hector intend:
 know, jove goddess-mother came,
 (old ocean’s daughter, silver-footed dame,)
 comest thou heaven; comest alone,
 god impels courage thy own:
 human hand weighty gates unbarr’d,
 boldest youth dared
 pass outworks, elude guard.
 cease; lest, neglectful high jove’s command,
 show thee, king! thou tread’st hostile land;
 release knees, thy suppliant arts give o’er,
 shake purpose soul more.”
 
sire obey’d him, trembling o’eraw’d.
 achilles, like lion, rush’d abroad:
 automedon alcimus attend,
 (whom honour’d, since lost friend,)
 unyoke mules horses went,
 led hoary herald tent;
 next, heap’d high, numerous presents bear,
 (great hector’s ransom,) polish’d car.
 two splendid mantles, carpet spread,
 leave: cover enwrap dead.
 call handmaids, assistant toil
 wash body anoint oil,
 apart priam: lest unhappy sire,
 provoked passion, rouse ire
 stern pelides; sacred age,
 jove’s command, check rising rage.
 done, garments o’er corse spread;
 achilles lifts funeral bed:
 then, body car laid,
 groans, calls loved patroclus’ shade:
 
“if, gloom never light must know,
 deeds mortals touch ghosts below,
 friend! forgive me, thus fulfil
 (restoring hector) heaven’s unquestion’d will.
 gifts father gave, ever thine,
 grace thy manes, adorn thy shrine.”[296]
 
said, and, entering, took seat state;
 full reverend priam sate;
 whom, composed, godlike chief begun:
 “lo! thy prayer restored, thy breathless son;
 extended funeral couch lies;
 soon morning paints eastern skies,
 sight granted thy longing eyes:
 now peaceful hours sacred night
 demand reflection, rest invite:
 thou, father! thus consumed woe,
 common cares nourish life forego.
 thus niobe, form divine,
 parent once, whose sorrows equall’d thine:
 six youthful sons, many blooming maids,
 one sad day beheld stygian shades;
 apollo’s silver bow slain,
 these, cynthia’s arrows stretch’d upon plain:
 pride chastised wrath divine,
 match’d bright latona’s line;
 two goddess, twelve queen enjoy’d;
 boasted twelve, avenging two destroy’d.
 steep’d blood, dust outspread,
 nine days, neglected, lay exposed dead;
 none weep them, inhume none;
 (for jove turn’d nation stone.)
 gods themselves, length relenting gave
 unhappy race honours grave.
 rock (for heaven’s high will)
 deserts wild now pours weeping rill;
 round bed whence achelous springs,
 watery fairies dance mazy rings;
 high sipylus’s shaggy brow,
 stands, sad monument woe;
 rock ever lasts, tears ever flow.
 
“such griefs, king! parents known;
 remember theirs, mitigate thy own.
 care heaven thy hector appear’d,
 shall lie unwept, uninterr’d;
 soon may thy aged cheeks tears drown’d,
 eyes ilion stream around.”
 
said, and, rising, chose victim ewe
 silver fleece, attendants slew.
 limbs sever reeking hide,
 skill prepare them, parts divide:
 coals separate morsels lays,
 and, hasty, snatches rising blaze.
 bread glittering canisters load,
 round board automedon bestow’d.
 chief portion placed,
 indulging shared sweet repast.
 now rage hunger repress’d,
 wondering hero eyes royal guest:
 less royal guest hero eyes,
 godlike aspect majestic size;
 here, youthful grace noble fire engage;
 there, mild benevolence age.
 thus gazing long, silence neither broke,
 (a solemn scene!) length father spoke:
 
“permit now, beloved jove! steep
 careful temples dew sleep:
 for, since day number’d dead
 hapless son, dust bed;
 soft sleep stranger weeping eyes;
 food, sorrows sighs!
 till now, encouraged grace give,
 share thy banquet, consent live.”
 
that, achilles bade prepare bed,
 purple soft shaggy carpets spread;
 forth, flaming lights, bend way,
 place couches, coverings lay.
 he: “now, father, sleep, sleep here;
 consult thy safety, forgive fear,
 lest argive, hour awake,
 ask counsel, orders take,
 approaching sudden open’d tent,
 perchance behold thee, grace prevent.
 report thy honour’d person here,
 king men ransom might defer;
 say speed, aught thy desire
 remains unask’d; time rites require
 inter thy hector? for, long stay
 slaughtering arm, bid hosts obey.”
 
“if thy will permit (the monarch said)
 finish due honours dead,
 thy grace accord: thee known
 fears ilion, closed within town;
 distance walls aspire
 hills ide, forests fire.
 nine days vent sorrows request,
 tenth shall see funeral feast;
 next, raise monument given;
 twelfth war, war doom’d heaven!”
 
“this thy request (replied chief) enjoy:
 till arms suspend fall troy.”
 
gave hand parting, prevent
 old man’s fears, turn’d within tent;
 fair briseïs, bright blooming charms,
 expects hero desiring arms.
 porch king herald rest;
 sad dreams care yet wandering breast.
 now gods men gifts sleep partake;
 industrious hermes awake,
 king’s return revolving mind,
 pass ramparts, watch blind.
 power descending hover’d o’er head:
 “and sleep’st thou, father! (thus vision said:)
 now dost thou sleep, hector restored?
 fear grecian foes, grecian lord?
 thy presence stern atrides see,
 thy still surviving sons may sue thee;
 may offer thy treasures yet contain,
 spare thy age; offer vain.”
 
waked word trembling sire arose,
 raised friend: god goes:
 joins mules, directs hand,
 moves silence hostile land.
 now xanthus’ yellow stream drove,
 (xanthus, immortal progeny jove,)
 winged deity forsook view,
 moment olympus flew.
 now shed aurora round saffron ray,
 sprang gates light, gave day:
 charged mournful load, ilion go
 sage king, majestically slow.
 cassandra first beholds, ilion’s spire,
 sad procession hoary sire;
 then, pensive pomp advanced near,
 (her breathless brother stretched upon bier,)
 shower tears o’erflows beauteous eyes,
 alarming thus ilion cries:
 
“turn steps, eyes employ,
 ye wretched daughters, ye sons troy!
 e’er ye rush’d crowds, vast delight,
 hail hero glorious fight,
 now meet dead, let sorrows flow;
 common triumph, common woe.”
 
thronging crowds issue plains;
 man woman walls remains;
 every face self-same grief shown;
 troy sends forth one universal groan.
 scæa’s gates meet mourning wain,
 hang wheels, grovel round slain.
 wife mother, frantic despair,
 kiss pale cheek, rend scatter’d hair:
 thus wildly wailing, gates lay;
 sigh’d sorrow’d day;
 godlike priam chariot rose:
 “forbear (he cried) violence woes;
 first palace let car proceed,
 pour boundless sorrows o’er dead.”
 
waves people word divide,
 slow rolls chariot following tide;
 even palace sad pomp wait:
 weep, place bed state.
 melancholy choir attend around,
 plaintive sighs, music’s solemn sound:
 alternately sing, alternate flow
 obedient tears, melodious woe.
 deeper sorrows groan full heart,
 nature speaks every pause art.
 
first corse weeping consort flew;
 around neck milk-white arms threw,
 “and oh, hector! oh, lord! (she cries)
 snatch’d thy bloom desiring eyes!
 thou dismal realms ever gone!
 abandon’d, desolate, alone!
 son, comfort pains,
 sad product now hapless love, remains!
 never manly age shall rise,
 increasing graces glad eyes:
 ilion now (her great defender slain)
 shall sink smoking ruin plain.
 now protects wives guardian care?
 saves infants rage war?
 now hostile fleets must waft infants o’er
 (those wives must wait them) foreign shore:
 thou too, son, barbarous climes shall go,
 sad companion thy mother’s woe;
 driven hence slave victor’s sword
 condemn’d toil inhuman lord:
 else greek whose father press’d plain,
 son, brother, great hector slain,
 hector’s blood vengeance shall enjoy,
 hurl thee headlong towers troy.[297]
 thy stern father never spared foe:
 thence tears, scene woe!
 thence many evils sad parents bore,
 parents many, consort more.
 gav’st thou thy dying hand?
 received thy last command?
 word thou would’st spoke, which, sadly dear,
 soul might keep, utter tear;
 never, never lost air,
 fix’d heart, oft repeated there!”
 
thus weeping maids makes moan,
 weeping handmaids echo groan groan.
 
mournful mother next sustains part:
 “o thou, best, dearest heart!
 race thou heaven approved,
 immortals even death beloved!
 sons barbarous bands
 achilles bound, sold foreign lands,
 felt chains, went glorious ghost,
 free, hero, stygian coast.
 sentenced, ’tis true, inhuman doom,
 thy noble corse dragg’d around tomb;
 (the tomb thy warlike arm slain;)
 ungenerous insult, impotent vain!
 yet glow’st thou fresh every living grace;
 mark pain, violence face:
 rosy fair! phœbus’ silver bow
 dismiss’d thee gently shades below.”
 
thus spoke dame, melted tears.
 sad helen next pomp grief appears;
 fast shining sluices eyes
 fall round crystal drops, thus cries.
 
“ah, dearest friend! gods join’d[298]
 mildest manners bravest mind,
 now twice ten years (unhappy years) o’er
 since paris brought trojan shore,
 (o perish’d, ere form divine
 seduced soft, easy heart mine!)
 yet ne’er fate, thee find
 deed ungentle, word unkind.
 others cursed authoress woe,
 thy pity check’d sorrows flow.
 proud brother eyed disdain,
 scornful sister sweeping train,
 thy gentle accents soften’d pain.
 thee mourn, mourn thee,
 wretched source misery.
 fate caused, ever bemoan;
 sad helen friend, now thou art gone!
 troy’s wide streets abandon’d shall roam!
 troy deserted, abhorr’d home!”
 
spoke fair, sorrow-streaming eye.
 distressful beauty melts stander-by.
 around infectious sorrow grows;
 priam check’d torrent rose:
 “perform, ye trojans! rites require,
 fell forests funeral pyre;
 twelve days, foes secret ambush dread;
 achilles grants honours dead.”[299]
 

[illustration: ] funeral hector
 

spoke, and, word, trojan train
 mules oxen harness wain,
 pour gates, fell’d ida’s crown,
 roll back gather’d forests town.
 toils continue nine succeeding days,
 high air sylvan structure raise.
 tenth fair morn began shine,
 forth pile borne man divine,
 placed aloft; all, streaming eyes,
 beheld flames rolling smokes arise.
 soon aurora, daughter dawn,
 rosy lustre streak’d dewy lawn,
 mournful crowds surround pyre,
 quench wine yet remaining fire.
 snowy bones friends brothers place
 (with tears collected) golden vase;
 golden vase purple palls roll’d,
 softest texture, inwrought gold.
 last o’er urn sacred earth spread,
 raised tomb, memorial dead.
 (strong guards spies, till rites done,
 watch’d rising setting sun.)
 troy moves priam’s court again,
 solemn, silent, melancholy train:
 assembled there, pious toil rest,
 sadly shared last sepulchral feast.
 honours ilion hero paid,
 peaceful slept mighty hector’s shade.[300]

[40] following argument iliad, corrected few
 particulars, translated bitaubé, is, perhaps, neatest
 summary ever drawn up:—“a hero, injured general,
 animated noble resentment, retires tent; a
 season withdraws troops war. this
 interval, victory abandons army, nine years been
 occupied great enterprise, upon successful termination of
 honour country depends. general, length
 opening eyes fault committed, deputes the
 principal officers army incensed hero, commission
 make compensation injury, tender magnificent
 presents. hero, according proud obstinacy character,
 persists animosity; army defeated, the
 verge entire destruction. inexorable man friend; this
 friend weeps him, asks hero’s arms, for
 permission go war stead. eloquence friendship
 prevails intercession ambassadors gifts of
 general. lends armour friend, commands not
 engage chief enemy’s army, reserves to
 honour combat, also fears his
 friend’s life. prohibition forgotten; friend listens to
 nothing courage; corpse brought back hero, and
 hero’s arms become prize conqueror. hero,
 given lively despair, prepares fight; receives
 divinity new armour, reconciled general and,
 thirsting glory revenge, enacts prodigies valour, recovers
 victory, slays enemy’s chief, honours friend superb
 funeral rites, exercises cruel vengeance body his
 destroyer; finally appeased tears prayers father
 slain warrior, restores old man corpse son,
 buries due solemnities.’—coleridge, p. 177, sqq.

[245] _the destinies ordain_.—“in mythology, also, iliad,
 purely pagan is, discover one important truth unconsciously
 involved, almost entirely lost view amidst nearly
 equal scepticism credulity subsequent ages. zeus jupiter is
 popularly taken omnipotent. distinct empire assigned to
 fate fortune; will father gods men absolute
 uncontrollable. seems true character homeric
 deity, necessary student greek literature
 bear constantly mind. strong instance iliad
 illustrate position, passage jupiter
 laments juno approaching death sarpedon. ‘alas me!’ says he
 ‘since fated (moira) sarpedon, dearest men, should
 slain patroclus, menoetius! indeed, heart is
 divided within ruminate mind, whether having
 snatched lamentable battle, at
 place alive fertile land lycia, whether
 now destroy hands menoetius!’ to
 juno answers—‘dost thou mean rescue death mortal man,
 long since destined fate (palai pepromenon)? may it—but we,
 rest gods, sanction it.’ clear both
 speakers, although sarpedon said fated die, jupiter
 might still, pleased, save him, place entirely of
 reach event, further, alternative, that
 jupiter destroy hands another.”—coleridge,
 p. 156. seq.
